# 3.31 Scheduling of L1 Processing Resources

## 3.31.0-3 Scheduling of L1 Processing Resources Document Owner Deputy Hao Chen; Shuangping Liao (ID: 11209838)

## 3.31.1 L1 Resource Allocator

### 3.31.1.0-1 L1 Resource Allocator Buffered UL for TDD in L1 Resource Allocator (ID: 11209853)

**3.31.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13449242`)

L1 Resource Allocator
When Buffered UL is used, as one function of "L1 Resource Allocator" in 5G-L2-PS starts scheduling L1 Processing Resources.

From Buffered UL point of view, L1 Resource Allocator shall perform an algorithm to select how many subcells shall be handled in RT in each cell (this algorithm is called "Buffered UL - Algo1"). Requirements are provided under 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5201\_replaced([11209903](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw2W6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall assume that Buffered UL is used when buffer UL feature is allowed (NRBTS.actTddPrePooling set to true)  [Before CNI-136563] OR when R&D parameter rdBufferedUlMode (see 5G\_L2\_1232\_replaced([11188091](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ4fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to “2: Test”  [End CNI-136563]

When Buffered UL is used, and if there are multiple subcells in a single cell, 5G-L2-PS shall perform slot level RT/NRT subcell selection inside a cell (this algorithm is called "Buffered UL - Algo2"). Requirements are provided under 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5214\_replaced([11209976](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw298fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When Buffered UL is used, 5G-L2-PS shall decide in which DL NR-slot the UL data shall be processed for the buffered subcells (this algorithm is called "Buffered UL - Algo3"). Requirements are provided under 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5216\_replaced([11209990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw298_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Buffered UL is only applicable for TDD FR1 gNB with Loner L1 HW.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

### 3.31.1.0-2 L1 Resource Allocator Subcell pooling for TDD in L1 Resource Allocator (ID: 11209864)

**3.31.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13455940`)

L1 Resource Allocator
When Subcell pooling **is used, as one function of "L1 Resource Allocator" in 5G-L2-PS starts scheduling L1 Processing Resources.**

From Subcell pooling (spatial stream pooling) point of view, L1 Resource Allocator shall perform an algorithm to select how many subcells are available for usage in each cell. The pooled subcell shall be used only by one cell on each NR-slot (i.e. minimum time granularity for the control is one NR-slot in L1).

5G-L2-PS shall assume that Subcell pooling is used when all of the below conditions are true:

* spatialStreamPoolingAllowed ==TRUE in PsCnfg\_AddressDistributionReq (see NRBTS.actSpatialStreamPooling)
* there are multiple subcells configured with the same dlSubcellPoolId/ulSubcellPoolId
* For cells that run on Loner L1 HW, bufferedUlAllowed==TRUE in PsCnfg\_AddressDistributionReq (see 5G\_UP\_1736\_replaced([11372408](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ud9QMPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [Before CNI-136563] and R&D parameter rdBufferedUlMode (see 5G\_L2\_1232\_replaced([11188091](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ4fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to “1: MetricBased" [End CNI-136563].

For cells that run on Loki **L1 HW, bufferedUlAllowed==FALSE in PsCnfg\_AddressDistributionReq (see 5G\_UP\_1736\_replaced([11372408](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ud9QMPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

If any of the above conditions is not fulfilled, the subcell which has the same subcellPoolId among multiple cells, shall NOT be used by 5G-L2-PS in any cell.

For cells that run on Loner L1 HW, there are two cases for the subcell pooling to be supported by 5GC002411 BB block feature:

Case1: Only UL subcell is pooled between 2 (\*) or 3 cells. There is no pooled DL subcell.

Case2: Both DL and UL subcells are pooled between 2 (\*) or 3 cells.

For cells that run on Loki **L1 HW, there only one case for the subcell pooling to be supported by CB006559 and CB006974 BB block feature:**

Case1: Only DL subcell is pooled between 2 (\*) or 3 cells. There is no pooled UL subcell.

In general, there shall be no separate assignment of DL and UL pooled subcell. Both DL and UL pooled subcell shall be given to the same cell. If only DL subcell is pooled or only UL subcell is pooled, pooling algorithm has no impact.

(\*) NOTE: This exists a case that only 1 or 2 cells are setup successfully under 3 cells deployment. Thus also the 1 or 2 cells case needs to be fully supported. For example, operator may commission 3 cells but locks one of them (i.e. set the NRCELL.administrativeState to locked) for any reason, or commission 3 cells and delete one cell after 3 cells setup successfully, subcell pooling is still activate in those cases.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

## 3.31.2 Buffered UL (TDD only)

### 3.31.2.0-1 Buffered UL (TDD only) Buffered UL L2 architecture and functional split (ID: 13459440)

**3.31.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13449931`)

Buffered UL (TDD only)
13449931:
Buffered UL (TDD only)
**Buffered UL L2 architecture and functional split**

Single-sector deployments in round robin mode

In case of single-sector deployments and Algo 1 in round robin mode, the 5G-L2-PS scheduler algorithms are impacted as follows:

In the "Cross-TTI timing" section, there is a block labeled "L1 resource allocator" which contains a sub-block labeled "Algo 1". An arrow points from "L1 resource allocator" downwards.
In the "Real time loop" section, there are three main components arranged horizontally. On the left is a block labeled "Pre-scheduler". An arrow labeled "CS1 list" points from "Pre-scheduler" to a block labeled "TD-scheduler". The "TD-scheduler" block also has a sub-block labeled "Algo 3" highlighted in yellow. An arrow points from the "L1 resource allocator" in the upper section to the "TD-scheduler" in the lower section.
To the right of the "TD-scheduler", there are multiple stacked blocks labeled "FD-scheduler (subcell 0)". An arrow labeled "1 CS2 list per FD-scheduler" originates from above the "FD-scheduler" blocks and points towards them. Arrows also originate from the "TD-scheduler" and point to each of the "FD-scheduler" blocks.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16632.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Multi-sector deployments in round robin mode

In case of multi-sector deployments and Algo 1 in round robin mode, the 5G-L2-PS scheduler algorithms are impacted as follows:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a block diagram illustrating a scheduling system. The diagram is divided into two main sections by a dashed line labeled "Cross-TTI timing" above and "Real time loop" below.
In the "Real time loop" section, there are several components:
- "Pre-scheduler": This component receives input and outputs a "CS1 list". There appear to be multiple instances of the "Pre-scheduler" stacked behind each other.
- "TD-scheduler (cell 1)": This component receives the "CS1 list" from the "Pre-scheduler" and also receives input from the "L1 resource allocator". It outputs to the "FD-scheduler". A yellow box labeled "Algo 3" is associated with this component.
- "FD-scheduler (subcell 0)": This component receives input from the "TD-scheduler (cell 1)". The diagram indicates "1 CS2 list per FD-scheduler", and there are multiple instances of the "FD-scheduler" stacked behind each other, suggesting parallel processing or multiple subcells.
In the "Cross-TTI timing" section, there is:
- "L1 resource allocator": This component contains a box labeled "Algo 1". It sends signals upwards to the "TD-scheduler (cell 1)" and also receives signals from the "TD-scheduler (cell 1)".
The arrows indicate the flow of data and control between these components. The "Pre-scheduler" feeds into the "TD-scheduler", which in turn feeds into the "FD-scheduler". The "L1 resource allocator" interacts with the "TD-scheduler".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16632.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

For Algo 1 description refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5201\_replaced([11209903](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw2W6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For Algo 3 description refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5216\_replaced([11209990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw298_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

#### 3.31.2.1 Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell)

##### 3.31.2.1.0-1 Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell) Algo 1 Overview (ID: 11209910)

**3.31.2.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13452385`)

Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell)
The L1 Resource Allocator shall perform an algorithm to select how many subcells shall be handled in RT/NRT in each cell (Buffered UL - Algo 1). The selected algorithm is Metric-based algorithm.

The "Buffered UL - Algo 1" selection is valid for one SFN.

To support more than 4 cells deployment on ABIL (for instance 8 cells configurations defined in 5G\_UP\_2695\_replaced([11391378](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufYzm_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), it is required to filter among all cells in L2-RT pool if buffered UL is activated in L2-RT pool, only the cells with at least 1 UL subcell with UL layers larger than 0 are handled with buffered UL functionality.

The Algo 1 (whatever the mode) shall apply to this filtered cell list instead of the whole cell list. After filtering, up to 4 cells case described below are eligible for Algo 1.

The "Buffered UL - Algo 1" need the following input:

-Cell load measurements

Output from "Buffered UL - Algo 1":

* Number of subcells handled RT in each cell

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

##### 3.31.2.1.0-2 Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell) Round robin algorithm (ID: 11209920)

**3.31.2.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12487766`)

Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell)
[Before CNI-136563]

When R&D parameter rdBufferedUlMode is set to “0: RoundRobin” or “2: Test” , the "Buffered UL - Algo 1" shall decide {number of RT subcells for each cell} based on SFN. On each SFN, {number of RT subcells for each cell} shall be either 0 or {number of configured subcell by PsCell\_CellSetupReq.ulSubcellList}

The following is an algorithm on how the {number of RT subcells for each cell} shall be decided based on SFN. The following assumptions are done:

* each cell is configured with the same amount of UL subcells
* 2 x capacity by Buffered UL

The SFN cycle depends on the number of configured cells:

When R&D parameter rdBufferedUlMode is set to “0: RoundRobin”:

1 cell (either with 1xC2/C4 or 2xC2 subcell)

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
|  | SFN=0 mod 1 |
| Cell 0 | 1 or 2 |

2 cells with 1xC2 subcell each

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | SFN=0 mod 2 |  | SFN=1 mod 2 |  |  |
| Cell 0 |  | 1 |  | 1 |  |  |
|  | Cell 1 |  | 1 |  | 1 |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

2 cells with 2xC2 subcell each

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | SFN=0 mod 2 |  | SFN=1 mod 2 |  |  |
| Cell 0 |  | 2 |  | 0 |  |  |
|  | Cell 1 |  | 0 |  | 2 |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

2 cells with 1xC4 subcell each

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | SFN=0 mod 2 |  | SFN=1 mod 2 |  |  |
| Cell 0 |  | 1 |  | 0 |  |  |
|  | Cell 1 |  | 0 |  | 1 |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

When R&D parameter rdBufferedUlMode is set to “2: Test”

1 or 2 cells

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | SFN=0 mod 2 |  | SFN=1 mod 2 |  |  |
| Cell 0 |  | 1 or 2 |  | 0 |  |  |
|  | Cell 1 |  | 0 |  | 1 or 2 |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

When R&D parameter rdBufferedUlMode is set to “0: RoundRobin” or “2: Test”

3 cells

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | SFN=0 mod 3 | SFN=1 mod 3 | SFN=2 mod 3 |
| Cell 0 | 1 | 1 | 0 |
| Cell 1 | 0 | 1 | 1 |
| Cell 2 | 1 | 0 | 1 |

4 cells

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | SFN=0 mod 4 | SFN=1 mod 4 | SFN=2 mod 4 | SFN=3 mod 4 |
| Cell 0 | 1 | 0 | 1 | 0 |
| Cell 1 | 0 | 1 | 0 | 1 |
| Cell 2 | 1 | 0 | 1 | 0 |
| Cell 3 | 0 | 1 | 0 | 1 |

When the list of cells is modified, the new number of cells shall be taken into account for the next decision.

NOTE: For 1 cell case, the L1 capability for the number of subcells shall be also taken into account. Also, it shall be considered which cells are configured on the same l1PoolId (it can be assumed that all subcells of one cell are configured within one l1PoolId, refer to 5G\_UP\_2474\_replaced([11389639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCmPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
|  | Any SFN |
| Cell 0 | min (numConfSubcell[0]; maxNumOfXXRtUlSubcell) |

*maxNumOfXXRtUlSubcell is defined based on 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5209\_replaced([11209950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw2W9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the configured UL subcell type*

[CNI-136563]

Round Robin will NOT be supported since CNI-136563.

[END CNI-136563]

##### 3.31.2.1.0-3 Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell) Metric-based algorithm (ID: 11209936)

**3.31.2.1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13452465`)

Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell)
The "Buffered UL - Algo1" shall decide number of RT subcells based on cell load measurement.

**RT UL subcell distribution**

The cell load measurements shall be used to distribute RT UL subcells between the cells as follows:

* The long term (over many SFNs) RT UL subcell distribution shall follow the ratio of the cell load as close as possible (exact match is not requested)
* When the cell load between cells is balanced (similar), the algorithm shall provide nearly equal long term RT UL subcell distribution for each cell
* When the cell load between cells is unbalanced, they should get RT resource in proportion of loads on the long term
* NOTE. If one cell cannot consume all available RT subcells, proportionality cannot always follow cell load since all available RT UL subcells shall be distributed
* e.g. in case of 3 or 4 cell configs with 1 UL subcell per cell and 2 RT UL subcells available, and if only two cells have load => regardless of the loads for the two cells, both cells will always get 1 RT UL subcell
* When the cell load measurement indicates this cell does not have any load, this cell shall NOT get any RT UL subcell
* If all RT UL subcells cannot be consumed by cells which have load, it is allowed to give RT UL subcells to a cell without load
* The cells shall be allocated with either 0 or "all configured PUSCH/PUCCH subcells" as RT on each SFN. It is not allowed to give "part of the configured PUSCH/PUCCH subcells" as RT.
* NOTE. Allocating both RT and NRT subcells to certain cell requires Algo 2 (RT/NRT Subcell Selection within a cell) which is not supported.

NOTE: Matric based algorithm shall be supported for configuration as 2 cells with 1 UL C4 subcell per cell**.**

NOTE: In future releases, for 1 cell case (which is not supported in scope of 5GC001120), the “L1 capability for the number of subcells per L1 instance” shall NOT be exceeded when allocating RT UL subcells as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5209\_replaced([11209950](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw2W9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

##### 3.31.2.1.0-4 Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell) Maximum number of Real-time subcells (ID: 11209950)

**3.31.2.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13452474`)

Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell)
L1 Resource Allocator shall have the following variables to control number of RT subcells for each subcell type:

maxNumOfC2RtUlSubcell = 2

maxNumOfC4RtUlSubcell = 1

maxNumOfD2RtUlSubcell = 2

L1 Resource Allocator distributes RT and NRT UL resources as below according to *Buffered UL - Algo 1 decision.*

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **BB block configuration** | **maxNbOfRTPerCell** | **nbOfRounds** | **nbOfRTPerRound** |
| 2 cells with 2 UL subcells C2 per cell | 2 | 1 | 2 |
| 2 cells with 1 UL subcell C4 per cell | 1 | 1 | 1 |
| 3 cells with 1 UL subcell C2 per cell | 1 | 2 | 1 |
| 4 cells with 1 UL subcell C2 per cell | 1 | 2 | 1 |
| 4 cells with 1 UL subcell D2 per cell | 1 | 2 | 1 |

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

##### 3.31.2.1.0-5 Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell) Interaction between buffered UL and subcell pooling (ID: 11209961)

**3.31.2.1.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13452479`)

Buffered UL - Algo 1 (Number of subcells handled RT/NRT in each cell)
When subcell pooling is used, there needs to prevent allocating both RT and NRT subcells to the cell with the pooled UL subcell. Only MetricBased mode is supported in subcell pooling.

When the subcell pooling is in  metric-based mode, and buffered UL is in metric-based mode, the "Buffered UL - Algo1" shall decide number of RT subcells based on cell load measurement.

The cells shall be allocated with either 0 or "all available PUSCH/PUCCH subcells" (see NOTE) as RT on each SFN. It is not allowed to give "part of the available PUSCH/PUCCH subcells" as RT.

When subcell pooling is activated, "all configured PUSCH/PUCCH subcells" are not available/allowed for scheduling of each cell in each SFN. Thus when above “RT UL subcell distribution” is performed, the number of PUSCH/PUCCH subcells available for usage in the next SFN shall be known. In this case, the cells shall be allocated with either 0 or "all available PUSCH/PUCCH subcells" as RT on each SFN.

Specifically, there are only two possible scenarios for RT subcell distribution for 3S-1CC deployments (BB block 5GC002411) where each cell (1/3 cells) is configured with 2 PUSCH/PUCCH subcells from which one subcell is static and one is pooled.

1. Cell which has the pooled subcell available for usage: 2 RT subcell. Other cell(s) which don’t have the pooled subcell available for usage: 0 RT subcell

2. Cell which has the pooled subcell available for usage: 0 RT subcell. Other cell(s) which don’t have the pooled subcell available for usage: 1 RT subcell. If there are only 2 cells configured, the second RT subcell cannot be used.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.31.2.2 Buffered UL - Algo 2 (RT/NRT Subcell Selection within a cell)

##### 3.31.2.2.0-1 Buffered UL - Algo 2 (RT/NRT Subcell Selection within a cell) Subcell Selection within a cell (ID: 13337598)

**3.31.2.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13452493`)

Buffered UL - Algo 2 (RT/NRT Subcell Selection within a cell)
There are two separate cases for RT/NRT Subcell Selection within a cell**.**

**Case A: All or none of the subcells for a cell are provided as RT by L1 Resource Allocator (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5201\_replaced([11209903](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw2W6PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

* Only Metric-Based mode is supported in such scenario.
* Includes the case of one subcell per cell.
* In this case, output from L1 Resource Allocator shall be directly followed by the RT/NRT Subcell Selection within a cell.

Only case A is supported within the scope of 5GC001120. Thus any advanced Algo2 is NOT needed.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

### 3.31.2.3 Buffered UL - Algo 3 (NRT slot selection)

#### 3.31.2.3.0-1 Buffered UL - Algo 3 (NRT slot selection) Algo 3 Overview (ID: 11209996)

**3.31.2.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13453777`)

Buffered UL - Algo 3 (NRT slot selection)
13453777:
Buffered UL - Algo 3 (NRT slot selection)

### "Buffered UL - Algo 3" shall decide in which DL NR-slot the UL data shall be processed NRT for the buffered subcells

Buffered UL slots are postponed to the next possible DL slot. Timing offset is fixed to the same value for each slot based on the configured frame structure. In the currently (**FR1:7:1:2 TD-LTE (5GC001116), 4:1 (5GC001208), Bi-periodic 7:3 (5GC001070)** FR2: 4:1 (5GC001127)) supported frame structures, there is always one Special slot followed by 1 or 2 UL slots. This means that when buffering is needed, buffered subcell of special slot will be handled in the first DL slot following the last UL slot, 1st UL slot would be handled in the second DL slot following UL slot, 2nd UL slot would be handled in the third DL slot following UL slot. Thus there is always 2 or 3 slots offset from air interface slot into slot for NRT processing. Ref below for example with FR2 (5GC001127) 4:1 DL:UL ratio).\*\*\*\*

[xls\_desc][Error extracting Excel content: Unable to start Tika server.][/xls\_desc][xls\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/attachments/m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file16648\_0.xls[/xls\_path]

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.31.2.3.0-2 Buffered UL - Algo 3 (NRT slot selection) Algo 3 depending on frame structure (ID: 11210010)

**3.31.2.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13453778`)

Buffered UL - Algo 3 (NRT slot selection)
Depending on the supported radio frame structure, the following cases have to be considered:

- The NR-slot S is followed by 1 NR-slot U

- NR-slot S shall be processed NRT in the 1st NR-slot D following the last NR-slot U

- NR-slot U shall be processed NRT in the 2nd NR-slot D following the last NR-slot U

- The NR-slot S is followed by 2 NR-slots U

- NR-slot S shall be processed NRT in the 1st NR-slot D following the last NR-slot U

- 1st NR-slot U shall be processed NRT in the 2nd NR-slot D following the last NR-slot U

- 2nd NR-slot U shall be processed NRT in the 3rd NR-slot D following the last NR-slot U

It means that UL data will be processed NRT with 2 or 3 NR-slots offset from air interface.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.31.2.3.0-3 Buffered UL - Algo 3 (NRT slot selection) Algo 3 for FR1 radio frame structure (ID: 11210023)

**3.31.2.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13453779`)

Buffered UL - Algo 3 (NRT slot selection)
13453779:
Buffered UL - Algo 3 (NRT slot selection)
The table below provides for each FR1 radio frame structure identified by the *Configuration-Index, the Algo 3 decision related to each NR-slot S and NR-slot U:*

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Configuration-Index** | **NR-slot n** | **Algo 3 decision** |
| 1 & 2 | 3/8/13/18 (S) | 5/10/15/0 (D) |
| 4/9/14/19 (U) | 6/11/16/1 (D) |  |
| 3 & 4 | 3/7/13/17 (S) | 5/10/15/0 (D) |
| 4/8/9/14/18/19 (U) | 6/11/12/16/1/2 (D) |  |
| 5 & 6 | 7/17 (S) | 10/0 (D) |
| 8/9/18/19 (U) | 11/12/1/2 (D) |  |
| 7 & 8 | 3/13 (S) | 6/16 (D) |
| 4/5/14/15 (U) | 7/8/17/18 (D) |  |

### 3.31.2.4 Buffered UL - L1 control

#### 3.31.2.4.0-1 Buffered UL - L1 control Buffered UL – L1 Interface   removed to CP3 (ID: 11210063)

**3.31.2.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11210076`)

Buffered UL - L1 control
[Before CNI-82237]

UlData Request Messages

bufferedUlConfig (5G\_L1\_IF\_166\_replaced([11513624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv3_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is a structure used in UlData\_PuschReceiveReq, UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, UlData\_PrachReceiveReq and UlData\_SrsReceiveReq messages to control buffered UL. 5G-L2-PS shall fill the structure as below:

* If buffered UL feature is not activated (note: never activated for FDD) or if buffered UL is NOT used for a given slot for the particular subcell, processInRealTime shall be set to TRUE, and slotForProcessing and sfnForProcessing are set to the same values as slot and sfn in the main level of the same message.
* If buffered UL is used for a given slot for the particular subcell, processInRealTime shall be set to FALSE, and slotForProcessing and sfnForProcessing with the appropriate SFN and slot numbers. The appropriate SFN and slot number is defined by "Buffered UL - Algo 3" (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5216\_replaced([11209990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw298_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* For configuration as 2 cells with 1 UL C4 subcell per cell, in UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message, processInRealTime shall be set to TRUE, and slotForProcessing and sfnForProcessing are set to the same values as slot and sfn in the main level of the same message, regardless buffered UL feature activation or not.

UlData Response Messages

bufferedUlResp (5G\_L1\_IF\_166\_replaced([11513624](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv3_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is a structure used in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs/HarqU, UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs/HarqD, UlData\_PrachReceiveInd, UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs messages to indicate the SFN and NR-slot index of the L1 processiong slot. There is no functional use for bufferedUlResp in 5G-L2-PS. However it shall be used for certain traces to capture the actual L1 processiong slot.

[CNI-82237]

content is removed to CP3 (Ref: 5G\_L2\_7548\_replaced([11174250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26iDrfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CNI-82237]

### 3.31.2.5-2 Buffered UL - Cell load measurement

**3.31.2.5-2.0-2**  (ID: `13453784`)

Buffered UL - Cell load measurement
For Buffered UL, it is assumed that all NRCELLGRPs and NRCELLs handled by the L2-RT instance are configured with the same frame structure.

Note: this is a non-functional requirement, serving as a reference for O&M. The configuration cannot be verified in L2, because one NRCELLGRP scheduler does not know how other schedulers are configured.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.31.2.5.0-1 Buffered UL - Cell load measurement Uplink cell load measurement for the Metric based algorithm (ID: 13459441)

**3.31.2.5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13453781`)

Buffered UL - Cell load measurement
**Uplink cell load measurement for the Metric based algorithm**

The 5G-L2-PS shall perform a cell load measurement which shall be used as input for L1 Resource Allocator

1. The cell load measurement shall be based on “sum of UL subcell usage for PUSCH and PUCCH”

* During each Special and UL slot, number of subcells used for PUCCH shall be accumulated
* During each Special and UL slot, number of subcells used for PUSCH shall be accumulated

 NOTE. Number of subcells used for PRACH shall NOT be used

 Rationale: PRACH is always received in every cell regardless of whether there is any load in the cell or not. Thus it will indicate there is load even for empty cell. Thus it shall not be cared.

 NOTE. Number of subcells used for SRS\_SU-MIMO and SRS\_BF shall NOT be used

1. At the end of the measurement period, "number of subcells used for PUCCH" and "number of subcells used for PUSCH" shall be accumulated together
2. NOTE. subcells used for PUCCH and PUSCH shall have the same weigh in the “sum of UL subcell usage for PUSCH and PUCCH” .
3. The measurement period for cell load measurement shall be 10ms. The load measurement shall be reset to 0 after the 10ms result are provided to L1 resource allocator
4. Rationale: a shorter measurement period than “L1 resource allocator period (which is 1 SFN = 10ms)” is never needed. Therefore 10ms is used for the measurement period of load.
5. NOTE. The measurement period does NOT need to be tied to SFN boundary even the measurement period is 10ms.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.31.2.5.0-2 Buffered UL - Cell load measurement UL subcell used metric (ID: 13459443)

**3.31.2.5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13453782`)

Buffered UL - Cell load measurement
The *UL subcell used metric is handled by the UL/DL TD-scheduler as follows:*

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **UL subcell used metric** | **Trigger** | **Metric action** |
| ulTdSched[x].Cell[y].ulSubcellUsed[z] | Cell setup | Initialize to 0 |
| Cell delete | Remove metric |  |
| Metric provided to L1 resource allocator | Reinitialize to 0 |  |
| UL subcell is used for PUSCH during UL slot (whatever RT/NRT processing) | Increment by +1 |  |
| UL subcell is used for PRACH during UL slot (whatever RT/NRT processing) | Do nothing |  |
| UL subcell is used for SRS SU\_MIMO during UL slot (whatever RT/NRT processing) | Do nothing |  |
| dlTdSched[x].Cell[y].ulSubcellUsed[z] | Cell setup | Initialize to 0 |
| Cell delete | Remove metric |  |
| Metric provided to L1 resource allocator | Reinitialize to 0 |  |
| UL subcell is used for PUCCH during special or UL slot (whatever RT/NRT processing) | Increment by +1 |  |

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.31.2.5.0-3 Buffered UL - Cell load measurement In case of more than 1 UL subcell per cell (ID: 13459445)

**3.31.2.5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13453783`)

Buffered UL - Cell load measurement
13453783:
Buffered UL - Cell load measurement
If needed (i.e. in case of more than 1 UL subcell per cell), each UL/DL TS-scheduler aggregates the *UL subcell used metrics related to a same cell as follows:*

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
ul/dlTdSched[x].Cell[x].ulMetric = $\sum\_{y=0}^{}$ ul/dlTdSched[x].Cell[x].ulSubcellUsed[y][/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16662.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

During the current radio frame (i.e. slot0 for FR1 and slot60 for FR2), each UL/DL TD-scheduler provides to L1 resource allocator their UL metric to apply during the next radio frame.

L1 resource allocator aggregates the *UL metric related to a same cell as follows:*

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a sans-serif font. The equation is:
`Cell[x].load = ulTdSched[x].Cell[x].ulMetric + dlTdSched[x]. Cell[x].ulMetric`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16662.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

The metrics are sent two slots in advance in order to be sure that when the *Buffered UL - Algo 1 will be run for the next radio frame (i.e. slot2 for FR1 and slot62 for FR2), L1 resource allocator will have received all inputs from each UL/DL TD-scheduler.*

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

## 3.31.3 Subcell Pooling (TDD only)

### 3.31.3.0-1 Subcell Pooling (TDD only) Subcell pool definition (ID: 11210133)

**3.31.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13456060`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
The DL/UL subcell pools are defined as follows:

- The DL subcell pool is composed of DL floating C4 subcells having the following characteristics:

- The DL floating C4 subcells belonging to the DL subcell pool have the same *dlSubcellPoolId*

- The UL subcell pool is composed of UL floating C2 subcells having the following characteristics

- The UL floating C2 subcells belonging to the UL subcell pool have the same *ulSubcellPoolId*

Note: For Loki L1 HW, each cell is configured with 1 static UL C4 subcell, so UL floating C2/C4 subcell is not applicable for Loki L1 HW.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

### 3.31.3.0-2 Subcell Pooling (TDD only) Subcell Pooling Algorithm (ID: 11210144)

**3.31.3.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13456134`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
The L1 Resource Allocator shall perform an algorithm to select how many UL/DL subcells shall be available for usage in each cell.  [Before CNI-136563] The selected algorithm is decided by R&D parameter rdSubcellPoolingMode (R&D parameter, see 5G\_L2\_1233\_replaced([11188068](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Fi3fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CNI-136563] The selected algorithm is Metric Based algorithm. [End CNI-136563]

The selection is valid for rdSubcellPoolingPeriod (R&D parameter, see 5G\_L2\_1234\_replaced([11188075](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Fi3vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) SFNs.

The following assumptions of subcell pooling are done:

For Loner L1 HW,

* each cell is configured with 2 (1 static + 1 pooled) UL C2 subcells
* each cell is configured with 1 (static) or 2 (1 static + 1 pooled) DL C4 subcells

For Loki L1 HW TDD L1 ,

* each cell is configured with 2 (1 static + 1 pooled) DL C4 subcells
* each cell is configured with 1 static UL C4 subcell
* when only one cell is configured, the pooled DL and/or UL subcell is always used by the single cell (i.e. no pooling)
* when more than one cell is configured, the pooled DL and/or UL subcells are mapped to the same eCPRI resource and thus cannot be used at the same time

Pooled subcell decision shall have an impact on at SFN boundary as specified by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5252\_replaced([11210271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4zIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If the DL subcell is pooled, the timing when the pooled DL subcell is usable is specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5256\_replaced([11210304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4zI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The new values for the "available UL subcell amount" and "available DL subcell amount" shall be used when FDM/MU-MIMO scheduling is allocating UEs to subcells (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4292\_replaced([11177281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuuP-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL FDM, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4372\_replaced([11142017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr2iJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL MU-MIMO and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4871\_replaced([11196450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwCepPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_4960\_replaced([11199244](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwMPk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL FDM)

The algorithm needs the following input:

* DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5244\_replaced([11210192](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4ME_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

**- DL L2 new data arrival estimate** of a cell (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5246\_replaced([11210209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))\*\*\*\*

* Spectral Efficiency of one DL Scheduling slot (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5250\_replaced([11210238](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* # PDSCH REs per PRB (static value) (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5248\_replaced([11210227](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Output from the algorithm:

* Number of available UL subcells for usage in each cell
* Number of available DL subcells for usage in each cell

NOTE:

* "Number of available DL subcells for usage in each cell" will be static if no DL subcell is pooled.
* "Number of available UL subcells for usage in each cell" will be static if no UL subcell is pooled.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

### 3.31.3.0-3 Subcell Pooling (TDD only) Round Robin Algorithm (ID: 11210162)

**3.31.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12443954`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
[Before CNI-136563] When R&D parameter rdSubcellPoolingMode is set to “0: RoundRobin”, the cell which get to use the pooled UL/DL subcell shall be decided based on SFN.

The following is an algorithm on how the {number of available UL subcells for each cell} and {number of available DL subcells for each cell} shall be decided.

numOfCellsSetup indicates how many cells are setup. In the scope of 5GC002093 is can be 1, 2 or 3.

rdSubcellPoolingPeriod is R&D parameters, refer to 5G\_L2\_1234\_replaced([11188075](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Fi3vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When deciding number of available UL/DL subcells for a SFN, calculate which cell (#0, #1 or #2) gets the pooled subcell as:

x = FLOOR [(SFN/subcellPoolingPeriod) MOD numOfCellsSetup]

Cell#x will have the pooled subcell, i.e.:

- if DL subcell is pooled and UL subcell is pooled

{number of available DL subcells} = 2

{number of available UL subcells} = 2

- if DL subcell is pooled and UL subcell is not pooled

{number of available DL subcells} = 2

{number of available UL subcells} = 1

- if DL subcell is not pooled and UL subcell is pooled

{number of available DL subcells} = 1

{number of available UL subcells} = 2

Other cells will have

{number of available UL/DL subcells} = 1

Here the SFN refers to the timing when the pooled UL subcell is usable.

When the list of cells is modified, the new number of cells shall be taken into account for the next decision.

[CNI-136563]

Round robin algorithm will not be supported since CNI-136563

[End CNI-136563]

---

### 3.31.3.0-4 Subcell Pooling (TDD only) Metric Based Algorithm (ID: 11210173)

**3.31.3.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12436598`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
[Before CNI-136563]  When R&D parameter rdSubcellPoolingMode is set to “1: MetricBased",[ CNI-136563] When subcell Pooling is used, MetricBased mode is the only supported mode.[End CNI-136563] the cell which get to use the pooled UL/DL subcell shall be decided based on a load based algorithm. Ideally, the objective of the algorithm is to maximize the capacity (throughput and latency) across the three cells by dynamically time-sharing the additional subcell considering both the offered load and the extent of MU-MIMO pairing possible in each cell. To achieve this, the following load-based algorithm performs time sharing of the additional sub-cell based on the individual cell loads. The load per cell is calculated in terms of the PRB demand ("Aggregate PRB demand") as defined by the formula below. Currently, the algorithm does not consider the orthogonality of the UEs in each cell, and hence the extent to which the UEs are amenable to MU-MIMO pairing. "Aggregate PRB demand" represents how many PRBs each cell is estimated to need to empty all DL buffers. To estimate this, there is need to maintain knowledge about how many bits have been transmitted on a single PRB in the past.

Considering different cell bandwidth mixing into same subcell pool, the "normalized aggregate PRB demand" is calculated based on "aggregate PRB demand" per cell bandwidth. The "normalized aggregate PRB demand" represents how many PRBs demanding per cell bandwidth to empty all DL buffers.

The following is an algorithm on how the {number of available UL subcells for each cell} and {number of available DL subcells for each cell} shall be decided.

Every subcellPoolingPeriod (R&D parameters, refer to 5G\_L2\_1234\_replaced([11188075](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Fi3vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) SFNs, "Normalized aggregate PRB demand" shall be calculated for each cell as:

Aggregate PRB demand = (DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell + rrmAvgNewDataArrivalEst) \*muScaleFactor/ ("# PDSCH REs per PRB" \* rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot), where

* DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell as calculated by in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5244\_replaced([11210192](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4ME_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmAvgNewDataArrivalEst as calculated by in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5246\_replaced([11210209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* # PDSCH REs per PRB is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5248\_replaced([11210227](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5250\_replaced([11210238](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* muScaleFactor is defined as below:

IF NIDD/actDlMuMimoEnh = FALSE

muScaleFactor = 1.0;

ELSE

For cell without floating subcell, muScaleFactor = 1.0;

For cell with floating subcell, muScaleFactor = max(0.1, numOfSchedTTIUsingFloatSubcell/numOfSchedTTI) \* 2.0;

- numOfSchedTTI is the number scheduled TTI in each reporting period.

- numOfSchedTTIUsingFloatSubcell is the number of scheduled TTI that utilizes floating subcell in each reporting period for DL MU-MIMO.

Normalized aggregate PRB demand = Aggregate PRB demand / dlBandwidth, where

* dlBandwidth in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message

The cell with highest "Normalized aggregate PRB demand" will have the pooled subcell, i.e.:

- if DL subcell is pooled and UL subcell is pooled

{number of available DL subcells} = 2

{number of available UL subcells} = 2

- if DL subcell is pooled and UL subcell is not pooled

{number of available DL subcells} = 2

{number of available UL subcells} = 1

- if DL subcell is not pooled and UL subcell is pooled

{number of available DL subcells} = 1

{number of available UL subcells} = 2

Other cells will have

{number of available UL/DL subcells} = 1

Should the highest "Normalized aggregate PRB demand" be equal among multiple cells, pooled subcell can be freely given to any of those cells with equally high "Normalized aggregate PRB demand".

When the list of cells is modified, the new number of cells shall be taken into account for the next decision.

---

### 3.31.3.0-5 Subcell Pooling (TDD only) Cell load measurement for Metric Based Algorithm (ID: 11210187)

**3.31.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11210192`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell for Metric Based Algorithm

---

**3.31.3.0-5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13455330`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
13455330:
Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
5G-L2-PS shall maintain "DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell" which shall be the SUM of RLC buffer for all DRB of all UEs in the cell.

DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell =  [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical summation symbol followed by the text "UE,bearers" below it. To the right of the summation symbol and "UE,bearers" is the text "currentDrbBufferSize". The summation symbol indicates that the quantity "currentDrbBufferSize" is being summed over all "UE,bearers".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16677.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]*, where*

*- currentDrbBufferSize : In bytes. Current DL RLC SDU buffer size*

NOTE. The same sum of data is maintained by DSS feature (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4686\_replaced([11172357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuLdgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

**3.31.3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11210209`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
DL L2 new data arrival estimate of a cell for Metric Based Algorithm

---

**3.31.3.0-5.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13455339`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
"DL L2 new data arrival estimate of a cell" (rrmAvgNewDataArrivalEst) is a cell specific variable and shall be calculated as a exponential filter at the end of every subcellPoolingPeriod.

Start value for rrmAvgNewDataArrivalEst shall be 0.

rrmAvgNewDataArrivalEst[n] = (1 - 1/rdAvgNewDataArrivalEstFilterCoeff) \* rrmAvgNewDataArrivalEst[n − 1] + 1/rdAvgNewDataArrivalEstFilterCoeff \* rrmInstNewDataArrivalEst

* rdAvgNewDataArrivalEstFilterCoefff is R&D parameters defined in 5G\_L2\_1236\_replaced([11188087](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ4PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmInstNewDataArrivalEst shall be caluculated as below

rrmInstNewDataArrivalEst = DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell [n] - DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell [n - 1] + Sum(TBS)[subcellPoolingPeriod]

* DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell [n - 1] is the value at the start of the subcellPoolingPeriod
* DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell [n] is the value at the end of the subcellPoolingPeriod
* Sum(TBS)[subcellPoolingPeriod] is the sum of scheduled DL TBS provided as tbSize IE in LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq) for all scheduled DL UEs in all the slots during the previous subcellPoolingPeriod.

Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5244\_replaced([11210192](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4ME_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL L2 buffer occupancy of a cell.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

**3.31.3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11210227`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)

# PDSCH REs per PRB for Metric Based Algorithm

---

**3.31.3.0-5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13455535`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)

# PDSCH REs per PRB **shall be defined as one static value (144).**

12 subcarriers x 12 PDSCH symbols = 144 // 1 symbol for PDCCH and 1 for DMRS is assumed

Rationale: It would be difficult to predict an accurate RE number usable for PDSCH in the future pooling period. Accurate number will be dynamic by features which control PDCCH symbol amount (5GC000791 and CB006555) and if PDSCH is used in SSB (5GC002534) or TRS slot (5GC002538) and so on. Also it will depend on which UEs happen to be scheduled and their radio conditions (such as how many DMRS symbols are going to be used). Static value has been used also in the metric based algo simulations.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

**3.31.3.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `11210238`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
Spectral Efficiency of one DL Scheduling slot for Metric Based Algorithm

---

**3.31.3.0-5.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `11210264`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
Spectral Efficiency of one DL Scheduling slot (rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot) represents average number bytes per resource element which has been used in the past for PDSCH transmission by 5G-L2-PS.

It is a cell specific variable and shall be calculated as a exponential filter in every DL slot where at least one UE specific PDSCH is scheduled.

PDSCH scheduled due to artificial load, RACH msg2, systemInformation and Paging shall be excluded from the Spectral Efficiency calculation.

Start value for rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot shall be 8. // 8 is rough average number based on rank2 and medium 64 QAM MCS.

rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot[n] = (1 - 1/rdAvgSpectralEffDlSlotFilterCoeff) \* rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot[n − 1] + 1/rdAvgSpectralEffDlSlotFilterCoeff \* rrmInstSpectralEffDlSlot

* rdAvgSpectralEffDlSlotFilterCoeff is R&D parameters defined in 5G\_L2\_1235\_replaced([11188082](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Fi3_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmInstSpectralEffDlSlot shall be caluculated as Sum(TBS) / SUM(REs), where

- Sum(TBS) is the sum of scheduled DL TBS in bytes of fresh transmission provided as tbSize IE in LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq) for all scheduled DL UEs in this slot, and

- SUM(REs) is the sum of scheduled number of REs  used for both fresh and retransmission for all scheduled DL UEs in this slot

Scheduled number of REs is known by 5G-L2-PS since it is used to decide the TBS as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4635\_replaced([11192394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvkkgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as number (Nre \* Nrb), where

* Nre is the number of data RE per RB, and
* Nrb is the number of allocated RB for the PDSCH
* For FR1-TDD with MU-MIMO enabled(NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh=True)

If scheduled UE is a virtual UE and if this virtual UE is allocated only at one subcell,

Scheduled number of REs for this virtual UE = scheduled number of REs within the RBGs [CB008927-P]/PRBs (when NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = True) [End CB008927-P]allocated to virtual UE

Else If scheduled UE is a virtual UE and is allocated at mutiple subcells N,

Scheduled number of REs for this virtual UE = N \* scheduled number of REs within the RBGs [CB008927-P]/PRBs (when NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = True) [End CB008927-P] allocated to the virtual UE

Else for any other UE scheduled on the primary subcell

Scheduled number of REs within the RBGs [CB008927-P]/PRBs (when NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = True) [End CB008927-P] allocated for this UE shall be considered.

End

* where: for DL: virtual/root UE list definition (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7430\_replaced([11144070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/ 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7454\_replaced([11142605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-afvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

### 3.31.3.0-6 Subcell Pooling (TDD only) Timing of pooled subcell distribution (ID: 11210271)

**3.31.3.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `13456287`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
13456287:
Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
In order to decide "how many subcells shall be handled in RT/NRT in each cell" by "Buffered UL - Algo 1", it needs to know "number of available UL subcells" for each control period. Selection for "how many UL subcells shall be handled in RT/NRT in each cell" is valid for one SFN according to requirement 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8524\_replaced([11209910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw2W7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Since "number of available UL subcell" will become dynamic with pooled UL subcell (either 1 or 2 UL subcells will be available for each cell even 2 subcells are configured), the L1 Resource Allocator shall decide which cell get the pooled UL subcell according to the below requirements in relation to time:

* the cell which gets to use the pooled UL subcell shall be controlled with the same (or multiple of) period as "how many UL subcells shall be handled in RT/NRT in each cell" selection period (e.g. one SFN, two SFN, etc.)
* the cell which gets to use the pooled UL subcell shall be changed only at the SFN boundary (to align with "# of RT UL subcell" selection period)

o SFN alignment refers to the pooled UL subcell. The rules on how to utilize the pooled DL subcell is separately given in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5256\_replaced([11210304](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4zI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**EXAMPLE:**

"# of available UL subcell" shall be changed only at the SFN boundary as below:

### 3.31.3.0-7 Subcell Pooling (TDD only) Timing between DL and UL pooled subcell usage (ID: 11210304)

**3.31.3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11210309`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
Timing between DL and UL pooled subcell usage on Loner

---

**3.31.3.0-7.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13455647`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
13455647:
Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
In TDD FR1, for cells that run on Loner L1 HW, when 5G-L2-PS notices there is a reduction for the available UL subcell AND available DL subcell amount in the next SFN for a cell, it shall stop using the pooled DL subcell and the pooled UL subcell when the corresponding UL slot based on k1/k2 value is in the next SFN (SFN from which reduced subcell amount is valid).

When 5G-L2-PS notices there is an increase for the available UL subcell AND available DL subcell amount in the next SFN for a cell, it shall start to use the pooled DL subcell when they are no further UL slots before the next SFN.

NOTE1: The above rules mean that no assumptions shall be made about the k1/k2 values of the other cell (k1/k2 is NOT necessarily aligned between cells). However the frame structure is assumed to be aligned between the cells which are pooling the DL/UL subcell.

Since k1/k2 may not be aligned, the cell which gains the pooled DL/UL subcell cannot determine whether the other cell stops using the pooled DL subcell until there are no further UL slots before subcell transfer.

Since frame structure is aligned, and if there are no further UL slots in certain cell before subcell transfer, there are also no further UL slots in the other cells. Thus the pooled DL subcell cannot be used by the other cells and the cell which gains it, can use it.

NOTE2: There may be certain slots before the pooled subcell transfer point in which the pooled subcell is NOT used by any cell (the exact waste depends on the used k1/k2 values, i.e. frame structure, PRACH configuration, availability of PRACH/PUCCH FDM and so forth). However when FD beamforming for PUCCH and PDCCH is available, DL and UL subcell allocation could be independent (i.e. if pooled subcell would be used only for PUSCH/PDSCH, while PUCCH/PDCCH would always utilize the static subcell) and this requirement should be updated.

NOTE3: In 8DL-4UL configuration, when the pooled DL subcell is no more available because of k1/k2, the DL scheduler shall consider that the pooled UL subcell is no more available for pairing as well

NOTE4: In 4DL-4UL configuration, when the pooled UL subcell is no more available because of k1/k2, the DL scheduler shall consider that the pooled UL subcell is no more available for pairing as well

**EXAMPLE:**

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a screenshot of a spreadsheet that illustrates a concept related to cellular network frame patterns. The spreadsheet is organized into rows and columns, with headers indicating "SFN" (System Frame Number), "slot", and "Frame pattern".
The "SFN" row is divided into two main sections, labeled "0" and "1", representing different system frame numbers. Within each SFN section, there are columns representing "slot" numbers from 0 to 19 for SFN 0, and 0 to 7 for SFN 1.

Another annotation points to the boundary between SFN 0 and SFN 1, with the text "subcell transfer point". |  | 10 | DL |  |  |
|  | 11 | DL |  |  |

|  | 13 | SP |  |  |
|  | 14 | UL |  |  |
|  | 15 | PR |  |  |
|  | 16 | DL |  |  |
|  | 17 | DL |  |  |
|  | 18 | DL |  |  |
|  | 19 | DL |  |  |
| 1 | 0 | DL | 1 | 2 |
|  | 1 | DL |  |  |
|  | 2 | DL |  |  |
|  | 3 | SP |  |  |
|  | 4 | UL |  |  |
|  | 5 | UL |  |  |
|  | 6 | DL |  |  |

* Loser cell: cell #0 will lose the pooled subcell at SFN = 1
* Winner cell: cell #1 will gain the pooled subcell at SFN = 1
* At slot 11, further usable UL slots before SFN switch (cell#0 uses k1=3 in this slot
* cell #0 which loses the pooled subcell can still use the pooled DL subcell and the pooled UL subcell
* At slot 12/13, no further usable UL slots before SFN switch (for example because PRACH uses UL slot 15, and cell#0 will use k1/k2=11/11 in this slot)
* cell #0 which loses the pooled subcell cannot use the pooled DL subcell and the pooled UL subcell anymore
* cell #1 which wins the pooled subcell cannot yet use it since there are further UL slots and cell#1 does not know if cell#0 will use the DL pooled subcell in these slots due to unknown k1/k2 value of cell#0
* At slot 16, no further UL slots before SFN switch
* cell #1 which wins the pooled subcell can start to use the pooled DL subcell

Note: This is only applicable for the cells allocated on Loner L1 HW.

**3.31.3.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11210326`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
Timing between DL and UL pooled subcell usage on Loki

---

**3.31.3.0-7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11210336`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
11210336:
Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
In TDD FR1, for cells that run on Loki L1 HW, when 5G-L2-PS notices there is an increase or reduction for the available DL subcell amount in the next SFN for a cell, it shall start or stop to use pooled DL subcell at the SFN boundary.

NOTE: The above rule means that UL subcell is static in each cell, even K1/K2 may not be aligned between cells in the same subcell pool, it does not impact DL subcell transfering between different cells, available DL subcell transfer point is always triggered at the SFN boundary.

### 3.31.3.0-8 Subcell Pooling (TDD only) TDD Basedband Pooling interaction with 5GC002538 "PDSCH Extension in SSB and TRS slots" (ID: 11210343)

**3.31.3.0-8.0-2**  (ID: `11210353`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
When subcell pooling is enabled (spatialStreamPoolingAllowed is set to True, refer 5G\_UP\_5230\_replaced([11368175](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udk1wvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB007112-A] or large baseband pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is set to True (refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (refer to 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to True) [End CB007112-A], and the function of "PDSCH Extension in the SSB and TRS slots" is enabled (NRCELL/actPdschRmCsirsForTracking is set to True), the following configurations and functions shall be supported:

When TD BF is enabled with eCPRI RUs, PDSCH scheduling in the SSB and TRS slots shall be scheduled in [Before CB007112-A] two subcells [CB007112-A] multiple subcells if BBRM assign more than one available subcells to the cell (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15314\_replaced([11212864](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDySvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB007112-A]. [Before CB007112-A] one is primary subcell and another is pooled subcell.[End CB007112-A] It means the available subcells which are candidates to be scheduled as PDSCH in the SSB and TRS slots are dynamically changed by baseband pooling function.

When FD BF is enabled with eCPRI RUs, PDSCH scheduling in the SSB and TRS slots shall be scheduled in primary subcell, no impact in pooled subcell.

### 3.31.3.0-9 Subcell Pooling (TDD only) Subcell Pooling NRCELLGRPs and NRCELLs configuration (ID: 11210360)

**3.31.3.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `13455650`)

Subcell Pooling (TDD only)
For subcell pooling, it is assumed that all NRCELLGRPs and NRCELLs handled by the L2-RT instance are configured with the same frame structure.

Note: this is a non-functional requirement, serving as a reference for O&M. The configuration cannot be verified in L2, because one NRCELLGRP scheduler does not know how other schedulers are configured.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

## 3.31.4 Scheduled UE per slot Pooling

### 3.31.4.1 Pooling Algorithm

#### 3.31.4.1.0-1 Pooling Algorithm Pooling Algorithm Overview (ID: 11210385)

**3.31.4.1.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13400384`)

Pooling Algorithm
13400384:
Pooling Algorithm
Pooling algorithm shall support load-metric based algorithm as defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6363\_replaced([11210707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For load-metric based algorithm, Baseband Resource manager(BBRM) shall use each cell’s averaged load measurement - Average number of scheduled UE per slot related to bearer (GBR and non-GBR) as input (defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6628\_replaced([11210812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and determine the “allowed maximum scheduled UE per slot per cell” (defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6548\_replaced([11211690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ElPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on L1 subpool, L1 pool and L2 subpool restriction.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to "BB pooling".
The flowchart begins with a "Start" node. From "Start", an arrow points to a diamond-shaped decision node labeled "BB pooling interval is started.".
There are two outgoing paths from this decision node:
1. A path labeled "YES" leads downwards to a rectangular process node. This node contains the text: "If bbPoolMode is "1: load-based", then go to load-based algorithm".
2. Another path, originating from the right side of the "BB pooling interval is started." diamond, leads to a parallelogram-shaped process node. This node contains the text: "BB pooling interval is SFN based, BBRM performs algorithm at the beginning of pooling period".
The flowchart visually represents a conditional check on whether the BB pooling interval has started, and based on that, it either proceeds to a load-based algorithm or performs a specific action related to SFN-based pooling.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04150835.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

During BB pooling period, BBRM shall distribute the scarce baseband pool resources. The resources, which are under control of the BBRM:

 for DL

o Number of PDSCH UEs per slot

 for UL in case of the Cell is not an SDL cell (which has no uplink), otherwise, each number should be 0.

o Number of PUSCH UEs per slot

o Number of PUCCH F1 for HARQ A/N per slot

o Number of PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N per slot

For each of the resource the BBRM calculate the resource share on cell basis.

For load-metric based algorithm, the resources which are needed for the scheduling of UEs with GBR bearers, shall be decided first followed by the needs of the UEs with non-GBR bearers. If multiple bearers are setup for a UE, the UE is only counted once for the number of UEs which can be scheduled per slot. The overall amount of resources the BBRM shall grant to the cells is the sum of the incrementally evaluated resource portions.

If NRBTS.actScheUePoolingEnh is 'FALSE' the load-metric based algorithm shall be based on 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6363\_replaced([11210707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Else (NRBTS.actScheUePoolingEnh is 'TRUE') the load-metric based algorithm shall be extended to Enhanced algorithm based on both the estimated demand and the actual measured historical usage ( 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32631\_replaced([11210789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BSPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Basically, the rules for determination the resource share are the same for DL and UL **except SDL cells.**

**Note: BBRM(UL) shall not include the SDL cells which have no uplink bandwidth in cellsetup stage for simple design.**

[CB014699-D]

**Note: When a cell supports critical traffic, no new cell load types are introduced for critical traffic, critical GBR shall be treated as GBR together with non-critical GBR, critical nonGBR shall be treated as nonGBR together with non-critical nonGBR.[End CB014699-D]**

---

#### 3.31.4.1.0-2 Pooling Algorithm Determination of the minimum resources for PUSCH &amp; PDSCH UEs per slot per cell (ID: 11210423)

**3.31.4.1.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `12787458`)

Pooling Algorithm
12787458:
Pooling Algorithm
If NRBTS.actScheUePoolingEnh is 'FALSE' the minimum of resources shall be defined as the following:

The minimum of resources, the BBRM shall assign to the cells, is defined by the O&M parameter bbPoolMinResource which provides the minimum portion in percent. Depending on the number of cells and the individual maximum number of resources available for the cell the minimum share is determined by the BBRM. The minimum resource Rmin,x is calculated as follows:

For the baseband pool resource PUSCH/PDSCH UE per slot

The minimum resource with respect to PUSCH/PDSCH UE per slot is given by:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$R\_{min,x}(i, t) = min { R\_{pool,x} \* \frac{bbPoolMinResource}{100} \* \frac{R\_{max,x}(i, t)}{\sum\_{k=1}^{K} R\_{max,x}(k, t)} } ; R\_{max,x}(i,t)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16713.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

With

 Rmin,x (i, t)

o Minimum granted resource of type X for cell i during time interval t (pooling period defined by bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))). If artificial load for EMF is enabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17863\_replaced([11183915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_PvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), one additional PDSCH UE shall be added to minimal resource, i.e. Rmin,x(i, t) = Rmin,x(i, t)+1.

In case of a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), it should be 0 for PUSCH UEs per slot.

 X

o Resource type which is

 PUSCH UEs per slot

 PDSCH UEs per slot

 RPool, x

o L1 Pool limit of resource x (e.g., scheduled UE per slot)  (defined by O&M parameter maxNumScheUePdschL1Pool or maxNumScheUePuschL1Pool for DL and UL respectively).

 bbPoolMinResource

o NIDD (hidden) parameter NRBTS/bbPoolMinResource

 Rmax,x (i, t)

o Maximum granted resource of type X for cell i during time interval t which is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Rmax,x (k,  t)

o Same as Rmax,x (i, t) however now for cell k

 xyz

o roundup to next integer value

Note: Theoretically the minimum scheduled PDSCH & PUSCH UE per slot calculation is related to several factors, like cell numbers within one pool, pool capacity and bbPoolMinResource configuration. For simplified implementation, the minimum scheduled PDSCH & PUSCH UE per slot is calculated based on L1 pool capacity, and the calculated minimum scheduled PDSCH & PUSCH UE per slot is applicable for L1 sub-pool and L2 sub-pool respectively in following load-metric pooling algorithm.

If NRBTS.actScheUePoolingEnh is 'TRUE' the minimum of resources shall be defined as the following:

Rmin,x (i, t)

With

 Rmin,x (i, t) should be defined as rdScheUePoolingMinResourceDL(5G\_UP\_ALG\_32702\_replaced([11215358](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxTC0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or rdScheUePoolingMinResourceUL(5G\_UP\_ALG\_32705\_replaced([11215373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxTC1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for DL or UL respectively, i.e., Rmin,x(i,t) = rdScheUePoolingMinResourceDL or rdScheUePoolingMinResourceUL

o Minimum granted resource of type X for cell i during time interval t (pooling period defined by bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))). [CB014542-C-UPD001] If artificial load for EMF is enabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17863\_replaced([11183915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_PvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), one additional PDSCH UE shall be added to minimal resource, i.e. Rmin,x(i, t) = Rmin,x(i, t)+1. Note that this step is executed only if there is remaining capacity in the L1 pool. [End CB014542-C-UPD001]

In case of a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), it should be 0 for PUSCH UEs per slot.

 X

o Resource type which is

 PUSCH UEs per slot

 PDSCH UEs per slot
