#### 3.31.4.1.0-4 Pooling Algorithm Round Robin based Algorithm (up to 26R1) (ID: 11210614)

**3.31.4.1.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12443960`)

Pooling Algorithm
12443960:
Pooling Algorithm
[Before CNI-136563] When the parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to '0:round-robin', this algorithm is selected to grant the total amount of scheduled UE per slot that can be used by a cell out of the total available scheduled UE per slot of the L1 subpool and L1 pool via round robin manner.

During each pooling period, all cell schedulers (5G L2-PS) shall send a resource request to the BBRM. In response to the received request the BBRM replies with a resource allocation to each cell scheduler". (BBRM only response to the request from the scheduler but is never at the initiative of the exchange).

**Algorithm Input:**

 up-to-date a list of cells, with corresponding L1 pool and L1 sub-pool configuration as defined in 5G\_UP\_1773\_replaced([11373109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueA6mfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 PDSCH and PUSCH UEs per slot capacity per L1 pool and L1 sub-pool configuration as defined in [11373764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueD98_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

 PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot capacity per L1 pool and L1 sub-pool configuration as defined in [11373764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueD98_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

 The minimum resource Rmin,x: minimum scheduled UE per slot per cell (DL/UL) as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 The maximum resource Rmax,x: maximum scheduled UE per slot per cell (DL/UL) as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Processing of BBRM for every pooling period:

 In the first step: The BBRM shall first reserve a minimum amount of required scheduled UE per slot for each cell (Rmin,x (i, t) defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 In the second step, the BBRM shall assign maximum amount of required scheduled UE per slot to one cell as the prioritized cell in the L1 pool (assume there is only one prioritized cell in the whole L1 pool). For the prioritized cell the following shall be calculated:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16719.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16719.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16719.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

 RPool, x

o L1 Pool limit of resource x (e.g., scheduled UE per slot) (defined by O&M parameter maxNumScheUePdschL1Pool or maxNumScheUePuschL1Pool for DL and UL respectively).

 NPool

o Number of cells within L1 Pool.

 Rmax,x (i, t) - refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

 In the third step,  the BBRM shall evenly assign the amount of required scheduled UE per slot to the remaining cells which has the same L1 subpool with prioritized cell (*pcell) considering the L1 subpool limit of resource.*

[image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16719.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

Note: This step is done if pooling at L1 subpool level applies according to the ASR rules below, otherwise it is skipped

 RL1subool, x

o L1 subpool limit of resource x (e.g., scheduled UE per slot) (defined by O&M parameter maxNumScheUePdschL1Sp or maxNumScheUePuschL1Sp for DL and UL respectively).

 NL1subpool

o Number of cells within L1 subpool where prioritized cell is allocated during the pooling period.

 i is the remaining cells which has the same L1 subpool with prioritized cell

 In the fourth step,  the BBRM shall evenly assign the amount of required scheduled UE per slot to the remaining cells which has different L1 subpool with prioritized cell considering the L1 subpool and L1 pool limit of resource.

[image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16719.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

 RL1subool, x

o L1 subpool limit of resource x (e.g., scheduled UE per slot) (defined by O&M parameter maxNumScheUePdschL1Sp or maxNumScheUePuschL1Sp for DL and UL respectively).

 NcellotherL1sps

o  the total amount of active cells in any other L1 subpool different from the one where the prioritized cell is located.

 i is the remaining cells which has the different L1 subpool from prioritized cell

The prioritized cell within the L1 subpool shall change between consecutive pooling period in a round robin manner between all cells in the L1 pool and L1 subpool.

Please note that here round down function is used to not exceed the L1 pool and subpool limit which may cause a little bit waste of resource. The Round robin algorithm is used for internal functionality test and is not delivered to customer, so it is acceptable here.

**Algorithm Output :**

 maxNumPdschPerSlotByBBRM: it is calculated as [image-5][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16719.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]

 maxNumPuschPerSlotByBBRM: it is calculated as [image-6][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16719.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]

 maxNumPucchF1PerSlotByBBRM: PUCCH F1 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8681\_replaced([11211775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9EnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 maxNumPucchF3PerSlotByBBRM: PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7948\_replaced([11211803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ro_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7949\_replaced([11211767](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9EnPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The algorithm follows the following ASR rules (Refer to 5G\_UP\_4567\_replaced([11373209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueBhqvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

1) The pooling decision as L1 pool and/or L1 sub-pool can be still cell specific, by considering only the primary subcell (p-subcell) of each cell.

2) If a L1 pool or L1 sub-pool contains no p-subcells or only 1 p-subcell, then pooling function can be skipped for that L1 pool or L1 sub-pool.

**Note: For an SDL cell without any uplink bandwidth, BBRM shall set maxNumPuschPerSlotByBBRM, maxNumPucchF1PerSlotByBBRM and maxNumPucchF3PerSlotByBBRM to 0.**

[CNI-136563]

Round robin algorithm will not be supported since CNI-136563

[End CNI-136563]

---

#### 3.31.4.1.0-5 Pooling Algorithm Load Metric based Algorithm (ID: 11210707)

**3.31.4.1.0-5.0-5**  (ID: `11210782`)

Pooling Algorithm
11210782:
Pooling Algorithm
When the NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to '1: load-metric', the amount of scheduled UE per slot available to be used by each cell in the same L1 Pool is determined by the BBRM in fair share manner based on the cell traffic load. The amount of scheduled UE per slot per cell is determined by the load metric based algorithm at pooling period N, and it will be valid for the next pooling interval time window starting from pooling period N+1.

The load metric per cell is calculated in terms of the resource required for GBR and/ nonGBR traffic service separately, and it is estimated as shown in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6630\_replaced([11211216](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6631\_replaced([11211393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note that the PxSCH messages (RA msg2, RA msg3, RA msg4) and SRB traffic are not considered for the cell load calculation for simplification, additionally those PxSCH messages are considered as minimum PxSCH resources.

The metric-based pooling algorithm is used to distribute the L1 Pooled scheduled UE per slot to each cell mapped to the same L1 pool.

**Algorithm Input:**

 up-to-date a list of cells, with corresponding L1 pool, L1 sub-pool and L2 sub-pool configuration as defined in 5G\_UP\_1773\_replaced([11373109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueA6mfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note: When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE, a cell list for PDSCH UE/TTI should consider both primary subcell and secondary subcell location with corresponding L1 pool and L1 subpool. A cell list for PUSCH UE/TTI should only consider primary subcell location with corresponding L1 pool and L1 subpool, as legacy implementation.

 PDSCH and PUSCH UEs per slot capacity per L1 pool, L1 sub-pool, and L2 sub-pool configuration as defined in [11373764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueD98_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

 PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot capacity per L1 pool, L1 sub-pool, and L2 sub-pool configuration as defined in [11373764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueD98_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

 The minimum resource Rmin,x: minimum scheduled UE per slot per cell (DL/UL) as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 The maximum resource Rmax,x: maximum scheduled UE per slot per cell (DL/UL) as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Load measurement related to bearer (x: GBR, and non-GBR) and resource (y: Scheduled UE per slot) measured for cell per pooling period as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6628\_replaced([11210812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* Load measurement related to Configured Grant (anticipatedCgSchedDensity, maxNcg as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16224\_replaced([11211015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* **[CB008600-F] Load measurement related to DC-GBR bearer and resource (y: Scheduled UE per slot) calculated for the cell as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31975\_replaced([11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** [End CB008600-F]\*\*\*\*

 PUCCH F3 demanding for 3CC CA in FDD FR1 as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6635\_replaced([11211875](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9rtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Algorithm processing in BBRM during pooling period:

 The BBRM shall first reserve a minimum amount of required scheduled UE per slot for each cell within a L1 subpool, is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* In the next step, the BBRM shall calculate scheduled UE per slot for CG traffic for each cell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20541\_replaced([11211108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where the amount of requested scheduled UE per slot for CG traffic shall be taken into consideration. In case CG traffic in one cell is zero (or not received by BBRM), the BBRM should skip this step and go next.
* **[CB008600-F] In the next step, the BBRM shall calculate scheduled UE per slot for DC-GBR traffic for each cell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31984\_replaced([11211200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where the amount of requested scheduled UE per slot for DC-GBR traffic shall be taken into consideration. In case DC-GBR traffic in one cell is zero (or not received by BBRM), the BBRM should skip this step and go next.**
* **[End CB008600-F]**

 In the next step, the BBRM shall calculate scheduled UE per slot for GBR traffic for each cell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6630\_replaced([11211216](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where the amount of requested scheduled UE per slot for GBR traffic shall be taken into consideration. In case GBR traffic in one cell is zero (or not received by BBRM), the BBRM should skip this step and go next.

 In the next step, the BBRM shall calculate scheduled UE per slot for non-GBR traffic for each cell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6631\_replaced([11211393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where the amount of requested scheduled UE per slot for non-GBR traffic shall be taken into consideration. In case nonGBR traffic in one cell is zero (or not received by BBRM), the BBRM should skip this step and go next.

 In the last step, the BBRM shall calculate the sum of scheduled UE per slot according to minimum resource allocation, CG,**[CB008600-F]DC-GBR**[End CB008600-F], GBR and non-GBR traffic allocation for each cell which is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6548\_replaced([11211690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ElPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The corresponding PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N is determined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7948\_replaced([11211803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ro_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

* The metric-based pooling algorithm shall be run per L1 pool, L1 subpool and L2 subpool independently, and the lowest value should be chosen as final available scheduled UE per slot per cell and sent to L2-PS in every pooling period.

**Algorithm Output:**

* maxNumPdschPerSlotByBBRM:it is calculated as [image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16725.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6548\_replaced([11211690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ElPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxNumPuschPerSlotByBBRM: it is calculated as [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16725.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6548\_replaced([11211690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ElPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxNumPucchF1PerSlotByBBRM: PUCCH F1 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8681\_replaced([11211775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9EnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxNumPucchF3PerSlotByBBRM: PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7948\_replaced([11211803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ro_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The algorithm follows the following ASR rules (Refer to 5G\_UP\_4567\_replaced([11373209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueBhqvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

1) The pooling decision as L1 pool and/or L1 sub-pool can be still cell specific, by considering only the primary subcell (p-subcell) of each cell.

2) If a L1 pool or L1 sub-pool contains no p-subcells or only 1 p-subcell, then pooling function can be skipped for that L1 pool or L1 sub-pool.

3) If a L2 sub-pool contains only one cell, then pooling function can be skipped for that L2 sub-pool.

4)   When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE, there are total two L1 pools and two L1 subpools per L1 pool on full BB board (in one L2-RT instance), DL subcells of one cell may be placed into two L1 pools/L1 subpools, PDSCH UE/TTI pooling shall behave as if all cells are located into one L1 pool and have the capacity of one individual L1 pool (or subpool) for PDSCH UE/TTI, PUCCH F1 and PUCCH F3.

5)   When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE, PUSCH UE/TTI pooling shall behave as if cells are located into two L1 pools and have the total two L1 pools capacity for PUSCH UE/TTI, do pooling function as legacy implementation.

6)  When large BB pooling is enabled on top of new deployment of L1 pool having 4 L1 subpools, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to FALSE (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3962\_replaced([11693584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D32e8P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))), scheduled UE/TTI pooling shall behave as well as legacy implementation, i.e., total L1 pool resources shall be shared and allocated to all cells per L1 pool completely.

Note: above scheduled UE per slot pooling algorithm shall be supported for eCPRI 7-2e, except large BB pooling and interworking with Configured Grant are not supported for eCPRI 7-2e. The corresponding features flags shall be disabled and sent to L2-PS. I.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3735\_replaced([11689933](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3Fp6P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) shall be set to FALSE, also Configured Grant (CG) feature shall be disabled, i.e. NRCELL.actUlCgType2(see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2384\_replaced([11692853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3q4tv9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) shall be set to FALSE.

---

#### 3.31.4.1.0-6 Pooling Algorithm Enhanced Scheduled UE per slot pooling algorithm based on both the estimated demand and the actual measured historical usage (ID: 11210789)

**3.31.4.1.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11210804`)

Pooling Algorithm
11210804:
Pooling Algorithm
When the NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to '1: load-metric', the BBRM shall determine the amount of scheduled UE per slot (available to be used by each cell in the same L1 Pool) in fair share manner, based on the cell traffic load for the actual measured historical usage of scheduled UEs/slot for all services including GBR and non-GBR, and the predictive demand for non-GBR only.

The extended metric-based pooling algorithm is used to distribute the L1 Pooled scheduled UE per slot to each cell mapped to the same L1 pool.

The amount of scheduled UE per slot per cell is determined at pooling period N, and it will be valid for the next pooling interval time window starting from pooling period N+1.

The load metric (actual measured historical usage of scheduled UEs/slot) per cell is calculated in terms of the resource required for GBR and/ nonGBR traffic service separately, and it is estimated as shown in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6630\_replaced([11211216](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6631\_replaced([11211393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note that the PxSCH messages (RA msg2, RA msg3, RA msg4) are not considered for the cell load calculation for simplification, additionally those PxSCH messages are considered as minimum PxSCH resources. Note for SRB it is included in GBR according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7945\_replaced([11210818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7946\_replaced([11210905](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL respectively.

Algorithm Input:

 up-to-date a list of cells, with corresponding L1 pool, L1 sub-pool and L2 sub-pool configuration as defined in 5G\_UP\_1773\_replaced([11373109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueA6mfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note: When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE, a cell list for PDSCH UE/TTI shall consider both primary subcell and secondary subcell location with corresponding L1 pool and L1 subpool. A cell list for PUSCH UE/TTI shall only consider primary subcell location with corresponding L1 pool and L1 subpool, as legacy implementation.

 PDSCH and PUSCH UEs per slot capacity per L1 pool, L1 sub-pool, and L2 sub-pool configuration as defined in 5G\_UP\_8411\_replaced([11374026](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueFzFPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot capacity per L1 pool, L1 sub-pool, and L2 sub-pool configuration as defined in 5G\_UP\_8411\_replaced([11374026](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueFzFPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 The minimum resource Rmin,x: minimum scheduled UE per slot per cell (DL/UL)  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be defined in terms of rdScheUePoolingMinResourceDL(5G\_UP\_ALG\_32702\_replaced([11215358](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxTC0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdScheUePoolingMinResourceUL(5G\_UP\_ALG\_32705\_replaced([11215373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxTC1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) respectively.

 The maximum resource Rmax,x: maximum scheduled UE per slot per cell (DL/UL) as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 Load measurement related to bearer (x: GBR, and non-GBR) and resource (y: Scheduled UE per slot) measured for cell per pooling period as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6628\_replaced([11210812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* [CB014542-C]Load measurement related to Configured Grant (anticipatedCgSchedDensity, maxNcg as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16224\_replaced([11211015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* Load measurement related to DC-GBR bearer and resource (y: Scheduled UE per slot) calculated for the cell as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31975\_replaced([11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB014542-C]

 PUCCH F3 demand for 3CC CA in FDD FR1 as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6635\_replaced([11211875](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9rtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Algorithm processing in BBRM during pooling period:

The extended metric-based pooling algorithm shall be run per L1 pool, L1 subpool and L2 subpool independently, and the lowest value should be chosen as final available scheduled UE per slot per cell and sent to L2-PS in every pooling period.

 The BBRM shall first reserve a minimum amount of required scheduled UE per slot for each cell within a L1 subpool, is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* [CB014542-C]In the next step, the BBRM shall calculate scheduled UE per slot for CG traffic for each cell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20544\_replaced([11211144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where the amount of requested scheduled UE per slot for CG traffic shall be taken into consideration. In case CG traffic in one cell is zero (or not received by BBRM), the BBRM should skip this step for this cell with zero traffic and go next.
* In the next step, the BBRM shall calculate scheduled UE per slot for DC-GBR traffic for each cell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31984\_replaced([11211200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where the amount of requested scheduled UE per slot for DC-GBR traffic shall be taken into consideration. In case DC-GBR traffic in one cell is zero (or not received by BBRM), the BBRM should skip this step for this cell with zero traffic and go next. [End CB014542-C]

 In the next step, the BBRM shall calculate scheduled UE per slot for GBR traffic for each cell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6630\_replaced([11211216](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where the amount of requested scheduled UE per slot for GBR traffic shall be taken into consideration. In case GBR traffic in one cell is zero (or not received by BBRM), the BBRM should skip this step for this cell with zero traffic and go next.

 In the next step, the BBRM shall calculate scheduled UE per slot for non-GBR traffic for each cell according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32798\_replaced([11211514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dhfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where the amount of requested scheduled UE per slot for non-GBR traffic shall be taken into consideration. In case nonGBR traffic in one cell is zero (or not received by BBRM), the BBRM should skip this step  for this cell with zero traffic and go next.

 In the last step, the BBRM shall calculate the sum of scheduled UE per slot according to minimum resource allocation, [CB014542-C]CG, DC-GBR,[End CB014542-C] GBR and non-GBR traffic allocation for each cell which is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6548\_replaced([11211690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ElPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The corresponding PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N is determined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7948\_replaced([11211803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ro_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Algorithm Output:

* maxNumPdschPerSlotByBBRM:it is calculated as [image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16727.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6548\_replaced([11211690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ElPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxNumPuschPerSlotByBBRM: it is calculated as [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16727.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6548\_replaced([11211690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ElPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxNumPucchF1PerSlotByBBRM: PUCCH F1 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8681\_replaced([11211775](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9EnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxNumPucchF3PerSlotByBBRM: PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7948\_replaced([11211803](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ro_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rationale:

The enhanced scheduled UEs/slot pooling algorithm shall consider both the estimated demand and the actual measured historical usage of scheduled UEs/slot as legacy algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6363\_replaced([11210707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on historical information only but without considering demand which may cause waste of pooled capacity and inter-cell fairness issues in the end user KPIs and may also cause algorithm being not able to recover from certain non-optimal conditions. The estimated demand is considered for non-GBR traffic only.

The algorithm follows the following ASR rules (Refer to 5G\_UP\_4567\_replaced([11373209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueBhqvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

1) The pooling decision as L1 pool and/or L1 sub-pool can be still cell specific, by considering only the primary subcell (p-subcell) of each cell.

2) If a L1 pool or L1 sub-pool contains no p-subcells or only 1 p-subcell, then pooling function can be skipped for that L1 pool or L1 sub-pool.

3) If a L2 sub-pool contains only one cell, then pooling function can be skipped for that L2 sub-pool.

4)   When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE, there are total two L1 pools and two L1 subpools per L1 pool on full BB board (in one L2-RT instance), DL subcells of one cell may be placed into two L1 pools/L1 subpools, PDSCH UE/TTI pooling shall behave as if all cells are located into one L1 pool and have the capacity of one individual L1 pool (or subpool) for PDSCH UE/TTI, PUCCH F1 and PUCCH F3.

5)   When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE, PUSCH UE/TTI pooling shall behave as if cells are located into two L1 pools and have the total two L1 pools capacity for PUSCH UE/TTI, do pooling function as legacy implementation.

6)  When large BB pooling is enabled on top of new deployment of L1 pool having 4 L1 subpools, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to FALSE (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3962\_replaced([11693584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D32e8P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))), scheduled UE/TTI pooling shall behave as well as legacy implementation, i.e., total L1 pool resources shall be shared and allocated to all cells per L1 pool completely.

Note: above scheduled UE per slot pooling algorithm shall be supported for eCPRI 7-2e, except large BB pooling and interworking with Configured Grant are not supported for eCPRI 7-2e. The corresponding features flags shall be disabled and sent to L2-PS. I.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3735\_replaced([11689933](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3Fp6P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) shall be set to FALSE, also Configured Grant (CG) feature shall be disabled, i.e. NRCELL.actUlCgType2(see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2384\_replaced([11692853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3q4tv9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) shall be set to FALSE.

---

### 3.31.4.2 Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation

#### 3.31.4.2.0-1 Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation Bookkeeping of allocated DL resources (ID: 11210818)

**3.31.4.2.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `12468219`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
12468219:
Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
The DL scheduler shall provide load measurements of the parameters which are required for the re-/distribution of the baseband pool resources. The load measurement is:

* Average number of PDSCH UEs scheduled in FD scheduler

The averaging of the load measurements shall be done by the arithmetic average. Separate load measurements shall be provided for GBR, and non-GBR bearers (indicated in the following by a small x) and the resources related to scheduled UEs (indicated in the following by a small y). The GBR load measurement shall additionally include the load measurements for the RA messages (RA msg2, RA msg4) and Signalling radio bearers (SRBs). The following equation describes the calculation rule for averaging the load measurements

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16734.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image, a corrupted file, or a deliberately black image with no discernible content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16734.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[Before CB014542-B]

If "pre-CS UEs" is more than 50, then average Loadx,y(i) = max(numMinUes, average Loadx,y(i)) for nonGBR.  where: numMinUes is 4 for TDD and 2 for FDD.

[CB014542-B]

If(NRBTS.actScheUePoolingEnh != true)

If "pre-CS UEs" is more than 50, then average Loadx,y(i) = max(4, average Loadx,y(i)) for nonGBR.

End If

[End CB014542-B]

Note: average Loadx,y(i) is the same variable as Loadx,y(i) with bar in math formula above.

"pre-CS UEs" means a complete candidate set without upper limit.

with:

Loadx,y(i): Load measurement related to bearer (x: GBR, and non-GBR) and resource (y: Scheduled UE per slot) measured for cell i in time *T*average*, ( The actual number of DL slots which PDSCH is scheduled shall be used in* T*average)*\*\*\*\*

t0: first slot in new measurement period,

x,y(i,t): Measurement related to bearer (x: GBR, and non-GBR) and resource (y: Scheduled UE per slot) measured for cell i in single slot.

*rdBbPoolDeprioritizedWeight is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25091\_replaced([11209479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwz6qfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*

[CB014542-B-UPD001]

The future demand Dx(i,t) for DL shall be defined as the following:

Dx(i,t)=(Number of pre-CS UEs to the resource type x including all traffic such as GBR and nonGBR)  / number of (DL (including special slot)) slots in one SFN(System Frame Number)

Rationale: Demand traffic Dx(i,t) is calculated and normalized by number of DL (including special slot)) slots in one SFN(System Frame Number) (Note for TDD this shall be dependent on frame structure). The normalization is based on the assumption that the latest value of number of Pre-CS UEs after normalization can just be scheduled within the pooling period. Note the latest value means instantaneous value of preCS UE at the time of load send to BBRM (DLMetricIndication), which is nothing but 0th slot for every bbPooling period.

[End CB014542-B-UPD001]

The measurement period and hence the time constant for averaging the load measurements *T*average *shall be conformed to the time period the BBRM redistributes the baseband resources and is defined by bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*\*\*

Note : Load measurement for GBR bearers (where x = GBR bearer) shall also consider and include the load measurement for the RA messages (RA msg2, RA msg4) and SRBs (Signalling radio bearers)

By the end of the measurement period:

If the excess demand requested for the DC-GBR service in the cell in the corresponding direction y, namely pxschDemandDcGbrExcess (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31975\_replaced([11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 0,

the load measurement of the GBR service is reduced by the maxGbrloadReductionPossible which is given by min(pxschDemandDcGbrExcess , LoadGBR,y(i))

pxschDemandDcGbrExcess is also reduced by the value of maxGbrloadReductionPossible and if still pxschDemandDcGbrExcess > 0

the load measurement of the nonGBR service is reduced by value of the maxNonGbrloadReductionPossible which is min(pxschDemandDcGbrExcess , Loadnon-GBR,y(i))

The resultant average load measurements shall be forwarded to the BBR and the load measurements shall be reset.

if NRBTS/NRDU/flexibleCaMode is set to value 3 (corresponding to NumberCellAmount) && dual cells setup in the L2-PS core && sum of active CA UE number of the two cells (counted only in Pcell) is greater than rdFDMReducedThresholdActiveCAUEnumber &&DPA split is disabled (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24678\_replaced([11124282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PCell shall exclude carrier aggregation DPA slots when calculate load measurement, which mean in the formula above, Taverage shall be decreased by DPA slots number during the period and  x,y(i,t) as 0 in DPA slot.

rdFDMReducedThresholdActiveCAUEnumber is defined in CP3.

Note that if multiple bearers are setup/multiplexed for a UE, the UE is only counted once for the number of UEs which can be scheduled per slot. So for both single GBR bearer case and multi-bearer (GBR bearer + non-GBR bearers) case only one is counted in GBR bearer.

Note that if multiple bearers are setup/multiplexed for a UE, the UE is only counted once for the number of UEs which can be scheduled per slot. So for both single non-GBR bearer case and multi-bearer (non-GBR bearers) case only one is counted in non-GBR bearer.

When DC-GBR bearer is also multiplexed with other bearers (GBR/nonGBR) for the UE, that PDSCH occasion shall either be counted as GBR nor a nonGBR bearer.

---

#### 3.31.4.2.0-2 Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation Bookkeeping of allocated UL resources (ID: 11210905)

**3.31.4.2.0-2.0-9**  (ID: `12469342`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
12469342:
Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
The UL scheduler shall provide load measurements of the parameters which are required for the re-/distribution of the baseband pool resources. The load measurement is:

* Average number of PUSCH UEs scheduled in FD scheduler

The averaging of the load measurements shall be done by the arithmetic average. Separate load measurements shall be provided for GBR, and non-GBR bearers (indicated in the following by a small x) and the resources related to scheduled UEs (indicated in the following by a small y). The GBR load measurement shall additionally include the load measurements for the RA message (RA msg3 (from DL grant) refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4775\_replaced([11194381](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv0cK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UL grant for contention resolution (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4777\_replaced([11194390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv0cLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and Signalling radio bearers (SRBs). The non-GBR load measurement shall additionally include the load measurements for SRs (Scheduling Requests) (i.e, srResp, PUSCH grant triggered by SR refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4788\_replaced([11194545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv1qUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The following equation describes the calculation rule for averaging the load measurements

[Before CB014542-B]

If "pre-CS UEs" is more than 50, then average Loadx,y(i) = max(numMinUes, average Loadx,y(i)) for nonGBR.  where: numMinUes is 4 for TDD and 2 for FDD.

[CB014542-B]

If(NRBTS.actScheUePoolingEnh != true)

If "pre-CS UEs" is more than 50, then average Loadx,y(i) = max(4, average Loadx,y(i)) for nonGBR.

End If

[End CB014542-B]

Note: average Loadx,y(i) is the same variable as Loadx,y(i) with bar in math formula above.

"pre-CS UEs" means a complete candidate set without upper limit.

with:

Loadx,y(i): Load measurement related to bearer (x: GBR, and non-GBR) and resource (y: Scheduled UE per slot) measured for cell i in time *T*average*,  ( The actual number of UL slots which PUSCH is scheduled shall be used in* T*average). A UE shall not be counted if it’s scheduled in a Configured Grant occasion.*\*\*\*\*

t0: first slot in new measurement period

x,y(i,t): Measurement related to bearer (x: GBR, and non-GBR) and resource (y: Scheduled UE per slot) measured for cell i in single slot. **A UE shall not be counted if it’s scheduled in a Configured Grant occasion.**

*rdBbPoolDeprioritizedWeight is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25091\_replaced([11209479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwz6qfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))*

[CB014542-B-UPD001]

The future demand Dx(i,t) for UL shall be defined as the following:

Dx(i,t)=(Number of pre-CS UEs to the resource type x including all traffic such as GBR and nonGBR)  / number of UL slots in one SFN(System Frame Number)

Rationale: Demand traffic Dx(i,t) is calculated and normalized by number of UL slots in one SFN(System Frame Number) (Note for TDD this shall be dependent on frame structure). The normalization is based on the assumption that the latest value of number of Pre-CS UEs after normalization can just be scheduled within the pooling period. Note the latest value means instantaneous value of preCS UE at the time of load send to BBRM (ULMetricIndication), which is nothing but 0th slot for every bbPooling period.

[End CB014542-B-UPD001]

The measurement period and hence the time constant for averaging the load measurements *T*average shall be conformed to the time period the BBRM redistributes the baseband resources and is defined by bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*

Note : Load measurement for GBR bearers (where x = GBR bearer) shall also consider and include the load measurement for the RA message (RA msg3 (from DL grant) refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4775\_replaced([11194381](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv0cK_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UL grant for contention resolution (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4777\_replaced([11194390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv0cLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and SRBs (Signalling radio bearers)

Note : Load measurement for non-GBR bearers (where x = non-GBR bearer) shall also consider and include the load measurement for SRs (Scheduling Requests) (i.e, srResp, PUSCH grant triggered by SR refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4788\_replaced([11194545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv1qUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

By the end of the measurement period:

If the excess demand requested for the DC-GBR service in the cell in the corresponding direction y, namely pxschDemandDcGbrExcess (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31975\_replaced([11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 0,

the load measurement of the GBR service is reduced by the maxGbrloadReductionPossible which is given by min(pxschDemandDcGbrExcess , LoadGBR,y(i))

pxschDemandDcGbrExcess is also reduced by the value of maxGbrloadReductionPossible and if still pxschDemandDcGbrExcess > 0

the load measurement of the nonGBR service is reduced by value of the maxNonGbrloadReductionPossible which is min(pxschDemandDcGbrExcess , Loadnon-GBR,y(i))

The resultant average load measurements shall be forwarded to the BBR and the load measurements shall be reset.

if NRBTS/NRDU/flexibleCaMode is set to 3 (corresponding to NumberCellAmount) && dual cells setup in the L2-PS core && sum of active CA UE number of the two cells (counted only in Pcell) is greater than rdFDMReducedThresholdActiveCAUEnumber&&DPA split is disabled (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24678\_replaced([11124282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), PCell shall exclude carrier aggregation DPA slots  when calculate load measurement, which mean in the formula above, Taverage shall be decreased by DPA slots number during the period and  x,y(i,t) as 0 in DPA slot(Measurement Processing cycle in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2936\_replaced([11123865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqmk8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rdFDMReducedThresholdActiveCAUEnumber is defined in CP3.

The scheduled PUSCH UEs due to Low Priority UL proactive grant (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4833\_replaced([11195231](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv6iyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or TCP Boost proactive grant (5G\_UP\_ALG\_16872\_replaced([11195403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7w8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **shall be excluded from PUSCH UE load report, including GBR and/or non-GBR bearer and/or DC-GBR bearer.**

Note that if multiple bearers are setup/multiplexed for a UE, the UE is only counted once for the number of UEs which can be scheduled per slot. So for both single GBR bearer case and multi-bearer (GBR bearer + non-GBR bearers) case only one is counted in GBR bearer.

Note that if multiple bearers are setup/multiplexed for a UE, the UE is only counted once for the number of UEs which can be scheduled per slot. So for both single non-GBR bearer case and multi-bearer (non-GBR bearers) case only one is counted in non-GBR bearer.

When DC-GBR bearer is also multiplexed with other bearers (GBR/nonGBR) for the UE, that PUSCH occasion shall either be counted as GBR nor a nonGBR bearer.

#### 3.31.4.2.0-3 Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation Bookkeeping of allocated UL resources for Configured Grant (CG) and calculation of anticipated CG scheduling density (ID: 11211015)

**3.31.4.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11211027`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
To be deleted after informing CFAM leader of 9215 as the update on the previous version of the requiremetn makes this new version useless.

Anticipated scheduling density for CG is calculated for the next period of duration T= [Before CB009215-D]NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod[CB009215-D]bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB009215-D] considering the CG allocations in the current period of duration T under evaluation as follows:

Consider j0 the first slot in the current period T under evaluation

sumNcg = 0;

maxNcg = 0;

In each slot j in the interval j0 … j0+T-1:

if a UE leaves CG firing state in slot j due to CG release (CG deactivate is not considered):

sumNcg  = sumNcg – k, where k is the number of CG occurrences since j0  for the UE

sumNcg  = sumNcg + Ncg(j)

if Ncg(j) > maxNcg

maxNcg = Ncg(j)

Additionally, in slot j0+T-1 only, if T < Tcg:

For each slot j in the interval  j0+T … j0+ Tcg:

sumNcg  = sumNcg + Ncg(j)

if Ncg(j) > maxNcg

maxNcg = Ncg(j)

anticipatedCgSchedDensity = sumNcg / (MAX(T',T'cg) \* maxNcg)

where:

- Tcg is the size of the CG pool in time domain as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14663\_replaced([11172788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuOgsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- T',T'cg is the number of UL slots in T,Tcg

- Ncg(j) number of CG UEs in a firing state (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15099\_replaced([11172972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuPu0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the slot j

- sumNcg = total number of CG scheduling

- maxNcg = MAX(every slot j, Ncg(j))

That is, the anticipated scheduling density is calculated for period T by considering the anticipated allocations over the entire period Tcg by removing the CG allocations that are deactivated or released.

Note that the evaluation has to be done for at least Tcg slots, otherwise CG occasions corresponding to UE with large CG periodicity could be missed.

---

#### 3.31.4.2.0-4 Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation Bookkeeping of Required DC-GBR DL/UL Resources (ID: 11211036)

**3.31.4.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11211040`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
Calculation of PxSCH allocation Demand for DC-GBR service per Slot

---

**3.31.4.2.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11211048`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
Every bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall calculate demand of the number of dynamic grant PxSCH allocations per slot in both DL/UL direction to serve the DC-GBR service in the cell, namely dcGbrPxschDemandPerSlot, as below:

pxschDemandDcGbr = ceil( pxschDemandDcGbrPerPoolingPeriod / numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod)

where

pxschDemandDcGbrPerPoolingPeriod is the total number of PxSCH allocations over pooling period required to serve the DC\_GBR service in the cell. It shall be computed as the sum of reqPxschGrantsPerPoolingPeriod (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31896\_replaced([11211056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of all the DC-GBR bearers configured in the cell.

j is the index of all DC-GBR bearers in the cell.

numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod is the number of scheduling slots (the slots with possible DL/UL grants) within the pooling period in the corresponding DL/UL direction. It shall be computed same as totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod as described in [11212148](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

In addition, gNB-DU shall also calculate excess PxSCH allocations requested for DC-GBR service in the cell from BBRM, namely excessRequestedDcGbrPxschDemand, as below

pxschDemandDcGbrExcess = pxschDemandDcGbr - requiredPxschDemandDcGbr

where

* requiredPxschDemandDcGbr is the the actual required number of dynamic grant PxSCH allocations per slot in both DL/UL direction to serve the DC-GBR service in the cell calculated as  pxschDemandDcGbrPerPoolingPeriod / numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod (without the ceil function).
* Eventually, In the same pooling period, gNB-DU shall reduce load measurements of the low prio services (GBR, nonGBR) in the corresponding direction (DL/UL) by the value of pxschDemandDcGbrExcess so that higher than needed DC-GBR PxSCH allocations requested for the DC-GBR service, namely pxschDemandDcGbr can be re-used for the PxSCH allocations of GBR and nonGBR services in the cell. Please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7945\_replaced([11210818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7946\_replaced([11210905](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the load measurement reductions of low prio services (GBR, nonGBR) in DL and UL respectively.
* Rationale: As the DC-GBR service is delay critical, higher than needed resources are requested for DC-GBR service from BBRM which would reduce the pooling efficiency. Hence, by reducing the resource demand of low priority services of the same cell which are not delay critical, the low priority services can utilise the excess allocated resources for DC-GBR services in the cell in the slots in which they are not used thereby freeing up resources for the other cells in the pool.

---

**3.31.4.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11211056`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
Maintenance of Required PxSCH allocations for a DC-GBR bearer per Pooling Period

---

**3.31.4.2.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11211064`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
gNB-DU shall calculate and maintain the required number of dynamic grant PxSCH allocations within any given BB pooling period, namely bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in both DL/UL direction for every DC-GBR bearer j configured in the cell as below

reqPxschGrantsPerPoolingPeriod (j)= ceil(maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j) / avgDcGbrBitsPerAllocation(j))

where

maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j) is the maximum data volume that is expected from the DC-GBR bearer j as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31898\_replaced([11211070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

avgDcGbrBitsPerAllocation shall present the average number of bits transmitted for the DC-GBR bearer j per PxSCH allocation. It shall be maintained as an exponential average and only the scheduling occurances with some data scheduled/received for the DC-GBR bearer shall be considered for the exponential averaging.

avgDcGbrBitsPerAllocation(j, t) = (1- 1/coeff) \* avgDcGbrBitsPerAllocation(j, t-1) + 1/coeff \* instDcGbrBitsPerAllocation (j,t)

where:

coeff is the expontential filter coefficient. It shall be set to a value of 200

The initial value of avgDcGbrBitsPerAllocation shall be set to the MDBV\_MAC of the corresponding DC-GBR bearer (see [11175619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)/[11196117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwApYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

instDcGbrBitsPerAllocation is the total number of bits scheduled/received for the corresponding PxSCH allocation.In DL, it shall be computed based on the scheduling of the PDSCH initial transmission whereas in UL, it shall be done based on the successful data reception on PUSCH transmission.

---

**3.31.4.2.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11211070`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
Maintenance of Maximum Data Volume Required for a DC-GBR bearer per Pooling period

---

**3.31.4.2.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11211075`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
gNB-DU shall calculate and maintain the maximum data volume in bits that would be expected to be trasmitted via dynamic grants per DC-GBR bearer within any given BB pooling period, namely bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in both DL/UL direction as per its configuration as below:

maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j) = max(0, min(maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriodBasedOnGFBR\_bits(j), maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriodBasedOnMDBV\_bits(j)) - ueCgCapacity)

where

* ueCgCapacity shall represent the configured data colume to be transmitted in the next pooling period via configured grants for the UE with DC-GBR bearer j, provided that it is in firing state at the end of current pooling window. If the UE with DC-GBR bearer have no configured CG profile or if it not in firing state, it shall be 0. In DL, it is irrelevent and hence it shall be always 0.
* maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriodBasedOnMDBV\_bits shall represent the maximum data volume in bits that would be expected from the DC-GBR bearer based on its configured short term max burst data rate (MDBV over PDB) which is calculated as below:
* maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriodBasedOnMDBV\_bits(j) = MDBVMAC/PDB \* poolingPeriod\_msecs

with

* MDBVMAC is the maximum data burst volume of the DC-GBR bearer along with L2 overheads as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31820\_replaced([11175619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_30958\_replaced([11196117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwApYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL/UL respectively.
* PDB is the packet delay budget of the DC-GBR bearer givan by NRDRB.delayCriticalGbrDrbParam.dlRanPdb [msec] /NRDRB.delayCriticalGbrDrbParam.ulRanPdb [msec] for DL/UL respectively
* poolingPeriod\_msecs is the pooling evaluation period given by bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriodBasedOnGFBR\_bits(j) shall represent the maximum data volume in bits that would be expected from the DC-GBR bearer in the next pooling period based on its configured guaranteed flow bitrate (GFBR over AW) which is calculated as below:
* maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriodBasedOnGFBR\_bits(j) = GFBRMAC(j)\*averagingWindow(j) - txDataVolAW-poolingPeriod(j)

with:

* GFBRMAC is the guranteed flow bitrate of the DC-GBR bearer including the L2 overheads as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31820\_replaced([11175619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_30958\_replaced([11196117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwApYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL and UL respectively.
* averagingWindow is the averaging window of the DC-GBR bearer over which GFBR is measured as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30379\_replaced([11175610](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuke8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_30953\_replaced([11196083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwACYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL and UL respectively.
* txDataVolAW-poolingPeriod is the successfully transmitted data volume in bits over the last (averagingWindow - poolingPeriod) period in the corresponding direction.

---

#### 3.31.4.2.0-5 Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation Overbooking factor for GBR and nonGBR resource evaluation (ID: 11211082)

**3.31.4.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11211096`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
11211096:
Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
An overbooking factor shall be considered in the resource evaluation for cells for that the resources are assigned only to bearers of higher priority (GBR and nonGBR). The scaling of the resources for the bearers of higher priority shall provide additional resources for the mitigation of the tense resource situation. The overbooking factor of GBR and nonGBR shall be calculated based on the following algorithms.

[docx\_desc][/docx\_desc][docx\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/attachments/m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file16754\_0.docx[/docx\_path]

with:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16754.002.png[/image\_path][/image-0]:               Average GBR load of resource x measured in cell i during time interval t-1

Rsum,x(i,t-1):      Total sum of resource x assigned to cell i during time interval t-1

o:              Overbooking factor

t:               Time interval the calculation refers to

i:               Index of the cell

x:               Resource for that the calculation relates to (UE DL, UE UL, or elementary PUSCH PRB)

The R&D parameters rdBbPoolOverbookGbr (proposed range: 1.000000, …, 1.500000; proposed default: 1.25) and rdBbPoolOverbooknonGbr (proposed range: 1.000000, …, 1.500000; proposed default: 1.25) shall define the overbooking factor.

---

#### 3.31.4.2.0-6 Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation Bookkeeping of allocated resources for UL CoMP (ID: 12747178)

**3.31.4.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12747317`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
**Calculation of PUSCH allocation Demand for UL CoMP service per Slot**

---

**3.31.4.2.0-6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12747186`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
Every bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall calculate demand of the number of dynamic grant PUSCH allocations per slot in UL direction to serve the UL CoMP service in the cell i, namely ulCompPuschDemandPerSlot, as below:

ulCompPuschDemandPerSlot(i) = ceil( ulCompPuschDemandPerPoolingPeriod (i) / numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod)

ulCompPuschDemandPerPoolingPeriod(i) = reqUlCompCombiningPerPoolingPeriod(i)  + reqUlCompCandSinrMeasPerPoolingPeriod(i)

where

ulCompPuschDemandPerPoolingPeriod is the total number of PUSCH allocations over pooling period required to serve the UL CoMP service/traffic in the cell. It shall be computed as the sum of reqUlCompCombiningPerPoolingPeriod ([12747325](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_51zX038uEfCiUemk-K-C4g)) for all the UL CoMP combining and reqUlCompCandSinrMeasPerPoolingPeriod ([12747360](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_BdHAEX8yEfCiUemk-K-C4g)) for call the candidate measurement handling .

numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod is the number of scheduling slots (the slots with possible UL grants) within the pooling period in the corresponding UL direction. It shall be computed same as totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod as described in [11212148](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

**3.31.4.2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `12747325`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
**Calculation of PUSCH allocation Demand for UL CoMP Combining**

---

**3.31.4.2.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12747326`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
Every bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall calculate demand of the number of dynamic grant PUSCH allocations in UL direction to serve the UL CoMP Combining in the cell i over pooling period, namely reqUlCompCombiningPerPoolingPeriod.

reqUlCompCombiningPerPoolingPeriod(i)=Sum(rrmNumUlCompCombUeSlot) over bbPoolEvalPeriod

rrmNumUlCompCombUeSlot is the total number of UL CoMP eligible UE per slot defined in [12740825: Select UE(s) for UL CoMP Basic PUSCH data reception](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_JDVHcHv5EfCiUemk-K-C4g)

---

**3.31.4.2.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `12747360`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
**Calculation of PUSCH allocation Demand for Candidate SINR measurement handling in  UL CoMP**

---

**3.31.4.2.0-6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12747361`)

Cell load measurement and scheduled UEs per slot demand estimation
Every bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall calculate demand of the number of dynamic grant PUSCH allocations per slot in UL direction to serve the demand for Candidate SINR measurement handling in UL CoMP service in the cell i, namely reqUlCompCandSinrMeasPerPoolingPeriod.

reqUlCompCandSinrMeasPerPoolingPeriod(i)=Sum(rrmNumCandSinrUeSlot) over bbPoolEvalPeriod.

rrmNumCandSinrUeSlot is the total number of UL CoMP candidate SINR measurement handling per slot defined in [12742860: Select UE(s) for UL CoMP Basic SINR Measurement](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_rQqEcHyeEfCiUemk-K-C4g)

---

### 3.31.4.3 Calculation of the resources for Configured Grant

#### 3.31.4.3.0-1 Calculation of the resources for Configured Grant Calculation of the resources for CG - Step 1 (ID: 11211108)

**3.31.4.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11211137`)

Calculation of the resources for Configured Grant
11211137:
Calculation of the resources for Configured Grant
Step 1: Resource share for CG users:

The calculation of the shared resources based on ideal conditions is defined by

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16757.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

with

Rideal shared,CG(i,t): Ideal shared CG resource interval t calculated for the cell i

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16757.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]: Average CG load during time interval t-1 measured for the cell i, calculated as follows:

If anticipatedCgSchedDensity > rdMaxCgSchedDensityWithoutAdditionalReservation/100 or maxNcg (i, t-1) = 0

[image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16757.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]  = maxNcg (i, t-1)

Else

[image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16757.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]  = 1+ MAX(0, maxNcg (i, t-1) - Rmin,x (i, t)),

Where:

* anticipatedCgSchedDensity, maxNcg are computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16224\_replaced([11211015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rdMaxCgSchedDensityWithoutAdditionalReservation (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16227\_replaced([11173585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuUnVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Rmin,x(i,t): Minimum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i, define in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rmax,x(i,t): Maximum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t given for the cell i, defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

t: Time interval the calculation refers to (pooling period defined by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod)

i: Index of the cell allocated to the baseband pool

x: Resource for that the calculation relates to (PUSCH UEs per slot equivalents)

Based on the ideal share and the restrictions, which are given by the utilized and available baseband pool resources, the shared CG resources can be calculated.

[image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16757.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

with

Rshared,CG(i,t): Shared CG resource during time interval t calculated for the cell i

RCG,pool,x(t): Available CG pool resources related to the resource type x during time interval t

The CG pool resources are the pool resources lessen by the minimum cell resource of all cells controlled by the BBRM (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The following equation defines the calculation rule.

[image-5][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16757.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]

with

Rpool,x: pool resources of resource X for the considered cell during time interval t depending on L2 subpool(defined by O&M parameter maxNumScheUePdschL2Sp or maxNumScheUePuschL2Sp for DL and UL respectively), L1 subpool(defined by O&M parameter maxNumScheUePdschL1Sp or maxNumScheUePuschL1Sp for DL and UL respectively), L1 pool(defined by O&M parameter maxNumScheUePdschL1Pool or maxNumScheUePuschL1Pool for DL and UL respectively).

j:   Index of the cell

Npool: Number of cells in baseband pool, whether it is L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool will be corresonding to Rpool,x

---

#### 3.31.4.3.0-2 Calculation of the resources for Configured Grant Calculation of the resources for CG - Step 2 (ID: 11211144)

**3.31.4.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11211162`)

Calculation of the resources for Configured Grant
11211162:
Calculation of the resources for Configured Grant
Step 2: Resource share for CG users for L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool:

The shared CG resources shall be calculated for each cell within L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool respectively where this cell is allocated according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20541\_replaced([11211108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and make the minimum one of the three as the final value for each cell. For simplicity, it is called Rminshared,CG(i,t): which represents shared CG resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16760.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB008224-D]

Note: For the SDL cells, the Rminshared,CG,x(i,t) should be 0.

[End CB008224-D]

### 3.31.4.4 Calculation of resources for DC-GBR bearer

#### 3.31.4.4.0-1 Calculation of resources for DC-GBR bearer Calculation of resources for DC-GBR bearer - Step 1 (ID: 11211175)

**3.31.4.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11211194`)

Calculation of resources for DC-GBR bearer
11211194:
Calculation of resources for DC-GBR bearer
Step 1: Resource share for DC-GBR users:

The calculation of the shared resources based on ideal conditions is defined by

[Before CB008600-F-UPD005]  
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$R\_{idealShared, DC-GBR}(i,t) = \max{\min{Load\_{DC-GBR}(i,t-1); R\_{max,x}(i, t) - R\_{min,x}(i, t)}, 0}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/056ae912-3d09-4273-a3d8-c30ff3d315f7.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB008600-F-UPD005]  
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula is:
$R\_{idealShared, DC-GBR}(i,t) = \max{\min{\sqrt{Load\_{DC-GBR}(i,t-1)}, R\_{max,x}(i,t) - R\_{min,x}(i,t) - R\_{minShared,CG}(i,t)}, 0}$
The formula defines $R\_{idealShared, DC-GBR}(i,t)$ as the maximum of the minimum of two terms, and zero. The first term is the square root of $Load\_{DC-GBR}(i,t-1)$. The second term is $R\_{max,x}(i,t) - R\_{min,x}(i,t) - R\_{minShared,CG}(i,t)$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/729159d5-91bf-45e2-8c03-bb6e1709b9dd.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[End CB008600-F-UPD005]

with

Rideal shared,DC-GBR(i,t): Ideal shared DC-GBR resource interval t calculated for the cell i

[image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16763.002.png[/image\_path][/image-2]: Average DC-GBR load during time interval t-1 measured for the cell i, given by dcGbrPxschDemandPerSlot, calculated as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31975\_replaced([11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) at the end of last pooling period.

Rmin,x(i,t): Minimum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i, define in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rmax,x(i,t): Maximum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t given for the cell i, defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rmax,x(i,t): Maximum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t given for the cell i, defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

RminShared,CG,x(i,t):      Minimum shared CG resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see [11211144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

t: Time interval the calculation refers to (pooling period defined by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod)

i: Index of the cell allocated to the baseband pool

x: Resource for that the calculation relates to

Based on the ideal share and the restrictions, which are given by the utilized and available baseband pool resources, the shared DC-GBR resources can be calculated.

[image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16763.003.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

with

Rshared,DC-GBR(i,t): Shared DC-GBR resource during time interval t calculated for the cell i

RDC-GBR,pool,x(t): Available DC-GBR pool resources related to the resource type x during time interval t

The DC-GBR pool resources are the CG pool resources lessen by the CG cell resource of all cells controlled by the BBRM (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The following equation defines the calculation rule.

[image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16763.004.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

with

R*pool,x:  configured capacity (in terms of pooled resources X) for the considered pool:*

 L2 subpool: the capacity is defined by the O&M parameters maxNumScheUePdschL2Sp and maxNumScheUePuschL2Sp for DL and UL respectively;

 L1 subpool: the capacity is defined by the O&M parameters maxNumScheUePdschL1Sp and maxNumScheUePuschL1Sp for DL and UL respectively;

 L1 pool: the capacity is defined by the O&M parameters maxNumScheUePdschL1Pool and maxNumScheUePuschL1Pool for DL and UL respectively;

j:  Index of the cell

N*pool: number of cells hosted by the specific l2subpool/l1subpool/l1pool under consideration;*

Rminshared,CG:  Minimum shared CG resource during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20544\_replaced([11211144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Value is only relevant for UL direction and it's set to zero for DL direction.

The calculated RDC-GBR,pool,x(t) can be different for different pools of same type, as it depends on the resources already allocated to the cells hosted by the specific pool.

#### 3.31.4.4.0-2 Calculation of resources for DC-GBR bearer Calculation of the resources for DC-GBR - Step 2 (ID: 11211200)

**3.31.4.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11211210`)

Calculation of resources for DC-GBR bearer
11211210:
Calculation of resources for DC-GBR bearer
Step 2: Resource share for DC-GBR users for L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool:

The shared DC-GBR resources shall be calculated for each cell within L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool respectively where this cell is allocated according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31971\_replaced([11211175](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and make the minimum one of the three as the final value for each cell. For simplicity, it is called Rminshared,DC-GBR(i,t): which represents shared DC-GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool.
