### 3.31.4.5 Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer

#### 3.31.4.5.0-1 Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer - Step 1 (ID: 11211220)

**3.31.4.5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11211246`)

Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer
11211246:
Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer
Step 1: Dedicated resources assigned to GBR bearers

For each cell a minimum of baseband resources, which can be assigned to the GBR bearers, shall be provided. The dedicated resources, which represent the basic resource share the cell receives for the scheduling of the GBR bearers in time interval t, is the minimum of the load conditions evaluated in the last measurement interval t-1 and the calculated minimum of resources the BBRM assigns to the cells.  The rule for calculating the dedicated GBR resources is:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16769.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

with

Rdedicated,GBR,x(i,t): Dedicated resource related to the class of GBR bearers during time interval t (pooling period defined by [Before CB009215-D]NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod[CB009215-D]bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).[End CB009215-D]) calculated for the cell i

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16769.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]:  Average GBR load of resource x measured during time interval t-1 for cell i

Rmin,x(i,t):  Minimum cell resource of resource x (see 5G\_UL\_ALG\_7942)

t:  Time interval the calculation refers to (pooling period defined by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod [CB009215-D]for TDD/NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriodFdd for FDD.[End CB009215-D])

i:  Index of the cell

x:            Resource for that the calculation relates

Note that if multiple bearers are setup for a UE, the UE is only counted once for the number of UEs which can be scheduled per slot. So for both single GBR bearer case and multi-bearer (GBR bearer + non-GBR bearers) case only one is counted in GBR bearer.

---

#### 3.31.4.5.0-2 Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer - Step 2 (ID: 11211252)

**3.31.4.5.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11211362`)

Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer
11211362:
Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer
Step 2: Resource share for GBR bearers:

Whenever the load coming from the GBR bearers increase the amount of the dedicated resources (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10362\_replaced([11211220](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the BBRM shall assign in addition to the dedicated resources shared resources. The calculation of the add-on in resources shall be done in two steps. The first step provides the extra resources for ideal conditions for that the BBRM doesn’t have to scale the resources. The second step specifies the calculation rule for conditions for that the limitation of the available pool resources has to be considered.

The calculation of the shared resources based on ideal conditions is defined by

[Before CB008600-F-UPD005]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features, text, or objects.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16775.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB008600-F-UPD005]  
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a dark color on a white background. The equation is:
$R\_{idealShared,GBR}(i,t) = max{min{Load\_{GBR}(i,t-1) - R\_{dedicated,GBR,x}(i, t); R\_{max,x}(i, t) - R\_{min,x}(i, t) - R\_{minShared,DC-GBR,x}(i,t)}, 0}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/400b2c1a-c4b8-4220-849d-113029249915.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[End CB008600-F-UPD005]

with

Rideal shared,GBR,x(i,t): Ideal shared GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i

Rdedicated,GBR,x(i,t): Dedicated GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i

[image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16775.002.png[/image\_path][/image-2]: Average GBR load related to the resource type x during time interval t-1 measured for the cell i, defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6628\_replaced([11210812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rmin,x(i,t): Minimum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i, define in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rmax,x(i,t): Maximum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t given for the cell i, defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB008600-F-UPD005]

RminShared,DC-GBR,x(i,t):      Minimum shared DC-GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see [11211200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

[End CB008600-F-UPD005]

t: Time interval the calculation refers to (pooling period defined by bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))))

i: Index of the cell allocated to the baseband pool

x: Resource for that the calculation relates to (PDSCH UEs per slot equivalents, PUSCH UEs per slot equivalents)

Based on the ideal share and the restrictions, which are given by the utilized and available baseband pool resources, the shared GBR resources can be calculated.

[image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16775.003.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

with

Rshared,GBR,x(i,t):  Shared GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i

RGBR,pool,x(t):  Available GBR pool resources related to the resource type x during time interval t

The GBR pool resources are the pool resources lessen by the minimum cell resource of all cells controlled by the BBRM (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The following equation defines the calculation rule.

**[End CB008600-F]**

with

R*pool,x:  configured capacity (in terms of pooled resources X) for the considered pool:*

 L2 subpool: the capacity is defined by the O&M parameters maxNumScheUePdschL2Sp and maxNumScheUePuschL2Sp for DL and UL respectively;

 L1 subpool: the capacity is defined by the O&M parameters maxNumScheUePdschL1Sp and maxNumScheUePuschL1Sp for DL and UL respectively;

 L1 pool: the capacity is defined by the O&M parameters maxNumScheUePdschL1Pool and maxNumScheUePuschL1Pool for DL and UL respectively;

Value is only relevant for UL direction and it's set to zero for DL direction.

**[CB008600-F] Rminshared,DC-GBR:  Minimum shared DC-GBR resource during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31984\_replaced([11211200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).** [End CB008600-F]\*\*\*\*

The calculated RGBR,pool,x(t) can be different for different pools of same type, as it depends on the resources already allocated to the cells hosted by the specific pool.

#### 3.31.4.5.0-3 Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer - Step 3 (ID: 11211368)

**3.31.4.5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11211387`)

Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer
11211387:
Calculation of the resources for GBR bearer
Step 3: Resource share for GBR bearers for L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool:

The shared GBR resources shall be calculated for each cell within L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool respectively where this cell is allocated according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10363\_replaced([11211252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72dvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and make the minimum one of the three as the final value for each cell. For simplicity, it is called Rminshared,GBR,x(i,t): which represents shared GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool.

[CB008224-D]

Note: For the SDL cells, the Rminshared,GBR,x(i,t) should be 0.

[End CB008224-D]

### 3.31.4.6 Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource

#### 3.31.4.6.0-1 Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer w/o enhanced pooling algorithm - Step 1 (ID: 11211400)

**3.31.4.6.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12463323`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
12463323:
Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
Step 1: Resource share for non-GBR bearers
 
The remaining resources which can be assigned to the cells for the scheduling of the non-GBR bearers shall be evaluation by the BBRM. For this purpose the BBRM shall determine in a first step the total amount of resources, which are still under control of the BBRM after processing the resource requests of the GBR bearers. The equation for calculating the remaining resources is:

i: Index of the cell
x: Resource for that the calculation relates to (PDSCH UE per slot, PUSCH UE per slot)
 
Based on the maximum amount of the shared resources available for the non-GBR bearers, the average load measurements of the non-GBR bearers during the time interval t-1 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6628\_replaced([11210812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and the resources of the non-GBR pool the shared non-GBR resources can be calculated for the individual cells.
 
[image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features, text, or objects.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16783.002.png[/image\_path][/image-2]
where:
 
 *nonGbrMinLoad = 0.1*
[PR839206]
Additionally, if the cumulative sum of the reported nonGBR load and portion of nonGBR load reduced due to excessive reported DC-GBR demand (namely nonGbrLoadRedFromDcGbrExcess) across all the cells is lower than the total pool resources available for nonGBR bearers during time interval t, then the nonGBR load of each of the cells shall be increased by the same portion of nonGBR load reduced due to excessive reported DC-GBR demand of the corresponding cell to improve the fairness in the distribution of the excess pool resources after satisfying the reported demand requested for the nonGBR bearers in each of the cells.
[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is an "if" statement that compares a variable `RnonGBR.pool,x(t)` to a summation. The summation runs from `i=1` to `Npool`. The terms within the summation are `LoadnonGBR,x(i, t-1)` and `nonGbrLoadRedFromDcGbrExcess(i, t-1)`. The formula is written in a standard mathematical notation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/275265ee-53bb-4b21-bb4f-0866fe28a01e.png[/image\_path][/image-3]
[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a serif font. The equation is:
∀i ∈ Npool: LoadnonGBR,z(i,t-1) += nonGbrLoadRedFromDcGbrExcess(i,t - 1)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/96fbd3e2-72f1-4476-9f48-419b3803aaee.png[/image\_path][/image-4]
where, nonGbrLoadRedFromDcGbrExcess(i,t-1) shall represent the portion of nonGBR load which is reduced to accomodate for the excessive DC-GBR demand requested for the cell i at the end of the previous pooling period t-1. For details, pls refer to [11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). Note, it is possible that excessive DC-GBR demand (namely pxschDemandDcGbrExcess, see [11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) shall be used to reduce both GBR and/or nonGBR load of the cell. In that case, nonGbrLoadRedFromDcGbrExcess shall represent only portion of the reduced nonGBR load and not full excessive DC-GBR demand (namely pxschDemandDcGbrExcess).
[End PR839206] 
Rational: BBRM distributes the left BB pool resource (beside minimum resource and shared GBR resource) according to non-GBR traffic load. *nonGbrMinLoad is taken as minimum value of [image-5][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16783.003.png[/image\_path][/image-5] to make sure that all the remaining resources are distributed, even in the (corner) case that some or all cells report [image-6][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16783.004.png[/image\_path][/image-6]. In the case of some or all cells with 0 <= [image-7][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16783.005.png[/image\_path][/image-7]<* nonGbrMinLoad, those cells' nonGBR traffic loads are unified as *nonGbrMinLoad as minimum non-GBR traffic load.*\*\*
 
 
[image-8][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16783.006.png[/image\_path][/image-8]
 
with
 
[image-9][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16783.007.png[/image\_path][/image-9]: Average non-GBR load related to the resource type x during time interval t-1 measured for the cell i, defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6628\_replaced([11210812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
RnonGBR,pool,x(t): Available L1 pool, L1 subpool and L2 pool resources for non-GBR bearers during time interval t related to the resource type x. The non-GBR pool resources are the remaining resources after satisfaction of the GBR bearer’s need which is expressed by the GBR pool resource lessen by the sum of the shared GBR resources. The following equation defines the calculation rule
[image-10][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16783.008.png[/image\_path][/image-10]
Note that if multiple bearers are setup for a UE, the UE is only counted once for the number of UEs which can be scheduled per slot. So for both single non-GBR bearer case and multi-bearer (non-GBR bearers) case only one is counted in non-GBR bearer.

#### 3.31.4.6.0-2 Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer with enhanced pooling algorithm - Step 1 (ID: 11211514)

**3.31.4.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11211520`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
Overview

---

**3.31.4.6.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11211527`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
According to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32631\_replaced([11210789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6BSPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) the enhanced scheduled UEs/slot pooling algorithm shall consider both the actual measured historical usage of scheduled UEs/slot and the estimated demand for non-GBR traffic only.

Based on the principle above two rounds of resource allocation for the non-GBR bearer are specified in the following: Round I (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32803\_replaced([11211531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8diPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and Round II (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32804\_replaced([11211604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8djPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

The BBRM shall calculate the scheduled UEs/slot in two rounds of resource allocation for the non-GBR bearer [Before CB014542-C-UPD001] and calculate the scheduled UEs/slot for low priority between the two rounds [End CB014542-C-UPD001] as specified in the following:

* Round I for actual measured historical usage of scheduled UEs/slot (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32803\_replaced([11211531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8diPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),
* [Before CB014542-C-UPD001]**[CB014542-C] Low-Priority Demand-Based Allocation(s) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32817\_replaced([11211593](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8divvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** [End CB014542-C][End CB014542-C-UPD001]\*\*\*\*
* Round II for estimated demand for non-GBR traffic (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32804\_replaced([11211604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8djPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

**3.31.4.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11211531`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer in Enhanced Algorithm -Round I

---

**3.31.4.6.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11211586`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
11211586:
Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
Round I is to allocate the scheduled UE/slot demand up to the measured historical usage of the cell (multiplied by an overbooking factor). This round is executed first to ensure that the realistically usable portion of the scheduled UE/slot demand can be allocated at a higher priority than uncertain and speculative usage.

The Resource share for non-GBR bearers Rmax shared,nonGBR,x(i,t) shall be calculated the same as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10365\_replaced([11211400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) except the R'max,x(i,t) as in this this round only the maximum allocation of the cell shall be decreased based on the historical usage of the poolable resource.

[Before CB014542-B-UPD002]

R'max,x(i,t)= **min ( Rmax,x(i,t)- Rmin,x(i,t)-Rminshared,CG(i,t) - Rminshared,DC-GBR,x(i,t) - RminsharedGBR(i, t)**, max (T, (1 + O) \* Hx(i) **) )**\*\*\*\*

[CB014542-B-UPD002]

R'max,x(i,t)= **min ( Rmax,x(i,t)- Rmin,x(i,t)-Rminshared,CG(i,t) - Rminshared,DC-GBR,x(i,t) - RminsharedGBR(i, t)**, RoundupToInteger(Max(0, **max (T, (1 + O) \* Hx(i)** ) -Rmin,x(i,t)-(Rminshared,CG(i,t) + Rminshared,DC-GBR,x(i,t) + RminsharedGBR(i, t)) + LoadGbr)));***\****\*

[End CB014542-B-UPD002]

Rmax,x(i,t): Maximum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t given for the cell i, defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rmin,x(i,t):       Minimum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i, define in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rminshared,CG(i,t):  Rminshared,CG(i,t): Minimum shared CG resource (only relevant for UL direction, set to 0 for DL direction) related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell I after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20544\_replaced([11211144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Rminshared,DC-GBR,x(i,t):  Minimum shared DC-GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31984\_replaced([11211200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

RminsharedGBR(i, t):  Minimum shared GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10364\_replaced([11211368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72fPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB014542-B-UPD002]

LoadGbr: Average GBR load of resource x measured during time interval for cell i, defined and calculated in ([11210812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_IrZkkvvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB014542-B-UPD002]

T:  Typical Usage in a cell, defined by R&D parameter rdScheUePoolingTypicalUeSlotUsage (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32809\_replaced([11215385](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxTC1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/[11215385](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_e3DHYPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for TDD and rdScheUePoolingTypicalUeSlotUsageFDD ([12554031](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Yt-YECWZEfCNjfqfyUlvmw)) for FDD

O:  Overallocation Factor, defined by R&D parameter rdScheUePoolingOverAllocFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32811\_replaced([11215398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxTC2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Hx(i):  Average non-GBR load related to the resource type x during time interval t-1 measured for the cell i, i.e, [image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16788.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0],  defined and calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10365\_replaced([11211400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note that Hx(i) here does not contain the excessive DC-GBR demand..

t:  Time interval the calculation refers to (pooling period defined by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod for TDD or NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriodFdd for FDD respectively (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

i:  Index of the cell

x:  Resource for that the calculation relates to (PDSCH UE per slot, PUSCH UE per slot)

The remaining resources which can be assigned to the cells for the scheduling of the non-GBR bearers shall be evaluated by the BBRM. For this purpose the BBRM shall determine in a first step the total amount of resources, which are still under control of the BBRM after processing the resource requests of the GBR bearers. The equation for calculating the remaining resources is:

Rmax shared,nonGBR,x(i,t)=max(R'max,x(i,t), 0)

Rmax shared,nonGBR,x(i,t): Maximum amount of shared resources which are available for non-GBR bearers related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i

R'max,x(i,t): Maximum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t given for the cell i, derived from above calculation

Rmin,x(i,t): Minimum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i, define in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rminshared,GBR,x(i,t): Minimum shared GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10364\_replaced([11211368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72fPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$R\_{shared,nonGBR-R1,x}(i,t) = \min { R\_{max,shared,nonGBR\_x}(i,t); \frac{D3\_x(i,t)}{\sum\_{j=1}^{N\_{pool}} D3\_x(j,t)} \times R\_{nonGBR,pool,x}(t) }$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16788.003.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

with

RsharednonGBR-R1,x(i,t) The resources of the shared non-GBR resources after Round I

[Before CB014542-B-UPD001]

D3x(i,t) = max**((Sum of Number of pre-CS UEs to the resource type x per time interval t for the cell / number of (DL/UL, i.e, x) slots per time interval t for the cell i) - D2x(i,t), *nonGbrMinLoad \**). where* nonGbrMinLoad = 0.1***\*\*\*

with

“pre-CS UEs” means a complete candidate set without upper limit. Please note that existing averages (details shall be defined in EFS) should be reused to get this value in order to save CPU consumption. And D2DL(i,t) and D2UL(i,t) are specified as the following respectively:

[CB014542-B-UPD001]

[Before CB014542-B-UPD002]

D3x(i,t) = max**(Dx(i,t) - D2x(i,t), *nonGbrMinLoad/100 \**). where* nonGbrMinLoad = 0.1***\*\*\*

[CB0145452-B-UPD002]

D3x(i,t) = max**(max(Dx(i,t), Hx(i)) - D2x(i,t), *nonGbrMinLoad/100 \**). where* nonGbrMinLoad = 0.1;***\*\*\*

D3x(i,t)=max(Min (R'max,x(i,t), D3x(i,t)), 0.0001)

[End CB014542-B-UPD002]

Dx(i,t) is the future demand defined for DL as specified in [11210818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ItVeQPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and UL as specified in [11210905](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_JGTX4PvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

[End CB014542-B-UPD001]

The non-GBR pool resources are the remaining resources after satisfaction of the GBR bearer’s need which is expressed by the GBR pool resource lessen by the sum of the shared GBR resources. The following equation defines the calculation rule

Note that if multiple bearers are setup for a UE, the UE is only counted once for the number of UEs which can be scheduled per slot. So for both single non-GBR bearer case and multi-bearer (non-GBR bearers) case only one is counted in non-GBR bearer.

**3.31.4.6.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11211593`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
Calculation of the resources for Low-Priority Demand-Based Allocation(s)

---

**3.31.4.6.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12746843`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
12746843:
Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
If NRCELL.actNrUlComp is not setting with "disabled", the the following is applied:

UL CoMP demand is considered as low-priority demand as UL CoMP is modelled as a best-effort service with specific demands and consumption of pooled resources.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$R\_{shared, LowPrio}(i,t) = \frac{ulCompPuschDemandPerSlot\_x(i,t)}{\sum\_{j=1}^{N\_{pool}} ulCompPuschDemandPerSlot\_x(j,t)} \times R\_{nonGBR, pool-LowPrio,x}(t)$
The formula calculates a shared resource allocation based on the demand of a specific user (i) at time (t) relative to the total demand from all users in the pool ($N\_{pool}$). It is then multiplied by a non-GBR (Guaranteed Bit Rate) resource allocation for the pool at time (t).[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-08251854.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$R\_{nonGBR, pool-LowPriox}(t) = \max \left{ R\_{GBR, pool,x}(t) - \sum\_{j=1}^{N\_{pool}} (R\_{minshared,GBR\_x}(j,t) + R\_{minshared,nonGBR-R1\_x}(j,t)), 0 \right}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-08251903.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

ulCompPuschDemandPerSlotx(i,t) is the granted PUSCH demand related for nonGBR bearer for UL CoMP per slot in cell i at interval t defined in [12747317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_FDZuIX8uEfCiUemk-K-C4g)

NPool   Number of cells within L1 Pool.

RGBR,pool,x(t) The GBR pool resources defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10363\_replaced([11211252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72dvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rminshared,GBR,x(i,t) Minimum shared GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10364\_replaced([11211368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72fPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

RminsharednonGBR-R1,x(i,t): Minimum shared nonGBR related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool after nonGBR bearer in Round I, calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10366\_replaced([11211629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8djvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

RnonGBR,pool-LowPrio,x(t): Available L1 pool, L1 subpool and L2 pool resources for non-GBR bearers during time interval t related to the resource type x. The calculated RnonGBR,pool-LowPrio,x(t) can be different for different pools of same type, as it depends on the resources already allocated to the cells hosted by the specific pool.

**3.31.4.6.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11211604`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer in Enhanced Algorithm -Round II

---

**3.31.4.6.0-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12749062`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
12749062:
Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
Round II is to allocate any remaining non-GBR scheduled UEs/slot demand up to the cell-level maximum and to reach the allocation of the previous pooling interval (multiplied by a graceful allocation factor), as long as remaining scheduled UEs/slot capacity exists in the pool. The purpose of this round is to handle speculative demand and speculative usage at a lower priority compared to round 1, and to soften the fluctuations between pooling intervals (unless required by sudden new real demands). This is to address behaviour that a new data burst likely happen in same (busy) cell than previous data burst. In practice, this historical allocation will be gradually forgotten and the allocation will tend towards the proportional allocation.

To enable graceful excess capacity allocation, increase the demand for this stage by

**D'x(i,t)** = max ( D5x(i,t)**, ( G \* Hx(i)** ) - Ax(i,t) **)*****\****\*

**D'x(i,t):  Remaining demand after the demands already served by previous steps(after nonGBR Round I)) have been deducted.**

D5x(i,t) = max**(Dx(i,t) -** Adx(i,t), **, *nonGbrMinLoad /100 \**) where* nonGbrMinLoad = 0.1******\****

Dx(i,t) is the future demand defined for DL as specified in [11210818](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ItVeQPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and UL as specified in [11210905](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_JGTX4PvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

**Adx(i,t):  Total allocation for real traffic** Adx(i,t) just after Round I (calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32984\_replaced([11211668](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9EkvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))\*\*\*\*

G:  Graceful Allocation Factor, defined by rdScheUePoolingGracefulAllocFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32814\_replaced([11215410](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxTC2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Hx(i):  [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression written in a sans-serif font. The expression is:
Load$*{nonGBR}$(i,t-1) + nonGbrLoadRedFromDcGbrExcess(i, t - 1)
The term "Load$*{nonGBR}$" is overlined, indicating it might be an average or a summation. The subscript "nonGBR" is in a smaller font size and is colored red, suggesting it might be a specific parameter or category. The rest of the expression consists of standard mathematical operators and function notations.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-07312142.png[/image\_path][/image-0].

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16788.001.png[/image\_path][/image-1]is Average non-GBR load related to the resource type x during time interval t-1 measured for the cell i,  defined and calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10365\_replaced([11211400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

nonGbrLoadRedFromDcGbrExcess(i,t-1) shall represent the portion of nonGBR load which is reduced to accomodate for the excessive DC-GBR demand requested for the cell i at the end of the previous pooling period t-1. For details, pls refer to [11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

**A**x(i,t):  NonGBR allocation together with minimum allocation after Calculation of the resources for nonGBR resources in Round I (calculated in  5G\_UP\_ALG\_32984\_replaced([11211668](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9EkvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*\*\*

t:  Time interval the calculation refers to (pooling period defined by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod for TDD or NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriodFdd for FDD respectively (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

i:  Index of the cell

x:  Resource for that the calculation relates to (PDSCH UE per slot, PUSCH UE per slot)

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$R\_{shared,nonGBR-R2,x}(i,t) = \frac{D'*{x}(i,t)}{\sum*{j=1}^{N\_{pool}} D'*{x}(j,t)} \times R*{nonGBR,pool-R2,x}(t)$
This equation defines a variable $R\_{shared,nonGBR-R2,x}(i,t)$ in terms of other variables. It appears to be a formula for calculating a shared component of a non-GBR (Generalized Beamforming Receiver) related to R2,x at time t for a specific index i. The formula involves a ratio of a term $D'*{x}(i,t)$ to the sum of $D'*{x}(j,t)$ over a pool of size $N\_{pool}$, multiplied by another term $R\_{nonGBR,pool-R2,x}(t)$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-08121930.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

The non-GBR pool resources are the remaining resources after satisfaction of the GBR bearer’s need which is expressed by the GBR pool resource lessen by the sum of the shared GBR resources and the shared nonGBR resources after Round I. The following equation defines the calculation rule

[CB008465-F]

If NRCELL.actNrUlComp is setting with "disabled" or it is not configured

[End CB008465-F]

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$R\_{nonGBR, pool-R2,x}(t) = \max { R\_{GBR, poolx}(t) - \sum\_{j=1}^{N\_{pool}} (R\_{minshared,GBR,x}(j, t) + R\_{minshared,nonGBR-R1,x}(j,t)); 0 }$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-05061912.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

[CB008465-F]

Else

[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation defines $R\_{nonGBR, pool-R2,x}(t)$ as the maximum of two values: $R\_{GBR, pool,x}(t)$ and a second value. The second value is calculated by subtracting a summation from $R\_{GBR, pool,x}(t)$. The summation runs from $j=1$ to $N\_{pool}$ and includes the terms $R\_{minshared,GBR,x}(j,t)$ and $R\_{minshared,nonGBR-R1,x}(j,t)$. Finally, $R\_{minshared,nonGBR-LowPrio,x}(j,t)$ is added to the summation. The entire expression is then compared with 0, and the maximum of these two values is taken.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-08252017.png[/image\_path][/image-4]

[End CB008465-F]

NPool   Number of cells within L1 Pool.

RGBR,pool,x(t) The GBR pool resources defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10363\_replaced([11211252](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72dvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rminshared,GBR,x(i,t) Minimum shared GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10364\_replaced([11211368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72fPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

RnonGBR,pool-R2,x(t): Available L1 pool, L1 subpool and L2 pool resources for non-GBR bearers during time interval t related to the resource type x. The calculated RnonGBR,pool-R2,x(t) according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10365\_replaced([11211400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) can be different for different pools of same type, as it depends on the resources already allocated to the cells hosted by the specific pool.

RminsharednonGBR-R1,x(i,t): Minimum shared nonGBR related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool after nonGBR bearer in Round I, calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10366\_replaced([11211629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8djvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008465-F]

RminsharednonGBR-LowPrio,x(i,t): Minimum shared nonGBR for Low Priority Service related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool after nonGBR bearer in Round I, calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10366\_replaced([11211629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8djvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008465-F]

Note that if multiple bearers are setup for a UE, the UE is only counted once for the number of UEs which can be scheduled per slot. So for both single non-GBR bearer case and multi-bearer (non-GBR bearers) case only one is counted in non-GBR bearer.

---

#### 3.31.4.6.0-3 Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer for L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool - Step 2 (ID: 11211629)

**3.31.4.6.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `12749122`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
12749122:
Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
Step 2: Resource share for non-GBR bearers for L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool:

The shared non-GBR resources shall be calculated for each cell within L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool respectively where this cell is allocated according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10365\_replaced([11211400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and make the minimum one of the three as the final value for each cell. For simplicity, it is called Rminshared,nonGBR,x(i,t): which represents shared non-GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool.

If NRBTS.actScheUePoolingEnh is 'FALSE' Rminshared,nonGBR,x(i,t) shall be got by the following:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16796.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Note: For the SDL cells, the Rminshared,nonGBR,x(i,t) should be 0.

Else **(i.e.,if NRBTS.actScheUePoolingEnh is 'TRUE') Rminshared,nonGBR,x(i,t) shall be got by running two rounds as the following:**

The min shared non-GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool in Enhanced Algorithm for both Round I and Round II shall be derived as the following:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation defines a variable `Rminshared.nonGBR-R1.x(i,t)` as the minimum of three other variables: `Rshared, nonGBR-R1.x (it) L2subpool`, `Rshared, nonGBR-R1.x (it) Lisubpool`, and `Rshared, nonGBR-R1.x(i,t) Lipool`. Finally the total min shared non-GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool in Enhanced Algorithm after Round I for nonGBR (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32803\_replaced([11211531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8diPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), [CB008465-F] Low Priority Demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32817\_replaced([11211593](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8divvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008465-F] and Round II(5G\_UP\_ALG\_32804\_replaced([11211604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8djPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be derived as the following:

[CB008465-F]

[End CB008465-F]

[CB008465-F]

#### 3.31.4.6.0-5 Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource Calculation of the overall amount of resource per cell (ID: 11211690)

**3.31.4.6.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `11211740`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
11211740:
Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
Overall amount of resource for each cell

After calculation of the resource need for GBR, and non-GBR bearers the overall amount of resource shall be calculated for each cell. Basically, the total share is the sum of the minimum resource and the shared resources for all resources which are under control of the BBRM. The following equation shows the rule for calculating the total amount of a certain resource.

[Before CB008600-F]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16803.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB008600-F]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16803.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[End CB008600-F]

with:

Rsum,x(i,t): Total sum of resource x calculated for cell i during time interval t

Rmin,x(i,t): Minimum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7942\_replaced([11210423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rmax,x(i,t): Maximum resource related to the resource type x during time interval t given for the cell i, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Rminshared,CG(i,t): Minimum shared CG resource (only relevant for UL direction, set to 0 for DL direction) during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20544\_replaced([11211144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB008600-F]

Rminshared,DC-GBR,x(i,t): Minimum shared DC-GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31984\_replaced([11211200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72cPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB008600-F]

Rminshared,GBR,x(i,t): Minimum shared GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10364\_replaced([11211368](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw72fPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Rminshared,nonGBR,x(i,t): Minimum shared non-GBR resource related to the resource type x during time interval t calculated for the cell i after checking L2 subpool, L1 subpool, L1 pool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10366\_replaced([11211629](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8djvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

t: Time interval the calculation refers to (pooling period defined by bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))).

i: Index of the cell

x:         Resource for that the calculation relates to (PDSCH UE per slot, PUSCH UE per slot)

The rounding of Rsum,x(i,t) to an integer value and the distribution of possible remaining resources shall refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28144\_replaced([11211748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9EmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: Above formula is applicable for scheduled PDSCH and/or PUSCH UEs per slot per cell

#### 3.31.4.6.0-6 Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource Calculation and allocation of the remaining resource to the cell (ID: 11211748)

**3.31.4.6.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11211761`)

Calculation of the resources for nonGBR bearer and final amount of resource
The rounding of Rsum,x(i,t) to an integer value and the distribution of possible remaining resources shall happen in the following way:

- Rsum,x(i, t) is rounded to the lower integer, for each cell i: RsumInt,x(i, t) = roundDown( Rsum,x(i, t) )

-    [PR766539]Below steps should be run several times until remaining resource per L1 pool is zero or candidate cell list is empty. To avoid the infinite loop in case of unexpected behaviour/configuration, the maximum number of attempt is equal to cell amount per L1 pool.[End PR766539]

- BBRM calculates the amount of remaining resources which can be distributed [PR766539] per L1 pool, L1 subpool and L2 subpool respectively [End PR766539]:

[Before PR766539]

remainingResources,x = maxNumScheUePxschL1Pool - SUM[i = cell handled by BBRM](RsumInt,x(i, t))

[PR766539]

Rleftpool,x(l1pool(i),t) = maxNumScheUePxschL1Pool - SUM[i = cell handled by BBRM](RsumInt,x(i, t))

Rleftpool,x(l1subpool(i),t) = maxNumScheUePxschL1Sp - SUM[i = cell handled by BBRM](RsumInt,x(i, t))

Rleftpool,x(l2subpool(i),t) = maxNumScheUePxschL2Sp - SUM[i = cell handled by BBRM](RsumInt,x(i, t))

[End PR766539]

where:

* maxNumScheUePxschL1Pool represents the total L1 pool capacity for PDSCH/PUSCH, respectively configured by maxNumScheUePdschL1Pool or maxNumScheUePuschL1Pool NIDD parameter.

[PR766539]

* maxNumScheUePxschL1Sp represents the total L1 subpool capacity for PDSCH/PUSCH, respectively configured by maxNumScheUePdschL1Sp or maxNumScheUePuschL1Sp NIDD parameter.
* maxNumScheUePxschL2Sp represents the total L2 subpool capacity for PDSCH/PUSCH, respectively configured by maxNumScheUePdschL2Sp or maxNumScheUePuschL2Sp NIDD parameter.

[End PR766539]

[Before PR766539]

- If remainingResources,x = 0, the following steps are skipped.

- The cells selected to get the remaining resources are those for which either the reported LoadGBR,x > 0 or the reported LoadnonGBR,x > 0. This is what we call ‘set of candidate cells’.

Note: when a scheduler reports LoadnonGBR,x = 0, the algorithm in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10365\_replaced([11211400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw8dgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) assumes LoadnonGBR,x > 0. The above definition of candidate cell considers the real LoadnonGBR,x reported by the scheduler.

In the following description the parameter numCandidateCells represents the amount of candidate cells. If numCandidateCells = 0, then all the cells are considered as candidate to get additional resources: numCandidateCells = ‘number of cells handled by BBRM’.

[PR766539]

The cells selected to get the remaining resources shall fulfill following conditions:

Rleftpool,x(l1pool(i),t) > 0 and

Rleftpool,x(l1subpool(i),t) > 0 and

Rleftpool,x(l2subpool(i),t) > 0 and

RsumInt,x(i, t) < Rmax,x(i,t)

Note: all cells are considered as candidate to get additional resources.

If Rleftpool,x(l1pool(i),t) == 0 or candidcate cell list is empty, the following steps are skipped.

[End PR766539]

- For those candidate cells the fractional part of Rsum,x(i,t) is calculated: RsumDec,x(i, t) = Rsum,x(i, t) – RsumInt,x(i, t);

- the candidate cells are sorted by decreasing RsumDec,x(i, t);

- The amount of resources which L2-PS tries to assign to each candidate cell (attempedResources,x) is calculated as below:

attempedResources,x = roundup( Rleftpool,x(l1pool(i),t) / numCandidateCells )

- BBRM selects each candidate cell according to the sorted order and gives it the additional resource amount:

additonalRes,x(i,t) = min( attempedResources,x , Rleftpool,x(l1pool(i),t), Rleftpool,x(l1subpool(i),t), Rleftpool,x(l2subpool(i),t), Rmax,x(i,t) - RsumInt,x(i,t) );

Rsum,x(i, t) = RsumInt,x(i, t) + additonalRes,x(i,t)

where:

* Rmax,x(i,t) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* Rleftpool,x(p,t) is the remaining capacity on the l1pool/l1subpool/l2subpool the cell belongs to;

- [PR766539] BBRM should repeat above steps until Rleftpool,x(l1pool(i),t) = 0 or candidate cell list is empty. [End PR766539]

---

#### 3.31.4.7 Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell

##### 3.31.4.7.0-1 Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell Calculation of PUCCH F1 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell (ID: 11211775)

**3.31.4.7.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13393351`)

Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell
13393351:
Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell
For FDD **[CB008224-D] which isn't an SDL cell** [End CB008224-D] and TDD FR1, the PUCCH F1 resource for HARQ A/N per slot per cell is calculated according to scheduled PDSCH UEs. **A simple proportional fairness algorithm should be used until PUCCH F1 per L1 pool resource is exhausted (defined in** [11373764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueD98_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). Below algorithm is applicable for both round-robin and metric-based pooling mode.\*\*\*\*

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16810.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

with

 a(i) = maxNumPdschPerSlotByBBRM of cell (i) which is defined in **[Before CNI-136563] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6361\_replaced([11210614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (round-robin pooling mode) or**[End CNI-136563] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6548\_replaced([11211690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ElPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (metric-based pooling mode)\*\*\*\*

 RL1pool, PUCCH F1

L1 Pool limit of PUCCH F1 for HARQ A/N (defined by NIDD hidden parameter maxNumPucchF1HarqL1Pool)

 RL1pool, PDSCH

L1 Pool limit of scheduled PDSCH UE (defined by NIDD hidden parameter maxNumScheUePdschL1Pool)

**[CB008224-D]For an SDL cell (which has no uplink), maxNumPucchF1PerSlotByBBRM should be 0.**[End CB008224-D]\*\*\*\*

---

##### 3.31.4.7.0-2 Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell Calculation of PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell for FR1 FDD (ID: 11211803)

**3.31.4.7.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13393342`)

Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell
13393342:
Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell
For FR1 FDD **[CB008224-D] which isn't an SDL cell**[End CB008224-D],  **[Before CNI-136563-A] when round-robin pooling mode is activated, the PUCCH F3 resource for HARQ A/N per slot per cell is calculated according to scheduled PDSCH UEs which is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6361\_replaced([11210614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N shall be assigned to prioritized cell with static PUCCH F3 resources, the remaining PUCCH F3 resources shall be assigned to other cells randomly among the remaining cells (excluding the prioritized cell) with static PUCCH resource per cell, until PUCCH F3 per L1 pool resource is exhausted(defined in 5G\_UP\_1775\_replaced([11372919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ud_sevvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**\*\*\*\*

For prioritized cell, PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N is static as 2 (refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2862\_replaced([11310025](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrM5BPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for #PRB(HARQ AN)). For non-prioritized cell, PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N is static as 1. It may cause several rounds to assign the PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N to non-prioritized cells, until PUCCH F3 per L1 pool resource is exhausted. **[End CNI-136563-A]**

For FDD FR1, when metric-based pooling mode is activated, current assumption is PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N processing is restricted and shall be scheduled only for 3CC(FDD Pcell) or FDD + TDD CA enabled scenarios. When BBRM receives PUCCH F3 demanding from one cell, BBRM assigns the static PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N on this cell. As a result PCell - SCell relations will not be distributed among cells within a L1 pool in a fair manner,**a simple round-robin algorithm should be used until PUCCH F3 per L1 pool resource is exhausted (PUCCH F3 per L1 pool limitation is defined in**[11373764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueD98_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For cell(i), rrmCAF3Ue(i) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6635\_replaced([11211875](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9rtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). If rrmCAF3Ue(i) >= 1, then assign one PUCCH F3 resource to cell(i). If PUCCH F3 per L1 pool resource still has more resources left, for cell(i), if rrmCAF3Ue(i) > 1, then assign one more PUCCH F3 resource to cell(i), until PUCCH F3 per L1 pool resource is exhausted.

As the consequence, maxNumPucchF3PerSlotbyBBRM should have following variable values:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_16813.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

**[CB008224-D]For an SDL cell (which has no uplink), maxNumPucchF3PerSlotByBBRM should be 0.**[End CB008224-D]\*\*\*\*

Note: Up to 2 PUCCH F3 per cell is based on the number of PUCCH F3 PRB used for HARQ A/N per UL slot for FDD as P(S)Cell, refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2862\_replaced([11310025](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrM5BPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for #PRB(HARQ AN).

---

##### 3.31.4.7.0-3 Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell Calculation of PUCCH F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell for FR1 TDD (ID: 11211831)

**3.31.4.7.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11211845`)

Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell
11211845:
Calculation of PUCCH F1 and F3 for HARQ A/N per slot per cell
For FR1 TDD, the PUCCH F3 resource for HARQ A/N per slot per cell is calculated according to scheduled PDSCH UEs, [Before PR663323] and assigned up to 6 PUCCH F3 resources for HARQ A/N per slot per cell [End PR663323]. A simple proportional fairness algorithm should be used until PUCCH F3 per L1 pool resource is exhausted (defined in 5G\_UP\_1775\_replaced([11372919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ud_sevvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Below algorithm is applicable for both round-robin and metric-based pooling mode.

[Before PR663323]

[End PR663323]

with

 a(i) = maxNumPdschPerSlotByBBRM of cell (i) which is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6361\_replaced([11210614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (round-robin pooling mode) or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6548\_replaced([11211690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw9ElPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (metric-based pooling mode)

### 3.31.4.8 Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features

#### 3.31.4.8.0-1 Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features Timing of scheduled UE per slot per cell usage (ID: 11211858)

**3.31.4.8.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11211870`)

Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features
If baseband pooling of scheduled UEs per slot is activated (i.e., NRBTS.actScheUePooling is set to TRUE), when 5G-L2-PS receives new scheduled UE per slot per cell grant at SFN N from BBRM at the beginning of the baseband pooling period ([Before CB009215-D]NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod[CB009215-D]bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).[End CB009215-D]):

– To ensure DPA (Distributed PUCCH Allocation) and L2-PS having consistent values of scheduled UE per slot per cell, the new scheduled UE per slot (including PUCCH F1/F3 resources) can be usable for DPA in SFN+1, but L2-PS shall use new allocated resources in SFN+2.

– During the transition time (SFN N and SFN N+1) of every pooling period, any allocation made in L2-PS (DL and/or UL scheduler) shall not exceed of the capacity restriction of the pooled resource on any level and not on any slot.

---

#### 3.31.4.8.0-2 Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features Serving Cell CA UEs Measurements for BaseBand pooling (ID: 11211875)

**3.31.4.8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11211881`)

Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features
If baseband pooling of scheduled UEs per slot is activated, in FDD cell, for every slot, DL scheduler shall always maintain a current cumulative of count of UEs (numCAF3Ues) that require PUCCH format 3 resources in that cell, all UEs in the pre-scheduler candidate list the scheduled PDSCH UEs shall be checked with below conditions.

 The corresponding cell is the P(S)cell of the UE

 The UE has at least 2 active FDD SCells or at least one active TDD SCell.

At the end of every measurement/pooling period, in each cell (i)

 DL scheduler shall calculate the number of UEs that require PUCCH format 3 resources in the next period (rrmCAF3Ue (i)) as below,

rrmCAF3Ue(i) = roundup (sum(numCAF3Ues(i, t)) / num of DL slots in the BB pooling period)

where t corresponds to the index of each of the DL slots in the pooling period.

 DL scheduler shall send rrmCAF3Ue(i) to the BBRM and the value of rrmCAF3Ue(i) shall be reset.

---

#### 3.31.4.8.0-3 Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features P(S)Cell  number of UE scheduled per slot reduction in DPA slot (ID: 11211886)

**3.31.4.8.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11211899`)

Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features
If Baseband pooling of scheduled UEs per slot is activated && NRBTS/NRDU/flexibleCaMode is set to NumberCellAmount (value 3) && there are more than one FDD cells setup in the same L2 subpool. L2-PS shall calculate DPASlotFDMReducedFactor in the DPA slot (Measurement Processing cycle in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2936\_replaced([11123865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqmk8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as:

For DL:

if sum(maxNumPdschPerSlotByBBRM(x,t))<rdDPASlotFDMReductionThresholdDL

DPASlotFDMReducedFactor=1;

else

DPASlotFDMReducedFactor=rdDPASlotFDMReductionThresholdDL/sum(maxNumPdschPerSlotByBBRM(x,t))

For UL:

if sum(maxNumPuschPerSlotByBBRM(x,t))<rdDPASlotFDMReductionThresholdUL

DPASlotFDMReducedFactor=1;

else

DPASlotFDMReducedFactor=rdDPASlotFDMReductionThresholdUL/sum(maxNumPdUchPerSlotByBBRM(x,t));

 maxNumPdschPerSlotByBBRM(x,t) stand for UE scheduled per slot in DL granted by BBRM for cell x in the same L2 subpool.

 maxNumPuschPerSlotByBBRM(x,t) stand for UE scheduled per slot in UL granted by BBRM for cell x in the same L2 subpool.

[CB012528-E]In FDD cell, when rdDynamicPucchAlloSplitEnable (5G\_UP\_ALG\_24678\_replaced([11124282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqpoQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is enabled, number of UE scheduled per slot reduction in DPA slot is not needed anymore ,DPASlotFDMReducedFactor for both DL and UL shall equal to 1.[End CB012528-E]

---

#### 3.31.4.8.0-4 Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features Interworking with LTE-NR DSS (ID: 11211905)

**3.31.4.8.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12680445`)

Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features
The interaction of scheduled PDSCH & PUSCH UEs per slot pooling with DSS enabled cell [CB007372-A-UPD001][CB007372-A] and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A][End CB007372-A-UPD001] shall be supported in a static way. When DSS is enabled (NRCELL.nrLteDssMode is set to '2:DL\_CRS\_TDM\_UL\_FDM' or '3:DSS\_Phase\_3'), CP-RT shall inform DSS (NRDSSLTE.*dssMaxNumberOfDlDcis) configuration via PsCell\_CellSetupReq message to L2-RT/BBRM, BBRM shall re-calculate Rmax,x (i, t) for NR DSS cell, which the air resources are granted statically to LTE due to NR-DSS activation on this cell. These resources shall not be allocated to the NR DSS cell, however shall be distributed to the other cells allocated to the same L1 pool, L1 sub-pool or L2 sub-pool.*

Rmax,x (i, t) is maximum granted resource of type X(scheduled UEs per slot) for cell i during time interval which is defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.31.4.8.0-5 Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features Interworking with DL Interference Generation - single cell (ID: 11211917)

**3.31.4.8.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11211929`)

Scheduled UEs per slot pooling interaction with RRM features
[Before PR711458]

DL interference generation requires one 'virtual' UE per slot in DL which shall be taken from the pool of available PDSCH UE per slot.

When NIDD parameter targetTotalLoad under MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL is greater than 0 (the feature DL interference generation is active) NRCELL/maxNumPdschAllocationPerSlot in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7943\_replaced([11210499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aPfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) should be subtracted by 1, i.e., maxNumPdschAllocationPerSlot - 1.

[PR711458]

DL interference generation has no impact on scheduled PDSCH UE pooling, since L2-PS checks available PDSCH UE for fake UE and stops generating artificial load in case of no available PDSCH UE (refer to  5G\_UP\_ALG\_16626\_replaced([11183121](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvH4nvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End PR711458]

## 3.31.5 Slow PRB Pooling

### 3.31.5.1 Slow PRB Pooling Framework

#### 3.31.5.1.0-1 Slow PRB Pooling Framework Slow PRB pooling Overview (ID: 11211947)

**3.31.5.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13400542`)

Slow PRB Pooling Framework
To support dynamic PRB pooling between cells of a L1 subpool, the BBRM (BaseBand Resource Manager) as part of L2RT shall allocate the amount of usable PRBs available to the cell schedulers. At the same time, such central PRB allocation avoids L1 overload.  
The available pooled PRBs shall be shared between cells mapped to the same L1 subpool.

Cell schedulers shall consume the granted PRBs for scheduling of UL and DL traffic on their respective air interfaces.

The BBRM shall re-evaluate the PRB allocations for cells within the L1 subpool once within a predefined period, called the slow pooling window or bbPoolEvalPeriod**.**

The value used as bbPoolEvalPeriod is**given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod for TDD/NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriodFdd for FDD respectively.**

PRB grants allocated to cell schedulers shall only be valid for the entire duration of the next slow pooling window.

PRB pooling shall be performed separately for

 DL stream PRBs per symbol

 UL stream PRBs per symbol

 PDSCH layer PRBs per symbol (for simplification reasons, not considered for pooling in 5GC001227)

 PUSCH layer PRBs per symbol (for simplification reasons, not considered for pooling in 5GC001227)

If NRBTS.actSlowPrbPoolingFddFr1Enh **= TRUE**

* PDSCH layer PRB pooling per symbol shall also be considered for FDD
* PUSCH layer PRB pooling per symbol shall also be considered for FDD

End If

Static PRB pooling between cells of the same L1 subpool is required for the support of CSI-RS for ACQ. This is done by grouping the cells of the L1 subpool into different subset cell groups, where cells of one subset group are configured concurrently to support WB symbols, whereas cells from other subsets are configured to support zero-allocation symbols during the concurrent symbol time. Allocation shall consider the maximum amount of cells supported per L1 pool per release. It shall avoid the need to introduce zero-allocation symbols to cells on air, when adding other cells at runtime.  
BBRM shall support such handling of CSI-RS for ACQ.

Note that L3RT shall support such handling of CSI-RS for TRS and maximum 2 subset cell group is assumed for CSI-RS for TRS (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). A group ID, csirsPoolingGroupId, is used to indicate to which subset cell group a cell corresponds to and CPRT sends csirsPoolingGroupId per cell to L2RT via PsCell\_CellSetupReq.

For all other TTIs and symbols, the cell schedulers shall use the PRB grants dynamically allocated by the BBRM.

**- If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**, SRS resource Pooling is enabled for NDM-SRS(periodic SRS) when more than 3 cells are deployed per L1 pool as in such case the capacity needed to support all cells simultaneously will exceed the available L1 pool capacity. This check and configuration is handled by CPRT\*\*\*\*

[CB014699-D]  
Note: When a cell supports critical traffic, no new cell load types are introduced for critical traffic, critical GBR shall be treated as GBR together with non-critical GBR, critical nonGBR shall be treated as nonGBR together with non-critical nonGBR.[End CB014699-D]

---

#### 3.31.5.1.0-2 Slow PRB Pooling Framework Conversion Between Cell-PRB and Stream PRB (ID: 11211964)

**3.31.5.1.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `13284984`)

Slow PRB Pooling Framework
The maximum pooled PRB capacity per L1 subPool is provided via NIDD parameters in NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity and the corresponding L1  max capacities of the L1 subPool are given in terms of stream-PRB (NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity-maxNumStreamPrbDlL1Sp/NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity-maxNumStreamPrbUlL1) and Layer-PRB (NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity-maxNumLayerPrbDlL1Sp/NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity-maxNumLayerPrbUlL1Sp). In the scope slow PRB pooling, slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'true' **or** slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), **or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed set to TRUE**, only the given stream-PRB capacity limit is considered for the slow pooling algorithm decision. Considering the actual L1 processing limitation of the subpool given in granularity of stream-PRB,  a conversion is required between the actual PRB demand/allocation per (sub)Cell to the equivalent stream-PRB and vice-versa. Therefore, for the algorithm:***\****\*

* the estimated Cell PRB demand shall be converted to equivalent stream-PRB demand
* the amount of stream-PRB granted to a cell by the algorithm shall be converted back to equivalent Cell PRB to be sent to the 5G L2PS.

Conversion between Cell-PRB and Stream-PRB for cell (i) shall be done as follows:

* streamPrbDemand (i) = cellPrbDemand (i)\*maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb(i)
* numAllocCellPrb (i)     = Floor ( numAllocStreamPrb(i) / maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb(i))

where:

* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb is

If NRBTS.actSlowPrbPoolingFddFr1Enh **= TRUE**

* **[CB013525-D] 8: for UL and 4 for DL with a cell with GA8 subcell,**[End CB013525-D]\*\*\*\*
* 4 : for a cell with A4 UL subcell or DL subcell
* 4 **: for a cell with A2 UL subcell in case of "Thor" L1 HW variant,  (refer Note 1 below)**
* 2 : for a cell with A2 UL subcell and L1 HW variants other than "Thor" (refer Note 1 below) or DL subcell
* 1 : for a cell with A1 UL subcell or DL subcell

Else

* 4 : for a subcell type A4 and 2 for a subcell type A2 and 1 for a subcell type A1 for DL,
* 4 : shall be used for UL, irresspective of a subcell type (A4/A2).

End If

* 2 : for a cell with C2 UL subcell **and L1 HW variants other than "Thor" (refer Note 1 below) or C2 DL subcell**
* 4 : for a cell with C4 UL subcell **or C4 DL subcell**
* 4 **: for a cell with C2 UL subcell in case of "Thor" L1 HW variant,  (refer Note 1 below)**
* 8: for a cell with C8 UL subcell
* Note: both layerPRB and streamPRB capacity limitation is taken into account within the PRB pooling algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* numAllocStreamPrb is number of stream PRB allocated to a to a cell(5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* If UL**/DL MU-MIMO is enabled then**
* the term Cell PRB shall refer to subcell PRB as the PRBs used by each subcell of the cell (primary/secondary) shall be counted separately.
* the amount of PRB demand estimated per cell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the amount of usable PRB allocated by the BBRM which indicated to the L2PS of the cell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) refers to the corresponding amount of subcell PRBs per cell, respectively.
* when number of subcell per cell is only one, all scheduling takes place on the single subcell, hence, the term subcell PRB (Cell PRB) is equivalent to the actual PRB used allocated by the L2-PS

Note 1 : L1 HW variant Thor has constraints that restrict the mapping of 2 streams with 2 layers. Thus, L1 uses 4 streams also for an A2/C2 subcell in UL. This restriction is only limited to UL and only to the "Thor" L1 HW variant. Please refer to the following L1 requirement BTSC\_L1\_Req\_10037/BTSC\_L1\_Req\_10466

---

#### 3.31.5.1.0-3 Slow PRB Pooling Framework Conversion Between Cell-PRB and Stream PRB for RIM-RS (ID: 11212003)

**3.31.5.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11212008`)

Slow PRB Pooling Framework
Conversion between Cell-PRB and Stream-PRB for RIM-RS transmission in cell(i) shall be done as follows:

If (actBeamforming is true) or (actBeamforming is false and dlMimoMode is "ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_2x2 or OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_2x2" (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) ,

streamPrbDemandRim(i) = prbDemandRim(i)\*2

Else If actBeamforming is false and dlMiMoMode is "ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_4x4 or OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_4x4" (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

streamPrbDemandRim(i) = prbDemandRim(i)\*4

End If

Note: actBeamforming and dlMimoMode are from PsCell\_CellSetupReq message (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 3.31.5.1.0-4 Slow PRB Pooling Framework Number of Streams and Layers Per Subcell (ID: 11212013)

**3.31.5.1.0-4.0-6**  (ID: `13284983`)

Slow PRB Pooling Framework
The maximum number of Streams and Layers supported for each PRB allocation in a cell is defined per subcell type

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type | numMaxStreamPerSubcell |  | numMaxLayerPerSubcell |  |
| DL | UL | DL | UL |  |
| C4 | 4 | 4 | 4 | 2 |
| C2 | 2 | If L1 HW variant Thor, then 4 (refer Note-3 below)else 2 | 2 | 2 |
| C8 | 8 | 8 | x | k(see NOTE-1) |

**NOTE-1: If ulSubcellType is C8 AND NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo is false, k shall be set to 2; If ulSubcellType is C8 AND NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo is true, k shall be set to 4;**

If NRBTS.actSlowPrbPoolingFddFr1Enh = TRUE received from higher layers (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), additionally :

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell Type | numMaxStreamPerSubcell |  | numMaxLayerPerSubcell |  |
| DL | UL | DL | UL |  |
| A4 | 4 | 4 | 4 | 2 |
| A2 | 2 | If L1 HW variant Thor, then 4 (refer Note-3 below)else2 | 2 | 2 |
| A1 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 |
| [CB0013525-D] GA8 (for UL, A4 for DL) | 4 | 8 | 4 | 2 [End CB0013525-D] |

End If

For a cell with a given subcell type,

* numLayerToStreamRatio = numMaxLayerPerSubcell/numMaxStreamPerSubcell
* streamToLayerScaleFactor = 2 only in UL for a cell with C2/A2 subcell and L1 HW variant other than "Thor" (refer Note 3 below), 1 in all other situations.

**NOTE-2: This factor is used during the inter L1 Subpool Pooling algorithm. It is added since the demands calculated during inter L1 SP pooling only consider the stream PRBs. The layer PRBs are calculated from the stream PRBs based on the numLayerToStreamRatio (in UL : 0.5 for C4/A4** subcells, 1 for C2/A2 **subcells on L1 HW variants other than "Thor" (refer Note-3 below), 0.5 for C2/A2 subcells on "Thor" L1 HW variant). Due to this conversion, the interL1 SP pooling algorithm provides additional PRBs to cells with C4/A4** subcells when compared to C2/A2 **subcells in UL on L1 HW variants other than "Thor" (refer Note-3 below). This factor is supposed to remove this bias and distribute the available resources evenly between all cells with any subcell types.*****\****\*

Note-3 : L1 HW variant Thor has constraints that restrict the mapping of 2 streams with 2 layers. Thus, L1 uses 4 streams also for an A2/C2 subcell in UL. This restriction is only limited to UL and only to the "Thor" L1 HW variant. Please refer to the following L1 requirement BTSC\_L1\_Req\_10037/BTSC\_L1\_Req\_10466

---

### 3.31.5.2 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation

#### 3.31.5.2.0-1 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation Cell Load Metric Definition (ID: 11212058)

**3.31.5.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11212068`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
The cell load measurement for the load-metric based algorithm is carried out in terms of the amount of aggregate PRB demand per cell.

An estimate of aggregate PRB demand for next bbPoolingPeriod ([Before CB009215-D]NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod[CB009215-D]bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB009215-D]) t is computed per cell for GBR and non GBR traffic load separately. The PRB demand is estimated based on the buffer size and aggregate data arrival rate information captured in the previous bbPooling interval (t -1).

---

#### 3.31.5.2.0-2 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation GBR and non-GBR Buffer occupancy of a cell (ID: 11212073)

**3.31.5.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12577803`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
For DL: the buffer occupancy of a cell in DL is estimated based on the aggregate buffer length (in bytes) of GBR  and non GBR bearers in separately which is maintained at 5G-L2-PS in the previous pooling period (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4561\_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Accordingly, the buffer length at time n is given by:

* gbrBufferLength( i,n) = sum( bufferedBytes [i,j,k,n]  )  : the sum of all bufferedbytes of all GBR bearers k from all UEs j in the cell i at time instant n
* nonGbrBufferLength( i,n) = sum( bufferedBytes[i,j,k,n]  ) : the sum of all bufferedbytes of all other bearers k other than the GBR[CB008600-F] and DC-GBR [End CB008600-F] from all UEs j in the cell i at time instant n.

where bufferedBytes is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4561\_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

Note:only Bearer type with 5QI =5QI1 is counted as GBR group for the PRB demand estimation in 22R1. In the future when several GBR bearer with various 5QI values are supported, the current check has to be extended to account all GBR bearers  in a addition to 5QI1

For UL: the buffer occupancy of a cell in UL is estimated as per the amount of data ( in bytes) in UE buffers per Logical channel group (LCG) which is maintained by 5G-L2-PS based on the BSRs and the received data amounts. Accordingly, the length of the GBR/nonGBR buffer of a cell i at time instant n is given by the sum of buffer size of all GBR/nonGBR DRBs of all UEs in the cell, respectively and it is given by:

* gbrBufferLength( i,n) = sum( rrmBufferedDataUlLcg\_bytes[i,j,k,n]  ) :  the sum of all  rrmBufferedDataUlLcg\_bytes of all LCG k containing only GBR DRB  from all UEs in the cell i at time instant n
* nonGbrBufferLength( i,n) = sum( rrmBufferedDataUlLcg\_bytes[i,j,k,n]  )  : the sum of all  rrmBufferedDataUlLcg\_bytes of all LCG k containing bearer other than GBR [CB008600-F] and DC-GBR [End CB008600-F] DRB  from all UEs in the cell i at time instant n

where rrmBufferedDataUlLcg\_bytes is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10514\_replaced([11203665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 3.31.5.2.0-3 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation New Data Arrival Estimation per Cell (ID: 11212086)

**3.31.5.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11212105`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
The new data arrival estimate of a cell is considered in the computation of the aggregate PRB demand estimate of a cell for the metric-based pooling algorithm. The new data arrival of a cell in bytes is estimated for GBR and non-GBR bearer separately in DL and UL, as follows:

For FDD: UL/DL

[CB009215-H]

If slowPrbPoolingAllowed = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = FALSE, then

[End CB009215-H]

* rrmInstNewGbrDataArrivalEst (i) = max [0, gbrBufferLength( i,n) - gbrBufferLength( i,n-1) + Sum(TBS of all GBR traffic over bbPoolingPeriod)
* rrmInstNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst (i) = max[0, nonGbrBufferLength( i,n) - nonGbrBufferLength( i,n-1) + Sum (TBS of all nonGBR traffic over bbPoolingPeriod)
* for UL with CG, TBS of a traffic (GBR/nonGBR) to be considered shall not include bytes carried over a PUSCH corresponding to a Configured Grant

For FR1-TDD [CB009215-H] and FDD:

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE, then

[End CB009215-H]

DL:

* rrmInstNewGbrDataArrivalEst (i) = max {0, gbrBufferLength( i,n) - gbrBufferLength( i,n-1) + SUM[all GBR traffic over bbPoolingPeriod]{TBS}}
* rrmInstNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst (i) = max {0, nonGbrBufferLength( i,n) - nonGbrBufferLength( i,n-1) +  SUM[all nonGBR traffic over bbPoolingPeriod]{TBS}}

UL:

* rrmInstNewGbrDataArrivalEst (i) = max {0, gbrBufferLength( i,n) - gbrBufferLength( i,n-1) +  SUM[all GBR over bbPoolingPeriod]{receivedDataAmount}}
* rrmInstNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst (i) = max {0, nonGbrBufferLength( i,n) - nonGbrBufferLength( i,n-1) + SUM[all nonGBR over bbPoolingPeriod]{receivedDataAmount }}
* for UL with CG, receivedDataAmount of traffic (Y = GBR/non GBR ) shall not include bytes received over a PUSCH corresponding to a Configured Grant

For UL CG overwritten by DG but on CG resources:

-  Same procedure as for UL with CG above is applied.

For UL CG overwritten by DG on different PUSCH resources than CG grant (at least 1 PRB outside CG grant):

- Denote:
