o DG\_total = total amount of X (see X below) in DG

o DG\_GBR = total amount of GBR X in DG

o DG\_nGBR = total amount of non GBR X in DG

o CG\_TBS =  TBS of the CG (see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_14664\_replaced([11172802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuOgs_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_15651\_replaced([11172853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuOgufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

- If CG profile is mapped to a GBR DRB:

o CG\_GBR = CG\_TBS  (that is, assume conservatively that CG is entirely carrying GBR)

o CG\_nGBR = 0

- Else

o CG\_GBR = 0 (that is, assume conservatively that GBR is sent entirely outside CG)

o CG\_nGBR = TBS of the CG

- EndIf

- Consider the following X from GBR/nonGBR to be counted to rrmInstNewGbrDataArrivalEst/ rrmInstNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst from a DG overwriting a CG:

o GBR from DG to count = MAX(0,  DG\_GBR – CG\_GBR)

o Non GBR from DG to count = MAX(0,  DG\_nGBR - CG\_nGBR)

- Where X is:

o FDD [CB009215-H]and slowPrbPoolingAllowed = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = FALSE [End CB009215-H] : scheduled bytes

[CB009215-H]

o FDD and slowPrbPoolingAllowed = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE : received bytes

[End CB009215-H]

o TDD: received bytes

where:

- i:  index of cell

- n    :  the end of past pooling period

- n-1 :  the beginning of past pooling period

-receivedDataAmount: successfully received GBR/nonGBR bytes from a UE (LoCtrl\_UlMaxPduReceiveInd).

* the computation is used for both DL and UL estimate using the respective buffer length values from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6784\_replaced([11212073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5yvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* rrmInstNewGbrDataArrivalEst /rrmInstNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst  is the data arrival estimate for one previous pooling window.
* The average data arrival estimate (rrmAvgNewGbrDataArrivalEst /rrmAvgNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst) per cell to be used in the metric-based algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6788\_replaced([11212354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be calculated as a exponential filter at the end of every bbPoolingPeriod and the filtering is done the same way for DL/UL in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5246\_replaced([11210209](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* TBS calculation for UL is done as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4621\_replaced([11192057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kviITvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (DL) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (UL):

-bbPoolingPeriod: [Before CB009215-D]NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod[CB009215-D]bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB009215-D]

Note1: TBS accounts only bytes of fresh transmission, multiple counts with retransmission shall not be counted.

Note2: information on buffer size and transmitted byte per bearer/LCG is maintained at L2 PS  (DL:5G\_UP\_ALG\_4561\_replaced([11186983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvXwMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and UL: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5120\_replaced([11203697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwgYqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

-Note3: the rationale to use receivedDataAmount instead of the scheduled TBS bytes in UL is to better estimate the PRB usage wrt GBR/nonGBR traffic of a UE with mixed GBR/nonGBR DRB traffic. In this scenario, the grant received by the UE for the scheduled TBS bytes is used by the UE first for GBR to fulfil the prioritized bit rate and rest to the nonGBR. Thus,  it is more accurate to estimate the GBR/nonGBR PRB usage as per the received bytes which reflects how UE actually fills TBS than the scheduled bytes how L2PS assumes.

---

#### 3.31.5.2.0-4 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation Spectral Efficiency per DL slot for Metric Based Algorithm (ID: 11212112)

**3.31.5.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11212118`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
Spectral Efficiency of one DL Scheduling slot (rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot) is computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5250\_replaced([11210238](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 3.31.5.2.0-5 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation Spectral Efficiency per UL slot for Metric Based Algorithm (ID: 11212124)

**3.31.5.2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11212136`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
Spectral Efficiency of one UL Scheduling slot (rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot) represents average number of bytes per resource element which has been used in the past for PUSCH transmission by 5G-L2-PS.

It is a cell specific variable and shall be calculated as a exponential filter in every UL slot where at least one UE PUSCH is scheduled.

Start value for rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot shall be 8, same assumption used  for DL in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5250\_replaced([11210238](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot [n] = (1 - 1/rdAvgSpectralEffUlSlotFilterCoeff) \* rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot [n − 1] + 1/rdAvgSpectralEffUlSlotFilterCoeff \* rrmInstSpectralEffUlSlot

* rdAvgSpectralEffUlSlotFilterCoeff is R&D parameters defined in 5G\_L2\_4661\_replaced([11188110](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ5PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmInstSpectralEffUlSlot shall be calculated as Sum(TBS) / SUM(REs), where
* Sum(TBS) is the sum of scheduled UL TBS of fresh transmissions (decided by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) for all scheduled UL UEs in this slot, and
* SUM(REs) is the sum of scheduled number of REs used for both fresh and retransmissions for all scheduled UL UEs in this slot

Scheduled number of REs is known by 5G-L2-PS since it is used to decide the TBS as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as number (Nre \* Nrb), where

* Nre is the number of data RE per RB, and
* Nrb is the number of allocated RB for the PUSCH

[CB007113-I]

* For FR1-TDD with MU-MIMO enabled,

If scheduled UE is a virtual UE and if this virtual UE is allocated only at the primary subcell,

Scheduled number of REs for this virtual UE = scheduled number of REs for [Before CB007113-I-UPD002] root [CB007113-I-UPD002] virtual  [End CB007113-I-UPD002] UE

Else If scheduled UE is a virtual UE and is allocated at both primary subcell and seconday subcell,

Scheduled number of REs for this virtual UE = 2 \* scheduled number of REs for [Before CB007113-I-UPD002] root [CB007113-I-UPD002] virtual  [End CB007113-I-UPD002] UE

Else for any other UE scheduled on the primary subcell

Scheduled number of REs for this UE shall be considered.

End

* where:
* for UL:  non-GBR /virtual/root UE list definition (5G\_UP\_ALG\_8271\_replaced([11146135](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), UL MU-MIMO receive mode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_12422\_replaced([11146260](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksDWe_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), MU-pairing (5G\_UP\_ALG\_8890\_replaced([11145770](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB007113-I]

---

#### 3.31.5.2.0-6 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation PRB Demand Estimation (ID: 11212141)

**3.31.5.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11212148`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
GBR, nonGBR, RIM and CG PRB Demand Estimation

---

**3.31.5.2.0-6.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `13322842`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
Every bbPoolingPeriod SFNs, the aggregate PRB demand per cell shall be calculated for DL/UL for GBR/nonGBR bearer separately as follows:

If deployment is FDD and **nrLteDssMode >= 2 and NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false:**

for DL:

prbDemandGbr(i)  = (gbrBufferLength(i,n) + rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor \* rrmAvgNewGbrDataArrivalEst ) / (cellSpectralEff(i)*totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod*maxNrDssRatio(i))

prbDemandNonGbr(i)  = (nonGbrBufferLength(i,n) + rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor \* rrmAvgNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst ) / (cellSpectralEff(i) *totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod*maxNrDssRatio(i))

Note: The lteNrDss**DlRatio.maxNrDssRatio (as provided in lteNrDssDlRatio in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message) is given as a percentage of number of subFrames allocated to NR.**

for UL:

prbDemandGbr(i)  = (gbrBufferLength(i,n) + rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor \* rrmAvgNewGbrDataArrivalEst ) / (cellSpectralEff(i)\*totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod)

prbDemandNonGbr(i)  = (nonGbrBufferLength(i,n) + rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor \* rrmAvgNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst ) / (cellSpectralEff(i)\*totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod)

else

for UL / DL:

-prbDemandGbr(i)  = (gbrBufferLength(i,n) + rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor \* rrmAvgNewGbrDataArrivalEst ) / (cellSpectralEff(i)\*totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod),

-prbDemandNonGbr(i)  = (nonGbrBufferLength(i,n) + rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor \* rrmAvgNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst ) / (cellSpectralEff(i)\*totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod),

where:

cellSpectralEff(i) = rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot \*"# PDSCH REs per PRB"    // for DL

cellSpectralEff(i) = rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot \*"# PUSCH REs per PRB"    // for UL

and

* prbDemand(i): cell PRB demand of cell i
* # PDSCH REs per PRB is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5248\_replaced([11210227](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* # PUSCH REs per PRB is taken as average (156 = 12 subcarriers x 13 PUSCH symbols)
* rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot: spectral efficiency of Dl slot defined as average number of bytes per resource element which has been used in the past for PDSCH transmission by 5G-L2-PS, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6883\_replaced([11212112](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot: spectral efficiency of Ul slot defined as average number of bytes per resource element which has been used in the past for PUSCH transmission by 5G-L2-PS, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6886\_replaced([11212124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* gbrBufferLength/nonGbrBufferLength given in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6784\_replaced([11212073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5yvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmAvgNewGbrDataArrivalEst /rrmAvgNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst as calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6785\_replaced([11212086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5zPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor :R&D parameter to estimate traffic arrival , default value 1, defined in 5G\_L2\_4662\_replaced([11188098](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ4vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod:

**-For FDD**

* total number of slots in the bbPoolingPeriod; Slots with noPdsch are not yet excluded and are counted as available slots. This is acceptable, because the amount of noPdsch slots per bbPoolingPeriod is same/static for all(!) type of pooled cells (non-DSS, DSS with/without rate-matching). If a feature introduces a dynamic assignment of noPdsch slots, this behaviour could be adapted.
* **For TDD**

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

* corresponds to the total number of UL or DL data slots within the bbPoolingPeriod**, respectively**.\*\*\*\*

**- for UL: if NRBTS/NRCELL/actInfTddFrameMuting = TRUE, muted slots (if any) shall be excluded.**

End

**- For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), prb demand is computed only for the UL**

-For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True, prb demand is computed only for the DL

Note1: for simplification, Cell spectral efficiency is used in DL/UL instead of the per-UE spectral efficiency for the PRB demand estimation.

Note2:  # PUSCH REs is estimated considering not always 14 symbols is used for PUSCH, as one symbols could be scheduled for aSRS during the pooling window.

[CB009089-A] Note3: prbDemandNonGbr (DL/UL) calculation is addtionally needed for nonGBR load report calculation for the purpose of load based mobility handover (see [13313700](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_G6bWWM6wEfCVOOJMfwsFiw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), [13313744](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UtdEgM60EfCVOOJMfwsFiw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). Hence, prbDemandNonGbr (DL/UL) needs to be calculated also when BB slow PRB pooling is disabled, but LB-HO load reporting is enabled with DL/UL nonGBR load component configuration (see [13313700](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_G6bWWM6wEfCVOOJMfwsFiw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), [13313744](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UtdEgM60EfCVOOJMfwsFiw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) [End CB009089-A]

- If NRCELL/actNrRim=3 **or=4, L2-PS in UL requests minimum PRB demand , prbDemandRim, of 48 PRBs for Remote Interference management (RIM) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_12970\_replaced([11101094](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knUAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  prbDemandRim will be used by BBRM to give cell level PRB resource with lower priority than non-GBR PRB demand.**

-Note: 48 PRBs was agreed during the design as it is the minimum of the supported values indicated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12970\_replaced([11101094](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knUAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* If NRCELL/actNrRim=1 or NRCELL/actNrRim= 2 , there shall be no PRB demand for RIM PRB by BBRM . L2 PS shall schedule such that RIM PRBs (not overlapping with UE scheduled PRB) + UE scheduled PRB does not exceed the PRB allocated by BBRM

When NRBTS/NRCELL.actUlCgType2 is set to True, a number of PRBs for Configured Grant reservation prbDemandCg shall be requested from BBRM. This request shall have the highest priority.

* prbDemandCg represent the maximum number of PRBs among all the slots over the maximum Configured Grant (CG) periodicity (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14663\_replaced([11172788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuOgsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) used by all the CG UEs in a firing state (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15099\_replaced([11172972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuPu0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ~~in the next pooling window~~, considering CG UES at the end of the current pooling window.

The resultant PRB demand of GBR, nonGBR, RIM, namely, prbDemandGbr, prbDemandNonGbr, prbDemandRim are reduced according to the value of the excess PRB demand requested for DC-GBR service in the cell as below:

If the excess demand requested for the DC-GBR service in the cell in the corresponding DL/UL direction, namely prbDemandDcGbrExcess (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32039\_replaced([11212195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 0,

prbDemandGbr is reduced by the maxGbrloadReductionPossible which is given by min(prbDemandDcGbrExcess , prbDemandGbr)

prbDemandDcGbrExcess is also reduced by the value of maxGbrloadReductionPossible and if still prbDemandDcGbrExcess > 0

prbDemandNonGbr is reduced by value of the maxNonGbrloadReductionPossible which is min(prbDemandDcGbrExcess , prbDemandNonGbr)

prbDemandDcGbrExcess is also reduced by the value of maxNonGbrloadReductionPossible and if still prbDemandDcGbrExcess > 0

prbDemandRim is reduced by value of the maxRimloadReductionPossible which is min(prbDemandDcGbrExcess , prbDemandRim)

The resultant average load measurements shall be forwarded to the BBRM.

---

**3.31.5.2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11212189`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
DC-GBR PRB Demand Estimation

---

**3.31.5.2.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11212195`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
PRB Demand Estimation for DC-GBR Service

---

**3.31.5.2.0-6.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11212201`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
Every bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall calculate demand of the estimation of PRB demand in both DL/UL direction for the DC-GBR service in the cell, namely prbDemandDcGbr, as below:

prbDemandDcGbr = sum of first 'n' entries in the list of requiredNumPrbsPerGrant (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32037\_replaced([11212205](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of all DC-GBR bearers in the cell, with the list being sorted in the descending order.

with

n = PxSCH demand of the DC-GBR service in the same DL/UL direction, namely dcGbrPxschDemandPerSlot (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31975\_replaced([11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), computed for the same pooling period.

Example: Given, DC GBR PDSCH Demand, namely dcGbrPdschDemandPerSlot, for pooling period k = 2 and there are 5 DC-GBR bearers in the cell with their requiredNumPrbsPerGrant values in DL direction = {20, 10, 40, 25, 50}. In that case, the prbDemandDcGbr for the DL direction for pooling period k = sum(50, 40) = 90.

In addition, gNB-DU shall also calculate excess DL/UL PRB demand requested for DC-GBR service in the cell from BBRM, namely prbDemandDcGbrExcess , as below

prbDemandDcGbrExcess = prbDemandDcGbr  - (sum of (maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j)/avgUeSE (i)) over all DC-GBR bearers j of UEs i in the cell)/numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod

where

* maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j) is the maximum data volume that is expected from the DC-GBR bearer j per pooling period as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31898\_replaced([11211070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* avgUeSE shall be the average of the spectral efficiency of the UE with DC-GBR bearer in the corresponding DL/UL direction as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32037\_replaced([11212205](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod is the number of scheduling slots (the slots with possible DL/UL grants) within the pooling period in the corresponding DL/UL direction. For details, pls refer to [11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
* Eventually, In the same pooling period, gNB-DU shall reduce PRB Demands of one or more of low prio services (GBR, nonGBR) in the corresponding direction (DL/UL) based on prbDemandDcGbrExcess so that higher than needed DC-GBR PRB demand requested for the DC-GBR service, namely prbDemandDcGbr can be re-used for the GBR and nonGBR services in the cell. Please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PRB demand reductions of low prio services (GBR, nonGBR) in DL and UL directions.
* Rationale: As the DC-GBR service is delay critical, higher than needed resources are requested for DC-GBR service from BBRM which would reduce the pooling efficiency. Hence, by reducing the resource demand of low priority services of the same cell which are not delay critical, the low priority services can utilise the excess allocated resources for DC-GBR services in the cell in the slots in which they are not used thereby freeing up resources for the other cells in the pool.

---

**3.31.5.2.0-6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11212205`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
PRB Demand Estimation for a DC-GBR bearer

---

**3.31.5.2.0-6.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11212212`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
gNB-DU shall compute the estimated number of DL/UL PRBs required per PxSCH allocation in a given slot for a given DC\_GBR bearer, namely requiredNumPrbsPerGrant, within any given pooling period as below

requiredNumPrbsPerGrant(j) =  maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j)/(reqPxschPerPoolingPeriod(j) \* avgUeSE)

where:

* maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j) is the maximum data volume estimated to be transmitted per DC-GBR bearer j within a pooling period, computed as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31898\_replaced([11211070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* reqPxschPerPoolingPeriod(j) is the required number of PxSCH allocations required for the DC-GBR bearer in the pooling period, computed as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31896\_replaced([11211056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* avgUeSE shall be the average of the spectral efficiency of the UE with DC-GBR bearer in the corresponding DL/UL direction represented in bits/cell Prb. It shall be maintained via an exponential averaging filter and all the UE PxSCH grants (including the grants without any data for DC-GBR bearer) shall be considered for the filter.
* Implementation Proposal: avgUeSE just represents the spectral efficiency of a UE in DL/UL and hence it can reuse the already existing similar parameters. For example: avgUeDlSE/avgUeUlSE computed as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24037\_replaced([11183451](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvK75PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G\_UP\_ALG\_24096\_replaced([11201565](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwXOuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) can be re-used also for DC-GBR UEs.

---

**3.31.5.2.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `12749861`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
UL-CoMP PRB Demand Estimation

---

**3.31.5.2.0-6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12749862`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
If NRCELL.actNrUlComp is not setting with "disabled",

gNB-DU shall compute the estimated number of UL PRBs required per PUSCH allocation in a given slot for each cell j for UL CoMP, namely prbDemandUlComp, which will be used by BBRM to give cell level PRB resource with lower priority than non-GBR PRB demand.

For the initialization:

prbDemandUlComp(j)= rdMinUlCompPrb defined in [12749884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_j31WhIJhEfCEI_OwRqP_sA)

For any given pooling period except the initialization as below

prbDemandUlComp(j) = sum (rrmScheduledPuschUlCompPrb (j)) over bbPoolEvalPeriod /numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod

rrmScheduledPuschUlCompPrb (which is defined in [12740825: Select UE(s) for UL CoMP Basic PUSCH data reception](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_JDVHcHv5EfCiUemk-K-C4g)) is the scheduled PUSCH UL CoMP PRB per slot.

bbPoolEvalPeriod, (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod is the number of scheduling slots (the slots with possible DL/UL grants) within the pooling period in the corresponding DL/UL direction. For details, pls refer to [11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

#### 3.31.5.2.0-7 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation Bookkeeping of the number of used PRBs for non-GBR (DL/UL) (ID: 12721304)

**3.31.5.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `12731395`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
When either actSlowPrbPoolingFddFr1Enh or actSlowPrbPooling is set to TRUE, or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced (11278751), the following procedure is applied during each pooling period:

For every slot, the L2PS computes the number of PRBs used separately for downlink (DL) and uplink (UL), considering non-GBR traffic, deprioritized GBR traffic, and nominal bit rate traffic. The following parameters are updated for each UE j in slot t:

rrmUsedDlPRBnonGBR(i, j, t): Number of PRBs used for non-GBR traffic for UE j in slot t (DL)

rrmUsedUlPRBnonGBR(i, j, t): Number of PRBs used for non-GBR traffic for UE j in slot t (UL)

Note: In case of MU-MIMO, if UE i is a virtual UE, then number of used PRBs calculated above, shall be multiplied by number of sub-cells used by the virtual UE.

L2PS then calculates a average of PRBs used in each BB pooling period as follows:

rrmAvgUsedDlPRBnonGBR(i, n) = Σ[j, t] (rrmUsedDlPRBnonGBR(i, j, t)) / totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod,

rrmAvgUsedUlPRBnonGBR(i, n) = Σ[j, t] (rrmUsedUlPRBnonGBR(i, j, t)) / totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod.

Where,

rrmAvgUsedDlPRBnonGBR(i, n): Average number of PRBs used per slot in DL for non-GBR traffic during pooling period n

rrmAvgUsedUlPRBnonGBR(i, n): Average number of PRBs used per slot in UL for non-GBR traffic during pooling period n

i: Cell index

j: UE index

t: Scheduling time (slot index)

n: Pooling period index

totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod: Total number of slots in the pooling period

Where  totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod:

For FDD:

The total number of slots (UL or DL) in the BB pooling period is counted. Slots with no PDSCH are not excluded and are considered available. This is acceptable because the number of no-PDSCH slots per pooling period is static for all types of pooled cells (non-DSS, DSS with/without rate-matching). If a feature introduces dynamic assignment of no-PDSCH slots, this behavior can be adapted.

For TDD:

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced (11278751), the value corresponds to the total number of UL or DL (including special slot) data slots within the BB pooling period, respectively.

For UL: If NRBTS/NRCELL/actInfTddFrameMuting = TRUE, muted slots (if any) are excluded from the count.

---

#### 3.31.5.2.0-8 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation Historical PRB usage of non-GBR traffic (DL/UL) (ID: 12721308)

**3.31.5.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `12731400`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
When either actSlowPrbPoolingFddFr1Enh is set to TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced (11278751) the L2PS calculates the historical PRB usage during each pooling period and reports this value to BBRM.

The historical average PRB usage for downlink and uplink non-GBR traffic is updated in each pooling period using an exponential moving average as follows:

AvgUsedDlPRBnonGBR(i, n) = AvgUsedDlPRBnonGBR(i, n-1) \* (1 - 1/rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff) + rrmAvgUsedDlPRBnonGBR(i, n) \* (1/rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff)

AvgUsedUlPRBnonGBR(i, n) = AvgUsedUlPRBnonGBR(i, n-1) \* (1 - 1/rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff) + rrmAvgUsedUlPRBnonGBR(i, n) \* (1/rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff)

The average number of streams PRBs used per cell is then calculated as:

AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i, n) = AvgUsedDlPRBnonGBR(i, n) \* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb

AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR(i, n) = AvgUsedUlPRBnonGBR(i, n) \* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb

Where:

AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i, n) and AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR(i, n) represent the average number of stream PRBs used per cell during BBRM pooling period n. And rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff is a value as specified in ([12723115)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7Ok1gG3_EfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i, n), AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR(i, n), AvgUsedDlPRBnonGBR(i, n), and AvgUsedUlPRBnonGBR(i, n) are the average historical usage of non-GBR traffic that is reported to BBRM in every BBRM period interval.

maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb is specified in ([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

---

#### 3.31.5.2.0-9 Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation Secondary Subcell PRB Utilization Factor (ID: 11212218)

**3.31.5.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11212223`)

Cell load measurement and PRB Demand Estimation
\* In FR1-TDD with MU-MIMO, more than one subcell can be used by the scheduler for spatial domain multiplexing.  Actual usage of secondary subcell depends on the occurence of MU-MIMO pairing over multiple subcell. Thus, this section estimates the secondary subcell PRB utilization factor defined as the fraction of PRB used by scheduler on the secondary from the maximum secondary subcell capacity defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* secondarySubcellPrbUtilizationFactor (n) = sum[ n-1, n]{#PRBs utilized on Secondary subcell} / max{1, sum[ n-1, n]{maxCellPrbSecondarySubCell }}

where:

* n : end of previous pooling period
* n-1: beginning of the previous pooling period
* The value is to be evaluated by L2PS of each cell and forwarded to BBRM together with the estimated PRB demand at the end of each pooling period
* The sum of the PRBs is done only for slots when there is data scheduled, slots with no data (PxSCH) shall be excluded.
* This formula is to be used for cells with more than one subcell,  if there is only primary subcell, L2PS shall return value of 0.
* This computation is to be done in UL-L2PS only.

---

### 3.31.5.3 Handling of Addition and Deletion of Cells

#### 3.31.5.3.0-1 Handling of Addition and Deletion of Cells Cell Setup and List Creation (ID: 11212236)

**3.31.5.3.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11212260`)

Handling of Addition and Deletion of Cells
- At cell startup, BBRM shall learn about mapping of cell to L1 pool and L1 subpool. At the same time, it shall learn about the relevant cell properties.

* The BBRM creates and maintains the list of the cells mapped to the same L1subpool.
* During cell setup, BBRM shall add the cell to the cell list per L1subpool.
* During cell setup, BBRM shall also learn the L1 pool & L1 subpool where the primary subcell of the cell is configured.
* As the updated cell list is yet to be considered by the BBRM to decide PRB allocation for the next pooling period, the number of allocated PRBs for the current pooling period to be indicated by BBRM to the new cell is 0 in response to the resource requests sent by the UL scheduler if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or by DL scheduler if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or if slowPrbPoolingAllowed is set to 'true', by the UL and DL schedulers, BBRM allocates the first PRB grant to this cell at the next pooling interval
* When interL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10386\_replaced([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):
* the capacity of the L1 subpool in UL or DL, respectively, may change due to the interL1subpool resource reallocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10384\_replaced([11212979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Thus, when a new cell is added, there may not be enough PRB capacity per subpool to guarantee at least the minimum PRB per cell configured by CPRT (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In this case, the cell will still be accepted but the PRB allocation for the cell will be zero until any next interL1Sp resource reconfiguration provides enough PRB capacity for the concerned L1Sp

[PR780074]

* If the current cell is the first cell to be added to the L1 pool (at gNB start-up or after all cells are deleted or after a reset), it shall be considered as a BBRM start-up and the the default L1 subpool capacities shall be used as for the first pooling period described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End PR780074]

* When TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), when a new cell is added to L1 pool, there may not be enough L1 UL fronthaul capacity to activate even its primary UL subcell due to the fact that L1 UL fronthaul capacity is shared among the already existing cells in L1 pool. So, it is not possible to activate the primary UL subcell of the new added cell. As a result, after cell addition, its active UL subcell list shall be considered empty and when the PRB allocation for each of cells in L1 Subpool is allocated by BBRM, PRB allocation for the cell shall be zero until the next UL subcell deactivation procedure is successful.

-In case dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the number of subcells that can be activated per L1 Pool/Subpool might already be at the maximum capacities supported by the L1 Pool. There may not be any available subcell resource that could be used even for the primary subcell of the newly added cell. In the next pooling period, on a successful execution of the ARM capacity based Subcell deactivation procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_18304\_replaced([11213877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), BBRM shall allocate at least 1 subcell to the cell, if the cell has its primary subcell in the L1 Pool, in any other situation, it is possible that the cell is not provided any subcell if it has very little load. For a cell with no active subcells, the PRB allocation from BBRM would be zero until at least 1 subcell is activated.

[CB012605-C]

NOTE : Above mentioned cell setup and cell list creation shall be supported for eCPRI 7-2e based layer PRB pooling (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE [CB012605-D] for DL/ slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE for UL [End CB012605-D]), except interworking with UL PRB muting and subcell deactivation in UL are not supported for eCPRI 7-2e. The corresponding features flags shall be disabled and sent to L2-PS. I.e., TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be set to FALSE, and ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be set to FALSE.

NOTE : With layer PRB pooling enabled (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE [CB012605-D] for DL/ slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE for UL [End CB012605-D]), the term "PRB" mentioned in this requirement shall be considered as "layer PRB".

[End CB012605-C]

---

#### 3.31.5.3.0-2 Handling of Addition and Deletion of Cells Cell List update via Cell Deletion (ID: 11212266)

**3.31.5.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11212279`)

Handling of Addition and Deletion of Cells
- when a cell is deleted from the L1subpool, the deleted cell shall be removed from the cell list  and the cell list per L1subpool shall be updated by the BBRM

[PR780074]

In case all cells are deleted from the L1 Pool, BBRM shall not send any further Pooling reconfiguration messages to L1 (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) until the first cell is added to the L1 Pool.

[End PR780074]

---

### 3.31.5.4 PRB Pooling Algorithm

#### 3.31.5.4.0-1 PRB Pooling Algorithm PRB pooling initialization (ID: 11212289)

**3.31.5.4.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11212312`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
At system startup, BBRM shall learn L1 Pool/subpool and its properties.

The L1 Pool capacities for

* DL: Max number of supported active subcells per pool
* UL: Max number of supported active subcells per pool

The L1 subpool capacities for

 DL: stream PRBs and layer PRBs per symbol

 UL: stream PRBs and layer PRBs per symbol

* DL: max stream PRBs available for Wideband signals per symbol
* DL: Max number of supported active subcells per subpool
* UL: Max number of supported active subcells per subpool

for different L1 subpool sizes, shall be initialized at system startup.

The values of the configuration parameters will be retrieved from the hidden NIDD (NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity) by L3RT and provided to L2RT.

Note: it is assumed that there is always enough pooled PRB processing capacity per L1subpool if rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddDl is “0”, per L1 pool if rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddDl is “1” at least to support the minimum PRB allocation configured by CPRT at cell setup (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

-When interL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10386\_replaced([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* the initial total stream/layer PRB capacity of the L1 subpool provided via the hidden NIDD (NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity) NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbInitCapacity for [Before CB009215-B] TDD [End CB009215-B] UL or DL, respectively, may change during run time due to the interL1subpool resource reallocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10384\_replaced([11212979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Thus, the updated value of the subpool capacity decided in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be applied.

-When dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  or ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and cellTechnology = TDD,

* Max subcell capacities for the L1 Pool are provided via the hidden NIDD NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Pool for DL & NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Pool for UL
* Max subcell capacities for each subpool in the L1 Pool are provided via the hidden NIDD NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Sp for DL & NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Sp for UL

[Before CB009215-B]-For FDD cells, such parameters shall not be used during PRB Pooling procedures, hence they can be ignored.[End CB009215-B]

---

#### 3.31.5.4.0-2 PRB Pooling Algorithm Round Robin Based PRB Pooling Algorithm (ID: 11212320)

**3.31.5.4.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `12444002`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
[Before CNI-136563] when the parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to '0:round-robin', this algorithm determines the total amount of usable PRBs (numAllocCellPrb) that can be granted to a cell out of the total available pooled PRBs of the L1-subpool via round robin fashion.

***\*- Algorithm Input :***\*

* uptodate list of active cells in the same L1subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp: stream-PRB capacity of the L1Subpool given for DL/UL in NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity
* maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp : Layer-PRB capacity of the L1Subpool given for UL in NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity
* numLayerToStreamRatio as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numMinPRBAlloc (DL/UL): minimum allocated PRB per cell (DL/UL) as defined in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **except for an SDL cell without any uplink bandwidth, numMinPRBAlloc(UL) shall be 0.**
* maxCellPrb corresponds to:

if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))),

if (NIDD:actUlMuMimo=TRUE **AND NIDD:nrCellType = xDL8UL)**

**or if subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) = TRUE**

maxCellPrb value defined 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

else

ulBandwidth for UL / dlBandwidth for DL,(PsCell\_CellSetupReq)

else

* for DL: maxCellPrb = UE bandwidth of largest DL dedicated BWP

for UL: maxCellPrb = UE bandwidth of largest UL dedicated BWP

-for FDD with DSS enabled or with PRB blanking, values as defined 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* for asymmetric FDD deployment case which is identified if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRCELL\_FDD/actAsymBwGuardband = True, the maxCellPrb in DL shall be as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1802\_replaced([11110656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGwJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

end

***\*- Algorithm Output :***\*

If subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and it is for DL only

* numAllocSubcell(i) and subcell ID list for cell(i): total amount of usable subcells (numAllocSubcell(i)) and subcell ID list (subcellList), granted per cell including the numMinPRBAlloc
* numAllocCellPrb(i): total usable cell PRB, granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell

else

* numAllocCellPrb(i): total usable Cell PRB /Subcell PRB, granted per cell including the numMinPRBAlloc.**For an SDL cell without any uplink bandwidth, numAllocCellPrb(i)  of the uplink shall be 0.**

**- Algorithm Steps:**

When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE, there are total two L1 pools and two L1 subpools per L1 pool on full BB board (in one L2-RT instance), DL subcells of one cell may be placed into two L1 pools/L1 subpools, so the following steps shall be repeated per L1 subpool. The total amount of usable subcells of the cell is the sum of usable subcells allocated from two L1 pools/subpools.

1) Convert the following input parameters corresponding to each cell into equivalent stream PRB using computation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* maxCellPrb(i)  ==> maxCellStreamPrb(i)
* numMinPRBAlloc(i) ==> numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i)
* numSubcellPrb(i)  ==> numSubcellStreamPrb(i) (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

If subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and it is for DL only

If primary subcell of cell i is located in the L1 SP then

numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) = numSubcellStreamPrb(i)

else

numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) = 0

End

End

2) Grant the minimum allocation for each cell as per the configured min value ;

* get the list of cells in the L1subpool with index i and give the initial minimum allocation per cell:

- numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) // initial allocation is done here

* calculate the amount of the remaining capacity per the L1subpool to be shared in the next step with round robin:

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE **or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))**

-Compute equivalent amount of Layer PRB for the initial min allocation

numMinLayerPRBAlloc (i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i) \*numLayerToStreamRatio (i)

-compute remaining capacity for the next steps

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)}.

L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)\*numLayerToStreamRatio (i)}.

Else

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare= maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)}.

End

3) First,  if L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare>0,  allocate as many PRB as possible to the prioritized cell, i=1, not more than maxCellStreamPrb (1)

* Note: set the first in the cell list (i=1) as a prioritized cell for the RR allocation

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE **or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))**

* update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = **min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}**

End

If L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare>= (maxCellStreamPrb(1) - numMinStreamPRBAlloc (1) )

numAllocCellStreamPrb(1) = maxCellStreamPrb(1)

Else

numAllocCellStreamPrb(1) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc (1) + L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare

End

* update the amount of the remaining capacity per the L1subpool to be shared in the next step:

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare= L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare + numMinStreamPRBAlloc (1) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(1).

4) Next, If L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare> 0, allocate additional PRB to other cells with i>1 in proportion to their maxCellStreamPrb(i):

* for i=2,3,...

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE **or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is True (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))**

* compute remaining capacity for the next allocation

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[for all j]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (j)}.

L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp - sum[for all j]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (j)\*numLayerToStreamRatio (j)}.

*- update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation*

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = **min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}**

-  Do allocaiton for cell i

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = **min{maxCellStreamPrb(i), numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i) + floor( L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare*maxCellStreamPrb(i)/sum[all j>=i]{maxCellStreamPrb(j)})\*\*}***\*

Else

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = **min{maxCellStreamPrb(i), numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i) + floor( L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare*maxCellStreamPrb(i)/sum[ all i>1]{maxCellStreamPrb(i)})\*\*}***\*

End

5)

If subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and it is DL only, compute the equivalent of subcell(s) granted per cell as follows:

* numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i), from numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) as shown in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Repeat from Step 1) to Step 5) until all L1 subpools are executed.
* numAllocSubcell(i) = sum (numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) for all L1 subpools).
* numAllocCellPrb(i) = numAllocSubcell(i) \* dlBandwidth

Note: if numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) is equal to 1 and primary subcell of cell i is located in the L1 SP, this subcell ID must be primary subcell. If numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) is equal to 1 and only non-primary subcells are located in the L1 SP, this subcell ID must be first non-primary subcell.

else

Compute the equivalent of Cell PRB /Subcell PRB granted per cell, numAllocCellPrb (i), from numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) as shown in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* The BBRM sends back the PRB or subcell grant to the 5G L2-PS of each cell scheduler (DL/UL) and the new grant is to be used starting from next SFN, SFN +1.
* The PRB or subcell grant corresponding to DL shall be sent for both DL and UL schedulers.
* In the next bbPoolingPeriod, the RR algorithm shifts the order of the cells in the list and takes the next cell as a prioritized (first) cell, and this goes in circular round every bbPoolingPeriod.
* The round robin based allocation is used to grant amount of usable PRB or subcell for UL and DL separately.
* For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**,  only UL resources are pooled and the BBRM determines the amount of UL PRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool)**

-For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))**,  only DL resources are pooled and the BBRM determines the amount of DL PRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool). Meanwhile, if subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) = TRUE, only DL resources are pooled and BBRM determines the total amount of DL subcells for each cell within 2 L1 subpools and use intra subpool pooling in each L1 subpool.**

* Slow PRB pooling shall align the selection of a prioritized cell within each slow pooling window with other pooling features used in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6361\_replaced([11210614](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw5aQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), to grant priority to the same cell during the same slow pooling window.
* For TDD FR1 with Mu-MIMO enabled in UL, number of used subcells per cell can be one or two, thus
* the term Cell PRB shall refer to the total subcell PRB as the PRBs used by each subcell of the cell (primary/secondary) shall be counted separately.
* maxCellPrb shall refer to the maximum number of total subcell PRBs that can be allocated across all subcells available in the cell.
* the amount of total usable PRB allocated to a cell by the BBRM (numAllocCellPrb) and which is indicated to the L2PS of the cell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) refers to the corresponding amount of usable subcell PRBs per cell.

when number of subcell per cell is only one, all scheduling takes place on single subcell, hence, the subcell PRB (Cell PRB) is equivalent to the actual PRB allocated by the L2PS.

[CNI-136563]

Round robin algorithm will not be supported since CNI-136563

[End CNI-136563]

---

#### 3.31.5.4.0-3 PRB Pooling Algorithm Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm (ID: 11212354)

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11212361`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Overview

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11212369`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section has been splitted via CNI-77484.

* Requirement valid upto 23R1 is under 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6788\_replaced([11212354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Requirement valid from 23R2 and onwards is under 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13233\_replaced([11212393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11212376`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm Overview [valid upto 23R1]

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11212383`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
When the NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to ''1:load-metric', the amount of PRB available to be used by each cell in the same L1 subPool is determined by the BBRM depending on a load metric defined based on the Cell's traffic load (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6504\_replaced([11212051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  Assuming the end of the previous bbPoolingPeriod (NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) is at SFN N,  the metric based algorithm determines a new allocation of PRB grant per cell (numAllocCellPrb) for the next bbPoolingPeriod based on cell load metric measured in the previous period until SFN N.

* [CB007113-C] With rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddUl  set to '1', the time at which the intra-subpool algorithm decision takes place for each subpool shall be synchronized across all the subpools in the same pool to ensure that any reconfiguration change at L1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is properly aligned time with the PRB capacity allocated to each cell. [End CB007113-C]

The load metric per cell is calculated in terms of Cell PRB demand ("Aggregate PRB demand" of a cell)  required for GBR and/ non GBR  traffic service and it is estimated separately for UL/DL as shown in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6504\_replaced([11212051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Metric-Based slow PRB allocation procedure is as follows

* At each cell, each DL/UL 5G-L2-PS determines the load metric of aggregate PRB demand at the end of each bbPoolingPeriod (NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) SFN N per DL/UL, respectively,.
* In the first SFN of each bbPoolingPeriod (SFN N+1), BBRM receives load metric with the aggregate PRB demand from each Cell's UL and DL scheduler followed by a request for the amount of available PRBs can be used by the cell starting from the next SFN.
* The BBRM determines the total amount of PRB grant to each cell of the same L1subPool based on the received load metric.
* The BBRM sends back the PRB grant to the 5G L2-PS of each cell scheduler (DL/UL) and the new grant is to be used starting from SFN N+2.
* The PRB grant corresponding to DL shall be sent for both DL and UL schedulers.

Note: during SFN N+1 (beginning of the new bbPoolingPeriod), each cell is using the old allocation as a new allocation is yet to be determined.

* The following metric-based PRB pooling algorithm shall be used to distribute the L1 subPool PRB capacity to each cell mapped to the same L1subpool:
* The algorithm is used to grant amount of usable PRB for UL and DL separately.

-Algorithm Input :

* uptodate list of active in the same L1subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp: stream-PRB capacity of the L1Subpool
* [CB007113-C] If rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddUl  set to '1'(5G\_L2\_6312\_replaced([11188119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is given for UL by parameter currentStreamPrbCapacityPerSp in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10384\_replaced([11212979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the updated value of the parameter decided during reconfiguration in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be used.

-  Else [End CB007113-C] is given for DL/UL in NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity

* [CB007113-B] maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp : Layer-PRB capacity of the L1Subpool
* [CB007113-C] If rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddUl  set to '1'(5G\_L2\_6312\_replaced([11188119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), is given for UL by parameter currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10384\_replaced([11212979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the updated value of the parameter decided during reconfiguration in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be used.
* Else, [End CB007113-C] is given for UL in NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity
* numLayerToStreamRatio as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CB007113-B]
* PrbDemandGbr/PrbDemandNonGbr  (DL/UL) as determined by L2PS 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numMinPRBAlloc (DL/UL)  as defined in 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxCellPrb corresponding to:
* [Before CB008917-D]ulBandwidth/dlBandwidth for UL/DL respectively (PsCell\_CellSetupReq 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB008917-D]

* for DL: maxCellPrb = UE bandwidth of largest DL dedicated BWP

for UL: maxCellPrb = UE bandwidth of largest UL dedicated BWP

[End CB008917-D]

* for FDD with DSS enabled or with PRB blanking, values as defined 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .
* for asymmetric FDD deployment case which is identified if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRCELL\_FDD/actAsymBwGuardband = True, the maxCellPrb in DL shall be as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1802\_replaced([11110656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGwJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-Algorithm Output :

* numAllocCellPrb(i): total usable Cell PRB grant per cell including the numMinPRBAlloc.
* Algorithm Steps:

Note1: allocation of PRB grant per cell is started in algorithm step2 with the configured min PRB value and updated in consecutive algorithm steps

Note2: Sorting of the cells in step(3) and step(4) is done to ensure that no PRBs are left unused during the PRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured or different maximum avaialble PRB due to PRB blanking. Hence, some cells with lower BW/max PRB which may not use their due share are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

1) Convert the following input parameters corresponding to each cell into equivalent stream PRB using computation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* maxCellPrb (i)  ==> maxCellStreamPrb(i)
* numMinPRBAlloc (i) ==> numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i)
* PrbDemandGbr(i)  ==> streamPrbDemandGbr(i)
* PrbDemandNonGbr  (i) ==> streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)

2) Grant the minimum allocation for each cell as per the configured min value ;

* get the list of cells in the L1subpool with index i and give the initial minimum allocation per cell:

[Before CB007113-C-UPD001]

- numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i) // initial allocation is done here

[CB007113-C-UPD001]

* With InterL1Sp PRB pooling enabled, the L1SP capacity may not be sufficient to support the minimum allocation for all cells of the SP,mainly when there is (are) newly added cell(s) to L1Sp with zero PRB BBRM grant in the past pooling period. In such case, BBRM shall deprioritize the min allocation to the newly added cells (if any) which has not yet received the first non-zero BBRM PRB grant as below;

IF slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE AND maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp < sum [for all i] {numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i)}; then

- Give the minimum allocation for the cells which had been receiving non-zero BBRM PRB grant in the previous pooling periods and set allocation to zero for the newly added cell :

o numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i); for all cells i with non-zero PRB BBRM grant in the past pooling period

o numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0; for any newly added cells with cells i with zero PRB BBRM grant in the past pooling period.

- Cells with no minimum allocation in this step (i.e., numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0), shall be excluded from participating in the remaining intraSp resource allocation step.

ELSE

- numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i) // initial allocation is done here

Note; due to the nature of the current intraSp resource allocation priority, the min allocation of the newly added cell can be satisfied as long as maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp >= sum [for all i] {numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i)}. With interL1Sp, however, if maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp was not increased after new cell addition, the remaining L1Sp capacity for the next step GBR demand based allocation would be reduced and any already admited GBR traffic in the other cells may suffer from congestion.

END

[End CB007113-C-UPD001]

* calculate the amount of the remaining capacity per the L1subpool to be shared:

[CB007113-B]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-Compute equivalent amount of Layer PRB for the initial min allocation

numMinLayerPRBAlloc (i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i) \*numLayerToStreamRatio (i)

-compute remaining capacity for the next steps

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)}.

L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)\*numLayerToStreamRatio (i)}

Else [End CB007113-B]

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare= maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)}.

End

3) First, if L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0,  allocate additional PRB based on GBR demand

* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandGbr(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandGbr value.
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if GBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = 0

Else

[CB007113-B]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE

* update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation

[Before PR663022]

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare \*streamPrbDemandGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandGbr(k)}

[PR663022]

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp \*streamPrbDemandGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandGbr(k)}

[End PR663022]

* AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i), streamPrbDemandGbr(i), AllocStreamPrbGbr(i)}
* compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare  = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

Else [End CB007113-B]

* AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - sum[for jk>=i]{streamPrbDemandGbr(k)}
* AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i), streamPrbDemandGbr(i), AllocStreamPrbGbr(i)}

End

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) .// update allocation of cell i

[CB007113-B]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = False [End CB007113-B]

* update the amount of the remaining capacity per the L1subpool to be shared in the next step:
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[all i] {numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)}  // remaining capacity to share further

[CB007113-B]

End [End CB007113-B]

4) Next, if L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare > 0, allocate additional PRB based on non-GBR demand

* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) , streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandNonGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandNonGbr value.
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if non-GBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

[CB007113-B]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE

-update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation

[Before PR663022]

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare) \*(maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))/sum[k>=i]{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}

[PR663022]

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp) \*(maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))/sum[k>=i]{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}

[End PR663022]

Else [End CB007113-B]

* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - sum[for j=i]{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}

End

* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)} //update value of AllocStreamPrbNonGbr

Else

[CB007113-B]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE

-update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation

[Before PR663022]

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare \*streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) + max{0, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare -AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) -  sum[N >k>i]{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}}}  // update value of AllocStreamPrbNonGbr

[PR663022]

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp \*streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) + max{0, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp -AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) -  sum[N >k>i]{(maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k))\* numLayerToStreamRatio (k)/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i)}}}  // update value of AllocStreamPrbNonGbr

[End PR663022]

Else [End CB007113-B]

* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - sum[for jk>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) + max{0, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare – sum[k<=i]{AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(k)}  -  sum[N >k>i]{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}}}  // update value of AllocStreamPrbNonGbr

End

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i

[CB007113-B]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE

-compute remaining capacity for the next cell

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

End

[End CB007113-B]

5) Compute equivalent of Cell PRB grant, numAllocCellPrb (i), from numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) as shown in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB007113-B] For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),  only UL resources are pooled and the BBRM determines the amount of UL PRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool). [End CB007113-B]

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11212393`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11212398`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm Overview

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `11212444`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
When the NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to ''1:load-metric', the amount of PRB available to be used by each cell in the same L1 subPool or in different L1 subpools **is determined by the BBRM depending on a load metric defined based on the Cell's traffic load (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6504\_replaced([11212051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  Assuming the end of the previous bbPoolingPeriod (bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) is at SFN N,  the metric based algorithm determines a new allocation of PRB grant per cell (numAllocCellPrb) for the next bbPoolingPeriod based on cell load metric measured in the previous period until SFN N.**

* **When interL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10386\_replaced([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the time at which the intra-subpool algorithm decision takes place for each subpool shall be synchronized across all the subpools in the same pool** or in different L1 subpools **to ensure that any reconfiguration change at L1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is properly aligned time with the PRB capacity allocated to each cell.**\*\*\*\*

The load metric per cell is calculated in terms of Cell PRB demand ("Aggregate PRB demand" of a cell)  required for GBR and/ non GBR  traffic service and it is estimated separately for UL/DL as shown in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6504\_replaced([11212051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and rdAllowZeroAllocBypass (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15040\_replaced([11215279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true, BBRM performs an additional procedure to select cells, in the same L1 Pool, that would be provided the ZAB privilege (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14549\_replaced([11213394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). **The ZAB allocation procedure shall be performed in the L1 pool after the intra-subpool pooling algorithm has been executed in all the sub pools of the L1 pool.**

Metric-Based slow PRB allocation procedure is as follows

* At each cell, each DL/UL 5G-L2-PS determines the load metric of aggregate PRB demand at the end of each bbPoolingPeriod (bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) SFN N per DL/UL, respectively,.
* In the first SFN of each bbPoolingPeriod (SFN N+1), BBRM receives load metric with the aggregate PRB demand from each Cell's UL and DL scheduler followed by a request for the amount of available PRBs can be used by the cell starting from the next SFN.
* The BBRM determines the total amount of PRB grant to each cell of the same L1subPool based on the received load metric. This shall apply to all subpools of the L1 pool or L1 pools**.**
* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed **= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the currentActiveDlSubcellList(5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** for any cell is empty **or ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** and the currentActiveUlSubcellList(5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for any cell is empty, such a cell shall not be considered for the PRB pooling algorithm in the current L1 subpool/L1 pool in DL/UL respectively, and as such, the amount of PRBs granted for such a cell in the current L1 subpool/L1 Pool shall be 0***\****\*
* The BBRM determines cells that would be granted ZAB privilege in the current pooling period. (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14566\_replaced([11213567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE and the currentActiveDlSubcellList(5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **for any cell is empty or ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE and the currentActiveUlSubcellList(5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for any cell is empty, such a cell shall not be considered for ZAB algorithm in the current L1 Pool, and as such, ZAB privilege shall not be granted for such a cell in the current L1 Pool**
* The BBRM sends back the PRB grant, numActiveDlSubcells, listOfActiveDlSubcells (the parameters are named numActiveUlSubcells, listOfActiveUlSubcells in UL) and ZAB information to the 5G L2-PS of each cell scheduler (DL/UL) and the new grant is to be used starting from SFN N+2.
* numActiveDlSubcells/numActiveUlSubcells = length(listOfActiveDlSubcells/listOfActiveUlSubcells) (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**)**
* The PRB grant corresponding to DL shall be sent for both DL and UL schedulers.

Note: during SFN N+1 (beginning of the new bbPoolingPeriod), each cell is using the old allocation as a new allocation is yet to be determined.

* The following metric-based PRB pooling algorithm shall be used to distribute the L1 subPool PRB capacity to each cell mapped to the same L1subpool:

**- The algorithm is used to grant amount of usable PRB for UL and DL separately.**

**-Algorithm Input :**

* Algorithm Input parameters are described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

**-Algorithm Output:**

If subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to TRUE and it is for DL only

{- numAllocSubcell(i) and subcell ID list for cell(i): total amount of usable subcells (numAllocSubcell(i)) and subcell ID list (subcellList), granted per cell including the numMinPRBAlloc

* numAllocCellPrb(i): total usable cell PRB, granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell

[PR835287]

* intermediateAllocCellPrb(i): total usable cell PRB before the last step (step7 in the following steps), granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell

[End PR835287] }

else

{- numAllocCellPrb: total usable Cell PRB,  /total Subcell PRB, granted per cell including the configured minimum allocation per cell numMinPRBAlloc.

[PR835287]

* intermediateAllocCellPrb(i): total usable cell PRB before the last step (step7 in the following steps), granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell

[End PR835287] }

**- Algorithm Steps:**

When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to TRUE, there are total two L1 pools and two L1 subpools per L1 pool on full BB board (in one L2-RT instance), DL subcells of one cell may be placed into two L1 pools/L1 subpools, so the following steps shall be repeated per L1 subpool. The total amount of usable subcells of the cell is the sum of usable subcells allocated from two L1 pools/subpools.

Note1: allocation of PRB grant per cell is started in algorithm step2 with the configured min PRB value and updated in consecutive algorithm steps.

1) Convert input parameters given in cell PRB (\*) to corresponding equivalent stream PRB using computation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true, convert prbDemandRim to streamPrbDemandRim for DL RIM-RS transmission according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22727\_replaced([11212003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) Each cell shall be allocated the minimum amount of stream-PRB as per the configured min value (numMinStreamPRBAlloc ) :5G\_UP\_ALG\_13342\_replaced([11212500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

3) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13342\_replaced([11212500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional stream-PRB to the cell based on CG demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20537\_replaced([11212532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

**[CB008600-F] 4) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20537\_replaced([11212532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional stream-PRB to the cell based on DC-GBR demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32043\_replaced([11212555](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9GfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));** [End CB008600-F]\*\*\*\*

4) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 **[Before CB008600-F](5G_UP_ALG_20537_replaced([11212532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**[CB008600-F](5G_UP_ALG_32043_replaced([11212555](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9GfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**[End CB008600-F], allocate additional stream-PRB to the cell based on GBR demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));**\*\*\*\*

5) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional stream-PRB to the cell based on Non GBR demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13352\_replaced([11212609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxCkIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

6) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13352\_replaced([11212609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxCkIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE and (NRCELL/actNrRim=3 or NRCELL/actNrRim=4),

distribute the remaining capacity in proportion to prbDemandRim (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) between cell **with RIM activated (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15004\_replaced([11212737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**
