6 bis) If actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE and **there is still any remaining capacity of the subpool (even if RIM allocation was not required, such as for DL TDD PRB Pooling), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13352\_replaced([11212609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxCkIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if RIM is not required; 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15004\_replaced([11212737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if RIM is also required) , in DL/UL, distribute and allocate the capacity between all the cells in the subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23856\_replaced([11212760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

7) If subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to TRUE and it is for DL only, compute the equivalent of subcell(s) granted per cell as follows:

* Compute numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp (i), from numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23856\_replaced([11212760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), using computation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Repeat from Step 1) to Step 6) until all L1 subpools are executed

If numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) >= numSubcellStreamPrb

numAllocSubcell (i) = sum (numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp (i) for all L1 subpools)

Else

numAllocSubcell (i) = 1

End If

- If "active cell amount N <=3", or {"active cell amount N > 3" and numAllocSubcell (i) > 1} then

numAllocCellPrb (i) = numAllocSubcell (i) \* numSubcellPrb(i)

End If

**Where active cells shall be configured and located in same BB board.**

Note: dlBandwidth (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if actSpecificBwpSize is false or cellBwp.bandwidth of DL dedicated BWP in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1835\_replaced([11111009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJzcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if actSpecificBwpSize is true.

Note: if numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) is equal to 1 and primary subcell of cell i is located in the L1 SP, the subcell ID must be primary subcell. If numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) is equal to 1 and only non-primary subcells are located in the L1 SP, the subcell ID must be first non-primary subcell.

Else

Compute equivalent of Cell/ subcell PRB grant, numAllocCellPrb, from numAllocCellStreamPrb(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23856\_replaced([11212760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), using computation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

End If

* For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))**,  DL and UL resources are pooled seperately and the BBRM determines the amount of DL and UL PRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool).**
* For slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**, DL and UL resources are separately pooled and the BBRM determines the amount of DL and UL PRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool).**
* For TDD FR1 with Mu-MIMO enabled in UL/DL, number of used subcells per cell can be one or two. For TDD FR1 with Mu-MIMO enabled in DL for up to 16 DL MIMO layers, number of used subcells per cell can be one to four,  thus
* the term Cell PRB shall refer to the total subcell PRB as the PRBs used by each subcell of the cell (primary/secondary) shall be counted separately.
* maxCellPrb shall refer to the maximum number of total subcell PRBs that can be allocated across all subcells available in the cell.
* the amount of total usable PRB allocated to a cell by the BBRM (numAllocCellPrb) and which is indicated to the L2PS of the cell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) refers to the corresponding amount of usable subcell PRBs per cell.

when number of subcell per cell is only one, all scheduling takes place on single subcell, hence, the subcell PRB (Cell PRB) is equivalent to the physical Cell PRB allocated by the L2PS.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11212449`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Input Parameters for Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11212495`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
-The input parameters for the load metric based PRB pooling algorithm are described in the table below:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Input Parameter** | **Values** |
| cell list per L1 subpool | 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp | if interL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10386\_replaced([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - UL/DL: currentStreamPrbCapacityPerSp (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) Else - UL/DL: NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity for FDD only if slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = FALSE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbInitCapacity for TDD /(FDD AND  slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) End |
| maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp | if interL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10386\_replaced([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) -UL/DL: currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) Else - UL/DL: NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbInitCapacity for TDD /(FDD AND  slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) End |
| numLayerToStreamRatio | 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| - streamPrbDemandGbr - streamPrbDemandNonGbr **- streamPrbDemandRim** - streamPrbDemandCg **[CB008600-F]-streamPrbDemandDcGbr** [End CB008600-F]\*\*\*\* | - PrbDemandGbr# - PrbDemandNonGbr# **- prbDemandRim#  for UL see** (  5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))***\*   - If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true, prbDemandRim is used by DL according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12045\_replaced([11160807](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3YfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). - prbDemandCg* (  5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** [CB008600-F]PrbDemandDcGbr#  (  5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[End CB008600-F]**\*\* |
| numMinStreamPRBAlloc | If artificial load for EMF is enabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17863\_replaced([11183915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_PvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))     max (Roundup (NRCELL.targetTotalLoadForEmf \* maxCellPrb# (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) / 100), numMinPRBAlloc# (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) else       numMinPRBAlloc# (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) End |
| maxCellStreamPrb | - UE dl bandwidth / UE ul bandwidth of largest DL/UL dedicated BWP. - For FDD, with DSS or PRB Blanking, then - maxCellPrb# (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - for TDD FR1 with enabled Specific BWP size function (actSpecificBwpSize is true), maxCellPrb# (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - for TDD FR1 with enabled PRB Blanking (actPRBBlanking is true), maxCellPrb# (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - For TDD FR1 with MU-MIMO enabled in UL/DL,  maxCellPrb# (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - If  actAsymBwGuardband=TRUE, then       - Available(usable) PRBs# (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1802\_replaced([11110656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGwJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |
| maxCellStreamPrbForGbr | if actSpecificBwpSize is TRUE  cellBwp.bandwidth# of DL/UL dedicated BWP else if actPRBBlanking is TRUE  dlBandwidth# of largest dedicated DL BWP - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL   ulBandwidth# of largest dedicated UL BWP  - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL else  ulBandwidth#(5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))/dlBandwidth#(5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) endif |

Input indicated in # are given in cell PRB resolution

* For TDD FR1 with Mu-MIMO enabled in UL **or DL, then**
* the term Cell PRB shall refer to subcell PRB as the PRBs used by each subcell of the cell (primary/secondary) shall be counted separately.
* maxCellPrb shall refer to the maximum number of subcell PRBs per L1 SP that can be allocated across all subcells available in the cell per L1 SP.
* maxCellStreamPrbForGbr shall refer to the maximum number of PRBs that can be allocated for GBR in a cell. Note: GBR UEs can not be paired by MU-MIMO.
* the amount of PRB demand estimated per cell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) refers to the corresponding amount of subcell PRB demand per cell.
* when number of subcell per cell is only one, all scheduling takes place on single subcell, hence, the subcell PRB (Cell PRB) is equivalent to the actual PRB allocated by the L2PS.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11212500`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation of the configured minimum resource per Cell

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11212525`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section provides an allocation of the configured minimum resource per Cell.

In case of a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), gNB-DU shouldn't allocate any UL minimum resource for the SDL cell.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Get the list of cells in the corresponding L1subpool with index i and give the initial minimum allocation per cell:

The minimum resource allocation needs to be provided by the primary subcell for each cell.

If primary subcell of cell i is located in the L1subpool then

[Before PR791584]

[CB010944-B]

If artificial load for EMF is enabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17863\_replaced([11183915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_PvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for cell i

ConfiguredLoadInStreamPRBForEmf =Roundup (NRCELL.emfTargetTotalLoad \* maxCellStreamPrb(i)) / 100);

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = max (ConfiguredLoadInStreamPRBForEmf , numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i))

Note: There's no need to protect the initial assignement for the target EMF cell and other normal cells, since only one cell can be configured as EMF cell and min stream PRB can be always guranteed with current TDD FR1 pooling configurations.

else

[End CB010944-B]

[End PR791584]

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i)

else

numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) = 0

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true, and numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) > 0

numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) = max(numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i), streamPrbDemandRim(i))

* With InterL1Sp PRB pooling enabled, the L1SP capacity may not be sufficient to support the minimum allocation for all cells of the SP, mainly when there is (are) newly added cell(s) to L1Sp with zero PRB BBRM grant in the past pooling period. In such case, BBRM shall deprioritize the min allocation to the newly added cells (if any) which has not yet received the first non-zero BBRM PRB grant as below;

If (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE) AND maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp < sum [for all i] {numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i)}; then

- Give the minimum allocation for the cells which had been receiving non-zero BBRM PRB grant in the previous pooling periods and set               allocation to zero for the newly added cell :

[PR791584]

If cell 'i' has a non-zero BBRM grant in the previous pooing period and there is a change in the artificial load for EMF for the cell (artificial load generation is enabled, or the NRCELL.emfTargetTotalLoad is increased) when compared to the previous pooling period

o numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numMinStreamPrbAlloc(i) granted to the cell 'i' in the previous pooling period

Else

[End PR791584]

o numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i); for all cells i with non-zero PRB BBRM grant in the past pooling period

o numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0; for any newly added cells with cells i with zero PRB BBRM grant in the past pooling period.

- Cells with no minimum allocation in this step (i.e., numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0), shall be excluded from participating in the remaining               intraSp resource allocation step.

[PR791584]

End

[End PR791584]

Else

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) // initial allocation is done here

Note; due to the nature of the current intraSp resource allocation priority, the min allocation of the newly added cell can be satisfied as long as maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp >= sum [for all i] {numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i)}. With interL1Sp, however, if maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp was not increased after new cell addition, the remaining L1Sp capacity for the next step GBR demand based allocation would be reduced and any already admitted GBR traffic in the other cells may suffer from congestion.

End

* calculate the amount of the remaining capacity per the L1subpool to be shared:

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = True

* Compute equivalent amount of Layer PRB for the initial min allocation
* numMinLayerPRBAlloc (i) = numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i) \*numLayerToStreamRatio (i)
* compute remaining capacity for the next steps
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)}.
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)\*numLayerToStreamRatio (i)}

Else

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare= maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)}.

End

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11212532`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on Configured Grant (CG) demand

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11212549`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB to a cell based on Configured Grant demand.[CB008224-D]In case of a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), gNB-DU shouldn't allocate any additional UL stream-PRB for Configured Grant .[End CB008224-D]

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare:  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13342\_replaced([11212500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandCg(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandCg value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandCg value.
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandCg(k)} =0; i.e. if CG demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* AllocStreamPrbCg(i) = 0

Else

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = True

* update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbCg(i) = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp \*streamPrbDemandCg(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandCg(k)}
* AllocStreamPrbCg(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb (i), streamPrbDemandCg(i), AllocStreamPrbCg(i)}
* compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbCg(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare  = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbCg(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

Else

* AllocStreamPrbCg(i) = (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - sum[for jk>=i]{streamPrbDemandCg(k)}
* AllocStreamPrbCg(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandCg(i), AllocStreamPrbCg(i)}

End

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbCg(i) .// update allocation of cell i

End

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = False AND slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = False AND slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = False

* update the amount of the remaining capacity per the L1subpool to be shared in the next step:
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[all i] {numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)}  // remaining capacity to share further

End

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no PRBs are left unused during the PRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured or different maximum available PRB due to PRB blanking. Hence, some cells with lower BW/max PRB which may not use their due share are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11212555`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on DC-GBR demand

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11212561`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB to a cell based on DC-GBR demand.In case of a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), gNB-DU shouldn't allocate any additional UL stream-PRB for DC-GBR .

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare:  5G\_UP\_ALG\_20537\_replaced([11212532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE) and it is for DL only,

If primary subcell of cell i is not located in the L1 subpool, then the cell i should not be considered in below procedure, and set

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0

Else

Below procedure shall be considered and executed.

End If

* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandDcGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandDcGbr value.
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandDcGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if CG demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i) = 0

Else

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = True

* update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i) = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp \*streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandDcGbr(k)}
* If actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is false (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) -  numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i), AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i)}

Else

AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrbForGbr(i) -  numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i), AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i)}

End If

* compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare  = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

Else

* AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i) = (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - sum[for jk>=i]{streamPrbDemandDcGbr(k)}
* AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i), AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i)}

End

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbDcGbr(i) .// update allocation of cell i

End

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = False AND slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = False AND slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = False

* update the amount of the remaining capacity per the L1subpool to be shared in the next step:
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[all i] {numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)}  // remaining capacity to share further

End

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no PRBs are left unused during the PRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured or different maximum available PRB due to PRB blanking. Hence, some cells with lower BW/max PRB which may not use their due share are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11212568`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on GBR demand

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-6.0-6**  (ID: `11212603`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB to a cell based on GBR demand. In case of a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), gNB-DU shouldn't allocate any additional UL stream-PRB for GBR.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: [Before CB008600-F] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20537\_replaced([11212532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB008600-F] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32043\_replaced([11212555](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9GfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB008600-F]

When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE) and it is for DL only,

If primary subcell of cell i is not located in the L1 subpool, then the cell i should not be considered in below procedure, and set

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0

Else

Below procedure shall be considered and executed.

End If

* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandGbr(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandGbr value.
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if GBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = 0

Else

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = True

* update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp \*streamPrbDemandGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandGbr(k)}
* If actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is false (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) -  numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandGbr(i), AllocStreamPrbGbr(i)}

Else

AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrbForGbr(i) -  numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandGbr(i), AllocStreamPrbGbr(i)}

End If

* compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare  = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

Else

* AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - sum[for jk>=i]{streamPrbDemandGbr(k)}
* AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb (i), streamPrbDemandGbr(i), AllocStreamPrbGbr(i)}

End

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbGbr(i) .// update allocation of cell i

End

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = False AND slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = False  AND slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = False

* update the amount of the remaining capacity per the L1subpool to be shared in the next step:
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum[all i] {numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)}  // remaining capacity to share further

End

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no PRBs are left unused during the PRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured or different maximum available PRB due to PRB blanking. Hence, some cells with lower BW/max PRB which may not use their due share are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-7**  (ID: `11212609`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on non GBR demand

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11212616`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Overview

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11212633`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Starting from 23R3, a new proportional based algorithm is introduced to allocate stream PRBs based on non-GBR demand.

[Before CB009215-AB-UPD001]

The new allocation mechanism is currently available only in TDD.

[CB009215-AB-B-UPD001]

The new allocation mechanism is available in TDD and FDD

[End CB009215-AB-UPD001]

It can be enabled in TDD using the NIDD parameter actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh.[CB009215-AB-UPD001]In FDD, the new allocation mechanism is enabled with enhanced FDD PRB pooling which is controlled by slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).[End CB009215-AB-UPD001]

The legacy algorithm is still to be maintained for the future releases pending the decision to mark it obsolete.

If actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh = TRUE [Before CB009215-AB-UPD001][03165922-24R1]and slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = FALSE[End 03165922-24R1][CB009215-AB-UPD001]or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE[End CB009215-AB-UPD001], the enhanced allocation mechanism shall be used as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24119\_replaced([11212679](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxCkLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Else, the legacy allocation mechanism shall be used as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24112\_replaced([11212640](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxCkJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11212640`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Legacy non-GBR demand based allocation

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11212672`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on non GBR demand. In case of a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), gNB-DU shouldn't allocate any additional UL stream-PRB for non GBR.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare:  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE) and it is for DL only,

If active cell amount N > 3 and primary subcell of cell i is not located in the L1 subpool and {([CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandDcGbr (i) + [End CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandGbr (i) + streamPrbDemandNonGbr (i)) < numSubcellStreamPrb(i) for cell i }, then

The cell i is not in the list in the corresponding L1 subpool and the cell i should not be considered in below procedure, and set numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0

Else

below procedure shall be considered and executed

End If

Where numSubcellStreamPrb(i) represent the maximum stream PRBs capacity per subcell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Where active cells shall be configured and located in same BB board.

* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) , streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandNonGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandNonGbr value.
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if non-GBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE

-update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* In case of UL: the following allocaiton is applied If afterNgbrGoToRimAllocation !=1
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp) \*(maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))/sum[k>=i]{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}

Else

* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - sum[for j=i]{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}

End

* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)} //update value of AllocStreamPrbNonGbr

Else

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE

-update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp \*streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}}

If  afterNgbrGoToRimAllocation !=1

* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) + max{0, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp -AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) -  sum[N >k>i]{(maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k))\* numLayerToStreamRatio (k)/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i)}}}  // update value of AllocStreamPrbNonGbr

End

Else

* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - sum[for jk>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) + max{0, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare – sum[k<=i]{AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(k)}  -  sum[N >k>i]{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}}}  // update value of AllocStreamPrbNonGbr

End

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE

-compute remaining capacity for the next cell

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

End

End

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no PRBs are left unused during the PRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured or different maximum available PRB due to PRB blanking. Hence, some cells with lower BW/max PRB which may not use their due share are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `11212679`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Enhanced non-GBR demand based allocation

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11212716`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on non GBR demand.In case of a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), gNB-DU shouldn't allocate any additional UL stream-PRB for non GBR.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If NRBTS.deactEnhPrbPoolAlgoUlMuMimo is False and if at least one cell of the subpool has more than one subcells & for FR1-TDD UL Only

* the allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on non GBR demand in this section shall be performed in two Rounds. Rationale: for more than one subcell per cell deployment case, instead of considering only the maxCellStreamPrb as allocation capacity limit to each cell, the two Round allocaiton first utilizes an estimate of percentage of the secondary subcell utilization by MU-MIMO (if any) and then if there is still remaining subpool capacity, the next round considers the maxCellStreamPrb. Thus, allocaiton shall be performed as described below:
* Round1: First provide additional stream-PRB allocation to each cell based on non GBR demand as described in Round1 specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26861\_replaced([11212724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), &
* Round2: if there is still remaining subpool capacity after Round1, distribute the capcity as described in this section using the following input parameter updated from Round1.
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26861\_replaced([11212724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numAllocCellStreamPrb :5G\_UP\_ALG\_26861\_replaced([11212724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* streamPrbDemandNonGbrTemp = streamPrbDemandNonGbr
* streamPrbDemandNonGbr = streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26861\_replaced([11212724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Else

* do allocation as described in this section using the following additional input parameters
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare:  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

End

When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE) and it is for DL only,

If active cell amount N > 3 and primary subcell of cell i is not located in the L1 subpool and {( [CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandDcGbr (i) + [End CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandGbr (i) + streamPrbDemandNonGbr (i)) < numSubcellStreamPrb(i) for cell i }, then

The cell i is not in the list in the corresponding L1 subpool and the cell i should not be considered in below procedure, and set numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0

Else

below procedure shall be considered and executed

End If

Where numSubcellStreamPrb(i) represent the maximum stream PRBs capacity per subcell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Where active cells shall be configured and located in same BB board

* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) , streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandNonGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandNonGbr value.
* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = True
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if non-GBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* Break loop. Stop processing this step for further cells.

Else

* update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp \*streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  max{0, min{AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i), (maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))}}

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i
* compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)
* End For
* End

If NRBTS.deactEnhPrbPoolAlgoUlMuMimo is False and if at least one cell of the subpool has more than one subcells & for FR1-TDD UL Only

* after Round 2 allocation is executed for all cells as described in this section, update the value of streamPrbDemandNonGbr for each cell with the total non-GBR demand streamPrbDemandNonGbrTemp:
* streamPrbDemandNonGbr= streamPrbDemandNonGbrTemp;

End

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no PRBs are left unused during the PRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured or different maximum available PRB due to PRB blanking and different non-GBR PRB demands. Hence, some cells with lower BW/max PRB which may not use their due share are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `11212724`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Round1 Intra-Subpool non-GBR demand based allocation

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-7.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11212729`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
\* This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on non GBR demand and allocation is limited to capacity of primary subcell and additional capacity for secondary subcells utilization estimated based PRB usage during the previous pooling period as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26875\_replaced([11212968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
\* This section is applicable for FR1-TDD UL only
\* This section is to be run if there is at least one cell within the Subpool with more than 1 subcell, other wise it is skipped.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare:  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* allocStreamPrbNonGbrLimitCell: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26875\_replaced([11212968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{allocStreamPrbNonGbrLimitCell(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) , streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandNonGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandNonGbr value.
* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if non-GBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* Break loop. Stop processing this step for further cells.

Else

* update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* Remaining capacity is distributed proportionally to the Non-GBR demand of the remaining cells
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp \*streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = max{  AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp - sum[N >k>i]{ min{allocStreamPrbNonGbrLimitCell(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k) , streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}\*numLayerToStreamRatio (k)/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i)} }
* Make sure that the allocated stream PRBs do not exceed the maximum capacity of the cell. Also ensure that the value is not less than 0.
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  max{0, min{AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i), (allocStreamPrbNonGbrLimitCell(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))}}
* Update, the nonGBR PRB demand of cell i, excluding the allocation in this round
* streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i) = streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i) – AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)
* Note: this updated demand value is to be used only in Round2 allocation, if any.

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i
* compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)
* End For
* End

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-8**  (ID: `11212737`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on RIM PRB demand

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-8.0-4**  (ID: `13251667`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on PRB demand for Remote Interference Management (RIM)

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare:  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13352\_replaced([11212609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxCkIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..*N-1:  where i= index of cell and* N is number of cells with RIM activated (NRCELL/actNrRim =3 or =4)\*\*

*- update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation*

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = **min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}**
* AllocStreamPrbRim(i) =  min{streamPrbDemandRim(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare *streamPrbDemandRim(i)/sum[*N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandRim(k)}}\*
* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)  = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)  + AllocStreamPrbRim(i) ;

*- compute remaining capacity for the next cell*

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare  = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbRim(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare     = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbRim(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

End

[CB014543-D,CB014543-E, CB014543-F]

If   histUsageAllowed = False, then

[End CB014543-D,CB014543-E, CB014543-F]

If actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh = FALSE and there is still remaining resource, after RIM PRB based demand allocation: L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare  >0, distribute the remaining resource to cells in the L1 subpool as below.

sort all cells in the subpool with maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) >0, in the increasing order of **min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)** }. **In case several cells have same value resulting from the** min operation and take random order for the cells with same value.***\****\*

For i=0,1,2,3 ..*N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and* N is number of cells in the sorted list\*\*

*-update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation*

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = **min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}**

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)+ **min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) +** max{0, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare -  sum[*N >k>i]**{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}**}}  // update value of AllocStreamPrbNonGbr****\****\*

*-compute remaining capacity for the next cell*

L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)

L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

End

[CB014543-D,CB014543-E, CB014543-F]

End

[End CB014543-D, CB014543-E, CB014543-F]

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-9**  (ID: `12763154`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on UL CoMP Demand

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `12763155`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on PRB demand for UL CoMP.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([12707884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_JpnqcmLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare:  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13352\_replaced([11212609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxCkIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..*N-1:  where i= index of cell and* N is number of cells with UL CoMP activated (NRCELL/actNrUlComp is not setting with "disabled" when it is configured)\*\*

*- update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation*

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = **min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}**
* AllocStreamPrbUlComp(i) =  min{streamPrbDemandUlComp(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare *streamPrbDemandUlComp(i)/sum[*N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandUlComp(k)}}\*
* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)  = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)  + AllocStreamPrbUlComp(i) ;
* numAllocUlCompCellPrb(i) is the cell PRB for UL CoMP converted from stream PRB for ULCoMP (i.e., AllocStreamPrbUlComp(i)) according to [11211964: Conversion Between Cell-PRB and Stream PRB](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ON0rUPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

*- compute remaining capacity for the next cell*

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare  = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbUlComp(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare     = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbUlComp(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

End

If actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh = FALSE and there is still remaining resource, after UL CoMP PRB based demand allocation: L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare  >0, distribute the remaining resource to cells in the L1 subpool as below.

* sort all cells in the subpool with maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) >0, in the increasing order of **min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)** }. **In case several cells have same value resulting from the** min operation and take random order for the cells with same value.***\****\*
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..*N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and* N is number of cells in the sorted list\*\*

*-update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation*

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = **min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}**
* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)+ **min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) +** max{0, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare -  sum[*N >k>i]**{maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)}**}}  // update value of AllocStreamPrbNonGbr****\****\*

*-compute remaining capacity for the next cell*

* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)

L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)

End

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-10**  (ID: `11212760`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Enhanced allocation of any remaining stream-PRB per cell

---

**3.31.5.4.0-3.0-3.0-10.0-3**  (ID: `13478540`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- This section describes the distribution of any remaining stream-PRBs after all other allocations per cell

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare:  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13352\_replaced([11212609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxCkIvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15004\_replaced([11212737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in case of UL and RIM activated)
* overAllocAvoidForCellStrPrbAllowed
* After all demand based allocations, if there is still remaining resource, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare > 0, distribute the remaining resource to cells in the L1 subpool as below.
* Sort all cells in the subpool with numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)>0 and { maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) >0 }, in the increasing order of **{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)** }. **In case several cells have same value resulting from the increasing order sorting operation and take random order for the cells with same value.**\*\*\*\*

Note: For a cell which has subcells configured over 2 L1 Pools, it is possible that the cells is not provided any stream PRBs in the L1 pool where the cell is configured with only secondary subcells (numAllocCellStreamPrb = 0).

* For i=0,1,2,3 ..*N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and* N is number of cells in the sorted list\*\*
* determine remaining L1 capacity checking stream/layer restrictions
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp =  **min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}**
* Calculate the total already-allocated capacity for all the cells after the current cell in the sorted list
* allocatedStreamPrbSubsequentInclusive (i) = **sum[k >= i]** {numAllocCellStreamPrb(k) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(k)**}**\*\*\*\*

**- Calculate the total maximum allocation potential remaining (until the cell-level maximums are reached) for all the cells after the current cell in the sorted list**

* potentialStreamPrbSubsequent(i) = **sum[k > i]** {(maxCellStreamPrb(k) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(k)) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(k)**}**\*\*\*\*
* Calculate the additional capacity to be allocated for the current cell from the remaining capacity proportionally to the demand-based allocation and make sure that all PRB capacity will be allocated before running out of allocation potential in the subsequent cells
* AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb = **max{floor{ L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp \* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) /(allocatedCellStreamPrbSubsequentInclusive (i) / numLayerToStreamRatio(i))** }, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp - potentialStreamPrbSubsequent(i) / numLayerToStreamRatio (i)**}**\*\*\*\*

**- Do not exceed the maximum allocation of the cell and do not allocate negative capacity**

• If overAllocAvoidForCellStrPrbAllowed = TRUE [PR883672] && partialZABAllowed ==False [End PR883672]

- Do not over-allocate to keep good ZAB granting probabilities

* AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb = min{AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb, max(cell BW Stream PRBs(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))}

• else

AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb = **min{AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb, (maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))**}\*\*\*\*

* AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb = **max{AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb , 0**}\*\*\*\*
* update total allocated capacity of the cell
* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb(i) + numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)
* compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare  - AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - (AllocRemainingCellStreamPrb(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i))

End

---

#### 3.31.5.4.0-4 PRB Pooling Algorithm Enhanced Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm (ID: 12705604)

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12706254`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Overview

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12729082`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
- An adaptive resource allocation system that dynamically distributes Physical Resource Blocks (PRBs) across multiple cells based on real-time traffic demand and historical usage patterns.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12706965`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Enhanced Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12707005`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Enhanced Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm Overview

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13388922`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
When the NIDD parameter “NRBTS.actSlowPRBPoolingEnh” is enabled, the amount of PRB available to be used by each cell in the same L1 subPool or in different L1 subpools is determined by the BBRM depending on a load metric defined based on the Cell's traffic load ([11212051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and historical usage of non-GBR traffic.  Assuming the end of the previous bbPoolingPeriod (bbPoolEvalPeriod ([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is at SFN N,  the enhanced metric-based algorithm determines a new allocation of PRB grant per cell (numAllocCellPrb) for the next bbPoolingPeriod based on the cell load metric measured in the previous period until SFN N, and wherein historical load usage of non-GRB traffic is taken into consideration.

* When interL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality is enabled ([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the time at which the intra-subpool algorithm decision takes place for each subpool shall be synchronized across all the subpools in the same pool or in different L1 subpools to ensure that any reconfiguration change at L1 ([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is properly aligned in time with the PRB capacity allocated to each cell.

The load metrics per cell is calculated in terms of Cell PRB demand ("Aggregate PRB demand" of a cell) required for GBR/non-GBR  traffic service ([11212051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_kw-5xvvsee-aqvopbp1qhq")) and historical usage of non-GBR traffic ([12721308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HO6TYG0aEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_ho6tyg0aefcmnyhxzzn44w?oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9")) and these are estimated separately for UL/DL.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE ([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and rdAllowZeroAllocBypass ([11215279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is true, BBRM performs an additional procedure to select cells, in the same L1 Pool, that would be provided the ZAB privilege ([11213394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The ZAB allocation procedure shall be performed in the L1 pool after the intra-subpool pooling algorithm has been executed in all the sub pools of the L1 pool. Note: When partial ZAB is enabled (partialZABAllowed = True), the BBRM determines the set of ZAB-privileged cells according to the specification in ([12804289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ui5xYp6QEfCkxIKMlo4L6w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

Enhanced Metric-Based slow PRB allocation procedure is as follows:

* At each cell, the DL/UL 5G-L2-PS calculates the load metric by analyzing both aggregate PRB demand and non-GBR load. The latter calculation is based on historical PRB usage of non-GBR per cell and is performed at the end of each bbPoolingPeriod (bbPoolEvalPeriod ([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) SFN N per DL/UL, respectively).
* In the first SFN of each bbPoolingPeriod (SFN N+1), BBRM receives load metric with the aggregate PRB demand from each Cell's UL and DL scheduler and historical usage of PRB for non-GBR traffic, followed by a request for available PRBs that can be used by the cell starting from the next SFN.
* The BBRM determines the total amount of PRB grant to each cell of the same L1subPool based on the received load metric. This shall apply to all subpools of the L1 pool or L1 pools.
* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE ([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the currentActiveDlSubcellList([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for any cell is empty or ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE ([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the currentActiveUlSubcellList([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for any cell is empty, such a cell shall not be considered for the PRB pooling algorithm in the current L1 subpool/L1 pool in DL/UL respectively, and as such, the amount of PRBs granted for such a cell in the current L1 subpool/L1 Pool shall be 0
* The BBRM determines cells that would be granted ZAB privilege in the current pooling period. ([11213567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE and the currentActiveDlSubcellList([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for any cell is empty or ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE and the currentActiveUlSubcellList([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for any cell is empty, such a cell shall not be considered for ZAB algorithm in the current L1 Pool, and as such, ZAB privilege shall not be granted for such a cell in the current L1 Pool
* The BBRM sends back the PRB grant, numActiveDlSubcells, listOfActiveDlSubcells (the parameters are named numActiveUlSubcells, listOfActiveUlSubcells in UL) and ZAB information to the 5G L2-PS of each cell scheduler (DL/UL) and the new grant is to be used starting from SFN N+2.
* numActiveDlSubcells/numActiveUlSubcells = length(listOfActiveDlSubcells/listOfActiveUlSubcells) ([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* The PRB grant corresponding to DL shall be sent to both DL and UL schedulers.

Note: During SFN N+1 (beginning of the new bbPoolingPeriod), each cell uses the old allocation, as a new allocation has yet to be determined.

* The following enhanced metric-based PRB pooling algorithm shall be used to distribute the L1 subPool PRB capacity to each cell mapped to the same L1subpool:
* The algorithm is used to grant an amount of usable PRB for UL and DL separately.

-Algorithm Input :

* Algorithm Input parameters are described in ([12707884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JlzheGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

-Algorithm Output:

If subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to TRUE and it is for DL only

* numAllocSubcell(i) and subcell ID list for cell(i): total amount of usable subcells (numAllocSubcell(i)) and subcell ID list (subcellList), granted per cell, including the numMinPRBAlloc
* numAllocCellPrb(i): total usable cell PRB, granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell
* intermediateAllocCellPrb(i): total usable cell PRB before the last step (step 7 in the following steps), granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell

else

* numAllocCellPrb: total usable Cell PRB,  total Subcell PRB, granted per cell, including the configured minimum allocation per cell numMinPRBAlloc.
* intermediateAllocCellPrb(i): total usable cell PRB before the last step (step7 in the following steps), granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell
* numAllocUlCompCellPrb: if NRCELL:actNrUlComp is not setting with "disabled": total useable cell PRB for UL CoMP defined in [12763154](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_a345UIO8EfCOGMMH109ICw), which is dedicated for UL CoMP and is not a part of numAllocCellPrb above.
* Algorithm Steps:

When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to TRUE, there are total two L1 pools and two L1 subpools per L1 pool on full BB board (in one L2-RT instance), DL subcells of one cell may be placed into two L1 pools/L1 subpools, so the following steps shall be repeated per L1 subpool. The total amount of usable subcells of the cell is the sum of usable subcells allocated from two L1 pools/subpools.

Note 1: allocation of PRB grant per cell is started in algorithm step 2 with the configured min PRB value and updated in consecutive algorithm steps.

1) Convert input parameters given in cell PRB (\*) to corresponding equivalent stream PRB using computation in ([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true, convert prbDemandRim to streamPrbDemandRim for DL RIM-RS transmission according to ([11212003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) Each cell shall be allocated the minimum amount of stream-PRB as per the configured min value (numMinStreamPRBAlloc), according to ([11212500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

3) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 ([11212500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), allocate additional stream-PRB to the cell based on CG demand ([11212532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

4) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 ([11212532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9FfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), allocate additional stream-PRB to the cell based on DC-GBR demand ([11212555](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9GfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

4\_1) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 ([11212555](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9GfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), allocate additional stream-PRB to the cell based on GBR demand ([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

5) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 ([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), allocate additional stream-PRB to the cell based on Non GBR load, i.e., Round-1 in ([12707888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y68fcGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA)).

6) Then, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 ([12707888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y68fcGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA)) and if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE and (NRCELL/actNrRim=3 or NRCELL/actNrRim=4),

distribute the remaining capacity in proportion to prbDemandRim ([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) between cell with RIM activated ([11212737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB015284-C]  intra power pooling step) , After the step 6) execution, if PwrPoolingFddAllowed=true

* BBRM shall suspend the execution of further PRB pooling steps.
* only when all the PRB pooling for all the L1 Subpools have reached this point, BBRM shall perform middle round of intra-power pooling (see [13237745: Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (middle round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_TmBNsr-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)),
* then BBRM shall skip the cells with allocated power from further PRB pooling steps and update the L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare of its L1 subPool.
* then BBRM shall resume further PRB pooling steps [End CB015284-C]

6\_1) Then, if there is still any remaining capacity of the subpool (even if RIM allocation was not required, such as for DL TDD PRB Pooling), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 ([12707888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y68fcGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA)) if RIM is not required; ([11212737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if RIM is also required) , in DL/UL, allocate additional capacity to the cells based on Non GBR load, i.e, Round-2 in ([12707889)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_rwXGQGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA).

6\_2) or, if there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 ([12707888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Y68fcGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA)) in UL and if slowPrbPoolingFddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE and NRCELL.actNrUlComp is not setting with "disabled",

distribute the remaining capacity in UL in proportion to prbDemandUlComp ([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)/[12749861](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_4McmkYJeEfCEI_OwRqP_sA)) between cells with UL CoMP activated in UL ([12763154](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_a345UIO8EfCOGMMH109ICw)).

6\_3) If actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE and **there is still any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare >0 in**([12707889)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_rwXGQGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA), in DL/UL, distribute and allocate the capacity between all the cells in the subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_23856\_replaced([11212760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB015284-C] intra power pooling step) then, if PwrPoolingFddAllowed=true,   
BBRM shall perform post round of intra-power pooling (see [13237746: Intra Power pooling procedure after the PRB pooling (post round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ZBCE4L-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), and update numAllocCellStreamPrb of the power pooling cell by excluding the excessive allocated PRBs according to minimum PSD principle for all the power pools if needed.  [End CB015284-C]

7) If subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to TRUE and it is for DL only, compute the equivalent of subcell(s) granted per cell as follows:

* Compute numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp (i), from numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) ([11212760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), using computation in ([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Repeat from Step 1) to Step 6) until all L1 subpools are executed

If numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) >= numSubcellStreamPrb

numAllocSubcell (i) = sum (numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp (i) for all L1 subpools)

Else

numAllocSubcell (i) = 1

End If

- If "active cell amount N <=3", or {"active cell amount N > 3" and numAllocSubcell (i) > 1} then

numAllocCellPrb (i) = numAllocSubcell (i) \* numSubcellPrb(i)

End If

Where active cells shall be configured and located in same BB board.

Note: dlBandwidth ([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if actSpecificBwpSize is false or cellBwp.bandwidth of DL dedicated BWP in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message ([11111009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJzcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if actSpecificBwpSize is true.

Note: if numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) is equal to 1 and primary subcell of cell i is located in the L1 SP, the subcell ID must be primary subcell. If numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) is equal to 1 and only non-primary subcells are located in the L1 SP, the subcell ID must be first non-primary subcell.

Else

Compute equivalent of Cell/ subcell PRB grant, numAllocCellPrb, from numAllocCellStreamPrb ([11212760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLOvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), using computation in ([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

End If

* For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE ([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and ([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)),  DL and UL resources are pooled separately, and the BBRM determines the amount of DL and UL PRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool).
* For slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE ([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), DL and UL resources are separately pooled and the BBRM determines the amount of DL and UL PRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool).
* For TDD FR1 with MU-MIMO enabled in UL/DL, number of used subcells per cell can be one or two. For TDD FR1 with MU-MIMO enabled in DL for up to 16 DL MIMO layers, number of used subcells per cell can be one to four,  thus
* the term Cell PRB shall refer to the total subcell PRB as the PRBs used by each subcell of the cell (primary/secondary) shall be counted separately.
* maxCellPrb shall refer to the maximum number of total subcell PRBs that can be allocated across all subcells available in the cell.
* the amount of total usable PRB allocated to a cell by the BBRM (numAllocCellPrb) and which is indicated to the L2PS of the cell ([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) refers to the corresponding amount of usable subcell PRBs per cell.

When the number of subcells per cell is only one, all scheduling takes place on a single subcell; hence, the subcell PRB (Cell PRB) is equivalent to the physical Cell PRB allocated by the L2PS.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12707884`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm

| - streamPrbDemandGbr - streamPrbDemandNonGbr - streamPrbDemandRim - streamPrbDemandCg [CB008465-F] - streamPrbDemandUlComp [End CB008465-F] | - PrbDemandGbr# - PrbDemandNonGbr# - prbDemandRim#  for UL see (  5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))   - If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true, prbDemandRim is used by DL according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12045\_replaced([11160807](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3YfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). - prbDemandCg *(  5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))* *[CB008465-F]* *- prbDemandUlComp ([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))* *[End CB008465-F]*\* |

| maxCellStreamPrbForGbr | if actSpecificBwpSize is TRUE  cellBwp.bandwidth# of DL/UL dedicated BWP else if actPRBBlanking is TRUE  dlBandwidth# of largest dedicated DL BWP - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL   ulBandwidth# of largest dedicated UL BWP  - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL else  ulBandwidth#(5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))/dlBandwidth#(5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) endif |

| AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR | Historical usage of UL used PRB for non-GBR traffic when histUsageAllowed =TRUE ([12721308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HO6TYG0aEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) |
| maxPcellStreamlPrb | The maximum number of DL and UL primary sub-cell PRBs that are calculated in ([12739292](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25v34HkDEfCdZt6bzaG3fw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). |

Input indicated in # is given in the cell PRB resolution

* For TDD FR1 with Mu-MIMO enabled in UL or DL, then
* the term Cell PRB shall refer to subcell PRB as the PRBs used by each subcell of the cell (primary/secondary) shall be counted separately.
* maxCellPrb shall refer to the maximum number of subcell PRBs per L1 SP that can be allocated across all subcells available in the cell per L1 SP.
* maxCellStreamPrbForGbr shall refer to the maximum number of PRBs that can be allocated for GBR in a cell. Note: GBR UEs can not be paired by MU-MIMO.
* the amount of PRB demand estimated per cell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) refers to the corresponding amount of subcell PRB demand per cell.
* when number of subcell per cell is only one, all scheduling takes place on single subcell, hence, the subcell PRB (Cell PRB) is equivalent to the actual PRB allocated by the L2PS.
