**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12707888`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation of Additional stream-PRB per cell based on non-GBR Load

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12710035`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Overview

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12729160`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
A new proportional-based algorithm is introduced to allocate stream PRBs based on non-GBR demand and non-GBR load.

The new allocation mechanism is available in TDD and FDD.

It can be enabled in TDD using the NIDD parameter actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh. In FDD, the new allocation mechanism is enabled with enhanced FDD PRB pooling, which is controlled by slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If histUsageAllowed = TRUE, the enhanced allocation mechanism shall be used as described in ([12710038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GtAbMGX-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g)) and ([12707889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_rwXGQGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) respectively.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12710038`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Enhanced non-GBR demand- and load-based allocation (Round-1)

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12729276`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on non-GBR demand and historical load when histUsageAllowed =TRUE ([12737865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1U3IUXhAEfCdZt6bzaG3fw "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_1u3iuxhaefcdzt6bzag3fw&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects%2f_pmhfqo3wee-rl47x_rccmw%2fcomponents%2f_fh7nqo3xee-rl47x_rccmw&oslc.configuration=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9")). In case a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), gNB-DU shouldn't allocate any additional UL stream-PRB for non-GBR.

* Given:
* Input parameters: as described in ([12707884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JlzheGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare:  5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13351\_replaced([11212568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9G_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxHistnonGBRCellStreamPrb(i) ([12765288](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6n_vEITnEfCOGMMH109ICw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE)

If active cell amount N > 3 and primary subcell of cell i is not located in the L1 subpool and {( streamPrbDemandDcGbr (i) + streamPrbDemandGbr (i) + streamPrbDemandNonGbr (i)) < numSubcellStreamPrb(i) for cell i}, then

The cell i is not in the list in the corresponding L1 subpool and the cell i should not be considered in the below procedure, and set numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0

Else

Below procedure shall be considered and executed

End If

Where numSubcellStreamPrb(i) represents the maximum stream PRBs capacity per subcell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Where active cells shall be configured and located on the same BB board

* sort the cells in the increasing order of  [Before PR875285] min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), maxHistnonGBRCellStreamPrb(i)}}. In case several cells have same value resulting from the outer min operation and if they have different values from the inner min operation, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of the result of the inner min operation. [PR875285] min( maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), min( streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i) or AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR(i))). Note: If several cells have the same value after sorting the list, select them at random in order. [End PR875285]
* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = True
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if non-GBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* Break loop. Stop processing this step for further cells.

Else

* update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = min (streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), maxHistnonGBRCellStreamPrb(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp\* streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(k)})
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  max{0, min{AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i), (maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))}}

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i

Store cell i nonGBR allocation from round 1 to compute the updated “demand” for round 2:

AllocStreamPrbNonGbrRound1(i) = AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)

* compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)
* End For
* End

Note: The cells are sorted to ensure that no PRBs are left unused during PRB allocation.

Rationale:

Different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured or different maximum available PRB due to PRB blanking and different non-GBR PRB demands. Hence, some cells with lower BW/max PRB, which may not receive their due share, are allocated first according to the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12707889`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation of any remaining stream-PRB per cell based on non-GBR Load (Round-2)

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13393352`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
This section provides an allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell, i.e., Round-2, based on non-GBR demand and historical load when histUsageAllowed =TRUE ([12737865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1U3IUXhAEfCdZt6bzaG3fw "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_1u3iuxhaefcdzt6bzag3fw&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects")). In the case that a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), the gNB-DU shouldn't allocate any additional UL stream-PRB for non-GBR.

- Given:

* Input parameters: as described in ([12707884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JlzheGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA))
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare w/o RIM activation ([12710038)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GtAbMGX-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and with activated RIM ([11212737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare w/o RIM activation ([12710038)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GtAbMGX-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) with activated RIM ([11212737](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true, the updated L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare by middle round of intra power pooling allocation (see  [13237745: Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (middle round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_TmBNsr-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))   [End CB015284-C]
* streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i) ([12775856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_paSLqIyXEfCrqOdGJPoCRA))

When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE)

If active cell amount N > 3 and primary subcell of cell i is not located in the L1 subpool and {( streamPrbDemandDcGbr (i) + streamPrbDemandGbr (i) + streamPrbDemandNonGbr (i)) < numSubcellStreamPrb(i) for cell i}, then

The cell i is not in the list in the corresponding L1 subpool and the cell i should not be considered in the below procedure, and set numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = 0

Else

Below procedure shall be considered and executed

End If

Where numSubcellStreamPrb(i) represents the maximum stream PRBs capacity per subcell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Where active cells shall be configured and located on the same BB board

* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i), streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i)}. In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2 value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2 value [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true, the cell with allocated power in the middle round of intra-power pooling shall be excluded from the sorted list  [End CB015284-C].
* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = True
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(k)} =0; i.e. if updated non-GBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* Break loop. Stop processing this step for further cells.

Else

* update L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare checking stream/layer capacity limitation
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp = min{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare/ numLayerToStreamRatio (i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare}
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) = min (streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i), L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShareTemp\* streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2 (i)/sum[N >k>=i]{ streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2 (k)})
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) =  max{0, min{AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i), (maxCellStreamPrb (i) - numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))}}

End

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) + AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i
* Compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare = L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare    = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocStreamPrbNonGbr(i) \* numLayerToStreamRatio(i)
* End For
* End

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `12775856`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm

### Stream PRB demand for nonGBR based allocation round 2

---

**3.31.5.4.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12775857`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
This section defines the updated nonGBR “demand” that will be used in allocation round 2 ([12707889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_rwXGQGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

streamPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i) = max{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)- AllocStreamPrbNonGbrRound1(i),  rdPrbPoolingGracefulAllocFactor \*[AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i) OR AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR(i)]- AllocStreamPrbNonGbrRound1(i)}

Where,

* streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i) – ([12775856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_paSLqIyXEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* AllocStreamPrbNonGbrRound1(i) – ([12710038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GtAbMGX-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* rdPrbPoolingGracefulAllocFactor - ([12722864)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_OvVvKW3vEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i)/AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR(i)  ([12721308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HO6TYG0aEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

---

#### 3.31.5.4.0-5 PRB Pooling Algorithm Max Primary SubCell Stream PRB Calculation (ID: 12739292)

**3.31.5.4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12739299`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Max Primary SubCell Stream PRB Calculation in FDD

---

**3.31.5.4.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12739306`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
The maximum number of DL and UL primary sub-cell PRBs that are calculated as follows:

IF nrLteDssMode >= 3:

If actPRBBlanking is FALSE (DSS, non-PRB blanking), calculation of maxPCellStreamPrb shall be done in the following way:

* For DL: maxPcellStreamlPrb = dlBandwidth \*numMaxStreamPerSubcell

If NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false

for UL:maxPcellStreamlPrb = (max(floor(maxNrDssRatio*LTEulchBW) + corr; PRB(NR PUCCH) + 6 (PRACH)))*numMaxStreamPerSubcell

else // NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true

for UL: maxPcellStreamlPrb = (floor(maxNrDssRatio*LTEulchBW) + numNrDedicatedPrb +1)* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

else If actPRBBlanking is TRUE (DSS, PRB blanking):   // DSS & blanking

for DL: maxPcellStreamlPrb = (dlBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL) \* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

If NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false

for UL: maxPcellStreamlPrb = max (floor (maxNrDssRatio\*(LTEulchBw -LTEulBlankedHighEdge – LTEulBlankedLowEdge)) + NRPRB\_deltaLowEdge + NRPRB\_deltaHighEdge; #PRB (NR PUCCH) + 6 (PRACH)) \* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

else // NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true

for UL: maxPcellStreamlPrb = (numMaxPossibleNrPrbsInLteSharedArea + numNrDedicatedPrb +1 - blankedPrbsInNrDedicatedArea) \* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

// This is the approximation, the actual maximum may be lower

lowEdge:

If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL <= corr/2  // blanking at NR side only, no LTE impact

NRPRB\_deltaLowEdge = corr/2 – nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL // remaining extra PRBs in NR

LTEulBlankedLowEdge = 0

Else // MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL > corr/2

// All extra PRBs in NR blanked and additional blanked in LTE

NRPRB\_deltaLowEdge = 0

LTEulBlankedLowEdge = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL - corr/2

highEdge:

If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL <=corr/2

NRPRB\_deltaHighEdge = corr/2 – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL

LTEulBlankedHighEdge = 0

Else // MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL > corr/2

NRPRB\_deltaHighEdge = 0

LTEulBlankedHighEdge = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL - corr/2

endif

Where:

- #PRB(NR PUCCH) =

If ((actInterNumerologyCa = 'FALSE' AND flexibleCAMode = '0') OR (flexibleCAMode>'0' AND longPUCCHconfigType='nonCAPUCCHconfig‘)) : // configuration without CA:

// 5GC001390 disabled AND 5GC001167 disabled; “0” means BasicCAmode, which means carrier aggregation not(!) supported.

If fdmConfig.actIncreasedFdmUsersPerSlot = TRUE: // CB006667 enabled

# PRB(NR PUCCH) = 8

else // CB006667 disabled

# PRB(NR PUCCH) = 6

endif

else // configuration with CA; CB006667 has no impact:

# PRB(NR\_PUCCH) = 10

Endif

-numMaxStreamPerSubcell refers to the number of stream PRB per subcell, as explained in [11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9")

For DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false

- for 10MHz: LTEulchBW = 50PRB; corr=2PRB

- for 15MHz: LTEulchBW = 75PRB; corr=4PRB

- for 20MHz: LTEulchBW = 100PRB; corr=6PRB

For DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true

- for NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.lteChBw equal to 10MHz: LTEulchBW = 50PRB

- for NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.lteChBw equal to 15MHz: LTEulchBW = 75PRB

- for NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.lteChBw equal to 20MHz: LTEulchBW = 100PRB

- numNrDedicatedPrbs = PRBs available in NR dedicated area ([12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

- blankedPrbsInNrDedicatedArea =

nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL if LTE is aligned at the top of the carrier

nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL if LTE is aligned at the bottom of the carrier

- blankedPrbsInNrSharedArea =

nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL if LTE is aligned at the bottom of the carrier

nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL if LTE is aligned at the top of the carrier

- numMaxPossibleNrPrbsInLteSharedArea=min ( floor(maxNrDssRatio\*LTEulchBW), LTEulchBW+3-blankedPrbsInNrSharedArea)

Note: +3 is added because there might be up to 3 NR PRBs between LTE shared area and NR guardband

Note:

- DSS is supported for 10/15/20 MHz cells only if NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false. For NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true the DSS is supported for 15/20/25/30/35/40/50 MHz and NR cell must have bigger cell bandwidth than LTE cell (configurations are verified in NIDD).

- The lteNrDssUlRatio.maxNrDssRatio (as provided in lteNrDssUlRatio in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message) is given as a percentage of number of PRBs of the associated LTE bandwidth (LTEulchBW). This is the maximum amount of PRBs NR can get. In case of blanking, the LTEblanked PRBs have to be excluded from the LTE bandwidth before calculating the share (see CRM.2049). Very exact value of maxNrDssRatio is available after DSS coordination phase with LTE. But for time being until dynamic update od sharing rate will be supported, the value as provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message is exact enough (so far operators have configured same share for LTE and NR).

* LTEulchBW is the amount of LTE PRBs according to the LTE carrier frequency.
* dlBandwidth/ulBandwidth is provided as amount of PRBs, provided by PsCell\_CellSetupReq message.

- prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL and prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL are provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message

- nrLteDssMode is provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message

* see CRM.2049 for sharing rate calculation in case of blanking; (CRM: "Common Resource Management" in DOORS Module RA System General Modules/Common Modules/Applications)
* see CRM.1024: Clarification about PRB numbering; (CRM: "Common Resource Management" in DOORS Module RA System General Modules/Common Modules/Applications)
* 5GC001390: Inter-band DL CA FDD - TDD FR1 SA (Option 2)
* 5GC001167: FDD DL CA up to 3 CCs

-CB006667: Increased number of FDM scheduled UEs per slot

Note:

This feature does not treat subframes 0/5/9 in DSS Ph3 in any special way.

The corresponding PRBs would not be available for other cells.

Else If actPRBBlanking is TRUE:

for DL: maxPcellStreamlPrb = (dlBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL) \* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

for UL: maxPcellStreamlPrb = (ulBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL)\* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

Note: prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL are provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message

Endif

---

**3.31.5.4.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12739304`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Max Primary SubCell Stream PRB Calculation in TDD

---

**3.31.5.4.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12739521`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
The maximum number of DL and UL primary sub-cell PRBs that are calculated as follows:

If actPRBBlanking is TRUE

for UL: maxPcellStreamlPrb = (ulBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL) \* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

for DL: maxPcellStreamlPrb = (dlBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL) \* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

Else

for UL: maxPcellStreamlPrb  = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

for DL: maxPcellStreamlPrb  = dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

EndIf

Note: prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL are provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message

where,

-numMaxStreamPerSubcell refers to the number of stream PRB per subcell, as explained in [11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9")

---

#### 3.31.5.4.0-6 PRB Pooling Algorithm Max Stream PRB Limit for non GBR load in historical usage (ID: 12765288)

**3.31.5.4.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12765290`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
This section defines the maximum stream PRB allocation limit for a cell that needs to be considered for non-GBR historical usage allocation.

maxHistnonGBRCellStreamPrb(i) =max {(**rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsage****F****dd** or***\**\*rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsage**T**dd**)***\****maxPcellStreamPrb(i), (1+ rdPrbPooilngOverAllocFactor)\* (AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i) OR AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR(i))}.

Where,

* **rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsage****F****dd** (***\*[12879240](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI__JJj47M7EfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)*\*), when**slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = True.
* **rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsage**T**dd (*****\*[12879244](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Hv1F3LM8EfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)*\*), when**If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True.
* rdPrbPoolngOverAllocFactor ([12722864)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_OvVvKW3vEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR/AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR ([12721308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HO6TYG0aEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* maxPcellStreamlPrb(i) is the maximum number of DL and UL primary sub-cell PRBs that are calculated in ([12739292](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25v34HkDEfCdZt6bzaG3fw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
* i is cell index

---

#### 3.31.5.4.0-7 PRB Pooling Algorithm Max Cell PRB Calculation (ID: 11212774)

**3.31.5.4.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11212778`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Max Cell PRB Calculation in FDD

---

**3.31.5.4.0-7.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12679161`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Note: The maximum numbers of DL and UL cell PRBs that are indicated to BBRM may be higher or equal to the actual maximums used by he cell. Maximums may differ because not all information is available at cell setup and approximations may be used.

IF nrLteDssMode >= 3:

If actPRBBlanking is FALSE (DSS, non-PRB blanking), calculation of maxCellPrb shall be done in the following way:

for DL: maxCellPrb = dlBandwidth

[CB007372-A-UPD001][CB007372-A]   
If NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A][End CB007372-A-UPD001]

for UL: maxCellPrb = max(floor(maxNrDssRatio\*LTEulchBW) + corr; #PRB(NR PUCCH) + 6 (PRACH) )

[CB007372-A-UPD001][CB007372-A]

else // NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true

for UL: maxCellPrb = floor(maxNrDssRatio\*LTEulchBW) + numNrDedicatedPrb +1

[End CB007372-A][End CB007372-A-UPD001]

else If actPRBBlanking is TRUE (DSS, PRB blanking):   // DSS & blanking

for DL: maxCellPrb = dlBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL - nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL

[CB007372-D]   
If NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-D]

for UL: maxCellPrb = max(floor(maxNrDssRatio\*(LTEulchBw -LTEulBlankedHighEdge – LTEulBlankedLowEdge)) + NRPRB\_deltaLowEdge + NRPRB\_deltaHighEdge; #PRB(NR PUCCH) + 6 (PRACH))

[CB007372-D]

else // NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true

for UL: maxCellPrb = numMaxPossibleNrPrbsInLteSharedArea + numNrDedicatedPrb +1 - blankedPrbsInNrDedicatedArea

// This is the approximation, the actual maximum may be lower

[End CB007372-D]

lowEdge:

If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL <= corr/2  // blanking at NR side only, no LTE impact

NRPRB\_deltaLowEdge = corr/2 – nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL // remaining extra PRBs in NR

LTEulBlankedLowEdge = 0

Else  // MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL > corr/2

// All extra PRBs in NR blanked and additional blanked in LTE

NRPRB\_deltaLowEdge = 0

LTEulBlankedLowEdge = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL - corr/2

highEdge:

If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL <=corr/2

NRPRB\_deltaHighEdge = corr/2 – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL

LTEulBlankedHighEdge = 0

Else  // MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL > corr/2

NRPRB\_deltaHighEdge = 0

LTEulBlankedHighEdge = MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL - corr/2

endif

where:

- #PRB(NR PUCCH) =

If **((actInterNumerologyCa = 'FALSE' AND flexibleCAMode = '0') OR (flexibleCAMode>'0' AND longPUCCHconfigType='nonCAPUCCHconfig‘)**) : // configuration without CA:\*\*\*\*

// 5GC001390 disabled AND 5GC001167 disabled; “0” means BasicCAmode, which means carrier aggregation not(!) supported;

If fdmConfig.actIncreasedFdmUsersPerSlot = TRUE: // CB006667 enabled

# PRB(NR PUCCH) = 8

else // CB006667 disabled

# PRB(NR PUCCH) = 6

endif

else // configuration with CA; CB006667 has no impact:

# PRB(NR\_PUCCH) = 10

endif

[CB007372-A-UPD001] [CB007372-A]  
      For DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false [End CB007372-A] [End CB007372-A-UPD001]

- for 10MHz: LTEulchBW = 50PRB; corr=2PRB

- for 15MHz: LTEulchBW = 75PRB; corr=4PRB

- for 20MHz: LTEulchBW = 100PRB; corr=6PRB

[CB007372-A-UPD001] [CB007372-A]  
  For DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true

- for NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.lteChBw equal to 10MHz: LTEulchBW = 50PRB

- for NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.lteChBw equal to 15MHz: LTEulchBW = 75PRB

- for NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.lteChBw equal to 20MHz: LTEulchBW = 100PRB

[End CB007372-A][End CB007372-A-UPD001]

[CB007372-A-UPD001][CB007372-A]

- numNrDedicatedPrbs = PRBs available in NR dedicated area ([12620260: Resource sharing in asymmetric DSS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_NsAEcDfZEfCYiuaHdt7wgQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

[End CB007372-A][End CB007372-A-UPD001]

[CB007372-D]

- blankedPrbsInNrDedicatedArea =

nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL if LTE is aligned at the top of the carrier

nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL if LTE is aligned at the bottom of the carrier

- blankedPrbsInNrSharedArea =

nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL if LTE is aligned at the bottom of the carrier

nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL if LTE is aligned at the top of the carrier

- numMaxPossibleNrPrbsInLteSharedArea=min ( floor(maxNrDssRatio\*LTEulchBW), LTEulchBW+3-blankedPrbsInNrSharedArea)

Note: +3 is added because there might be up to 3 NR PRBs between LTE shared area and NR guardband

[End CB007372-D]

Note:

- DSS is supported for 10/15/20 MHz cells only [CB007372-A-UPD001][CB007372-A] if NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=false. For NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true the DSS is supported for 15/20/25/30/35/40/50 MHz and NR cell must have bigger cell bandwidth than LTE cell (configurations are verified in NIDD). [End CB007372-A][End CB007372-A-UPD001] .

- The lteNrDssUlRatio.maxNrDssRatio (as provided in lteNrDssUlRatio in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message) is given as a percentage of number of PRBs of the associated LTE bandwidth (LTEulchBW). This is the maximum amount of PRBs NR can get. In case of blanking, the LTEblanked PRBs have to be excluded from the LTE bandwidth before calculating the share (see CRM.2049). **Very exact value of maxNrDssRatio is available after DSS coordination phase with LTE. But for time being until dynamic update od sharing rate will be supported, the value as provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message is exact enough (so far operators have configured same share for LTE and NR).**

* LTEulchBW is the amount of LTE PRBs according to the LTE carrier frequency.
* dlBandwidth/ulBandwidth is provided as amount of PRBs, provided by PsCell\_CellSetupReq message.

- prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL and prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL are provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message

- nrLteDssMode is provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message

* see CRM.2049 for sharing rate calculation in case of blanking; (CRM: "Common Resource Management" in DOORS Module RA System General Modules/Common Modules/Applications)
* see CRM.1024: Clarification about PRB numbering; (CRM: "Common Resource Management" in DOORS Module RA System General Modules/Common Modules/Applications)
* 5GC001390: Inter-band DL CA FDD - TDD FR1 SA (Option 2)
* 5GC001167: FDD DL CA up to 3 CCs

-CB006667: Increased number of FDM scheduled UEs per slot

Note:

This feature does not treat subframes 0/5/9 in DSS Ph3 in any special way.

The corresponding PRBs would not be available for other cells.

else If actPRBBlanking is TRUE:

for DL: maxCellPrb = dlBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL - nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL

for UL: maxCellPrb = ulBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL - nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL

Note: prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL are provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message

Note: maxCellPrb is not going to be negative, it is assured by PDL rules of nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL and lteNrDssMode.

endif

---

**3.31.5.4.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11212798`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Max Cell PRB Calculation in TDD

---

**3.31.5.4.0-7.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `12709840`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
If actSpecificBwpSize is TRUE in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message:

for DL: maxCellPrb = cellBwp.bandwidth of DL dedicated BWP in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message. Note: Specific BWP size function does not support multiple dedicated BWPs.

ElseIf actPRBBlanking is TRUE

for UL: maxCellPrb = ulBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL

for DL: maxCellPrb = dlBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL - nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL

Else

for UL: maxCellPrb = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

for DL: maxCellPrb = dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

EndIf

Note: prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL, prbBlanking.nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL are provided in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message

Note: maxCellPrb is not going to be negative, it is assured by PDL rule of nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL

For MU-MIMO enabled in UL (NIDD/actUlMuMimo=TRUE )/DL **(NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh=True)**

If the number of subcells for the cell determined as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15711\_replaced([11212838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDyRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is greater than 1

If PRB Blanking is deactivated (actPRBBlanking=FALSE)

For UL:

IF NRBTS/NRCELL.actDynUlResAlloc='true'

maxCellPrb = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + (numSubcells - 1) ***longPucchNumDynPuschPrb(5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))+* \*[CB012299-A-UPD009] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD009],**\***\*

maxCellPrbPrimarySubCell = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

maxCellPrbSecondarySubCell = longPucchNumDynPuschPrb(5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) +**[CB012299-A-UPD009] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD009]\*\*\*\*

Else

maxCellPrb = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + (numSubcells - 1) *(longPucchNumPuschPrb +**[CB012299-A-UPD006] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]**),***\***

maxCellPrbPrimarySubCell = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

maxCellPrbSecondarySubCell = longPucchNumPuschPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))+**[CB012299-A-UPD006] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]\*\*\*\*

End

where

**[CB012299-A-UPD006]  
- longPucchNumPuschPrb2 is received in cell setup message for the corresponding Bandwidth Part if dedicated BWPs are non-aligned (CB012299) without PRB blanking and   
two contiguous PUSCH regions, separated by PUCCH  are defined in the large BWP,**

otherwise is set 0.

**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]**

For DL: maxCellPrb = numSubcells  \* dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

**Else // PRB Blanking is activated (actPRBBlanking=TRUE)**

For UL:

IF NRBTS/NRCELL.actDynUlResAlloc='true'

maxCellPrb = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) +(numSubcells - 1) **\*longPucchNumDynPuschPrb(5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL - nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL,**

maxCellPrbPrimarySubCell = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL,

maxCellPrbSecondarySubCell = longPucchNumDynPuschPrb(5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Else

maxCellPrb = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + (numSubcells - 1) **\*longPucchNumPuschPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL - nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL,**

maxCellPrbPrimarySubCell = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL - nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL,

maxCellPrbSecondarySubCell = longPucchNumPuschPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

EndIF

For DL:

maxCellPrb = numSubcells \* (dlBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL)

EndIf

else

If PRB Blanking is activated (actPRBBlanking=TRUE)

for UL: maxCellPrb = ulBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeUL – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeUL

for DL: maxCellPrb = dlBandwidth - nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL - nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL

Else // PRB Blanking is deactivated (actPRBBlanking=FALSE)

for UL: maxCellPrb = ulBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

for DL: maxCellPrb = dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

EndIf

end

where,

numSubcells = number of subcells for the cell determined as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15711\_replaced([11212838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDyRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 3.31.5.4.0-8 PRB Pooling Algorithm Determination of Number of Subcells for a given Cell (ID: 11212838)

**3.31.5.4.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `11212856`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
The number of subcells (DL/UL) per cell (per L1 SP) for the calculation of max Cell PRBs described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be calculated as below

DL:

* if nrCellType = 4DLxUL, number of subcells per cell = 1
* if nrCellType = 8DLxUL, number of subcells per cell = 2
* if nrCellType = 16DLxUL,

[CB013288-A]

* if subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (refer 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE
* number of subcells per cell per L1 SP = 2
* else
* number of subcells per cell per L1 SP = 4
* end if

[End CB013288-A]

* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) :

number of subcells per cell = length(currentActiveDlSubcellList) for the cell for the current pooling period described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (the list is calculated in the previous pooling period).

proposedActiveDlSubcellList generated for the next pooling period (described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18304\_replaced([11213877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used instead of currentActiveDlSubcellList if the "number of subcells per cell" is required while performing the Inter L1 subpool reconfiguration described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

UL:

* If TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

Number of active subcells per cell =  len(current/proposedActiveUlSubcellList) for the cell for the corresponding pooling period resulting from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15493\_replaced([11213691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). proposedActiveUlSubcellList shall be used while the re-allocation of resources between L1-subpools (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10384\_replaced([11212979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and currentActiveUlSubcellList shall be used for the PRB allocation for each of cells within L1 subpool (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6787\_replaced([11212320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6788\_replaced([11212354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The rationale is explained in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15493\_replaced([11213691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* If ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) :

number of subcells per cell = length(currentActiveUlSubcellList) for the cell for the current pooling period described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (the list is calculated in the previous pooling period).

proposedActiveUlSubcellList generated for the next pooling period (described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18304\_replaced([11213877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used instead of currentActiveUlSubcellList if the "number of subcells per cell" is required while performing the Inter L1 subpool reconfiguration described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* else:

[Before CB013288-A]

if nrCellType = xDL8UL, number of subcells per cell = 2 , otherwise it is 1

[CB013288-A]

if nrCellType = xDL8UL,

if ulSubcellType = C8

* number of subcells per cell = 1

else

* number of subcells per cell = 2

end if

else

* number of subcells per cell = 1

end if

* end if

[End CB013288-A]
