#### 3.31.5.4.0-9 PRB Pooling Algorithm Large Baseband Pooling (ID: 11212864)

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11212871`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Round Robin Based Pooling Algorithm Overview on Large BB pooling

---

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12444015`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
[Before CNI-136563]

When large BB pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed=TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))=TRUE) and the NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to '''0:round-robin'', this algorithm determines the total amount of usable subcells (numAllocSubcell) that can be granted to a cell out of the total available subcells within 2 L1 pools via round robin fashion.

BBRM manage 2 L1 pools and there has maximum 4 C4 subcells (equal to 16 \* 273 stream-PRBs) in each L1 pool. Considering the actual L1 processing limitation of the subpool given in granularity of stream-PRB, the PRB pooling algorithm compute the allocation usable PRB resource at PRB granularity for each cell. However, in large BB pooling actual allocation to each cell is performed in subcell resolution. Large BB pooling adapts DL PRB pooling algorithm with following changes.

1) BBRM supports round robin pooling algorithm per L1 SP until this function is proceed for all L1 SPs. If there has 2 L1 pools and 4 L1 SPs, BBRM should repeat round-robin pooling algorithm and get the intermediate results per L1 SP. Round robin PRB pooling algorithm is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6787\_replaced([11212320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) In round robin pooling algorithm, per L1 SP the minimum PRB allocation (numMinPRBAlloc) is based on primary subcell for each cell. In case of no primary subcell located in L1 SP, the minimum PRB allocation (numMinPRBAlloc) should be skipped and set to 0.

3) In round robin pooling algorithm, per L1 SP, the maximum PRB allocation (maxCellPrb) shall be limited to 2 C4 (equal to 8 \* bandwidth stream-PRBs) for each cell. Maximum Cell PRB (maxCellPrb) calculation (per L1 SP) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

4) In round robin pooling algorithm, per L1 SP, the allocated usable stream-PRB (numAllocStreamPrb) shall convert to the amount of subcell. Conversion between stream-PRB and subcell calculation (per L1 SP) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5) In round robin pooling algorithm, the total allocated usable subcells of one cell shall be sum of allocated usable subcells of one cell per L1 SP of all L1 SPs.

[CNI-136563]

Round robin algorithm will not be supported since CNI-136563

[End CNI-136563]

---

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11212881`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Load Metric Based Pooling Algorithm Overview on Large BB pooling

---

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11212894`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
When large BB pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed=TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))=TRUE) and the NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to ''1:load-metric'', this algorithm determines the total amount of usable subcells (numAllocSubcell) that can be granted to a cell out of the total available subcells within 2 L1 pools via load-metric fashion.

1) BBRM supports load metric pooling algorithm per L1 SP until this function is proceed for all L1 SPs. If there has 2 L1 pools and 4 L1 SPs, BBRM should repeat load-metric pooling algorithm and get the intermediate results per L1 SP. Load metric PRB pooling algorithm is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13411\_replaced([11212398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) In load metric pooling algorithm, per L1 SP the minimum PRB allocation (numMinPRBAlloc) is based on primary subcell for each cell. In case of no primary subcell located in L1 SP, the minimum PRB allocation (numMinPRBAlloc) should be skipped and set to 0. "Allocation of the configured minimum resource per Cell" is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13342\_replaced([11212500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxB9EPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and "Minimum Resource Reservation Per L1 Subpool" is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10411\_replaced([11213042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

3) In load metric pooling algorithm, per L1 SP, the maximum PRB allocation (maxCellPrb) shall be limited to 2 C4 (equal to 8 \* bandwidth stream-PRBs) for each cell. Maximum Cell PRB (maxCellPrb) calculation (per L1 SP) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

4) In load metric pooling algorithm, per L1 SP, the allocated usable stream-PRB (numAllocStreamPrb) shall convert to the amount of subcell. Conversion between stream-PRB and subcell calculation (per L1 SP) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5) In load metric pooling algorithm, the total allocated usable subcells of one cell shall be sum of allocated usable subcells of one cell per L1 SP of all L1 SPs.

6)   In load metric pooling algorithm, inter-L1 subpool reconfiguration shall also be adapted to subcell resolution, i.e., the proposed subpool capacity shall be stream PRBs which is times of integer number of subcell, which is compliant to subcell resolution. "New Subpool Capacity Computation for InterL1 Subpool Reconfiguration" is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[CB010713-A]**

7)   Introduce freeSubcellWeightPerCell(i) per cell which is used to balance remaining subcell allocation between L1 pools/subpools, this parameter shall be initialized as 1.0 per pooling period, it is global parameter in PRB pooling algorithm through all L1 pools/subpools.

Introduce rdSubcellWeight as R&D parameter, which is defined for the remaining subcell weight calculation.

freeSubcellWeightPerCell(i) = 1.0

rdSubcellWeight = 0.5

**[End CB010713-A]**

---

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-3**  (ID: `11212900`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Conversion between Stream PRB and Subcell

---

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11212914`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is TRUE and subcellDeactivationAllowed is TRUE), DL PRB pooling use subcell resolution which means BBRM allocates usable PRB resources to L2-PS with the granularity of subcell.

Considering the actual L1 processing limitation of the subpool given in granularity of stream-PRB, a conversion is required from the allocated usable stream-PRBs to the equivalent subcell per cell per L1 subpool, following steps computation are defined as below.

Step 1) Calculation numSubcellStreamPrb(i) for cell (i) shall be done as follows:

* numSubcellPrb(i) [Before CB009915-B] = dlBandwidth(i) [CB009915-B] is defined as

If actPRBBlanking is TRUE

numSubcellPrb(i) = dlBandwidth(i) – nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL(i) – nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL(i)

Else

numSubcellPrb(i) = dlBandwidth(i)

EndIf [End CB009915-B]

* numSubcellStreamPrb(i) = numSubcellPrb(i) \* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb(i)

where:

* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb is 4 for a subcell type C4 and 2 for a subcell type C2 for DL;
* dlBandwidth(i) for cell i refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if actSpecificBwpSize is false or cellBwp.bandwidth of DL dedicated BWP in PsCell\_CellSetupReq message (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1835\_replaced([11111009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJzcPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if actSpecificBwpSize is true.

Step 2) Conversion from stream PRB to Subcell for cell (i) shall be done as follows:

numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) = rounddown (numAllocStreamPrb(i) / numSubcellStreamPrb(i))

 If the primary subcell of cell i is located in the L1 SP and numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) = 0 then

numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i) =1

Where: numAllocStreamPrb is number of stream PRB allocated to a cell(5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Step 3) Allocation remaining subcell to each cell per L1 SP, get new value of numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i), refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15549\_replaced([11212922](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: step 3) is only required for "load-based" pooling algorithm (the NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to ''1:load-metric')

---

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-4**  (ID: `11212922`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation remaining subcell to each cell

---

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11212933`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE) and it is for DL only, the rounddown of numAllocCellPrb for cell i to subcell unit (an integer value) and the distribution of possible remaining resources shall happen in the following way:

- RsubcellInit(i) = numAllocSubcellPerL1Sp(i), refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- BBRM calculates the amount of remaining stream PRBs per L1 SP which can be distributed:

[Before PR755635]

remainingStreamPrbL1Sp = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp - sum{[all cells i=k in same L1 SP]( RsubcellInit(i) \* numSubcellStreamPrb(i)}

[PR755635]

remainingStreamPrbL1Sp = maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp

For all cells i (i =0, 1..k active cells in L1SP)

If numAllocStreamPrb(i) <= numSubcellStreamPrb(i) and the primary subcell of cell i is in the L1 SP

remainingStreamPrbL1Sp = remainingStreamPrbL1Sp - numAllocStreamPrb(i)

Else

remainingStreamPrbL1Sp = remainingStreamPrbL1Sp - RsubcellInit(i) \* numSubcellStreamPrb(i)

End If

[End PR755635]

where:

* maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp represent the maximum stream PRBs capacity per L1 SP, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numSubcellStreamPrb(i) represent the maximum stream PRBs capacity per subcell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh = FALSE

- The cells selected to get the remaining stream PRBs are those for which either the reported LoadGBR,x > 0 or the reported LoadnonGBR,x > 0. This is what we call ‘set of candidate cells’.

Else

-     All cells per L1 SP should be selected to get the remaining stream PRBs.

[Before PR755635] If (remainingStreamPrbL1Sp < numSubcellStreamPrb(i)) or (RsubcellInit(i) = N) for cell i (i =0, 1... active cells in L1SP), where: N is the maximum number of subcells for cell i per L1 SP determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15711\_replaced([11212838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDyRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the following steps are skipped.

- The cells selected to get the remaining stream PRBs are those for which the reported LoadnonGBR,x > 0. This is what we call ‘set of candidate cells’. [End PR755635]

In the following description the parameter numCandidateCells represents the amount of candidate cells. If numCandidateCells = 0, then all the cells are considered as candidate to get additional resources: numCandidateCells = ‘number of active cells per L1 SP handled by BBRM’.

- [Before CB010713-A]

For those candidate cells the fractional part is calculated: RsubcellDec(i) = max { (numAllocStreamCellPrb(i) / numSubcellStreamPrb(i) - RsubcellInit(i)) , 0}

[CB010713-A]

For those candidate cells the fractional part is calculated: RsubcellDec(i) = max { (numAllocStreamCellPrb(i) / numSubcellStreamPrb(i) - RsubcellInit(i)) \* freeSubcellWeightPerCell(i) , 0}

[End CB010713-A]

* the candidate cells are sorted by decreasing RsubcellDec(i);
* BBRM selects each candidate cell according to the sorted order and gives it the remaining stream PRBs, until the remaining stream PRB are allocated to candidate cells or the maximum subcell of the cell is reached.

If (remainingStreamPrbL1Sp >= numSubcellStreamPrb(i) and RsubcellInit(i) < N)  for cell i

remainingSubcellL1Sp = rounddown (remainingStreamPrbL1Sp / numSubcellStreamPrb(i))

additionalRsubcell(i) = min (remainingSubcellL1Sp, N - RsubcellInit(i) );

Rsubcell(i) = RsubcellInit(i) + additionalRsubcell(i)

numAllocStreamPrb(i) = Rsubcell(i) \* numSubcellStreamPrb(i)

remainingStreamPrbL1Sp = remaingStreamPrbL1Sp - (additionalRsubcell(i) \* numSubcellStreamPrb(i))

[CB010713-A]

freeSubcellWeightPerCell(i) = freeSubcellWeightPerCell(i) \* rdSubcellWeight

[End CB010713-A]

[PR755635]

Else If (remainingStreamPrbL1Sp < numSubcellStreamPrb(i)), then

numAllocStreamPrbDiff(i) = numSubcellStreamPrb(i) - numAllocStreamPrb(i)

If numAllocStreamPrbDiff(i) >= 0 and the primary subcell of cell i is in the L1 SP

If remainingStreamPrbL1Sp > numAllocStreamPrbDiff(i)

numAllocStreamPrb(i) = numSubcellStreamPrb(i)

remainingStreamPrbL1Sp = (remainingStreamPrbL1Sp - numAllocStreamPrbDiff(i))

Else

numAllocStreamPrb(i) = numAllocStreamPrb(i) + remainingStreamPrbL1Sp

remainingStreamPrbL1Sp = 0

End If

Else if numAllocStreamPrbDiff(i) < 0

numAllocStreamPrb(i) = Rsubcell(i) \* numSubcellStreamPrb(i)

End If

[End PR755635]

End If

Where: N is the maximum number of subcells for cell i per L1 SP determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15711\_replaced([11212838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDyRvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB010713-A]

freeSubcellWeightPerCell(i) is initialized per pooling period, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15387\_replaced([11212881](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDyTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdSubcellWeight is defined for remaining subcell weight calculation, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15387\_replaced([11212881](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDyTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB010713-A]

End For

---

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-5**  (ID: `11212940`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
Allocation remaining subcell to each L1 Subpool

---

**3.31.5.4.0-9.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11212961`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE) and it is for DL only, allocate remaining subcell to subpools, until no subcell unallocated.

For i=0,1... totalNumOfSubPoolsInPool – 1

* newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i) = rounddown (newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i) / maxStreamPrbPerSubcell)

If the primary subcell of cell is located in the L1 SP i and newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i) <= 1

If newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i) > maxStreamPrbPerSubcell

newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i) = total number of primary subcells in L1 SP i

Else

newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i) = 1

End If

End If

End For

where:

* maxStreamPrbPerSubcell = numSubcellStreamPrb(j) for cell j which has largest cell bandwidth in L1 Pool
* numSubcellStreamPrb(j) for cell j represents the maximum stream PRBs capacity per subcell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

remainingSubcellPerPool = {rounddown (poolMaxNumStreamPrb / maxStreamPrbPerSubcell) - sum [all Sp k] {newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp (k)}

If remainingSubcellPerPool <= 0, the following steps are skipped.

[Before PR778254]

For those candidate L1 SPs the fractional part is calculated:

For i=0,1... totalNumOfSubPoolsInPool – 1

subcellPerSPDec(i) = {max (newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i) / maxStreamPrbPerSubcell - newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i)), 0}

End For

The candidate L1 SPs are sorted by decreasing subcellPerSPDec(i), BBRM selects each candidate L1 SPs according to the decreasing order and gives it the remaining subcells, until the remaining subcells are allocated to L1 SPs (no subcells unallocated).

For the candidate L1 SPs sorted by decreasing subcellPerSPDec(i),

If (remainingSubcellPerPool > 0)

newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i) ++

remainingSubcellPerPool --

End If

End For

[PR778254]

For those candidate L1 SPs, a sorting metric based on the allocated Stream PRBs from Inter L1 SP Pooling is calculated as :

For i=0,1... totalNumOfSubPoolsInPool – 1

* subcellPerSPDec(i) = {max (newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i) / (totalStreamPrbGbrDemandPerSp(i) + totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(i))), 0}

End For

The candidate L1 subpools 'i' are sorted in the increasing order of subcellPerSPDec(i). The remaining subcells are allocated to the subpools as below :

For each subpool 'i' from the sorted list of subpools

If remainingSubcellPerPool <= 0

* stop further processing for all remaining candidate subpools

End If

* Get the list of cells that are allocated to subpool 'i' //Select all cells including the ones which have only secondary subcells in the subpool 'i'
* maxRequiredSubcells(i) = 0

For each cell 'j' from the list of cells

If ((prbDemandGbr(j) + prbDemandNonGbr(j)) / dlBandwidth(j)) <= 1 AND cell 'j' has its primary subcell configured in subpool 'i'

* maxRequiredSubcells(i) = maxRequiredSubcells(i) + 1

Else

* maxRequiredSubcells(i) = maxRequiredSubcells(i) + min {floor((prbDemandGbr(j) + prbDemandNonGbr(j)) / dlBandwidth(j)), [Before PR795303] Number of subcells configured for cell 'j' in subpool 'i' [PR795303] Number of subcells proposed for cell 'j' in subpool 'i'  [End PR795303]}

End If

End For

* maxRequiredSubcells(i) = min{maxRequiredSubcells(i), length(proposedActiveDlSubcellList(i))}

If (newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i) >= maxRequiredSubcells(i))

* Continue to next subpool

End If

* newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i) = newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i) + 1
* remainingSubcellPerPool = remainingSubcellPerPool - 1

End For

If remainingSubcellPerPool > 0

Allocate the remaining subcells to each subpool 'i' in the ordered list of subpools starting from the last subpool until the proposed number of active DL subcells for the subpool (refer Note 1 below) is reached before allocating to the next subpool

End If

where,

* newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp(i) is the allocated stream PRBs to the subpool 'i' during Inter L1 subpool pooling (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* totalStreamPrbGbrDemandPerSp(i) is the GBR stream PRB demand of the subpool 'i' (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(i) is the Non-GBR stream PRB demand of the subpool 'i' (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* prbDemandGbr(j) is the GBR PRB demand for the cell 'j' used as an input to the intra L1 subpool pooling algorithm (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* prbDemandNonGbr(j) is the Non-GBR PRB demand for the cell 'j' used as an input to the intra L1 subpool pooling algorithm (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* dlBandwidth(j) is the number of PRBs in DL for cell 'j' (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* length(proposedActiveDlSubcellList(i)) is the number of active subcells proposed for the subpool 'i' based on the subcell deactivation procedures (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18900\_replaced([11213883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

// Note 1: in case subcell deactivation procedures are not activated, proposedActiveDlSubcellList(i) = sum[all cells 'j' configured in subpool 'i']{Number of subcells configured for cell 'j' in subpool 'i'}

[End PR778254]

Note: Current algorithm has risk of wasting subcell resource in case of mixing cell bandwidth in same L1 pool. This algorithm will be improved by CB010713 which supports PRB granularity of PRB pooling for primary subcell and subcell granularity of PRB pooling for secondary subcells.

---

#### 3.31.5.4.0-10 PRB Pooling Algorithm PRB Allocation Capacity Limit for A cell Based on Secondary Subcell Utilization (ID: 11212968)

**3.31.5.4.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11212972`)

PRB Pooling Algorithm
This section defines the PRB allocation limit per a cell considering secondary subcell utilization reported by L2PS as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26873\_replaced([11212218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). This allocation limit is to be used during the nonGBR based PRB allocaiton to a cell and it is defined as capacity of primary subcell plus portion of the secondary subcell capacity estimated to be utilized in the previous pooling period and additional mimum margin capacity:

* allocPrbNonGbrLimitCell = floor(min{ maxCellPrb,  maxCellPrbPrimarySubCell + (secondarySubcellPrbUtilizationFactor*(1 - rdMinSecondarSubcellCapacityMargin) + rdMinSecondarSubcellCapacityMargin )* maxCellPrbSecondarySubCell  })
* allocStreamPrbNonGbrLimitCell is stream PRB equivalent of allocPrbNonGbrLimitCell converted as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Where:
* maxCellPrb described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxCellPrbPrimarySubCell : the max number of cell PRB capacity of primary subcell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* rdMinSecondarSubcellCapacityMargin : the portion of the secondary subcell capacity, in fraction, to be considered for resource distribution described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26912\_replaced([11209530](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw0hsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),( default value = 0.1).
* maxCellPrbSecondarySubCell: the max number of PRB capacity of secondary subcell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* This section is applicable for FR1-TDD UL only

---

### 3.31.5.5 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools

#### 3.31.5.5.0-1 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools InterL1 Subpool PRB pooling (ID: 11212985)

**3.31.5.5.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `12574859`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
-With interL1 subpool PRB pooling, part or all of the PRB processing capacity (stream/layer PRB resources) of subpool(s) can be shifted between the subpool(s) mapped to same L1pool (l1 instance) enabling a redistribution of capacities where there is a need of additional capacity. Such re-allocation of resources between subpools is carried out by the BBRM in non-realtime or slow pooling fashion (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and targeting to address the imbalance of load and availability of unused resources within the subpools (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10387\_replaced([11213171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFnhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

-With interL1 subpool PRB pooling if dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed **= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** or ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and in case of TDD, BBRM shall also consider deactivating a certain number of subcells from any of the subpools of a L1 Pool based on required loads of the cells in the L1 pool as long as the maximum subcell capacities of the L1 Pool/subpool mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6539\_replaced([11212289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are exceeded. The list of activated subcells shall be used in the Inter L1 Subpool Pooling algorithm of the corresponding pooling period to define the max Stream PRB capacities of each subpool.\*\*\*\*

-The output of the L1 ARM capacity subcell deactivation procedure shall be used in the next pooling period while performing the PRB Pooling distribution with Intra-L1SubPool Pooling for TDD.

* Once BBRM decides new resource(PRB) allocation per each subpool, the subpool capacity update is carried out via subpool resource reconfiguration and synchronization procedure as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* The interL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality is enabled/disabled [Before CNI-137616-B] via an R&D flag rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddUl (5G\_L2\_6312\_replaced([11188119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for TDD in UL or rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddDl (5G\_L2\_7674\_replaced([11188131](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ6PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for TDD in DL or rdAllowInterL1SpPoolingFdd (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19197\_replaced([11215293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in FDD DL/UL.In addition to R&D flags activation, to enable interL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality for a given L1 pool, [End CNI-137616-B] when there shall be more than one L1 subpool per L1 pool. InterL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality activation shall be at L1 pool level, meaning in one L2 pool we can have L1 pool with several L1 SP with interL1 subpool PRB pooling is activated and L1 pool with only one L1SP where interL1 subpool PRB pooling is not activated.

---

#### 3.31.5.5.0-2 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools Initialization of InterL1 Subpool PRB pooling and Parameter Definitions (ID: 11213021)

**3.31.5.5.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11213038`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
-At system startup, BBRM shall learn the subpool list within the L1 pool and initializes the subpool capacity in UL/DL with a configured per subpool capacity value given by the NIDD described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6539\_replaced([11212289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). This NIDD given initial UL/DL subpool capacity is considered as default subpool capacity and corresponding stream/layer PRB capacities are referred by defaultStreamPrbCapacityPerSp/ defaultLayerPrbCapacityPerSp, respectively.

-[Before PR714295] With interL1 subpool PRB pooling, rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddUl  set to '1'(5G\_L2\_6312\_replaced([11188119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddDl (5G\_L2\_7674\_replaced([11188131](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ6PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) set to '1' [PR714295] With interL1 subpool PRB pooling functionality enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10386\_replaced([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End PR714295], the subpool capacity may change from one pooling period to another due to the pooling decisions and re-allocation of resources between the subpools. Thus, the actual Stream/Layer PRB capacities of a subpool at any given pooling period is given by currentStreamPrbCapacityPerL1Sp/ currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp, respectively.

* Therefore, at the BBRM startup (first pooling period),
* currentStreamPrbCapacityPerSp = defaultStreamPrbCapacityPerSp.
* currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp    = defaultLayerPrbCapacityPerSp.
* The maximum amount of stream/layer PRBs available on the L1 Pool level is equal to the sum of the stream/layer PRB capacities of all subpools within the L1 pool
* poolMaxNumStreamPrb = sum[ all subpool per pool]{defaultStreamPrbCapacityPerSp}
* poolMaxNumLayerPrb    = sum[ all subpool per pool]{defaultLayerPrbCapacityPerSp}
* With interL1 subpool PRB pooling, the BBRM decides to reallocate resources between the different subpools in a pool at run time and sends reconfiguration request to L1 to apply the new subpool capacities (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The corresponding destination address of the L1 pool of the subpools for which the reconfiguration request it to be sent from BBRM shall be negotiated and provided by L1 during the pooling initialization phase. Thus, BBRM sends resource reconfiguration pool address request to L1 when the cell setup request is received for a cell mapped to one of the UL/DL subpool of the pool. In the response, L1 provides the destination pool address to be used later when subpools capacity reconfiguration is to be requested.

---

#### 3.31.5.5.0-3 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools Minimum Resource Reservation Per L1 Subpool (ID: 11213042)

**3.31.5.5.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11213076`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
[CB008224-D] In case of a Cell is an SDL cell (which has no uplink), gNB-DU shouldn't reserve any UL PRB for the SDL cell. Otherwise,[End CB008224-D] The minimum amount of Stream/Layer PRB that shall always be reserved in UL/DL per subpool is given by minStreamPrbCapacityPerSp/ minLayerPrbCapacityPerSp, respectively and the value is equal to the total Stream/Layer PRB equivalent amount of the minimum PRBs (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of all cells within the subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6850\_replaced([11212236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to TRUE the minimum resource allocation needs to be provided by the primary subcell for each cell.

While calculating minStreamPrbCapacityPerSp, the total stream PRB equivalent of the minimum PRBs for each cell shall be multiplied by the streamToLayerScaleFactor for the cell

If primary subcell of cell i is located in the L1subpool then

stream PRB equivalent of min PRB for cell(i) is equal to amount of the minimum PRBs (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

else

stream PRB equivalent of min PRB for cell(i) is equal to 0

End

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true,

minStreamPrbCapacityPerSp = sum[for all cells i in the subpool]{max("stream PRB equivalent of min PRB for cell(i)" \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i), maxStreamPrbForRimRs(i)(5G\_UP\_ALG\_22610\_replaced([11213161](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFnfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))))\* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}

Else

minStreamPrbCapacityPerSp = sum[for all cells i in the subpool]{"stream PRB equivalent of min PRB for cell(i)" \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}

End If

where, streamToLayerScaleFactor(i) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the minimum amount of Stream/Layer PRBs in DL shall be reserved for a cell only if :

* the result of the subcell deactivation procedure in DL for the next pooling period (5G\_UP\_ALG\_18304\_replaced([11213877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), provides at least 1 active DL subcell for the cell in the pool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_18326\_replaced([11214008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND
* the cell has its primary DL subcell in the L1 pool.

---

#### 3.31.5.5.0-4 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools Maximum Potential Resource Per L1 Subpool (ID: 11213083)

**3.31.5.5.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `11213107`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
- The maximum number of PRBs (cells/streams/layers) that can be used by each cell within the subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6850\_replaced([11212236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is restricted by the BWs of each cell. Thus, the maximum amount of PRB resource (cells/streams/layers) per subpool is the sum of the maximum capacities of all cells within the subpool.

* Maximum stream PRB per subpool (maxSpStreamPrb) is defined as the sum of the potential maximum number of stream PRBs (equivalent stream PRB of cell BW PRBs) that can be used by each cells within the subpool multiplied by the streamToLayerScaleFactor for the cell as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

maxSpStreamPrb = sum[for all cells i within subpool]{"potential max number of stream PRBs (equivalent stream PRB of cell BW PRBs) that can be used by cell(i)" \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}

where, streamToLayerScaleFactor(i) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

When TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in UL, the maximum number of PRBs that can be used by the cell is further limited by the subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15396\_replaced([11213669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Only the active subcells proposed by subcell deactivation mechanism for the cell i for the next pooling period, namely proposedActiveUlSubcellList(i), shall be considered for the calculation of maximum number of PRBs that can be used by the cell. For details, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) , 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15493\_replaced([11213691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB009890-A]

If  dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB009890-B] or ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB009890-B], the calculation for the maximum number of PRBs for a cell shall consider only the list of active subcells proposed at the end of the L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure for the cell 'i' for the next pooling period. The procedure is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18304\_replaced([11213877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The list of proposed active subcells for a cell is given by proposedActiveDlSubcellList(i) [CB009890-B] in DL & proposedActiveUlSubcellList(i) in UL [End CB009890-B] described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18326\_replaced([11214008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB009890-A]

---

#### 3.31.5.5.0-5 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools Total L1 Capacity Demand per SubPool (ID: 11213111)

**3.31.5.5.0-5.0-7**  (ID: `11213155`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
At the beginning of every pooling period, the BBRM computes the total amount of stream PRB demands per subpool for all subpools mapped to the same L1 pool based on the load metrics received from the L2PS of each active cells within the subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6788\_replaced([11212354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The load metric from each cell received by the BBRM provides the amount of PRB demands for GBR and nonGBR traffics of the cell.

When large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE) and it is for DL only,

if active cell amount N > 3 and primary subcell of cell i is **not located in the L1subpool and {(**[CB008600-F]streamPrbDemandDcGbr + **[End CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandGbr (i) + streamPrbDemandNonGbr (i)) < numSubcellStreamPrb(i) for cell i }, then**\*\*\*\*

The cell i is **not in the list in the corresponding L1 subpool and the cell i should** not be considered in below procedure, and set\*\*\*\*

**[CB008600-F]streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i) within Sp = 0**[End CB008600-F]\*\*\*\*

streamPrbDemandGbr(i) within Sp = 0

streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i) within Sp = 0

Else

below procedure shall be considered and executed

End If

Where numSubcellStreamPrb(i) represent the maximum stream PRBs capacity per subcell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Where active cells shall be configured and located in same BB board.

For UL FR1 TDD  slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = TRUE, L2PS of Cells with RIM activated (NRCELL/actNrRim=3) also provides additinal PRB demand for RIM to the BBRM (prbDemandRim, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

L2PS of Cells with Configured Grant activated, i.e.  NRBTS/NRCELL.actUlCgType2 set to True, provide additional PRBs demand for Configured Grant reservation to BBRM (prbDemandCg, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), Thus, BBRM maintains the total capacity demand for each subpool as total demand per subpool for GBR and nonGBR services separately as:

* totalStreamPrbCgDemandPerSp = sum[for all cells i within Sp]{streamPrbDemandCg(i) \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}
* **[CB008600-F] totalStreamPrbDcGbrDemandPerSp = sum[for all cells i within Sp]{streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i) \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}**[End CB008600-F]\*\*\*\*
* totalStreamPrbGbrDemandPerSp = sum[for all cells i within Sp]{streamPrbDemandGbr(i) \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}
* totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp = sum[for all cells i within Sp]{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i) \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}
* totalStreamPrbRimDemandPerSp = sum[for all cells i within Sp]{streamPrbDemandRim(i) \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}

where, streamToLayerScaleFactor(i) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* The sum of the PRB demands (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6504\_replaced([11212051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the minimum PRBs (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) indicated by each cell within a SP (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6504\_replaced([11212051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) may exceed the maximum PRB available in cell BW (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Thus, the maximum PRB demand per SP that may receive an allocation from the BBRM, when possible, shall be limited takng this restriction into account and defined (in equivalent stream PRB) as:
* maxStreamPrbCgAllocLimitSp =  sum[all cell i in Sp] {min{streamPrbDemandCg (i), maxCellStreamPrb(i) – numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i)} \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}
* **[CB008600-F]**
* If actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is false (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

**maxStreamPrbDcGbrAllocLimitSp =  sum[all cell i in Sp] {min{streamPrbDemandDcGbr (i), max{0, maxCellStreamPrb(i) – numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i)** - streamPrbDemandCg}} \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}\*\*\*\*

Else

maxStreamPrbDcGbrAllocLimitSp =  sum[all cell i in Sp] {min{streamPrbDemandDcGbr (i), max{0, maxCellStreamPrbForGbr(i) – numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) **- streamPrbDemandCg}} \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}**

* End If
* **[End CB008600-F]**
* If actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is false (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

**maxStreamPrbGbrAllocLimitSp =  sum[all cell i in Sp] {min{streamPrbDemandGbr (i), max{0, maxCellStreamPrb(i) – numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i)** - streamPrbDemandCg**[CB008600-F] - streamPrbDemandDcGbr**[End CB008600-F]}} \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}***\****\*

Else

maxStreamPrbGbrAllocLimitSp =  sum[all cell i in Sp] {min{streamPrbDemandGbr (i), max{0, maxCellStreamPrbForGbr(i) – numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) **- streamPrbDemandCg**[CB008600-F] - streamPrbDemandDcGbr**[End CB008600-F]}} \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}**\*\*\*\*

End If

**If NRBTS.deactEnhPrbPoolAlgoUlMuMimo is False and if at least one cell of a subpool has more than one subcells** & for FR1-TDD UL Only\*\*\*\*

* maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp = sum[all cell i in Sp] {min{~~allocStreamPrbNonGbrLimitCell~~streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), max{0,~~maxCellStreamPrb~~allocStreamPrbNonGbrLimitCell(i)- numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) – streamPrbDemandGbr(i) **- streamPrbDemandCg**[CB008600-F] - streamPrbDemandDcGbr**[End CB008600-F]}} \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}**\*\*\*\*
* where,
* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* allocStreamPrbNonGbrLimitCell defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26875\_replaced([11212968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Else**

* maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp = sum[all cell i in Sp] {min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), max{0,maxCellStreamPrb(i)- numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) – streamPrbDemandGbr(i) **- streamPrbDemandCg**[CB008600-F] - streamPrbDemandDcGbr**[End CB008600-F]}} \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)}**\*\*\*\*

where, streamToLayerScaleFactor(i) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**End**

-For synchronized reconfiguration of resources across the subpools (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the time at which the cell load metric indication is received by the BBRM across all subpools (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6504\_replaced([11212051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5xvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in a pool shall aligned.

---

#### 3.31.5.5.0-6 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools Max Stream PRB for RIM-RS in a Cell (ID: 11213161)

**3.31.5.5.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11213165`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
Max stream PRBs used by RIM-RS transmission in a cell depends on the configuration in a cell, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12970\_replaced([11101094](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knUAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13003\_replaced([11101155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knUnd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13006\_replaced([11101164](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knUnevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

maxStreamPrbForRimRs = 0

If (actBeamforming is true) or (actBeamforming is false and dlMimoMode is "ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_2x2 or OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_2x2" (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))),

If dlBandwidth >10MHz and dlBandwidth < 40MHz,

maxStreamPrbForRimRs = 48\*2=96 stream PRBs

Else If dlBandwidth >=40MHz,

maxStreamPrbForRimRs = 96\*2=192 stream PRBs

End If

Else If actBeamforming is false and dlMiMoMode is "ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_4x4 or OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_4x4" (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

If dlBandwidth >10MHz and dlBandwidth < 40MHz,

maxStreamPrbForRimRs = 48\*4=192 stream PRBs

Else If dlBandwidth >=40MHz,

maxStreamPrbForRimRs = 96\*4=384 stream PRBs

End If

End If

Note: actBeamforming, dlMimoMode and dlBandwidth are from PsCell\_CellSetupReq message (5G\_L2\_IF\_73\_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 3.31.5.5.0-7 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools InterL1 Subpool Capacity Reconfiguration Decision (ID: 11213171)

**3.31.5.5.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11213182`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
- The BBRM triggers reconfiguration of subpool capacity in UL[CB008940-G]/DL[End CB008940-G] in order to allow the total pool capacity re-distribution across the subpools to address the need of additional capacity and to better redistribute the pool capacity following resource imbalance between the subpools.

* The subpool capacity reconfiguration is to be done periodically and the BBRM triggers the reconfiguration procedure every pooling period as indicated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB007112-B-UPD001]

* When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE, there are total two L1 pools and two L1 subpools per L1 pool on full BB board (in one L2-RT instance). BBRM shall manage subpool capacity reconfiguration independently for two L1 pools, no interaction between two L1 pools.

[End CB007112-B-UPD001]

---

#### 3.31.5.5.0-8 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools Synchronization Between L1 and L2 for Subpool Capacity Reconfiguration (ID: 11213186)

**3.31.5.5.0-8.0-4**  (ID: `11213236`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
11213236:
Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
Once BBRM decides for the reconfiguration of subpool capacity(5G\_UP\_ALG\_10387\_replaced([11213171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFnhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), it sends out a reconfiguration request message, UlPool\_BbResourceReconfReq in UL or DlPool\_BbResourceReconfReq in DL, to L1 as depicted in Figure 1 below. The reconfiguration request is sent during the same SFN the new allocation proposal is computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ( i.e. the second SFN of the pooling window) and this request message includes:

* the new reconfiguration capacity proposed for each subpool in the L1 pool: proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp/proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp(5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* explicit indication of the time when the new subpool capacity shall be reconfigured and applied at L1, which is second SFN of the next pooling window.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a flowchart illustrating inter and intra L1 subpool PRB pooling and subpool capacity reconfiguration procedures, specifically considering subcell deactivation. The flowchart is organized by SFN (System Frame Number) and pooling intervals.
The top row indicates SFN values from N to N+15. Below this, pooling intervals are shown, with `poolingInterval(n)` spanning from SFN N to N+5, `poolingInterval(n+1)` from N+6 to N+11, and `poolingInterval(n+2)` from N+12 to N+15.
The main body of the flowchart depicts various procedures and their timing. Key elements include:
\* **XXPool\_BbResourceReconfReq**: A request message with parameters like SP Capacity, proposed stream PRB capacity per SP, and proposed layer PRB capacity per SP. It is marked to be applied at SFN=N+6.
\* **XXPool\_BbResourceReconfResp**: A response message indicating success (0) or failure (1).
\* **update:SP capacity**: An action to update SP capacity.
\* **newCap(#1), newCap(#2)**: These represent new capacity allocations.
\* **SubcellDeact(#1), SubcellDeact(#2), SubcellDeact(#3)**: These indicate subcell deactivation events.
\* **Num Active Subcells**: This likely represents the count of active subcells.
\* **InterL1Sp (#1), InterL1Sp(#2), InterL1Sp(#3)**: These denote inter L1 subpool operations.
\* **IntraL1Sp**: This denotes intra L1 subpool operations.
The bottom section of the flowchart shows the actions for three cells: Cell#1(L2PS), Cell#2(L2PS), and Cell#3(L2PS). Each cell is shown to `apply newAlloc` at different points in time, aligning with the pooling intervals.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  | [/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_17035.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

-Note: SubcellDeact represents all the subcell deactivation procedures that are executed before the Inter-L1 Subpool Pooling Procedure for the next Pooling Interval ( i.e. the second SFN of the pooling window as mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). These include :

* UL subcell deactivation procedure to support cells which do not support PRB muting explained in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15396\_replaced([11213669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It is applicable only in UL and when TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed is set to TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* L1 ARM capacity based Subcell Deactivation Procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18304\_replaced([11213877](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It is applicable if dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in DL and ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in UL.

-Note: XXPool\_BbResourceReconfReq/XXPool\_BbResourceReconfResp: represents DL/ULPool\_BbResourceReconfReq or DL/ULPool\_BbResourceReconfResp messages and shall refer to the corresponding resource reconfiguration request/response messages used for DL/UL PRB pooling, respectively.

* The decision of reconfiguration by the BBRM and applying of the new subpool capacity by L1 is done in a separate pooling window due to the time needed by L1 to synchronize and reconfigure a new subpool capacity. Moreover, it is also required that the SFN at which L2PS of cells in a subpool starts to use the new PRB allocation received from the BBRM ( 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6959\_replaced([11213357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxG1mfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the SFN at which new capacity reconfiguration is done by L1, shall be aligned.
* After UlPool\_BbResourceReconfReq/DlPool\_BbResourceReconfReq is sent, BBRM expects to receive response (UlPool\_BbResourceReconfResp/DlPool\_BbResourceReconfResp) from L1 before the end of the same pooling window, in which request was sent, about the status of the reconfiguration request, in UL/DL. Thus
* if received response status is 'success' (0):
* BBRM updates currentStreamPrbCapacityPerSp/currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp with the proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp/proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp values(5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) agreed with L1.
* If TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in UL, BBRM updates currentActiveUlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool with the proposedActiveUlSubcellList. The rationale is described in  5G\_UP\_ALG\_15493\_replaced([11213691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DL, BBRM updates currentActiveDlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool with the proposedActiveDlSubcellList.
* If ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in UL, BBRM updates currentActiveUlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool with the proposedActiveUlSubcellList.
* if received response status is 'failure' (1):
* BBRM keeps  currentStreamPrbCapacityPerSp/currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp unchanged.
* If TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in UL, BBRM keeps the currentActiveUlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool unchanged. The rationale is described in  5G\_UP\_ALG\_15493\_replaced([11213691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DL, BBRM keeps the currentActiveDlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool unchanged.
* If ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in UL, BBRM keeps the currentActiveUlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool unchanged.
* If UlPool\_BbResourceReconfResp for UL or DlPool\_BbResourceReconfResp for DL, is not received by the BBRM at all, it is uncertain about the reconfiguration attempt by L1, hence, BBRM shall take the minimum of subpool capacities between the new proposed allocation and the current allocation, i.e.
* currentStreamPrbCapacityPerSp = min{currentStreamPrbCapacityPerSp, proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp};
* currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp    = min{currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp , proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp};
* If TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE, in UL, currentActiveUlSubcellList = intersection{currentActiveUlSubcellList, proposedActiveUlSubcellList} for each of the cells in L1 pool. The rationale is described in  5G\_UP\_ALG\_15493\_replaced([11213691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DL, currentActiveDlSubcellList = intersection{currentActiveDlSubcellList, proposedActiveDlSubcellList} for each of the cells in L1 pool.
* If ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in UL, currentActiveUlSubcellList = intersection{currentActiveUlSubcellList, proposedActiveUlSubcellList} for each of the cells in L1 pool.
* Once reconfiguration is done, the new subpool capacity value (currentStreamPrbCapacityPerSp/currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp) will be used by the intra-subpool PRB pooling algorithm computation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6788\_replaced([11212354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) carried out in the next pooling window.
* Once reconfiguration is done, the new list of active subcells i.e. currentActiveDlSubcellList in DL and currentActiveUlSubcellList in UL will be used by the intra-subpool PRB pooling algorithm computation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6788\_replaced([11212354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) carried out in the next pooling window.
* The currentActiveDlSubcellList shall be forwarded to L2-PS as listOfActiveDlSubcells.
* The currentActiveUlSubcellList shall be forwarded to L2-PS as listOfActiveUlSubcells.

-If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = FALSE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), all the DL subcells for each cell in the L1 Pool shall always be considered to be active, currentActiveDlSubcellList = All DL subcells configured for the cell in the L1 Pool

-If ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = FALSE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), all the UL subcells for each cell in the L1 Pool shall always be considered to be active, currentActiveUlSubcellList = All UL subcells configured for the cell in the L1 Pool

* When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is set to TRUE and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is set to TRUE, there are total two L1 pools and two L1 subpools per L1 pool on full BB board (in one L2-RT instance). BBRM shall manage subpool capacity reconfiguration independently for two L1 pools, no interaction between two L1 pools. For instance, if the reconfiguration of subpool capacity is successful in one L1 pool and the reconfiguration of subpool capacity is failed in another L1 pool, BBRM should follow the behavior of "received response status is 'success' (0)" and "received response status is 'failure' (1)" as above as independent procedure.

[PR735996]

If there is only one subpool in the L1 pool, the reconfiguration request message should not be sent to the L1, and

 BBRM keeps currentStreamPrbCapacityPerSp/currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp unchanged (which should be equal to defaultStreamPrbCapacityPerSp/defaultLayerPrbCapacityPerSp.)

 If TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in UL, BBRM updates currentActiveUlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool with the proposedActiveUlSubcellList. The rationale is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15493\_replaced([11213691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DL, BBRM updates currentActiveDlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool with the proposedActiveDlSubcellList.

 If ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in UL, BBRM updates currentActiveUlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool with the proposedActiveUlSubcellList.

[END PR735996]

---

#### 3.31.5.5.0-9 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools New Subpool Capacity Computation for InterL1 Subpool Reconfiguration (ID: 11213243)

**3.31.5.5.0-9.0-5**  (ID: `11213275`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
-At the second SFN of each pooling period, BBRM computes new stream/layer PRB capacity allocation proposals for each subpool of the L1 pool and this computed allocation proposal values will be used when subpool capacity reconfiguration is decided by the BBRM(5G\_UP\_ALG\_10387\_replaced([11213171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFnhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The SFN in which this computation is carried out and the L1/L2 synchronization described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) may take place is the same, rationale is provided 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-The new allocation proposal per subpool (Sp) is computed from poolMaxNumStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on the minimum subpool resource need to be reserved (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10411\_replaced([11213042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the total stream PRB demand determined per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and maxSpStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_11762\_replaced([11213083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The computation for each subpool is done in the following order:

(1) Firstly, new allocation proposal to support the minimum capacity needed per subpool is computed.

* newMinStreamPrbAllocationPerSp  = newMinStreamPrbCapacityPerSp (as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10411\_replaced([11213042](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

(1bis) From the remaining pool stream PRBs after (1), if any, if NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlCgType2 is set to True in any of the cells of the subpool, new allocation proposal is computed in proportion to the total CG stream PRB demand per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). At each subpool, the additional allocation in this step shall not exceed its CG stream PRB demand.

* Sort SPs in the pool in decreasing order of total CG demand and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list.
* newCgStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = floor{(remainingStreamPrbPerPool – newCgStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(j))\*totalStreamPrbCgDemandPerSp(i)/sum[k>=i]{totalStreamPrbCgDemandPerSp(k)}}; where i, j are index of SP with j<i
* where: remainingStreamPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - sum[all Sp k] {newMinStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k)}

[CB008600-F]

(1bisbis) From the remaining pool stream PRBs after (1bis), if any, new allocation proposal is computed in proportion to the total DC-GBR stream PRB demand per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). At each subpool, the additional allocation in this step shall not exceed its DC-GBR stream PRB demand and maxStreamPrbDcGbrAllocLimitSp (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* Sort SPs in the pool in the increasing order of min{ totalStreamPrbDcGbrDemandPerSp(i), maxStreamPrbDcGbrAllocLimitSp } and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list.
* newDcGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = floor{(remainingStreamPrbPerPool – newDcGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(j))\*totalStreamPrbDcGbrDemandPerSp(i)/sum[k>=i]{totalStreamPrbDcGbrDemandPerSp(k)}}; where i, j are index of SP with j<i
* newDcGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = min{maxStreamPrbDcGbrAllocLimitSp(i), newDcGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) }

where: remainingStreamPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumStreamPrb -  sum[all Sp k] {newMinStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) +  newCgStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k)}

[End CB008600-F]

(2) From the remaining pool stream PRBs after [Before CB008600-F] (1)[CB008600-F](1bisbis)[End CB008600-F], if any, new allocation proposal is computed in proportion to the total GBR stream PRB demand per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). At each subpool, the additional allocation in this step shall not exceed its GBR stream PRB demand and maxStreamPrbGbrAllocLimitSp (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* Sort SPs in the pool in the increasing order of min{ totalStreamPrbGbrDemandPerSp(i), maxStreamPrbGbrAllocLimitSp } and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list.
* newGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = floor{(remainingStreamPrbPerPool – newGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(j))\*totalStreamPrbGbrDemandPerSp(i)/sum[k>=i]{totalStreamPrbGbrDemandPerSp(k)}}; where i, j are index of SP with j<i
* newGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = min{maxStreamPrbGbrAllocLimitSp(i), newGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) }
* where: remainingStreamPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumStreamPrb -  sum[all Sp k] {newMinStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) +  newCgStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [CB008600-F]+ newDcGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB008600-F]}

(3) From the remaining pool stream PRBs after (2), if any, new allocation proposal is computed in proportion to the total nonGBR stream PRB demand per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). At each subpool, the additional allocation in this step shall not exceed its nonGBR stream PRB demand and maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If NRBTS.tmpActFeat2.bit7 is False and if at least one cell of a subpool has more than one subcells & for FR1-TDD UL Only

* the remaining pool stream PRBs after (2) is distributed between subpools in two Rounds. Rationale: in the presence of multiple subcell per cell deployment case, instead of considering only the maxCellStreamPrb as allocation capacity limit to each cell for the maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp, the two Round allocation first takes into account an estimate of percentage of the secondary subcell utilization by MU-MIMO (if any) in the maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp and then if there is still remaining subpool capacity, the next round considers the maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp computed from maxCellStreamPrb. Thus, the additional resource allocaiton in this step shall be performed as described below:
* First, provide additional additional allocaiton to each subpool in Round1 specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26879\_replaced([11213282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Next, if there is still remaining pool capacity after Round1, provide additional allocation as described in this step section using updated values from Round1:
* totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp = totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSpRound2 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26879\_replaced([11213282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp = maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSpRound2(5G\_UP\_ALG\_26879\_replaced([11213282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* remainingStreamPrbPerPool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26879\_replaced([11213282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSpRound1=newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26879\_replaced([11213282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp = 0 : initialize this value for all SPs.

Else

* do this step allocation as described below, and use input for remaining pool capacity as computed below:
* remainingStreamPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - sum[all Sp k] {newMinStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) + newCgStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [CB008600-F]+ newDcGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB008600-F]} + newGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k)}

End

* Sort SPs in the pool in the increasing order of min{ totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(i), maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp} and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list
* newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = floor{(remainingStreamPrbPerPool – newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(j))\*totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp (i)/sum[k>=i]{totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(k)}}; where i, j are index of SP with j<i
* newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = min{maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(i), newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) }

If NRBTS.tmpActFeat2.bit7 is False and if at least one cell of a subpool has more than one subcells & for FR1-TDD UL Only

* update total non-GBR demand based allocation for each SP from Round1 and Round2
* newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp + = newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSpRound1
* if there exist Sp with totalStreamPrbRimDemandPerSp (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) >0, distribute remaining capacity (if any) after the non-GBR load based allocation is done to these Sp in proportion to their totalStreamPrbRimDemandPerSp. The additional capacity is added to newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp.

(4) Allocate remaining pool stream PRBs, if any, to each subpool up to maxSpStreamPrb of a subpool is reached. If actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh = FALSE the allocation is done in a certain priority order such that the subpool with the higher priority shall reach its maxSpStreamPrb before the subpool with lower priority gets any allocation. Starting from the first subpool (lowest priority) in the list, a lower priority subpool in the list may get an allocation only if the amount of remaining pool stream PRB capacity is more than the total stream PRBs needed for the higher priority subpools (the later subpools in the list) to reach their maxSpStreamPrb. If actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh = TRUE, each subpool is allocated the remaining stream PRBs in a proportional manner based on the total previously allocated stream PRBs to each subpool. Each subpool can only be allocated the streamPRBs only upto its maxSpStreamPrb capacity.

* To create the subpools list with increasing priority order, sort the subpools in the pool in increasing order of maxSpStreamPrb. In case of subpools in the list with same maxSpStreamPrb, prioritize them in increasing order of (maxSpStreamPrb – newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp). If this cannot break the tie, no sorting (keep random subpool order list).
* Given from step (1) to (3):
* newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i) = newMinStreamPrbAllocationPerSp  (i) + newCgStreamPrbAllocationPerSp (i) [CB008600-F]+ newDcGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB008600-F] + newGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp (i) + newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp (i)
* remainingStreamPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - sum [all Sp k] {newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (k)}
* For each subpool in the sorted order list with newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i) > 0:

If actBbPoolTddFr1AlgEnh = FALSE  and slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = FALSE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

* newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i) = min{maxSpStreamPrb(i), newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp(i) + max {0, remainingStreamPrbPerPool - sum [all Sp k>i] {maxSpStreamPrb(k) – newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (k)}}}
* remainingStreamPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - sum [all Sp k] {newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (k)}

Else

If newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i) = 0

* Do not allocate any resources to this subpool
* AllocStreamPrbSp(i) = 0

Else

* Calculate the total already-allocated capacity for all the subpools after the current subpool in the sorted list
* allocatedStreamPrbSubsequentInclusive(i) = sum[all Sp k>=i] { newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp(k) }
* Calculate the total maximum allocation potential remaining (until the subpool-level maximums are reached) for all the subpools after the current subpool in the sorted list
* potentialStreamPrbSubsequent(i) = sum[all Sp k>i] { maxSpStreamPrb(k) – newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp(k) }
* Calculate the additional capacity to be allocated for the current subpool from the remaining capacity proportionally to the demand-based allocation and make sure that all PRB capacity will be allocated before running out of allocation potential in the subsequent subpools
* AllocStreamPrbSp = max{floor(remainingStreamPrbPerPool \* newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp(i) / allocatedStreamPrbSubsequentInclusive(i)),remainingStreamPrbPerPool - potentialStreamPrbSubsequent(i)}
* Do not exceed the maximum allocation of the subpool and do not allocate negative capacity
* AllocStreamPrbSp = min {AllocStreamPrbSp , maxSpStreamPrb(i) - newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp(i)}
* AllocStreamPrbSp = max {AllocStreamPrbSp , 0}

-Add the capacity allocated at this iteration to the total cumulative allocation of the subpool

* newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp(i) = newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp(i) + AllocStreamPrbSp
* Deduct the capacity allocated at this iteration from the total remaining capacity:
* remainingStreamPrbPerPool = remainingStreamPrbPerPool - AllocStreamPrbSp

End If

End If

(5) Allocate the rest of remaining stream PRBs of the pool, if any, equally between the subpools

* This step ensures that no stream PRB capacity of the pool remain unallocated. Any possible additional stream PRB capacity allocated in this step, (5), may not be used by the subpool as allocation up to the maxSpStreamPrb may already be satisfied in (4).

For i=0,1... totalNumOfSubPoolsInPool – 1

* remainingStreamPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - sum [all Sp k] {newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (k)}
* newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i) = newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp(i) + floor {remainingStreamPrbPerPool/ (totalNumOfSubPoolsInPool - i)}

End

* If large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE) and it is for DL only, allocate remaining subcell to subpools, until no subcell unallocated. Allocation remaining subcell to each L1 SP, get new value of newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i), refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21205\_replaced([11212940](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* The new stream PRB capacity reallocation proposal for each subpool becomes the sum of the new allocations computed in (1) to (5); i.e.
* If large BB pooling is activated (i.e., subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is set to TRUE) and it is for DL only,

proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp(i) = newTotalAllocSubcellPerSp(i) \* maxStreamPrbPerSubcell

where:

* maxStreamPrbPerSubcell = numSubcellStreamPrb(j) for cell j which has largest cell bandwidth in L1 Pool
* numSubcellStreamPrb(j) for cell j represents the maximum stream PRBs capacity per subcell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15391\_replaced([11212900](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

remainingStreamPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - sum [all Sp k]{proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp(k)}

If remainingStreamPrbPerPool > 0, then

proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp(0) = proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp(0) + remainingStreamPrbPerPool

End

Else

proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp(i) = newTotalAllocStreamPrbSp (i)

End If

* With interL1subpool PRB pooling, distribution of pool capacity between subpools is done on stream PRB basis, and the corresponding new layer PRB capacity for each SP is then determined from the new stream PRB capacity value allocated to each subpool. With the interL1subpool PRB pooling the ratio of the total amount of layer/stream PRB capacities shall always be maintained to be same as the ratio of the default configured layer/stream capacity values per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))); i.e. for each subpool index i,
* proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp(i) = floor{proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp(i)\*defaultLayerPrbCapacityPerSp(i)/defaultStreamPrbCapacityPerSp(i)};
