#### 3.31.5.5.0-10 Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools Round1 Inter-Subpool non-GBR demand Based resource Distribution (ID: 11213282)

**3.31.5.5.0-10.0-2**  (ID: `11213293`)

Re-allocation of Resources Between L1 Subpools
\* This section describes Round1 allocation procedure for Inter-subpool capacity dustribution for allocation Step(3), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), considering maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) evaluated based on  allocStreamPrbNonGbrLimitCell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26875\_replaced([11212968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
\* This section is applicable for FR1-TDD UL only

* Input:
* totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10392\_replaced([11213111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFndvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* poolMaxNumStreamPrb, newMinStreamPrbAllocationPerSp, newCgStreamPrbAllocationPerSp, [CB008600-F] newDcGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp, [End CB008600-F] newGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp : 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Output:
* newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp
* totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSpRound2,
* maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSpRound2,
* Sort SPs in the pool in the increasing order of min{ totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp, maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp} and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list
* newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = floor{(remainingStreamPrbPerPool – newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(j))\*totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp (i)/sum[k>=i]{totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(k)}};
* newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = max{newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i),  remainingStreamPrbPerPool – newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(j) - sum[k>i] { min{ totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(k), maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(k)} }}
* newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = min{maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(i), newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(i) }
* where:
* remainingStreamPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - sum[all Sp k] {newMinStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) + newCgStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k) + [CB008600-F] + newDcGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp[End CB008600-F] + newGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k)}
* i, j are index of SP with j<i
* After allocation is done, update remaining pool capacity, maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp & total nonGBR demand of each subpool by the allocation made in Round1, these updated values are to be used in Round2,  ( if executed)
* totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSpRound2 (i)  = totalStreamPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp (i) – newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp (i)
* remainingStreamPrbPerPool = remainingStreamPrbPerPool - sum[all Sp k] {newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp(k)
* maxStreamPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSpRound2 = sum[all cell i in Sp] {min{streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i), max{0,maxCellStreamPrb(i)- numMinStreamPRBAlloc(i) [CB008600-F] - streamPrbDemandDcGbr[End CB008600-F] – streamPrbDemandGbr(i) - streamPrbDemandCg}} \* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i)} - newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp.
* where:
* streamToLayerScaleFactor(i) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

newNonGbrStreamPrbAllocationPerSp the allocation given in Round1 for the SP.

### 3.31.5.6 Potential Usable PRB Computation for GBR PRB Load Monitoring

#### 3.31.5.6.0-1 Potential Usable PRB Computation for GBR PRB Load Monitoring Overview (ID: 11213304)

**3.31.5.6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11213309`)

Potential Usable PRB Computation for GBR PRB Load Monitoring
With PRB pooling enabled, the amount of usable PRBs to be used by L2PS of a cell to compute the GBR PRB load to be reported to the RAC (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5020\_replaced([11201171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwULafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL)/(5G\_UP\_ALG\_4516\_replaced([11183145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvIfo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL) shall be determined from the bbrmUsableCellPrb which is defined by the BBRM considering the PRB allocated to the cell and any additional potential PRB capacity share for GBR service that may be available to the cell from the L1Pool. The additional potential PRB capacity share for each cell in the same L1Pool is determined by the BBRM based on the availability of the free GBR potential L1pool capacity, share factor per cell and amount of allowed overbooking of the PRB resource among the sharing cells in the L1Pool, rdBbrmGbrLoadReportOverbookingFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13370\_replaced([11209039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwxeY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The value of bbrmUsableCellPrb shall be calculated differently based on the type of PRB pooling being used. This value shall be determined in every pooling period.

* When stream PRB pooling is enabled i.e. slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE, bbrmUsableCellPrb (for DL/UL)shall be determined as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12403\_replaced([11213315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxG1k_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* When layer PRB pooling is enabled i.e. slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE [CB012605-D]for DL/slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE for UL[End CB012605-D], bbrmUsableCellPrb (for DL[CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D])shall be determined as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26885\_replaced([11213345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxG1l_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 3.31.5.6.0-2 Potential Usable PRB Computation for GBR PRB Load Monitoring Usable PRB computation for GBR PRB load based on stream PRB pooling (ID: 11213315)

**3.31.5.6.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11213337`)

Potential Usable PRB Computation for GBR PRB Load Monitoring
- With UL/DL PRB pooling (Note: in case of DL PRB pooling for TDD FR1, both slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is true (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), the amount of usable PRBs to be used by L2PS of a cell to compute the UL/DL GBR PRB load to be reported to the RAC (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5020\_replaced([11201171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwULafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL)(5G\_UP\_ALG\_4516\_replaced([11183145](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvIfo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL) shall be determined from the bbrmUsableCellPrb which is defined by the BBRM considering the PRB allocated to the cell and any additional potential PRB capacity share for GBR service that may be available to the cell from the L1Pool. The additional potential PRB capacity share for each cell in the same L1Pool is determined by the BBRM based on the availability of the free GBR potential L1pool capacity, share factor per cell and amount of allowed overbooking of the PRB resource among the sharing cells in the L1Pool, rdBbrmGbrLoadReportOverbookingFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13370\_replaced([11209039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwxeY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The value of bbrmUsableCellPrb for UL/DL is determined every pooling period with the algorithm below:

-Algorithm Input:

* poolMaxNumStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* For each cell within the L1Pool, i.e. cells in each L1 SP of the L1 pool, (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* maxCellStreamPrbForGbr: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numMinStreamPRBAlloc:  numMinPRBAlloc# (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* AllocStreamPrbGbr (Step -3 in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6788\_replaced([11212354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* [CB008600-F] AllocStreamPrbDcGbr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6788\_replaced([11212354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB008600-F]
* rdBbrmGbrLoadReportOverbookingFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13370\_replaced([11209039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwxeY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):
* Input indicated with '#' are given in cell PRB resolution and the corresponding value needs to be converted to the equivalent stream PRB capacity using conversion rule defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Same value of rdBbrmGbrLoadReportOverbookingFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13370\_replaced([11209039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwxeY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is applied for all cells of the L1Pool.

-Algorithm Output:

* bbrmUsableCellPrb

-Algorithm:

For each cell i, in the L1Pool:

* If large BB pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed=TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))=TRUE),
* bbrmUsableStreamPrb (i) = maxCellStreamPrbForGbr (i) in the L1 Pool which has primary subcell of the cell

bbrmUsableStreamPrb(i) calculation depends only on the L1 Pool which has primary subcell of the cell. Note: Considering only L1 Pool which has primary subcell allows to limit bbrmUsableStreamPrb(i) for GBR load to 1 subcell whatever the number of subcells of the cell for a cell deployed on more than 1 L1 Pool. It should not be presumed which type of subcell, primary or seconday, handle the GBR traffic.

Else

* bbrmUsableStreamPrb (i) = min {maxCellStreamPrbForGbr (i), AllocStreamPrbGbr (i) [CB008600-F] + AllocStreamPrbDcGbr (i)  [End CB008600-F] +numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i) + (rdBbrmGbrLoadReportOverbookingFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13370\_replaced([11209039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwxeY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \*(1- cellShare (i)) + cellShare (i)) \* poolPotentialStreamPrbs},
* where:
* poolPotentialStreamPrbs = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - sum[all cell k of L1Pool]{AllocStreamPrbGbr (k) [CB008600-F] + AllocStreamPrbDcGbr (i)  [End CB008600-F] + numMinStreamPRBAlloc(k)}
* cellPotentialStreamPRBs (i) = maxCellStreamPrbForGbr (i) -  AllocStreamPrbGbr (i) [CB008600-F] - AllocStreamPrbDcGbr (i)  [End CB008600-F] - numMinStreamPRBAlloc (i).
* cellShare (i)  = cellPotentialStreamPRBs (i)  / sum [all cell k of L1Pool]{cellPotentialStreamPRBs (k) }

End If

* For each cell in the L1Pool, the equivalent cell PRB amount of the computed bbrmUsableStreamPrb,i.e. bbrmUsableCellPrb, shall be determined by stream PRB to cell PRB conversion rule defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-At each pooling period, the bbrmUsableCellPrb is sent to the UL/DL L2PS of the cell by the BBRM at the same time when the PRB allocation determined by the PRB pooling algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is sent to the cell by the BBRM (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6839\_replaced([11213362](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxG1mvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

#### 3.31.5.6.0-3 Potential Usable PRB Computation for GBR PRB Load Monitoring Usable PRB computation for GBR PRB load based on layer PRB pooling (ID: 11213345)

**3.31.5.6.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12536338`)

Potential Usable PRB Computation for GBR PRB Load Monitoring
- With UL/DL **layer PRB pooling (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE for DL/slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE for UL), the value of bbrmUsableCellPrb for DL/UL is determined every pooling period with the algorithm below:**

**-Algorithm Input:**

* poolMaxNumLayerPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26493\_replaced([11214467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* For each cell within the L1Pool, i.e. cells in each L1 SP of the L1 pool, (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* maxCellLayerPrbForGbr: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numMinLayerPRBAlloc: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* AllocLayerPrbGbr (Step - 2 in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25713\_replaced([11214271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* [CB008600-F] AllocLayerPrbDcGbr (Result of DC-GBR allocation step in [11214271: Load Metric Based LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm Overview](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) [End CB008600-F]
* rdBbrmGbrLoadReportOverbookingFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13370\_replaced([11209039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwxeY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):
* Same value of rdBbrmGbrLoadReportOverbookingFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13370\_replaced([11209039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwxeY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is applied for all cells of the L1Pool.

**-Algorithm Output:**

* bbrmUsableCellPrb

**-Algorithm:**

For each cell i, in the L1Pool:

* bbrmUsableLayerPrb (i) = min {maxCellLayerPrbForGbr (i), AllocLayerPrbGbr (i) **[CB008600-F] + AllocLayerPrbDcGbr (i)**[End CB008600-F] + numMinLayerPRBAlloc (i) + (rdBbrmGbrLoadReportOverbookingFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13370\_replaced([11209039](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwxeY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) *(1- cellShare (i)) + cellShare (i)) \* poolPotentialLayerPrbs},*\*\*\*
* where:
* poolPotentialLayerPrbs = poolMaxNumLayerPrb - sum[all cell k of L1Pool]{AllocLayerPrbGbr (k) **[CB008600-F] + AllocLayerPrbDcGbr (k)**[End CB008600-F] + numMinLayerPRBAlloc(k)}\*\*\*\*
* cellPotentialLayerPrbs (i) = maxCellLayerPrbForGbr (i) **- AllocLayerPrbGbr (i)** **[CB008600-F] - AllocLayerPrbDcGbr (i)**[End CB008600-F] - numMinLayerPRBAlloc (i).\*\*\*\*
* cellShare (i)  = cellPotentialLayerPrbs (i)  / sum [all cell k of L1Pool]{cellPotentialLayerPrbs (k) }
* For each cell in the L1Pool, the equivalent cell PRB amount of the computed bbrmUsableLayerPrb,i.e. bbrmUsableCellPrb, shall be determined by layer PRB to cell PRB conversion using **numReqFdPrb defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (use Rank1 during the conversion assuming the lowest possible transmission shceme).**

-At each pooling period, the bbrmUsableCellPrb is sent to the DL/UL L2PS of the cell by the BBRM at the same time when the PRB allocation determined by the PRB pooling algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25712\_replaced([11214266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is sent to the cell by the BBRM (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27908\_replaced([11213385](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxG1nvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

### 3.31.5.7 Timing for New PRB Resource Grant and Usage by L2PS

#### 3.31.5.7.0-1 Timing for New PRB Resource Grant and Usage by L2PS Timing for New PRB grant reception by L2PS (ID: 11213362)

**3.31.5.7.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11213380`)

Timing for New PRB Resource Grant and Usage by L2PS
-When 5G-L2-PS receives a new resource grant (PRB grant and active [CB009890-A]DL/[End CB009890-A]UL subcell list grant) at SFN N from BBRM to be used during the current pooling period:

* the new grant shall be started to be used from the next SFN (SFN N+1), not in the same SFN N when the new grant was received.
* any future allocation made in DL/UL during the current time windows at a transition time (SFN N) and the new allocation pointing to slots in the next pooling period, the allocation shall consider the new received grant to be available as the usable resource limit.
* In DL slots where PDCCH have to be sent to grant UL traffic, if the k2 points to a UL slot after the beginning of a new pooling period where new grant is to be used, the new received UL resource grant should be considered as the limit to respect.
* For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if the new PRB grant received by L2PS from the BBRM for the next pooling period is reduced compared to the UL PRB grant from BBRM being used in the current pooling window, then the 5G-L2-PS shall limit the number of PRBs allowed for initial UL transmission of a UE during the transient phase to the rrmMaxNumPuschPrbPoolingLimit (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5010\_replaced([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value computed based on the new UL PRB allocation received for the next pooling period. The transient phase is the time between L2PS receives new UL PRB allocation from BBRM and starts to use it.

[CB009890-A]

* The active DL subcell list grant received from BBRM (listOfActiveDlSubcells; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13411\_replaced([11212398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall only be considered in L2-PS when dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Otherwise, all configured DL subcells shall be considered always active.

[End CB009890-A]

* The active UL subcell list grant received from BBRM ([CB009890-B]currentActiveUlSubcellList listOfActiveUlSubcells; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13411\_replaced([11212398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB009890-B]) shall only be considered in L2-PS when TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE [CB009890-B] OR  ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB009890-B]. Otherwise, all configured UL subcells shall be considered always active.

-If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE, after a new Cell is added to cell pool list, this Cell receives UL PRB grant of 0 (numAllocCellPrb=0) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6850\_replaced([11212236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the current pooling period until the BBRM allocates at least the minimum amount of PRB to be used in UL in the next pooling period. So, While numAllocCellPrb=0, all UL scheduling shall be blocked (inc. PRACH) as there is no available PRB to be used in the cell.

If TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), after a new cell is added, this cell receives active UL subcell list as empty until the cell is considered in the subsequent pooling period in UL subcell deactivation procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15432\_replaced([11213701](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) when it activates atleast its UL primary subcell. So, while the received active UL subcell list is empty, all UL scheduling shall be blocked including PRACH as it has no active UL subcell.

---

#### 3.31.5.7.0-2 Timing for New PRB Resource Grant and Usage by L2PS Timing for New grant reception by L2PS for eCPRI 7-2e (ID: 11213385)

**3.31.5.7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11213389`)

Timing for New PRB Resource Grant and Usage by L2PS
-When 5G-L2-PS receives a new resource grant (layer PRB grant [CB012605-H]and active DL/UL subcell list grant[End CB012605-H]) at SFN N from BBRM to be used during the current pooling period:

* the new grant shall be started to be used from the next SFN (SFN N+1), not in the same SFN N when the new grant was received.
* any future allocation made in DL[CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D] during the current time windows at a transition time (SFN N) and the new allocation pointing to slots in the next pooling period, the allocation shall consider the new received grant to be available as the usable resource limit.
* In DL slots where PDCCH have to be sent to grant UL traffic, if the k2 points to a UL slot after the beginning of a new pooling period where new grant is to be used, the new received UL resource grant should be considered as the limit to respect.

[CB012605-D]

* For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3723\_replaced([11693470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D31Qwf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))), if the new layer PRB grant received by L2PS from the BBRM for the next pooling period is reduced compared to the UL layer PRB grant from BBRM being used in the current pooling window, then the L2PS shall limit the number of layer PRBs allowed for initial UL transmission of a UE during the transient phase to the rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value computed based on the new UL layer PRB allocation received for the next pooling period. The transient phase is the time between L2PS receives new UL layer PRB allocation from BBRM and starts to use it.

-If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE, after a new cell is added to cell pool list, this cell receives UL layer PRB grant of 0 (numAllocCellLayerPrb=0) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25709\_replaced([11214021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the current pooling period until the BBRM allocates at least the minimum amount of layer PRB to be used in UL in the next pooling period. So, while numAllocCellLayerPrb=0, all UL scheduling shall be blocked (inc. PRACH) as there is no available layer PRB to be used in the cell.[End CB012605-D]

[CB012605-H]

* The active DL subcell list grant received from BBRM (listOfActiveDlSubcells; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27687\_replaced([11214642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall only be considered in L2-PS when slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE and dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3723\_replaced([11693470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D31Qwf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))
* The active UL subcell list grant received from BBRM, all configured UL subcells shall be considered always active.[End CB012605-H]

### 3.31.5.8 Zero Allocation Bypass

#### 3.31.5.8.0-1 Zero Allocation Bypass Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) overview (ID: 11213401)

**3.31.5.8.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11213433`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
When slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DL, if a certain number of cells are allocated some symbols to transmit wideband signals (CSI-RS for channel acquisition, or TRS) in a slot, the other cells in the same L1 Pool are not allowed to perform any kind of transmission in the same symbols of the slot. Such symbols are referred to as Zero Allocation Symbols since there are no PRBs allocated on such symbols for any kind of DL transmission.

However, if rdAllowZeroAllocBypass (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15040\_replaced([11215279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true, BBRM can allow certain cells to bypass this restriction and still perform DL transmissions in the Zero Allocation symbols. This is referred to as Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB)

ZAB privilege is granted by BBRM to the cells of an L1 Pool every pooling period, such that the sum of :

* the total number of stream PRBs allocated to the ZAB cells and
* the Wideband stream PRBs required by the cells transmitting the Wideband signals.
* for cells spread across 2 L1 pools, the total number of stream PRBs allocated to the cell in the L1 Pool where the algorithm will be executed if it has been granted ZAB privilege in the another L1 Pool.
* max stream PRBs required for RIM-RS transmission by the cells that detect Remote Interference and have not been granted ZAB privilege. If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true, requested stream PRBs for RIM-RS transmission only by the cells which request RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period and have not been granted ZAB privilege.

does not exceed the L1 Pool's capacity.

poolMaxNumStreamPrb >= Sum{Allocated Stream PRBs to ZAB cells} + Sum[all subpools per pool]{maxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp} + Sum{Allocated Stream PRBs of cells which have ZAB privilege in any other L1 Pool} + reservedStreamPrbForRimRs

where,

poolMaxNumStreamPrb = The maximum amount of stream PRBs available on the L1 Pool level described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

maxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp = The maximum amount of stream PRBs available for Wideband signalling in the L1Subpool given for DL in NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6539\_replaced([11212289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is true, each cell can have its subcells spread across 2 L1 pools (with 2 L1 subpools per L1 pool), BBRM shall consider as Wideband Stream PRB:

maxWbPoolStreamPrb = Sum[all subpools per pool]{rdMaxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp16DL}

where,

rdMaxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp16DL is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26571\_replaced([11215307](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbyvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true,

If numCellsInPool > 3,

reservedStreamPrbForRimRs **= min(Sum{Requested RIM-RS PRBs of cells which request RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period},  (numCellsInPool -maxNumcellsWithSimultaneousWbTransmission)\*maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell) - rimRsPrbsOfAllZabCells**

Else

reservedStreamPrbForRimRs = 0

End If

rimRsPrbsOfAllZabCells is all requested RIM-RS PRBs of cells which are selected as ZAB and also request RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period.

Else

reservedStreamPrbForRimRs **= maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell \* (numCellsInPool - maxNumcellsWithSimultaneousWbTransmission -** numCellsWithZabPrivilege)\*\*\*\*

End If

maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell = Max Stream PRBs required for RIM-RS for a cell described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

numCellsInPool = Total number of cells in the L1 Pool

maxNumcellsWithSimultaneousWbTransmission = Parameter "M" described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

numCellsWithZabPrivilege = Number of cells that have been granted ZAB privilege

ZAB privilege is provided to the cells with the highest absolute configured (based on number of configured subcells for the cell) loads as long as they satisfy the L1 Capacity condition in the formula above.

* Absolute configured (based on number of configured subcells for the cell) Cell load calculation is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14565\_replaced([11213462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note: parameters numMinStreamPRBAlloc,**[CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandDcGbr,** [End CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandGbr, streamPrbDemandNonGbr of each cell are used in the calculation and they are re-used from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in Load Metric Based Pooling Algorithm.\*\*\*\*
* ZAB cells selection based on their loads is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14566\_replaced([11213567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

After selecting all cells which will be granted the ZAB privilege, BBRM informs the L2-PS of each cell in every pooling period if the cell has been granted the ZAB privilege.

ZAB privilege will be updated every pooling period along with the allocated Cell PRBs.

Newly setup cells during the pooling period shall suspend all DL scheduling and other wideband transmissions until next Pooling Period. This is to avoid exceeding the L1 Pool capacity in case of WB transmissions in the new cell colliding with PDSCH transmission from a cell with ZAB privilege.

~~When~~ If large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is true, each cell can have its subcells spread across 2 L1 pools (with 2 L1 subpools per L1 pool).

If "active cell amount N <=3", then

The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall not be executed, BBRM just simply return ZAB privilege as TRUE to all cells (up to 3 cells) since the L1 capacity is always respected in case of total WB transmission plus PDSCH transmission from ZAB privilege cell.

Hence, no RIM-RS reservation needs to be considered.

Else if ("active cell amount N > 3"), then

The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall be executed per L1 pool.

RIM-RS reservation needs to be considered, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22571\_replaced([11213633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIqyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

End If

Where active cells shall be configured and located in same BB board.

For such a cell which is spread across 2 L1 Pools, the ZAB privilege shall stay consistent across both L1 Pools. If the cell is granted the ZAB privilege in one of the L1 Pools, it shall also be granted the ZAB privilege in the other pool as long as there is capacity in the other pool, else the cell shall not be granted the ZAB privilege in any of the L1 pools.

ZAB procedure shall be executed sequentially over all L1 Pools configured in the BBRM in every pooling period only after the intra L1 SP pooling procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13233\_replaced([11212393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has been successfully executed on all L1 subpools of all configured L1 Pools.

The L1 pools to execute ZAB selection should follow "consolidate cell list" with decreasing order of cell load (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25757\_replaced([11213508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

End If

**[05533578]**

Note:

* For each L1 DL pool, 3 csirsPoolingGroups initialized with L1Pool DL max wideband signal stream PRBs as available stream PRBs , and csirsPoolingGroupId is from 0 to 2.
* BBRM maintains a list of active cell's
* The current implementation always assumes 3 CSI-RS pooling groups. In case there is no active cell in other pooling groups, it results in unnecessary loss of symbol periods for presumed CSI-RS transmissions from other pooling groups.
* This solution addresses the problem that it is assumed that all CSI-RS Pooling Groups are active at any given instance. If not all CSI-RS Pooling Groups are active, symbols are wasted due to applying ZA limitations irrespective of whether other pooling groups are active or not.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed is true,

If "activeCsiRsPoolingGroups N=1", then

// 2-Sector Case: In a 2-sector deployment, only one CSI-RS Pooling Group is active. Other CSI-RS Pooling Group offsets and related Zero Allocation  can be ignored.

The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall not be executed, BBRM just simply return ZAB privilege as TRUE to all cells (up to 3 cells) since the L1 capacity is always respected in case of total WB transmission plus PDSCH transmission from ZAB privilege cell.

All cells in the corresponding csirspoolingGroupId are allowed to use othercsirsPoolingGroup CSI-RS-ACQ and CSI-IM symbols.

[Before PR881837]

Else if "activeCsiRsPoolingGroups N>1", then

// more than one CS-RS Pooling Group's Active

[PR881837]

Else if "activeCsiRsPoolingGroups 1<N<3", then

// 3-Sector Case: In a 3-sector deployment, typically two CSI-RS Pooling Groups are active, while a third remains inactive

Two CSI-RS Pooling Groups are active. The third CSI-RS Pooling Group remains inactive. The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall not be executed.

For all the cells in the two active CSI-RS Pooling groups: ZAB privilege shall be considered for the symbols (used to transmit wideband signals like 'CSI-RS' or 'TRS'), which are in the slots on the inactive csirsPoolingGroup. This shall be considered irrespective whether ZAB privilege is granted or not in the active CSI-RS Pooling group(s).

Though each active CSI-RS Pooling group has to apply the Zero Allocation rules for the symbols (used to transmit wideband signals like 'CSI-RS' or 'TRS'), which are in the slots on the other active CSI-RS Pooling group.

Else if "activeCsiRsPoolingGroups N>=3", then

// All three CS-RS Pooling Group's Active

Internal Note: The number of activeCsiRsPoolingGroups is internally derived in the L2PS submodules (EFS). Between BBRM and L2PS-SCH, in the ResourceResp message from BBRM to L2-SCH, a new field “field activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask” has been added:

activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask = 0x1 -> // 0th bit set : cells present in csirsPoolingGroupId=0 only

activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask = 0x2 -> //1st bit set:  cells present in csirsPoolingGroupId=1 only

activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask = 0x4 -> //2nd bit set: cells present in csirsPoolingGroupId=2 only

Based on the information from activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask, the amount of activeCsiRsPoolingGroups is calculated.

If activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask=0x1 or activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask=0x2 or activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask=0x4, ZAB grant in L2-PS SCH is overwritten.

In every pooling period, for each L1 Pool BBRM traverses through the cell list and computes activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask based on the csi-rs pooling group Id information of each cell.

When a cell is newly added or deleted, activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask will be updated in the next BB period.

This functionality is controlled by a rd-parameter:

rdZabOptimization   - This parameter enables/disables the ZAB optimization solution.

default: 3     Online modificable. Step Size: 1[0..3], Online Modifiable: Yes"

0 - disabled,

1 - enable single csiRsPoolingGroup active solution,

2 - enable two csiRsPoolingGroups active solution,

3 - enable Both, one or two csiRsPoolingGroups active solution.

[End PR881837]

The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall be executed per L1 pool.

End If

Where active cells shall be configured and located in same BB board.

ZAB procedure shall be executed sequentially over all L1 Pools configured in the BBRM in every pooling period only after the intra L1 SP pooling procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13233\_replaced([11212393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has been successfully executed on all L1 subpools of all configured L1 Pools.

The L1 pools to execute ZAB selection should follow "consolidate cell list" with decreasing order of cell load (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25757\_replaced([11213508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

End If

[End 05533578]

Note : Due to the available L1 Pool capacity and the allocated PRBs to all the cells in the pool, it is possible that none of the cells in the pool is provided the ZAB privilege.

---

#### 3.31.5.8.0-2 Zero Allocation Bypass Wideband Stream PRB Calculation (ID: 11213438)

**3.31.5.8.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11213458`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
BB Pooling allows multiple cells to perform Wideband Signal Transmission in DL. However, in case cellTechnology = TDD only, CP-RT can allocate UE specific CSI-RS to different cells in separate CsiRsPoolingGroups on the same symbol (i.e. there is no consideration for CsiRsPoolingGroups during the allocation). The allocation considers :

Sum {all wideband signals on same symbol per pool} <=  Sum[all subpools per pool]{maxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp}

where,

maxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp = The maximum amount of stream PRBs available for Wideband signalling in the L1Subpool given for DL in NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6539\_replaced([11212289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Hence, BBRM shall consider as Wideband Stream PRB :

maxWbPoolStreamPrb = Sum[all subpools per pool]{maxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp}

where,

maxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp = The maximum amount of stream PRBs available for Wideband signalling in the L1Subpool given for DL in NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6539\_replaced([11212289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB010713-A, PR750378]

If large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is true, each cell can have its subcells spread across 2 L1 pools (with 2 L1 subpools per L1 pool), BBRM shall consider as Wideband Stream PRB:

maxWbPoolStreamPrb = Sum[all subpools per pool]{rdMaxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp16DL}

where,

rdMaxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp16DL is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26571\_replaced([11215307](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbyvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB010713-A, PR750378]

---

#### 3.31.5.8.0-3 Zero Allocation Bypass Absolute Configured Cell Load Calculation (ID: 11213462)

**3.31.5.8.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11213486`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Absolute configured Cell Load calculation shall be calculated by BBRM for all cells in the L1 Pool.

Algorithm Input :

* List of cells in the pool
* [CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandDcGbr, [End CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandGbr, streamPrbDemandNonGbr of each cell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14549\_replaced([11213394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxConfiguredCellStreamPrb of each cell described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21671\_replaced([11213493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Algorithm Output :

* absConfiguredCellLoad[i]: absolute configured Cell Load for Cell i, i ϵ {0, 1 .. N-1} where N is number of Cells

Algorithm Steps:

For each cell i:

absConfiguredCellLoad[i]=([CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandDcGbr[i]+ [End CB008600-F]streamPrbDemandGbr[i]+ streamPrbDemandNonGbr[i])/maxConfiguredCellStreamPrb[i]

---

#### 3.31.5.8.0-4 Zero Allocation Bypass Max Configured Cell Stream PRB Calculation (ID: 11213493)

**3.31.5.8.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11213503`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Maximum configured stream PRB for each cell in the L1 Pool shall be calculated as below.

Algorithm Input :

* dlBandwidth : Cell DL Bandwidth (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* numConfiguredSubcells : Configured number of DL subcells for the cell in the L1 Pool [CB010713-A](For a cell with subcells configured over multiple L1 Pools, consider only the DL subcells that are configured for the cell in the L1 Pool where the ZAB algorithm is currently being executed)[End CB010713-A]
* numMaxStreamPerSubcell : Max number of streams supported by the subcell configured in the cell (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Algorithm Output :

* maxConfiguredCellStreamPrb : Maximum Configured Stream PRBs for the cell in the L1 Pool

Algorithm Steps:

* maxConfiguredCellStreamPrb  = dlBandwidth \* numConfiguredSubcells \* numMaxStreamPerSubcell

---

#### 3.31.5.8.0-5 Zero Allocation Bypass Consolidate cell list creation (ID: 11213508)

**3.31.5.8.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11213515`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
In case of multiple L1 pools under same L2-RT instance, BBRM needs to create a consolidate cell list with dreasing order of cell load.

Algorithm Input:

* List of cells in the L1 pool
* Absolute configured load of each cell: absConfiguredCellLoad (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14565\_replaced([11213462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Algorithm Output:

* BBRM generates a new consolidate cell list which shall consider following rules:

1) go through all cells in all L1 pools

2) if the subcells of one cell are located in one L1 pool, the cell load is calculated as the value of absConfiguredCellLoad

3) If the subcells of one cell spread across 2 L1 pools, the cell load of primary subcell located in L1 pool shall be taken into account with the value of absConfiguredCellLoad

3) new cell list with decreasing order of cell load according to the value of absConfiguredCellLoad

---

#### 3.31.5.8.0-6 Zero Allocation Bypass PRB Reservations (ID: 11213520)

**3.31.5.8.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11213526`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Reservations for RIM-RS

---

**3.31.5.8.0-6.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11213549`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
When granting ZAB privilege, there is a need to reserve PRBs for RIM-RS (Remote Interference Management - Reference Signal) transmission in DL for each cell in the L1 Pool if actBbPoolTddFr1Enh is false. If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true, only need to reserve PRBs for RIM-RS transmission for the cells which request RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period.

RIM-RS transmissions can collide with CSI-RS as well as PDSCH transmissions since it shall be transmitted on the last 2 DL symbols of a slot (5G\_UP\_ALG\_12969\_replaced([11101057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knTZX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Further more, RIM-RS transmission could use up to 96 PRBs over 2 streams (5G\_UP\_ALG\_12970\_replaced([11101094](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knUAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 is false. If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 are true, RIM-RS transmission could use up to 96 PRBs over 4 streams (5G\_UP\_ALG\_12423\_replaced([11101140](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knUncvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

hence,

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolExtensionTddFr1 are true,

maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell = 384 (96 PRBs \* 4 Streams)

Else

maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell = 192 (96 PRBs \* 2 Streams)

End If

If slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RIM-RS is never sent, hence, maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell = 0

While reserving the capacity for RIM-RS in the L1 Pool, BBRM shall consider the following :

* actDisableNrRimRsAtGnbLevel (from PsCnfg\_AddressDistributionReq message) which activates/deactivates the disabling of remote interference management RS on gNB level
* Number of Cells in the L1 Pool, N
* Max cells with simultaneous Wideband transmission (Eg. CSI-RS) per pool, M = 2 (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7787\_replaced([11278829](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNffvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Since the cells with WB transmissions would be able to transmit also RIM-RS, they can be ignored from the reservation.

[CB010713-A]

* Number of cells that do not have their primary subcell in the L1 Pool, Q
* Since RIM-RS is always transmitted on the primary subcell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_12735\_replaced([11160843](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktQ3ZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), there is no need to consider any reservation for RIM-RS for the cells which do not have their primary subcell in the L1 Pool.
* Number of cells which have subcells configured in other L1 Pools, that have been granted ZAB privilege in the other(or previous) L1 pools and have their primary subcell in the current L1 Pool, P
* Such cells will be granted ZAB also in the current L1 Pool, thus, they can already transmit RIM-RS as part of its numMinStreamPrbAlloc (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and ignored from the reservation.

[CNI-110226]

Note : For the first L1 Pool where the ZAB procedure is executed, P = 0

[End CNI-110226]

[End CB010713-A]

* No cell has been granted the ZAB privilege yet.
* A cell under consideration for ZAB privilege can accommodate the RIM-RS as part of its numMinStreamPRBAlloc (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), hence it can also be ignored from the reservation.
* Requested RIM-RS PRBs of cells in the pooling period, streamPrbDemandRim[i], i=0..N-1. Note: The calculation below can be done more simple also with streamPrbDemandRim = 0 which indicates no RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period.

Based on the above considerations, RIM-RS reservation for an L1 Pool is given as :

If actDisableNrRimRsAtGnbLevel from PsCnfg\_AddressDistributionReq message is false,

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true,

If N <= 3,

rimRsL1Reservation = 0

Else

[Before CNI-110226]

rimRsL1Reservation = min(Sum{streamPrbDemandRim[i], i=0..N-1}, (N-M)\* maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell)}

[CNI-110226]

rimRsL1Reservation = min{(Sum[all cells ‘i’ in the L1 pool which have their primary subcell configured in the current L1 pool]{streamPrbDemandRim[i]} – Sum[all cells ‘j’ in P] {streamPrbDemandRim[j]}), max{0, (N-M-P-Q)\*maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell}}

[End CNI-110226]

Note: In worst case, wideband capacity can be used up by cells which does not request RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period, and then requested RIM-RS PRBs for all cells which request RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period shall be considered to reserve. In case all cells request to transmit RIM-RS, the max capacity(without considering ZAB) for RIM-RS to reserve is [Before CNI-110226] (N-M)*maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell [CNI-110226] max{0, (N - M - P - Q)*maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell}[End CNI-110226]. WB transmission shall consider both Cell Specific CSI-RS/TRS and UE Specific CSI-RS, BBRM does not know the allocation of UE Specific CSI-RS in CPRT.

End If

Note: In this case, cells which does not request RIM-RS transmission for the pooling period may be selected as ZAB cells and maybe no ZAB capacity for the cells which request RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period. Not need to reserve PRBs for RIM-RS for ZAB cells which request RIM-RS transmission for the pooling period, will be handled dynamically during ZAB Cell Selection in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14566\_replaced([11213567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Else

[Before CB010713-A]

rimRsL1Reservation = max{0, maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell \* (N - M - 1)}

[CB010713-A]

[Before CNI-110226]

rimRsL1Reservation = max{0, maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell \* (N - M - Q - P - 1)}

[CNI-110226]

rimRsL1Reservation = max{0, maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell \* (N - M - Q - P )}

[End CNI-110226]

[End CB010713-A]

End If

Else

rimRsL1Reservation = 0

End If

If slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), RIM-RS is never sent, hence, rimRsL1Reservation = 0

[CNI-110226]

While executing the ZAB procedure on an L1 Pool, rimRsL1Reservation shall be calculated for all remaining L1 Pools where the ZAB procedure is still to be executed. Thus, while executing for the first L1 pool, P = 0 for all remaining L1 Pools

[End CNI-110226]

---

**3.31.5.8.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11213557`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Reservations for ZAB Cells from other L1 Pools

---

**3.31.5.8.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11213561`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
For cells which have subcells configured over multiple L1 Pools, the ZAB privilege needs to stay consistent across all the L1 Pools where the cell is configured.

If such a cell was granted the ZAB privilege in one of the other(or previous) L1 pools where it is configured, BBRM needs to reserve the capacity for the cell while allocating ZAB privilege for the other cells in the L1 Pool.

The reserved capacity (zabReserveCellsOtherPools) should consider the Stream PRBs allocated to the cell in the L1 Pool where the ZAB algorithm is currently being executed.

The reservation capacity can be calaculated as below :

* zabReserveCellsOtherPools = 0
* For each cell 'i' in the L1 Pool which has subcells configured also in other L1 Pools
* If : cell 'i' has ZAB privilege in any other L1 Pool
* zabReserveCellsOtherPools = zabReserveCellsOtherPools + numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)
* End If
* End for

where:

* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = Total Stream PRB allocation as per the Intra L1 PRB Pooling algorithm (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13233\_replaced([11212393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the cell in the L1 Pool where the ZAB algorithm is being executed.

(numAllocCellStreamPrb is calaculted individually per L1 Pool, hence we need to reserve the allocation provided by the BBRM in the L1 Pool where the ZAB algorithm is currently beiong executed)

Reserved ZAB capacity for cells = zabReserveCellsOtherPools

Note : Such cells shall be considered to already have ZAB privilege and hence not considered in the list of cells for the L1 Pool where the ZAB algorithm is currently being executed.

---

#### 3.31.5.8.0-7 Zero Allocation Bypass Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) Cell Selection (ID: 11213567)

**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11213573`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) Cell Selection for 23R3

---

**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11213579`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
If rdAllowZeroAllocBypass (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15040\_replaced([11215279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is false, no cell shall be provided the ZAB privilege and the below mentioned procedure need not be executed.

Cell selection algorithm to provide the ZAB privilege to cells in the same L1 Pool involves the following steps :

1) Sort all cells in the decreasing order of their absolute loads (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14565\_replaced([11213462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

2) Consider providing each cell with ZAB privilege as long as the L1 Pooling capacity is not exceeded or the list of cells is not exhausted.

Algorithm Input

[Before CB008940-I-UPD001]

1) List of cells in the pool

2) Absolute load of each cell : absCellLoad (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14565\_replaced([11213462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

3) Number of stream PRBs allocated to each cell : numAllocCellStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

4) Total stream PRBs of the CsiRsPoolingGroup with highest sum of wideband stream PRBs : maxWbCsiRsPoolingGrpStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14562\_replaced([11213438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

5) Total stream PRBs of the CsiRsPoolingGroup with 2nd highest sum of wideband stream PRBs:  2ndMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGrpStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14562\_replaced([11213438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

6) CsiRsPoolingGroupId of the CsiRsPoolingGroup which has highest sum of wideband stream PRBs: CsiRsPoolingGroupIdWithMaxWb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14562\_replaced([11213438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

7) Total Stream PRB capacity of the L1 Pool : poolMaxNumStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB008940-L]

8) L1 Capacity reserved for RIM-RS transmission : rimRsL1Reservation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB008940-L]

[CB008940-I-UPD001]

1) List of cells in the L1 pool or L1 pools

2) Absolute load of each cell : absCellLoad (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14565\_replaced([11213462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

3) Number of stream PRBs allocated to each cell : numAllocCellStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

4) Number of stream PRBs reserved for Wideband signals per pool: maxWbPoolStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14562\_replaced([11213438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

5) Total Stream PRB capacity of the L1 Pool : poolMaxNumStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB008940-L]

6) L1 Capacity reserved for RIM-RS transmission : rimRsL1Reservation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB008940-L]

[End CB008940-I-UPD001]

Algorithm

Sort the list of cells in the decreasing order of their cell load (absCellLoad)

Let,

* Sum of numAllocCellStreamPrb of all cells provided with ZAB privilege : numAllocStreamPrbZabCells = 0.

[Before CB008940-I-UPD001]

* ZAB Capacity for all CsiRsPoolingGroups: zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - maxWbCsiRsPoolingGrpStreamPrb

[CB008940-I-UPD001]

* ZAB Capacity for all CsiRsPoolingGroups: zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - maxWbPoolStreamPrb

[End CB008940-I-UPD001]

[Before CB008940-I-UPD001]

* extra ZAB Capacity in L1 Pool for the CsiRsPoolingGroup which has highest sum of wideband stream PRBs: extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup = maxWbCsiRsPoolingGrpStreamPrb – 2ndMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGrpStreamPrb. Note: The CsiRsPoolingGroup which has highest sum of wideband stream PRBs will have more ZAB Capacity, when wideband stream PRBs of other CsiRsPoolingGroups are less than wideband stream PRBs of the CsiRsPoolingGroup which has highest sum of wideband stream PRBs.

[CB008940-I-UPD001]

The section in the before Tag above shall not be considered henceforth, and shall be removed in later release inheritances of this requirement.

[End CB008940-I-UPD001]

* [CB008940-L] rimRsZabReservation = rimRsL1Reservation [End CB008940-L]

For : Each cell 'i' from the sorted list of cells (starting from the cell with the highest load)

[Before CB008940-I-UPD001]

If cell 'i' is from the CsiRsPoolingGroup which CsiRsPoolingGroupId != CsiRsPoolingGroupIdWithMaxWb, (Note: In this case, cell 'i' can only use ZAB Capacity from zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups)

[CB008940-I-UPD001]

The section in the before Tag above shall not be considered henceforth, and shall be removed in later release inheritances of this requirement.

[End CB008940-I-UPD001]

[Before CB008940-L]

If : (zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups >= numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells), then;

[CB008940-L]

If : (zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups >= numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells +  rimRsZabReservation ), then;

[End CB008940-L]

* Add cell 'i' to the list of cells with ZAB privilege
* numAllocStreamPrbZabCells = numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells

[CB008940-L]

* rimRsZabReservation = max{0, (rimRsZabReservation - maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell)} [End CB008940-L]

Else

* Do not provide ZAB privilege to cell 'i'

End

[Before CB008940-I-UPD001]

Else

Note: In this case, cell 'i' is from CsiRsPoolingGroup which CsiRsPoolingGroupId =  CsiRsPoolingGroupIdWithMaxWb, cell 'i' shall first use ZAB Capacity from extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup, cell 'i' shall start to use ZAB Capacity from zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups when extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup are used up.

[Before CB008940-L]

If : (zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups + extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup >= numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells), then;

[CB008940-L]

If : (zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups + extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup >= numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells + rimRsZabReservation ), then;

[End CB008940-L]

Add cell 'i' to the list of cells with ZAB privilege

If numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) <=  extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup,

extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup = extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup -  numAllocCellStreamPrb (i)

Else

numAllocStreamPrbZabCells = numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) - extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells

extraZabCapacityForMaxWbCsiRsPoolingGroup = 0

End

[CB008940-L] rimRsZabReservation = max{0, (rimRsZabReservation - maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell)} [End CB008940-L]

Else

Do not provide ZAB privilege to cell 'i'

End

End

[CB008940-I-UPD001]

The section in the before Tag above shall not be considered henceforth, and shall be removed in later release inheritances of this requirement.

[End CB008940-I-UPD001]

End For

where:

maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Algorithm Output

1) List of cells with ZAB privilege

Note : Newly added cells which do not have any PRBs allocated to them by the BBRM (numAllocCellStreamPrb = 0) shall not be provided the ZAB privilege.

**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11213587`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) Cell Selection for 23R4 (last obsoleted non-split version)

---

**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11213592`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
If rdAllowZeroAllocBypass (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15040\_replaced([11215279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is false, no cell shall be provided the ZAB privilege and the below mentioned procedure need not be executed.

Cell selection algorithm to provide the ZAB privilege to cells in the same L1 Pool involves the following steps :

* Sort all cells in the decreasing order of their absolute loads (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14565\_replaced([11213462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Consider providing each cell with ZAB privilege as long as the L1 Pooling capacity is not exceeded or the list of cells is not exhausted.

Algorithm Input

* List of cells in the L1 pool or L1 pools
* Absolute [CB009890-A-UPD002]configured[End CB009890-A-UPD002] load of each cell : [Before CB009890-A-UPD002]absCellLoad[CB009890-A-UPD002]absConfiguredCellLoad[End CB009890-A-UPD002](5G_UP_ALG_14565_replaced([11213462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Number of stream PRBs allocated to each cell : numAllocCellStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Number of stream PRBs reserved for Wideband signals per pool: maxWbPoolStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14562\_replaced([11213438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Total Stream PRB capacity of the L1 Pool : poolMaxNumStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* L1 Capacity reserved for RIM-RS transmission : rimRsL1Reservation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Algorithm

Sort the list of cells in the decreasing order of their cell load [Before CB009890-A-UPD002](absCellLoad)[CB009890-A-UPD002](abcConfiguredCellLoad)[End CB009890-A-UPD002]

Let,

* Sum of numAllocCellStreamPrb of all cells provided with ZAB privilege : numAllocStreamPrbZabCells = 0
* ZAB Capacity for all CsiRsPoolingGroups: zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - maxWbPoolStreamPrb
* rimRsZabReservation = rimRsL1Reservation

For : Each cell 'i' from the sorted list of cells (starting from the cell with the highest load)

If : (zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups >= numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells +  rimRsZabReservation ), then;

* Add cell 'i' to the list of cells with ZAB privilege
* numAllocStreamPrbZabCells = numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells
* rimRsZabReservation = max{0, (rimRsZabReservation - maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell)}

Else

* Do not provide ZAB privilege to cell 'i'

End

End For

where:

maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Algorithm Output

1) List of cells with ZAB privilege

Note : Newly added cells which do not have any PRBs allocated to them by the BBRM (numAllocCellStreamPrb = 0) shall not be provided the ZAB privilege.

**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `11213597`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) Cell Selection Overview

---

**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11213610`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Note: The requirement has been split into

- Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) Cell Selection Overview which is 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22586\_replaced([11213597](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIqw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

- Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) Cell Selection Input which is 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22852\_replaced([11213616](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIqxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

- Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) Cell Selection Algorithm which is 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22571\_replaced([11213633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIqyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

This split is valid from 24R1.

If rdAllowZeroAllocBypass (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15040\_replaced([11215279](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbxvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is false, no cell shall be provided the ZAB privilege and the below mentioned procedure need not be executed.

If slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), this algorithm shall run only in DL

[CB010713-A-UPD001]

If large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is true, each cell can have its subcells spread across 2 L1 pools

If "active cell amount N <=3", then

The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall not be executed, BBRM just simply return ZAB privilege as TRUE to all cells (up to 3 cells) since the L1 capacity is always respected in case of total WB transmission plus PDSCH transmission from ZAB privilege cell.

Hence, no RIM-RS reservation needs to be considered.

Else if ("active cell amount N > 3"), then

The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall be executed per L1 pool.

RIM-RS reservation needs to be considered, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22571\_replaced([11213633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIqyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

End If

End If

Where active cells shall be configured and located in same BB board.

[End CB010713-A-UPD001]

Cell selection algorithm to provide the ZAB privilege to cells in the same L1 Pool involves the following steps :

[Before PR742058]

[CB010713-A]

* From all the cells in the L1 Pool, consider only the cells which have not been granted ZAB privilege in any other L1 Pool.
* Cells which are not configured in any other L1 Pool shall always be considered.

[End CB010713-A]

* Sort [Before CB010713-A]all [CB010713-A]the selected [End CB010713-A]cells in the decreasing order of their absolute loads (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14565\_replaced([11213462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[PR742058]

* In case of multiple L1 pools under same L2-RT instance, the L1 pools to execute ZAB selection should follow "consolidate cell list" with decreasing order of cell load (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25757\_replaced([11213508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End PR742058]

* Consider providing each cell with ZAB privilege as long as the L1 Pooling capacity is not exceeded or the list of cells is not exhausted.

[CB010713-A]

* For cells with subcells configured in other L1 Pools, ZAB privilege shall be granted only if there is enough capacity to provide ZAB privilege to the cell in all the L1 pools where it is configured.
* Cells which are configured also in other L1 Pools and have ZAB privilege in the other L1 Pools shall be granted ZAB privilege also in the current L1 Pool.

[End CB010713-A]

---

**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `11213616`)

**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11213629`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Algorithm Input

* List of cells in the L1 pool [Before CB010713-A] or L1 pools [End CB010713-A]
* Absolute configured load of each cell : absConfiguredCellLoad (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14565\_replaced([11213462](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Number of stream PRBs allocated to each cell : numAllocCellStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Number of stream PRBs reserved for Wideband signals per pool: maxWbPoolStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14562\_replaced([11213438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Total Stream PRB capacity of the L1 Pool : poolMaxNumStreamPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* L1 Capacity reserved for RIM-RS transmission : rimRsL1Reservation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Requested RIM-RS PRBs of each cell in the pooling period, streamPrbDemandRim (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[PR742058]

* In case of multiple L1 pools under same L2-RT instance, the L1 pools to execute ZAB selection should follow "consolidate cell list" with decreasing order of cell load (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25757\_replaced([11213508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End PR742058]

[CB010713-A]

* L1 Capacity reserved for Cells which have ZAB privilege in other L1 Pools : zabReserveCellsOtherPools (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21675\_replaced([11213557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* For each L1 Pool 'p' except the current L1 Pool configured in BBRM
* Number of stream PRBs reserved for Wideband signals for the L1 Pool 'p' : maxWbPoolStreamPrb(p) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14562\_replaced([11213438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Total Stream PRB capacity of the L1 Pool 'p' : poolMaxNumStreamPrb(p) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* L1 Capacity reserved for RIM-RS transmission for the L1 Pool 'p' : rimRsL1Reservation(p) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Sum of Allocated Stream PRBs of Cells with ZAB privilege in L1 Pool 'p' : numAllocStreamPrbZabL1Pool(p)
* If the ZAB algorithm has not yet been executed in L1 Pool 'p'; then, numAllocStreamPrbZabL1Pool(p) = 0
* End For

[End CB010713-A]
