**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-5**  (ID: `11213633`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) Cell Selection Algorithm

---

**3.31.5.8.0-7.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11213647`)

Zero Allocation Bypass
Algorithm:

[CB010713-A]

Select the following cells from the L1 Pool :

* Cells which do not have subcells configured in any other L1 Pool
* Cells which do have subcells configured in other L1 Pools and do not have ZAB privilege in the other Pools

[End CB010713-A]

Sort the list of cells in the decreasing order of their cell load (absConfiguredCellLoad)

Let,

* Sum of numAllocCellStreamPrb of all cells provided with ZAB privilege : numAllocStreamPrbZabCells = [Before CB010713-A] 0 [CB010713-A] zabReserveCellsOtherPools [End CB010713-A].
* ZAB Capacity for all CsiRsPoolingGroups: zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - maxWbPoolStreamPrb
* rimRsZabReservation = rimRsL1Reservation
* [CNI-110226] currentL1Pool = The current L1 Pool where ZAB procedure is being executed[End CNI-110226]

For : Each cell 'i' from the sorted list of cells (starting from the cell with the highest load)

[Before CNI-110226]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true,

If cell 'i' requests RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period (streamPrbDemandRim[i] >0) ,

* rimRsZabReservation = rimRsZabReservation -  streamPrbDemandRim[i]

End If

End If

[CNI-110226]

If : (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE AND cell ‘i’ has its primary subcell in currentL1Pool) // Remove RIM-RS demand required by cell 'i' in currentL1Pool since it can be accommodated in the Minimum Allocation of the cell

If : actBbPoolTddFr1Enh = TRUE

* rimRsZabReservation = max{0, (rimRsZabReservation -  streamPrbDemandRim[i])}

Else

* rimRsZabReservation = max{0, (rimRsZabReservation - maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell)}

End If

End If

[End CNI-110226]

If : (zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups >= numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells + max{0, rimRsZabReservation} ), then;

[CB010713-A]

If : (cell 'i' has subcells configured in other L1 pools),

For : Each L1 Pool 'p' where cell 'i' is configured, except the currentL1Pool

[Before CNI-110226]

If : (poolMaxNumStreamPrb(p) < maxWbPoolStreamPrb(p) + rimRsL1Reservation(p)  + numAllocStreamPrbZabL1Pool(p) + numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)(p))

* Do not provide ZAB privilege to cell 'i'.
* Continue to evaluate next cell.

End If

[CNI-110226]

Let,

* maxRequiredStreamPrbPool(p) = maxWbPoolStreamPrb(p) + rimRsL1Reservation(p) + numAllocStreamPrbZabL1Pool(p) + numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)(p)

If : (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE AND cell ‘i’ has its primary subcell in L1 Pool 'p') // Remove RIM-RS demand required by cell 'i' in Pool 'p' since it can be accommodated in the Minimum Allocation of the cell

If : actBbPoolTddFr1Enh = TRUE

* maxRequiredStreamPrbPool(p) = max{0, (maxRequiredStreamPrbPool(p) -  streamPrbDemandRim[i])}

Else

* maxRequiredStreamPrbPool(p) = max{0, (maxRequiredStreamPrbPool(p) -  maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell)}

End If

End If

If : (poolMaxNumStreamPrb(p) < maxRequiredStreamPrbPool (p))

* Do not provide ZAB privilege to cell 'i' in currentL1Pool.

If : (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE AND cell ‘i’ has its primary subcell in currentL1Pool) // Add back the RIM-RS demand required by cell 'i' in currentL1Pool to the RIM reservation since the cell did not get the ZAB privilege

If : actBbPoolTddFr1Enh = TRUE

* rimRsZabReservation = rimRsZabReservation + streamPrbDemandRim[i]

Else

* rimRsZabReservation = rimRsZabReservation + maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell

End If

End If

* Continue to evaluate next cell in currentL1Pool

End If

[End CNI-110226]

End For

End If

[End CB010713-A]

* Add cell 'i' to the list of cells with ZAB privilege
* numAllocStreamPrbZabCells = numAllocCellStreamPrb (i) + numAllocStreamPrbZabCells

[CB010713-A]

If : (cell 'i' has subcells configured in other L1 pools), then;

For each L1 Pool 'p' where cell 'i' is configured, except the currentL1Pool

* numAllocStreamPrbZabL1Pool(p) = numAllocStreamPrbZabL1Pool(p) + numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)(p)

[Before CNI-110226]

If : (cell 'i' has its primary subcell in L1 Pool 'p'), then;

* rimRsL1Reservation(p) = max{0, (rimRsL1Reservation(p) - maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell)}

End If

[CNI-110226]

If : (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE AND cell ‘i’ has its primary subcell in L1 Pool 'p') // Remove RIM-RS demand required by cell 'i' in Pool 'p' from RIM reservation in Pool 'p' since the cell will get ZAB privilege also in Pool 'p'

If : actBbPoolTddFr1Enh = TRUE

* rimRsL1Reservation(p) = max{0, (rimRsL1Reservation(p) - streamPrbDemandRim[i])}

Else

* rimRsL1Reservation(p) = max{0, (rimRsL1Reservation(p) - maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell)}

End If

End If

[End CNI-110226]

End For

End If

[End CB010713-A]

Else

* Do not provide ZAB privilege to cell 'i'

[Before CNI-110226]

* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true,

If cell 'i' requests RIM-RS transmission for the pooling period (streamPrbDemandRim[i]>0),

rimRsZabReservation = rimRsZabReservation +  streamPrbDemandRim[i]

End If

End If

[CNI-110226]

If : (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE AND cell ‘i’ has its primary subcell in currentL1Pool) // Add back the RIM-RS demand required by cell 'i' in currentL1Pool to the RIM reservation since the cell did not get the ZAB privilege

If : actBbPoolTddFr1Enh = TRUE

* rimRsZabReservation = rimRsZabReservation + streamPrbDemandRim[i]

Else

* rimRsZabReservation = rimRsZabReservation + maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell

End If

End If

[End CNI-110226]

End If

End For

where:

maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB010713-A]

numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)(p) = numAllocCellStreamPrb for cell 'i' in L1 Pool 'p' (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB010713-A]

Algorithm Output

1) List of cells with ZAB privilege

Note : Newly added cells which do not have any PRBs allocated to them by the BBRM (numAllocCellStreamPrb = 0) shall not be provided the ZAB privilege.

---

### 3.31.5.9 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass

#### 3.31.5.9.0-1 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Overview (ID: 12804798)

**3.31.5.9.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12804812`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
When slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_7785\_replaced([11278788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNePvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for DL, if a certain number of cells are allocated some symbols to transmit wideband signals (CSI-RS for channel acquisition, or TRS) in a slot, the other cells in the same L1 Pool are not allowed to perform any transmission in the same symbols of the slot. Such symbols are referred to as Zero Allocation Symbols because no PRBs are allocated for any DL transmission on these symbols.

However, if partialZABAllowed is true in DL, BBRM can allow specific cells to bypass this restriction proportionally to the historical usage of non-GBR traffic and GBR/DC demand, considering the algorithm described below, and perform DL transmissions in the Zero Allocation symbols. This is referred to as Partial Zero Allocation Bypass (ZAB) as explained in this section.

Partial ZAB privilege is granted by BBRM to the cells of an L1 Pool every pooling period, such that the sum of:

* the total number of streams PRBs allocated to the Partial ZAB cells and
* the Wideband stream PRBs required by the cells transmitting the Wideband signals.
* max stream PRBs required for RIM-RS transmission by the cells that detect Remote Interference and have not been granted partial ZAB privilege. If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed and actBbPoolTddFr1Enh are true, requested stream PRBs for RIM-RS transmission are only provided by the cells that request RIM-RS transmission in the pooling period and have not been granted partial ZAB privilege.

does not exceed the L1 Pool's capacity.

poolMaxNumStreamPrb >= Sum{Allocated Stream PRBs to cells with Partial ZAB privilege} + Sum[all subpools per pool]{maxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp}

where,

poolMaxNumStreamPrb = The maximum amount of stream PRBs available on the L1 Pool level described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

maxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp = The maximum amount of stream PRBs available for Wideband signalling in the L1Subpool given for DL in NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6539\_replaced([11212289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note: The allocation of RIMRS is ensured in the stream PRBs allocated to cells in the first step of the partial ZAB algorithm.

The partial ZAB algorithm aims to allocate static symbol PRB resources among multiple cells based on their demand and load, ensuring fair and efficient distribution. It works in several rounds (RIM-RS allocation, Round 1 resource allocation, Round 2 resource allocation, and remaining resources allocation), progressively allocating partial ZAB resources and updating the remaining capacity and demand.

* Note: Round 1 and Round 2 are only executed for the current L1 pool the cell belongs to, even if large baseband pooling is enabled.
* The RIMRS allocation for the cells with RIMRS demand is executed.
* Then, when there is still remaining ZAB capacity, as long as they satisfy the L1 Capacity condition in the formula above, the first round of Partial ZAB PRB allocation based on their loads is described in ([12819683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MQkrwKk5EfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* Then, if there are remaining resources in the first round of partial ZAB resource allocation, and, as long as they satisfy the L1 Capacity condition in the formula above, the partial ZAB Algorithm in Round-2 in ([12823739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mhO_0KpwEfCrANRYxAlR5A)) is executed.
* Finally, if there are remaining partial ZAB resources, after the step above (i.e., round-2), the cells (including earlier excluded cells) are sorted out with {numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)- numAllocPartialZABPrbRound2> 0} in increasing order. (i.e., remaining partial ZAB PRB in ([12824293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SfRqYKqREfCrANRYxAlR5A) ) and used as input to the remaining step of the partial ZAB algorithm.

BBRM informs the L2-PS of each cell in every pooling period about the partial ZAB PRBs allocation that is granted.

Newly set up cells during the pooling period shall suspend all DL scheduling and other wideband transmissions until the next Pooling Period. This is to prevent exceeding the L1 Pool capacity in cases where WB transmissions in the new cell collide with PDSCH transmissions from a cell with ZAB privilege.

The L1 pool to execute Partial ZAB selection should follow "unified cell list" with decreasing order of cell load as specified in RIMRS, round 1 and round 2, and the remaining partial ZAB PRB allocation. As the cell lists with ZAB privilege differ in various steps of the algorithms, i.e., RIMRS, Round-1, Round-2, and the remaining ZAB prb allocation, the cell lists are unified.

**[05533578]**

Note:

* For each L1 DL pool, 3 csirsPoolingGroups initialized with L1Pool DL max wideband signal stream PRBs as available stream PRBs , and csirsPoolingGroupId is from 0 to 2.
* BBRM maintains a list of active cell's
* The current implementation always assumes 3 CSI-RS pooling groups. In case there is no active cell in other pooling groups, it results in unnecessary loss of symbol periods for presumed CSI-RS transmissions from other pooling groups.
* This solution addresses the problem that it is assumed that all CSI-RS Pooling Groups are active at any given instance. If not all CSI-RS Pooling Groups are active, symbols are wasted due to applying ZA limitations irrespective of whether other pooling groups are active or not.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true or slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed is true,

If "activeCsiRsPoolingGroups N=1", then

// 2-Sector Case: In a 2-sector deployment, only one CSI-RS Pooling Group is active. Other CSI-RS Pooling Group offsets and related Zero Allocation  can be ignored.

The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall not be executed, BBRM just simply return ZAB privilege as TRUE to all cells (up to 3 cells) since the L1 capacity is always respected in case of total WB transmission plus PDSCH transmission from ZAB privilege cell.

All cells in the corresponding csirspoolingGroupId are allowed to use othercsirsPoolingGroup CSI-RS-ACQ and CSI-IM symbols.

[Before PR881837]

Else if ("activeCsiRsPoolingGroups N>1"), then

// more than one CS-RS Pooling Group's Active

[PR881837]

Else if ("activeCsiRsPoolingGroups 1<N<3"), then

// 3-Sector Case: In a 3-sector deployment, typically two CSI-RS Pooling Groups are active, while a third remains inactive

Two CSI-RS Pooling Groups are active. The third CSI-RS Pooling Group remains inactive. The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall not be executed.

For all the cells in the two active CSI-RS Pooling groups: ZAB privilege shall be considered for the symbols (used to transmit wideband signals like 'CSI-RS' or 'TRS'), which are in the slots on the inactive csirsPoolingGroup. This shall be considered irrespective whether ZAB privilege is granted or not in the active CSI-RS Pooling group(s).

Though each active CSI-RS Pooling group has to apply the Zero Allocation rules for the symbols (used to transmit wideband signals like 'CSI-RS' or 'TRS'), which are in the slots on the other active CSI-RS Pooling group.

Else if ("activeCsiRsPoolingGroups N>=3"), then

// All three CS-RS Pooling Group's Active

I

nternal Note: The number of activeCsiRsPoolingGroups is internally derived in the L2PS submodules (EFS). Between BBRM and L2PS-SCH, in the ResourceResp message from BBRM to L2-SCH, a new field “field activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask” has been added:

activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask = 0x1 -> // 0th bit set : cells present in csirsPoolingGroupId=0 only

activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask = 0x2 -> //1st bit set: cells present in csirsPoolingGroupId=1 only

activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask = 0x4 -> //2nd bit set: cells present in csirsPoolingGroupId=2 only

Based on the information from activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask, the amount of activeCsiRsPoolingGroups is calculated.

If activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask=0x1 or activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask=0x2 or activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask=0x4, ZAB grant in L2-PS SCH is overwritten.

In every pooling period, for each L1 Pool BBRM traverses through the cell list and computes activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask based on the csi-rs pooling group Id information of each cell.

When a cell is newly added or deleted, activeCsiRsPoolingGroupMask will be updated in the next BB period.

This functionality is controlled by a rd-parameter:

rdZabOptimization   - This parameter enables/disables the ZAB optimization solution.

default: 3     Online modificable. Step Size: 1[0..3], Online Modifiable: Yes"

0 - disabled,

1 - enable single csiRsPoolingGroup active solution,

2 - enable two csiRsPoolingGroups active solution,

3 - enable Both, one or two csiRsPoolingGroups active solution.

[End PR881837]

The procedure mentioned in this requirement shall be executed per L1 pool.

End If

Where active cells shall be configured and located in same BB board.

ZAB procedure shall be executed sequentially over all L1 Pools configured in the BBRM in every pooling period only after the intra L1 SP pooling procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13233\_replaced([11212393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has been successfully executed on all L1 subpools of all configured L1 Pools.

The L1 pools to execute ZAB selection should follow "consolidate cell list" with decreasing order of cell load (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25757\_replaced([11213508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDtvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

End If

[End 05533578]

Note: Due to the available L1 Pool capacity and the allocated PRBs to all the cells in the pool, none of the cells in the pool may be provided with the partial ZAB privilege.

#### 3.31.5.9.0-2 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Algorithm Input (ID: 12819678)

**3.31.5.9.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12819679`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
\* List of cells in the L1 pool
\* totalStreamPrbDemand ([12804810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5D5wsJ6yEfCkxIKMlo4L6w))
\* numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) : Number of stream PRBs allocated to each cell as specified in ([12705604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BizfAGFPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
\* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb: Number of stream per cell as specified in ([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_kw-supvsee-aqvopbp1qhq&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconf"))
\* maxWbPoolStreamPrb: Number of stream PRBs reserved for Wideband signals per pool as specified in (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14562\_replaced([11213438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
\* maxHistCellStreamPrb: Maximum Historical Stream PRB for Partial ZAB Allocation as specified in ([12819675)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI__mQZcKkxEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
\* poolMaxNumStreamPrb: Total Stream PRB capacity of the L1 Pool as specified in (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
\* rimRsL1Reservation: L1 Capacity reserved for RIM-RS transmission as specified in (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15671\_replaced([11213526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDufvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
\* streamPrbDemandRim: Requested RIM-RS PRBs of each cell in the pooling period as specified in (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

#### 3.31.5.9.0-3 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Partial ZAB PRB Allocation for Cell with RIMRS Demands (ID: 12823121)

**3.31.5.9.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12823122`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
Algorithm:

Select the following cells from the L1 Pool:

* Cells with PRBs reserved for RIM-RS are determined as follows: if actBbPoolTddFr1Enh = FALSE, all cells are included; otherwise, only cells with streamPrbDemandRim[i] > 0 are included.
* Exclude the cells that do have "numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)" = 0, i.e., when the cell is newly added.

Let,

* ZAB Capacity for all CsiRsPoolingGroups in the current pool: partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups = poolMaxNumStreamPrb  – maxWbPoolStreamPrb
* rimRsZabReservation  = rimRsL1Reservation, Note: if "rimRsZabReservation ==0", the following algorithm, i.e., RIMRS algorithm, is not executed.
* currentL1Pool = The current L1 Pool where the ZAB procedure is being executed

If: (partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups  > = max{0, **rimRsZabReservation}** **, then;**

For: Each cell 'i' from the list of selected cells in the current pool

Let partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) be initialized to zero.

If: (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE)

If: actBbPoolTddFr1Enh = TRUE

partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) = partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) + streamPrbDemandRim(i)

Else

partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) = partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) + maxNumRimRsStreamPrbPerCell(i)

End If

partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) = min( partialZabAllocatedPrb(i), numAllocCellStreamPrb(i))

Add cell 'i' to the list of cells with ZAB privilege

End If

End For

partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups = partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups - rimRsZabReservation

Else

Break the partial ZAB algorithm. //The partial ZAB capacity can not be allocated to any cells due to the RIM-RS allocation restriction.

End If

Algorithm Output

1. List of cells with ZAB privilege in RIMRS allocation step.
2. zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups
3. partialZabAllocatedPrb(i). [Note: if cell is FDD technology, the value will be zero.]

---

#### 3.31.5.9.0-4 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Partial Zero Allocation Bypass based Resource Allocation Algorithm (Round-1) (ID: 12819683)

**3.31.5.9.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12823136`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
The following additional inputs are considered for the algorithm:

* partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups  and partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) from ([12823121](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_crpEcqpUEfCrANRYxAlR5A))

Algorithm

* Algorithm is executed when partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups  is greater than zero.
* Exclude cells with “totStreamPrbDemand” ([12804810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5D5wsJ6yEfCkxIKMlo4L6w)) less than “ZAB threshold(partialZabAllocThreshold)” ([12823126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Kh4-5KpWEfCrANRYxAlR5A))
* Exclude the cell that does have "numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)" = 0, i.e., when the cell is added newly.
* Sort the cells in the increasing order of [Before PR875285] min{numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) - partialZabAllocatedPrb(i), min{totStreamPrbDemand(i), maxHistCellStreamPrb (i)}}. In the case of several cells having the same value resulting from the outer min operation and if they have different values from the inner min operation, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of the result of the inner min operation. [PR875285] min{numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) - partialZabAllocatedPrb(i), min{totStreamPrbDemand(i), AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i) + streamPrbDemandDcGbr[i]+ streamPrbDemandGbr[i])). Note: If several cells have the same value after sorting the list, select them at random in order. [End PR875285]

For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1: where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

* AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i) = min (totStreamPrbDemand(i),maxHistCellStreamPrb(i), zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups\* totStreamPrbDemand(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{totStreamPrbDemand(k)})
* AllocPartialZabStreamPrb (i) =  max{0, min{ AllocPartialZabStreamPrb (i), (numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)- partialZabAllocatedPrb(i))}}
* Add cell 'i' to the list of cells with ZAB privilege
* partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups = partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups – AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i) //Update the remainig capacity for current L1Pool
* partialZabAllocatedPrb(i)= partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) + AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i)//Update the PRB allocated for cell “i”

End for

Algorithm Output

1. List of cells with ZAB privilege for round 1
2. partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups
3. partialZabAllocatedPrb(i)

---

#### 3.31.5.9.0-5 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Partial Zero Allocation Bypass based Resource Allocation Algorithm (Round-2) (ID: 12823739)

**3.31.5.9.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12824043`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
The following additional inputs are considered for the algorithm:

* partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups and partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) from ([12819683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MQkrwKk5EfCrANRYxAlR5A))
* streamPrbDemandRound2(i) ([12823797](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fI_GRap4EfCrANRYxAlR5A))

Algorithm

* Algorithm is executed when partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups  is greater than zero.
* Exclude cells with “totStreamPrbDemand” ([12804810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5D5wsJ6yEfCkxIKMlo4L6w)) less than “ZAB threshold(partialZabAllocThreshold)” ([12823126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Kh4-5KpWEfCrANRYxAlR5A)).
* Exclude the cell that does have "numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)" = 0, i.e., when the cell is added newly.
* Sort the list of the cells from Round1 in the increasing order of min{ numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)- partialZabAllocatedPrb(i), streamPrbDemandRound2(i)}. In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different streamPrbDemandRound2 value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their streamPrbDemandRound2 value.

For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1: where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

* AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i) = min (streamPrbDemandRound2(i), zabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups \* streamPrbDemandRound2 (i)/sum[N >k>=i]{ streamPrbDemandRound2 (k)})
* AllocPartialZabStreamPrb (i) =  max{0, min{ AllocPartialZabStreamPrb (i), (numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)- partialZabAllocatedPrb(i))}}
* Add cell 'i' to the list of cells with ZAB privilege
* partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups = partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups – AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i) //Update the remainig capacity for current L1Pool
* partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) = partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) + AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i) )//Update the PRB allocated for cell “i”

End for

Algorithm Output

1. List of cells with ZAB privilege for round 2
2. partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups
3. partialZabAllocatedPrb(i)

---

#### 3.31.5.9.0-6 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Partial Zero Allocation Bypass based Resource Allocation for the Remaining ZAB Resources (ID: 12824293)

**3.31.5.9.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `12824423`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
The following additional inputs are considered for the algorithm:

* partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups and partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) from ([12823739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_mhO_0KpwEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb(i) specified in ([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_kw-supvsee-aqvopbp1qhq&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconf"))
* [CB014543-G-UPD002] totalStreamPrbDemand[i] specified in ([12804810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5D5wsJ6yEfCkxIKMlo4L6w "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_5d5wsj6yefckxikmlo4l6w&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconf")) [End CB014543-G-UPD002]

Algorithm

* Sort the list of all cells, including all removed cells from the previous steps [Before CB014543-G-UPD002] in increasing order of  (numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)- partialZabAllocatedPrb(i)). [CB014543-G-UPD002] in decreasing order of their cell demand totalStreamPrbDemand[i] ([12804810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5D5wsJ6yEfCkxIKMlo4L6w "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_5d5wsj6yefckxikmlo4l6w&oslc_config.context=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconf")). Note: if multiple cells have the same order, their selection order will be randomized. [End CB014543-G-UPD002]
* Exclude the cell that does have "numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)" = 0, i.e., when the cell is added newly.

For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1: where i is the index of the sorted cell and N is the number of cells in the sorted list

If: (partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups > 0), then;

If (numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)- partialZabAllocatedPrb(i)) <=partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups

AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i) = numAllocCellStreamPrb(i)- partialZabAllocatedPrb(i)

Else

AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i) = partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups

End If

* Add cell 'i' to the list of cells with ZAB privilege
* partialZabAllocatedPrb(i)= partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) + AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i) )//Update the PRB allocated for cell “i”

Else

* Do not provide ZAB privilege to cell(i) in the current L1Pool.
* Continue to evaluate the next cell in the current L1Pool.

End If

* partialZabAllocCellPrb (i) =  Floor (partialZabAllocatedPrb(i)/maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb(i) // convert stream partial ZAB prb of cell(i) to cell prb.
* partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups = partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups - AllocPartialZabStreamPrb(i) + (partialZabAllocatedPrb(i) mod  maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb(i)) //Update the remaining capacity for current L1Pool
* Note: If partialZabAllocCellPrb(i) < maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb(i), then don't add the cell(i) to the ZAB privilege list, and do not update partialZabCapacityForAllCsiRsPoolingGroups.

End for

Algorithm Output

1. List of cells with ZAB privilege from RIMRS, Round-1, Round-2, and remaining ZAB resource allocation algorithms
2. partialZabAllocatedPrb(i)
3. partialZabAllocCellPrb (i)

Note: partialZabAllocCellPrb (i) and the unified list of cells with ZAB privilege are indicated to L2PS.

Note: As the cell lists with ZAB privilege differ in various steps of the algorithms, i.e., RIMRS, Round-1, Round-2, and the remaining ZAB PRB allocation, the cell lists are unified.

---

#### 3.31.5.9.0-7 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Determination of Total Stream PRB Demand for Cells in Partial ZAB Algorithm (ID: 12804810)

**3.31.5.9.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `12817933`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
BBRM shall calculate Total Stream PRB demand of all cells in the L1 Pool.

**Algorithm Input :**

* List of cells in the pool
* streamPrbDemandDcGbr, streamPrbDemandGbr, streamPrbDemandNonGbr of each cell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14549\_replaced([11213394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxConfiguredCellStreamPrb of each cell described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21671\_replaced([11213493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxIDsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**Algorithm Output :**

* totalStreamPrbDemand[i]: total Stream demand of Cell i, i ϵ {0, 1 .. N-1} where N is the number of Cells

**Algorithm Steps:**

For each cell i:

totalStreamPrbDemand[i]=streamPrbDemandDcGbr[i]+ streamPrbDemandGbr[i]+ streamPrbDemandNonGbr[i])

---

#### 3.31.5.9.0-8 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Maximum Stream PRB Limit for Partial ZAB Algorithm with Historical Usage Allocation (ID: 12819675)

**3.31.5.9.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `12819676`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
This section defines the maximum stream PRB allocation limit for a cell that needs to be considered for partial ZAB historical usage allocation.. Here, the algorithm considers both historical non-GBR and DC-GBR and GBR demand.

maxHistCellStreamPrb (i) =max {(rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsageFdd or rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsageTdd)*maxPcellStreamPrb(i), (1+ rdPrbPooilngOverAllocFactor)* (AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i) + streamPrbDemandDcGbr[i]+ streamPrbDemandGbr[i]).

Where,

* streamPrbDemandDcGbr, streamPrbDemandGbr  of each cell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14549\_replaced ([11213394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsageFdd ([12879240](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI__JJj47M7EfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), when slowPrbPoolingFddFr1EnhAllowed = True
* rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsageTdd ([12879244](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Hv1F3LM8EfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), when If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True
* rdPrbPoolngOverAllocFactor ([12722864)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_OvVvKW3vEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR ([12721308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HO6TYG0aEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* maxPcellStreamlPrb(i) is the maximum number of DL primary sub-cell PRBs that are calculated in ([12739292](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25v34HkDEfCdZt6bzaG3fw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
* i is cell index

---

#### 3.31.5.9.0-9 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Determination of Minimum Partial ZAB Threshold (ID: 12823126)

**3.31.5.9.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `12823128`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
This requirement determines the minimum threshold for partial ZAB allocation, by which the Algorithm decides whether to consider the cell for ZAB privilege or exclude it from the ZAB privilege list.

Algorithm Input:

* rdPartialZabAllocRatio ([12824446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DC3C4aqVEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* dlBandwidth: Cell DL Bandwidth (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Algorithm:

* partialZabAllocThreshold = rdPartialZabAllocRatio \* dlBandwidth

Algorithm Output:

* partialZabAllocThreshold

---

#### 3.31.5.9.0-10 Partial Zero Allocation Bypass Determination of Stream PRB demand for Partial ZAB Resource Allocation in Round-2 (ID: 12823797)

**3.31.5.9.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `12823798`)

Partial Zero Allocation Bypass
This algorithm computes PRB demand for Round 2 in the partial ZAB resource allocation algorithm.

Algorithm Input:

* rdPrbPoolingGracefulAllocFactor - ([12722864)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_OvVvKW3vEfCmnYHxzZN44w)
* AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR/AvgUsedStreamUlPRBnonGBR  ([12721308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HO6TYG0aEfCmnYHxzZN44w))
* streamPrbAllocRound1(i) = partialZabAllocatedPrb(i), as specified  in Round-1 ([12819683](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_MQkrwKk5EfCrANRYxAlR5A))
* streamPrbDemandDcGbr, streamPrbDemandGbr  of each cell, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14549\_replaced ([11213394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxHcoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Algorithm:

* streamPrbDemandRound2(i) = max{totStreamPrbDemand(i) - streamPrbAllocRound1(i),  rdPrbPoolingGracefulAllocFactor \* (AvgUsedStreamDlPRBnonGBR(i)  + streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i)+ streamPrbDemandGbr(i) ) - streamPrbAllocRound1(i))

Algorithm Output:

* streamPrbDemandRound2(i)

---

### 3.31.5.10 Subcell Deactivation Procedures

#### 3.31.5.10.0-1 Subcell Deactivation Procedures Overview (ID: 11213656)

**3.31.5.10.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11213663`)

Subcell Deactivation Procedures
When supporting dynamic PRB pooling, there is also a need to pool the number of subcells configured in L1 Pool / L1 Subpool.

The subcell pooling could be based on multiple factors and can be run in DL or UL. Each subcell pooling procedure is enabled/disabled based on a flag received from higher layers.

The list of subcell pooling procedures and is mentioned below.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Deactivation Procedure | TDD |  | FDD |  |
| DL Feature Flag | UL Feature Flag | DL Feature Flag | UL Feature Flag |  |
| Subcell Deactivation to support cells not supporting UL PRB Muting (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15396\_replaced([11213669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | Not supported | TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed | Not supported | Not supported |
| L1 Arm Capacity based Subcell Deactivation (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18301\_replaced([11213855](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed | ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed | Not supported | Not supported |

The current list of such procedures is required only for FR1.

Certain subcell deactivation procedures need to run in a particular order.

In UL, the following order should be followed if and when the respective feature flags are enabled:

* L1 Arm Capacity based Subcell Deactivation (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18301\_replaced([11213855](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Subcell Deactivation to support cells not supporting UL PRB Muting (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15396\_replaced([11213669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

#### 3.31.5.10.1 UL Subcell Deactivation to support cells not supporting UL PRB Muting

##### 3.31.5.10.1.1 Subcell Deactivation Framework

###### 3.31.5.10.1.1.0-1 Subcell Deactivation Framework Overview (ID: 11213679)

**3.31.5.10.1.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11213685`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
The cells which are connected to RF units that do not support UL PRB muting requires the max. stream PRB capacity of its UL subcell in UL L1 fronthaul even though only few PRBs are scheduled in the subcell. However, UL L1 fronthaul capacity of our baseband unit is limited too and is given by hidden NIDD parameter maxNumFHStreamPRBULL1Pool. As a result, high capacity cell sets (For ex. 3 cells with 4 layers UL MU-MIMO cell set) cannot be enabled, independently of UL PRB muting support of their connected RF units, unless an additional BB pooling mechanism is applied to limit the usage of UL L1 fronthaul resources in L1 pool, in addition to existing UL PRB pooling mechanism described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

So, UL subcell deactivation mechanism described in this section is introduced to avoid overload in UL L1 fronthaul. The UL subcell deactivation mechanism shall work on the scope of L1 pool and available UL stream PRB reception capacity in the L1 fronthaul interface per L1 pool shall be retrieved from the hidden NIDD (NRBTS/bbPoolCapacity.maxNumFHStreamPRBULL1Pool). Only the load-metric based UL subcell deactivation algorithm shall be supported. It shall work on subcell resolution and primary subcells of all cells shall always be activated to guarantee all UL reception except PUSCH. During every BB pooling period, the secondary subcells are activated considering cell load and UL stream PRB reception capacity in L1 fronthaul.

This functionality is applied only in UL in FR1-TDD deployments and it can be enabled/disabled via the C-Plane flag TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: When TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed is set to true, it is assumed that the configured UL L1 fronthaul capacity of the L1 pool shall atleast be large enough to activate the primary subcells of all cells in an L1 pool.

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.1.0-2 Subcell Deactivation Framework Interworking with UL PRB Pooling (ID: 11213691)

**3.31.5.10.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11213695`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
In BBRM, UL subcell deactivation mechanism shall work in combination with UL PRB pooling algorithm described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10384\_replaced([11212979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), during every BB pooling period, UL subcell deactivation procedure shall be executed just before the inter-L1 subpool UL PRB resource sharing algorithm described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10384\_replaced([11212979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the resultant proposed active UL subcell list, namely proposedActiveUlSubcellList (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15439\_replaced([11213708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), shall be considered in inter-L1 subpool algorithm executed in the same BB pooling period for the calculation of maximum cell capacity for each of the cells in the L1 pool ( see details in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). However, for each cell i in L1 pool, similar to new UL L1 subpool capacities, proposedActiveUlSubcellList(i) shall be considered as the new active UL subcell list, namely currentActiveUlSubcellList(i), only for the next BB pooling period and only after the successful re-configuration of L1 subpool capacities between L2 & L1 as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The details of the handling of success/failure cases of L1 subpool capacity re-configuration procedure is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In next BB pooling period, the resultant currentActiveUlSubcellList(i) from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10389\_replaced([11213186](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be applied to the intra-L1 subpool UL PRB pooling algorithm described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the calculation of maximum capacity for each of the cells in L1 subpool and it shall be applied for L2PS scheduling at the same SFN and slot as the resultant UL PRB grant (numAllocCellPrb) from intra-L1 subpool UL PRB pooling algorithm so that both are aligned (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6959\_replaced([11213357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxG1mfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

##### 3.31.5.10.1.2 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-1 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Subcell Deactivation Algorithm (ID: 11213708)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11213713`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
When TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed is set to TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_9169\_replaced([11279052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpTbm_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), UL subcell deactivation procedure described below shall be executed every BB pooling period, to limit the required number of UL L1 FH stream PRB of the L1 pool to value lower than configured L1 UL FH capacity, given by NIDD parameter maxNumFHStreamPRBULL1Pool. The details of execution timeline of subcell deactivation procedure in combination with UL PRB pooling algorithm and the subsequent usage of the resultant proposed active UL subcell list (proposedActiveUlSubcellList) for each of the cells in L1 pool are described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15493\_replaced([11213691](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Algorithm Input:

* Algorithm Input parameters are described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15442\_replaced([11213718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Algorithm Output:

* The proposed list of active UL subcells (proposedActiveUlSubcellList(i)) for each of the cell i in the L1 pool.

Algorithm Steps:

* Initialization of subcell deactivation algorithm parameters as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15445\_replaced([11213744](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* If the trigger conditions specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15784\_replaced([11213766](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ44fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is satisfied:
* [PR705300] Deactivate the UL secondary subcells for cells for which UL MUMIMO is disabled as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22224\_replaced([11213776](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ44_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End PR705300]
* compute numActiveSubcells(i) for each of cells i in L1 pool using the subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15454\_replaced([11213789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ45fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* [PR701399] Run the subcell-reactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20567\_replaced([11213799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ45_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to utilise the residual L1 FH capacity, if any. [End PR701399]
* Derive the proposedActiveUlSubcellList for each of the cell i in L1 pool for the next BB pooling period from the computed numActiveSubcells(i) from the above steps.

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-2 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Input Parameters for Load-Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm (ID: 11213718)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11213736`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
The input parameters for the load metric based subcell deactivation algorithm are described below:

* Cell List per L1 pool.
* The configured UL subcell list for each of the cell in L1 pool.
* if ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_18301\_replaced([11213855](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is triggered in the L1 Pool, the available number of active subcells in UL determined at the end of the L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_18313\_replaced([11213949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKgAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* The UL PRB muting capability of each of the cell in L1 pool. If the UL PRB muting capability of a cell is not known to BBRM, then the cell shall be considered as a non-mutable cell.
* The maximum UL non-mutable empty subcell PRBs for each of the cell, namely maxULNonMutedStreamPRBTDDCell, given by hidden NIDD parameter NRBTS.maxULNonMutedPRBTDDCell
* Total UL processing stream PRB capacity per L1 pool given by poolMaxNumStreamPrb (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10391\_replaced([11213021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFAZPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* The minimum stream PRB capacity for each of the cell i in L1 pool, given by numMinStreamPrbAlloc (i) in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  Note, If NRBTS/NRCELL.actUlCgType2 is set to True, numMinStreamPrbAlloc shall include mandatory reservation for Configured Grant as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* The configured maximum L1 UL fronthaul stream PRB capacity per L1 pool given by hidden NIDD parameter NRBTS/bbPoolCapacity.maxNumFHStreamPRBULL1Pool.
* The PRB demand for each of the cell i in the L1 pool, given by [CB008600-F] PrbDemandDcGbr(i), [End CB008600-F] PrbDemandGbr(i), PrbDemandNonGbr(i), prbDemandCg(i) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-3 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Initialization of Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Parameters (ID: 11213744)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11213760`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
This requirement the initialization of parameters required for the subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15454\_replaced([11213789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ45fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* Convert the following input parameters corresponding to each cell i into equivalent stream PRB using computation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxULNonMutedPRBTDDCell(i) --> maxULNonMutedStreamPRBTDDCell(i)
* PrbDemandGbr(i) --> streamPrbDemandGbr(i)
* PrbDemandNonGbr(i) --> streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)
* PrbDemandCg(i) --> streamPrbDemandCg(i)
* [CB008600-F] PrbDemandDcGbr(i) --> streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i) [End CB008600-F]
* The total stream PRB demand for each of the cell i shall be calculated as sum over its PRB demand for all traffic.
* totalStreamPrbDemand(i) = streamPrbDemandGbr(i) + streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i) + streamPrbDemandCg(i)[CB008600-F] + streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i) [End CB008600-F]
* For each cell 'i' in the L1 Pool, at the start of the subcell deactivation procedure, the number of active subcells (numActiveSubcells(i)) shall consider :
* if ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_18301\_replaced([11213855](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is triggered in the L1 Pool,
* the number of active subcells in UL determined at the end of the L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_18313\_replaced([11213949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKgAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* else
* all UL subcells configured for the cell
* end if
* During the subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15454\_replaced([11213789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ45fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), numActiveSubcells(i) might be reduced to limit the L1 FH reception capacity.

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-4 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Decision To Trigger Subcell Deactivation Algorithm (ID: 11213766)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11213771`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
BBRM shall execute the subcell deactivation procedure to limit the required L1 FH stream PRBs described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15454\_replaced([11213789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ45fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) only if all the below conditions are satisfied.

* [CB009827-D] Atleast one of cells configured in L1 pool doesn't support UL PRB muting [End CB009827-D]
* Atleast one of the cells configured in L1 pool has configured UL secondary subcells.

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-5 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Subcell Deactivation for cells with UL MUMIMO disabled (ID: 11213776)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11213781`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
BBRM shall deactivate the UL secondary subcells for all cells in L1 pool which have UL-MUMIMO disabled.

As a result, For each cell i in L1 pool with UL MUMIMO disabled (NRCELL.actUlMuMimo=False):

* numActiveSubcells(i) = 1 (i.e. only the primary UL subcell is active)

Note: If UL-MUMIMO is disabled for a cell, it is never allocated with UL secondary subcells even though the remaining available L1 UL FH capacity is large enough to activate it. The rationale is that those cells never use the UL secondary subcells and there is no need for UL secondary subcell allocation.

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-6 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Subcell Deactivation Algorithm to UL Limit L1 FH Capacity (ID: 11213789)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11213795`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
This requirement describes the load metric based subcell deactivation procedure to limit the UL L1 FH capacity.

Given:

* Input parameters as given in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15442\_replaced([11213718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15445\_replaced([11213744](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* [PR705300] Updated numActiveSubcells(i) for each cell in L1 pool resultant from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22224\_replaced([11213776](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ44_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR705300]

Output:

* Resultant numActiveSubcells(i) for each of the cells in the L1 pool [Before PR701399] required to achieve the required L1 FH capacity [PR701399] used in the subsequent subcell re-activation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20567\_replaced([11213799](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ45_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End PR701399].

Steps:

* Calculate reqL1FHStreamPrbCapacity of the L1 pool as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15433\_replaced([11213812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ46fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* For each cell i in L1 pool, calculate normalizedPrbDemand as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15452\_replaced([11213833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ47fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* While reqL1FHStreamPrbCapacity > maxNumFHStreamPRBULL1Pool:
* Sort the cells in the increasing order of normalizedPrbDemand
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list
* If numActiveSubcells (i) > 1: //Atleast one subcell is required to activate its primary subcell.
* numActiveSubcells (i) = numActiveSubcells (i) - 1
* Re-calculate normalizedPrbDemand for the cell i as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15452\_replaced([11213833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ47fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Re-calculate reqL1FHStreamPrbCapacity of the L1 pool as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15433\_replaced([11213812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ46fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Break For loop //The cell list need to be re-sorted considering the changed normalizedPrbDemand of cell i
* End If
* If cell list search is exhausted without finding a matching cell for subcell deactivation
* Log a warning message due to the fact that configured L1 FH capacity is not enough even to activate the primary subcell of all cells.
* End while loop.
* End If
* End For
* End While

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-7 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Subcell Re-Activation Algorithm to re-utlise residual L1 FH Capacity (ID: 11213799)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11213805`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
This requirement describes the load metric based subcell-reactivation procedure to allocate the residual L1 FH capacity after the execution of subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15454\_replaced([11213789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ45fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Rationale: If the cells configured in the L1 pool are of mixed BW, it is possible in some cases that first low BW subcell and then high BW subcell are deactivated as per load-metric based subcell deactivation procedure. In that case, it is possible that the residual L1 FH capacity remaining might be enough to additionally support the already deactivated low BW subcell.

Let eligibleCellList shall include the cells i in the L1 pool for which atleast one UL subcell is deactivated in subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15454\_replaced([11213789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ45fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Algorithm:

* While maxNumFHStreamPRBULL1Pool - reqL1FHStreamPrbCapacity >= maxStreamPrbPerSubcell(i) of cell i with smallest UL BW in eligibleCellList
* sort cells in eligibleCellList in the decreasing order of normalizedPrbDemand
* For i = 0,1,2,3 ...N-1: where i= index of sorted cell and N is the number of cells in sorted eligibleCellList
* if maxStreamPrbPerSubcell(i) <= maxNumFHStreamPRBULL1Pool - reqL1FHStreamPrbCapacity:
* numActiveSubcells(i) ++ //Activate the subcell for cell i
* if numActiveSubcells(i) == number of active subcells for cell i given during the initialization of the subcell de-activation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15445\_replaced([11213744](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* remove the cell i from eligibleCellList
* re-calculate normalizedPrbDemand(i)
* re-calculate reqL1FHStreamPrbCapacity
* Break for loop //The cell list need to be re-sorted considering the changed normalizedPrbDemand of cell i
* End If
* End for
* End while

Output:

* Resultant numActiveSubcells(i) for each of the cells in the L1 pool required to achieve the required L1 FH capacity.

Where,

* maxNumFHStreamPRBULL1Pool is Max UL L1 FH streamPrb capacity given in  5G\_UP\_ALG\_15442\_replaced([11213718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numActiveSubcells(i) is the number of active UL subcells of cell i. Please note that this value changes during the algorithm execution and always the current value shall be taken.
* reqL1FHStreamPrbCapacity shall be calculated as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15433\_replaced([11213812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ46fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* normalizedPrbDemand(i) of a cell i shall be calculated as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15452\_replaced([11213833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ47fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxStreamPrbPerSubcell(i) for any given cell i is given by the cell's UL bandwidth, namely ulBandwidth (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) converted into stream PRBs according to its subcell type as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-8 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Calculation of required L1 Fronthaul Capacity (ID: 11213812)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11213818`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
The required UL L1 fronthaul capacity for an L1 pool shall be calculated as below,

[Before CB009827-D]

reqL1FHStreamPrbCapacity = maxStreamPrbNonMutableCells

[CB009827-D]

reqL1FHStreamPrbCapacity = min(maxStreamPrbAllocMutableCells + maxNonMutedEmptyStreamPrbMutableCells, maxStreamPrbMutableCells) + maxStreamPrbNonMutableCells

[End CB009827-D]

where,

[CB009827-D]

* maxStreamPrbAllocMutableCells = poolMaxNumStreamPrb - minStreamPrbNonMutableCells
* minStreamPrbNonMutableCells = sum of {numMinStreamPrbAlloc(i)} over all non-mutable cells i
* maxNonMutedEmptyStreamPrbMutableCells = sum of {maxULNonMutedStreamPRBTDDCell(i)} over all mutable cells i
* maxStreamPrbMutableCells = sum of {numActiveSubcells(i) \* maxStreamPrbPerSubcell(i)} over all mutable cells i
* maxULNonMutedStreamPRBTDDCell(i) for each of the cell i is given in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15442\_replaced([11213718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB009827-D]

* maxStreamPrbNonMutableCells = sum of {numActiveSubcells(i) \* maxStreamPrbPerSubcell(i)} over all non-mutable cells i
* maxStreamPrbPerSubcell(i) for any given cell i is given by the cell's UL bandwidth, namely ulBandwidth (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) converted into stream PRBs according to its subcell type as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before CB009827-D] Note: All cells shall be considered non-mutable cells, regardless of its UL PRB muting capability. [End CB009827-D]

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-9 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Calculation of Max. PUSCH Stream PRB for a Cell (ID: 11213820)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `12709836`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
During the execution of subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15439\_replaced([11213708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), The maximum number of stream PRBs available for PUSCH in a given cell i, namely maxNumCellPuschStreamPrb(i),  is given by

* maxNumCellPuschPrb(i) = numActiveSubcells (i) \* maxNumPuschPrbPerSubcell (i)
* maxNumCellPuschPrb(i) shall be converted into equivalent stream PRB, namely maxNumCellPuschStreamPrb(i), using computation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

where,

**[CB012299-A-UPD006] If dedicated BWPs are non-aligned (CB012299) without PRB blanking and   
two contiguous PUSCH regions, separated by PUCCH  are defined in the large BWP**

maxNumPuschPrbPerSubcell(i) = longPucchNumPuschPrb  + longPucchNumPuschPrb2

(see [12460720](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ePC1kApeEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

else

**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]**

maxNumPuschPrbPerSubcell(i) = longPucchNumPuschPrb of the largest dedicated BWP configured for the cell i (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2876\_replaced([11310329](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TrPVSPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note:

* when /NRBTS/NRCELL.actDynUlResAlloc='true', the above calculated maxPuschPrbPerSubcell <= the actual number of maximum PUSCH PRBs available per subcell < ulBandwidth. The actual number of maximum PUSCH PRBs might vary dynamically in a slot-by-slot basis by reusing unused PRBs in P-CSI region. For simplicity, maxNumPuschPrbPerSubcell considers only the static PUSCH region which is considered to be a better approximation than the complete bandwidth under high load.

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-10 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Calculation of Normalized PRB Demand for a Cell (ID: 11213833)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11213840`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
During the execution of subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15439\_replaced([11213708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), at every step, PRB utlization ratio for a cell i, namely normalizedPrbDemand(i), is calculated as given below

normalizedPrbDemand(i) = totalStreamPrbDemand(i) / maxNumCellPuschStreamPrb(i)

where,

* totalStreamPrbDemand(i) is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15445\_replaced([11213744](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJR3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxNumCellPuschStreamPrb(i) is calculated as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15447\_replaced([11213820](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ46_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 3.31.5.10.1.2.0-11 Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm Proposed Active UL Subcell List for each cell in L1 pool (ID: 11213842)

**3.31.5.10.1.2.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11213848`)

Load Metric Based Subcell Deactivation Algorithm
After the execution of subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15454\_replaced([11213789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxJ45fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), proposed active UL subcell list for each cell in L1 pool for the next BB pooling period is given by

For each cell i in L1 pool:

proposedActiveUlSubcellList (i) = First 'n' configured UL subcells for the cell i

where,

n= numActiveSubcells(i) for the cell i

Note: For a given cell i, its UL primary subcell is the subcell in index=0 of its configured UL subcell list. So, if numActiveSubcells(i) =1, its primary subcell will be activated and its subsequent secondary UL subcells will be activated provided that numActiveSubcells (i) > 1.

---

#### 3.31.5.10.2 L1 ARM Capacity based Subcell Deactivation

##### 3.31.5.10.2.1 L1 Capacity Limitation

###### 3.31.5.10.2.1.0-1 L1 Capacity Limitation Overview (ID: 11213864)

**3.31.5.10.2.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11213871`)

L1 Capacity Limitation
The CPU resources in the L1 ARM controller are finite and can support only a certain number of subcells per L1 Subpool as well as per L1 Pool.

With TDD, there is a need to support an increasing number of cells on the same non-scalable L1 resources.

One mechanism to achieve this result is to deactivate certain subcells of some cells such that more cells can be accommodated within the available resources.

The procedure defined in this section describes a mechanism to deactivate some subcells of some cells in the L1 Pool. The cells selected for deactivation are decided based on their PRB demands.

The procedure is executed in every BB pooling period in DL [CB009890-B]/UL[End CB009890-B] such that the result of the procedure is used in the Inter-L1 Subpool Pooling algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10386\_replaced([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the corresponding BB pooling period, and then again in case of a successful sub pool reconfiguration procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10387\_replaced([11213171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxFnhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), by the load metric based Intra-L1 Subpool Pooling algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6788\_replaced([11212354](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the next BB pooling period.

* The capacity limits for the max number of subcells supported by the L1 per subpool and per pool are provided by hidden NIDD params NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1SP/NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Pool for DL [CB009890-B] & NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Sp/NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Pool for UL.

The deactivation procedure is run separately in DL and UL, controlled individually as below:

[End CB009890-B]

-if dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) : the subcell deactivation procedure shall be run in DL

[CB009890-B]

-if ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) : the subcell deactivation procedure shall be run in UL

[End CB009890-B]

[CB009890-C]

In every BB pooling period, the subcell deactivation procedure shall ensure that if a cell has its primary DL subcell in the L1 pool, then at least 1 DL subcell shall remain active for such a cell. In other cases, all the DL subcells of a cell in the L1 Pool can be deactivated.

[End CB009890-C]

---

##### 3.31.5.10.2.2 Subcell Deactivation Framework

###### 3.31.5.10.2.2.0-1 Subcell Deactivation Framework Subcell Deactivation Procedure (ID: 11213883)

**3.31.5.10.2.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11213888`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
When dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB009890-B] or ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB009890-B], the L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure shall be executed in DL [CB009890-B] or UL respectively [End CB009890-B] in every BB pooling period. The procedure shall be executed before the Inter-L1 Subpool pooling algorithm for the next pooling period as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10386\_replaced([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

This algorithm shall be run separately in DL and UL for each L1 Pool. The decision to execute the algorithm shall depend on the flags mentioned below that are received during pool configuration from higher layers:

* dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for DL

[CB009890-B]

* ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for UL

[End CB009890-B]

Algorithm Input:

* Algorithm Input parameters are described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18307\_replaced([11213894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Algorithm Output:

* The proposed list of active DL[CB009890-B]/UL [End CB009890-B] subcells (proposedActiveDlSubcellList(i)[CB009890-B]/proposedActiveUlSubcellList(i)[End CB009890-B]) for each of the cell 'i' in the L1 pool.

Algorithm Steps:

* Initialization of deactivation algorithm parameters as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18310\_replaced([11213914](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* If any of the trigger conditions specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18581\_replaced([11213936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are satisfied,
* compute numActiveSubcells(i) for each cell 'i' in the L1 pool using the subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18313\_replaced([11213949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKgAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Else
* all the subcells configured for a cell in the pool shall be considered as active
* End If
* Derive the proposedActiveDlSubcellList[CB009890-B]/proposedActiveUlSubcellList[End CB009890-B] for each of the cell in L1 pool for the next pooling period from the computed numActiveSubcells as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18326\_replaced([11214008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 3.31.5.10.2.2.0-2 Subcell Deactivation Framework Input Parameters for L1 ARM capacity based Subcell Deactivation (ID: 11213894)

**3.31.5.10.2.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11213907`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
The input parameters for the L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation algorithm are described below:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Input Parameter** | **Value** |
| List of cells in L1 Pool | 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| Configured DL/UL **subcell list for each cell in** any of the L1 Pool\*\*\*\* | 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| L1 Pool & L1 subpool where the Primary DL subcell for each cell is configured | 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| - streamPrbDemandGbr - streamPrbDemandNonGbr - streamPrbDemandCg **[CB008600-F] - streamPrbDemandDcGbr** [End CB008600-F]\*\*\*\* | - PrbDemandGbr# - PrbDemandNonGbr# - prbDemandCg# (From 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6786\_replaced([11212141](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw_g1vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[CB008600-F] - PrbDemandDcGbr#** [End CB008600-F]\*\*\*\* |
| maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp | Maximum number of subcells supported per L1 subpool, provided by the hidden NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Sp for DL & NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Sp for UL |
| maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool | Maximum number of subcells supported per L1 pool, provided by the hidden NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Pool for DL & NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Pool for UL |
| numActiveSubcells (i) | Number of active DL/UL **subcells per cell ‘i’ in the L1 pool** |

Input indicated in # are given in cell PRB resolution

---

###### 3.31.5.10.2.2.0-3 Subcell Deactivation Framework Input Parameter Initialization (ID: 11213914)

**3.31.5.10.2.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11213928`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
Initialization of the input parameters for the Subcell deactivation procedure defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18307\_replaced([11213894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is described below.

* Convert the following input parameters corresponding to each cell i into equivalent stream PRB using computation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* PrbDemandGbr(i) --> streamPrbDemandGbr(i)
* PrbDemandNonGbr(i) --> streamPrbDemandNonGbr(i)
* PrbDemandCg(i) --> streamPrbDemandCg(i)
* [CB008600-F] PrbDemandDcGbr(i) --> streamPrbDemandDcGbr(i) [End CB008600-F]
* For each cell 'i' in the L1 Pool

//Initialize the numActiveSubcells(i) in DL as below

If enhanced DL MU-MIMO is enabled (NRCELL.actDlMuMimoEnh = TRUE) for cell 'i' :

* numActiveSubcells(i) = Total number of configured DL subcells for cell 'i' in the L1 Pool
* Else
* If cell 'i' has its primary DL subcell in the L1 Pool :
* numActiveSubcells(i) = 1 // If MU-MIMO is disabled and the cell has multiple DL subcells, only 1 DL subcell is used, and it will always be the primary DL subcell.
* Else
* numActiveSubcells(i) = 0
* End If
* End If

//Initialize the numActiveSubcells(i) in UL as below

* If UL MU-MIMO is enabled (NRCELL.actUlMuMimo = TRUE) for cell 'i' :
* numActiveSubcells(i) = Total number of configured UL subcells for cell 'i' in the L1 Pool
* Else
* If cell 'i' has its primary UL subcell in the L1 Pool :
* numActiveSubcells(i) = 1 // If MU-MIMO is disabled and the cell has multiple UL subcells, only 1 subcell is used, and it will always be the primary UL subcell.
* Else
* numActiveSubcells(i) = 0
* End If
* End If
* End For

---

###### 3.31.5.10.2.2.0-4 Subcell Deactivation Framework Conditions to Trigger Subcell Deactivation (ID: 11213936)

**3.31.5.10.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11213940`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
The L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure shall be triggered if any of the following condition are satisfied :

* numActiveSubcellsPerPool > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool or
* for at least 1 L1 subpool in the L1 Pool : numActiveSubcellsPerSubpool > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp

[CB009890-B]

The condition shall be checked separately in DL and UL considering the subcells configured in DL/UL for each L1 Pool/Subpool

[End CB009890-B]

where:

- numActiveSubcellPerPool = sum [all cells 'i' in the L1 Pool] {numActiveSubcells(i)}

- maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18307\_replaced([11213894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- numActiveSubcellsPerSubpool = sum [each L1 Subpool k in L1 Pool] [all cells 'i' in L1 Subpool(k)]{numActiveSubcells(i)}

- maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18307\_replaced([11213894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 3.31.5.10.2.2.0-5 Subcell Deactivation Framework Subcell Deactivation Algorithm (ID: 11213949)

**3.31.5.10.2.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11213956`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
Subcell deactivation algorithm shall be executed for each L1 pool in every pooling period if any of the trigger conditions mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18581\_replaced([11213936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are satisfied.

[CB009890-B]

This algorithm shall be executed separately for DL and UL in every pooling period for each L1 pool

[End CB009890-B]

Given:

* Input parameters provided in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18307\_replaced([11213894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & initialised as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18310\_replaced([11213914](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Output:

numActiveSubcells(i) for each of the cells in the L1 pool.

Steps:

* For each cell 'i' in L1 pool, calculate absolutePrbDemand(i) as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18321\_replaced([11213994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Let numActiveSubcellsInPool = sum [all cells 'i' in L1 pool]{numActiveSubcells(i)}

[Before CB009890-A-UPD001]

* Let numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp =  0

[CB009890-A-UPD001]

* For each L1 Subpool in the L1 Pool
* Let numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp = sum [all cells 'i' in L1 Subpool]{numActiveSubcells(i)}
* While numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp :
* Sort all cells 'i' in the L1 Subpool in increasing order of their absolutePrbDemand(i)
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list
* Let minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell = (Total number of primary subcells of the cell(i) in the L1 Subpool) //At least one subcell is required to activate its primary subcell.
* If (numActiveSubcells (i) > minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell)
* numActiveSubcells (i) = numActiveSubcells (i) - 1
* numActiveSubcellsInPool = numActiveSubcellsInPool - 1
* numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp = numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp - 1
* Re-calculate absolutePrbDemand(i) for the updated cell as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18321\_replaced([11213994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Break For loop
* End If
* End For
* If (No cells were updated)
* Break While loop
* End If
* End While
* End For

[End CB009890-A-UPD001]

* While numActiveSubcellsInPool > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool:
* Sort all cells 'i' in the L1 pool in increasing order of their absolutePrbDemand(i)
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

[Before CB009890-A-UPD001]

* numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp = sum [all cells 'k' in the same subpool of cell(i)]{numActiveSubcells(k)}
* Let minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell = 1 //At least one subcell is required to activate its primary subcell.

[CB009890-C]

* If (cell(i) does not have its primary DL subcell in the L1 pool AND the deactivation procedure is being executed for DL) : //If the cell has its primary subcell in the L1 Pool, at least one subcell is required to activate its primary subcell, else all subcells can be deactivated
* minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell = 0
* End If

[End CB009890-C]

* If (numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp OR numActiveSubcellsInPool > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool) AND (numActiveSubcells (i) > minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell )

[CB009890-A-UPD001]

* Let minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell = (Total number of primary subcells of the cell(i) in the L1 Pool) //At least one subcell is required to activate its primary subcell.
* If (numActiveSubcells (i) > minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell )

[End CB009890-A-UPD001]

* numActiveSubcells (i) = numActiveSubcells (i) - 1
* numActiveSubcellsInPool = numActiveSubcellsInPool - 1
* Re-calculate absolutePrbDemand(i) for the updated cell as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18321\_replaced([11213994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Break For loop
* End If
* End For
* If (No cells were updated)
* Break While loop
* End If
* End While

[CB009890-C]

The information about the L1 Pool/subpool where the cell's primary subcell is configured is part of the set of input parameters described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18307\_replaced([11213894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB009890-C]

---

###### 3.31.5.10.2.2.0-6 Subcell Deactivation Framework Total Stream PRB Demand Calculation (ID: 11213964)

**3.31.5.10.2.2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11213976`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
Total stream PRB demand for each cell shall consider all the stream PRB demands mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18307\_replaced([11213894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The PRB demands to be considered might be different in DL and UL.

Total stream PRB demand in DL :

totalStreamPrbDemand = [CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandDcGbr + [End CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandGbr + streamPrbDemandNonGbr

Total stream PRB demand in UL :

totalStreamPrbDemand = [CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandDcGbr + [End CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandGbr + streamPrbDemandNonGbr + streamPrbDemandCg

---

###### 3.31.5.10.2.2.0-7 Subcell Deactivation Framework Maximum Stream PRBs for a Cell (ID: 11213983)

**3.31.5.10.2.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11213990`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
Maximum Stream PRBs for each cell shall be calculated as described below

maxStreamPrbCell = maxCellPrb \* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb

where :

maxCellPrb is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where, instead of using the number of subcells calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), numActiveSubcells shall be used.

maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6782\_replaced([11211964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-SuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

###### 3.31.5.10.2.2.0-8 Subcell Deactivation Framework Absolute PRB Demand Calculation (ID: 11213994)

**3.31.5.10.2.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11214002`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
Absolute PRB demand for each cell shall be calculated as described below

[CB009890-C]
