If numActiveSubcells = 0

absolutePrbDemand = 0

Else

[End CB009890-C]

absolutePrbDemand = totalStreamPrbDemand / maxStreamPrbCell

where :

totalStreamPrbDemand is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18318\_replaced([11213964](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

maxStreamPrbCell is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18323\_replaced([11213983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB009890-C]

numActiveSubcells is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18307\_replaced([11213894](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf-PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB009890-C]

---

###### 3.31.5.10.2.2.0-9 Subcell Deactivation Framework Proposed Active Subcell List Creation (ID: 11214008)

**3.31.5.10.2.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11214013`)

Subcell Deactivation Framework
The proposed active subcell list for each cell in L1 pool [CB009890-B]for DL and UL[End CB009890-B] for the next BB pooling period is created as described below.

For each cell 'i' in L1 pool:

proposedActiveDlSubcellList (i) = First 'n' configured DL subcells for the cell 'i', starting with the primary subcell (the subcell in index=0 of the cell(i) configured DL subcell list)

[CB009890-B]

proposedActiveUlSubcellList (i) = First 'n' configured UL subcells for the cell 'i', starting with the primary subcell (the subcell in index=0 of the cell(i) configured UL subcell list)

[End CB009890-B]

where,

n= numActiveSubcells(i) for the cell 'i' [CB009890-B] in DL and UL respectively [End CB009890-B]

[CB009890-C]

Note:

* If numActiveSubcells(i) for a cell in DL = 0, no subcells shall be activated for the cell in DL
* It is possible that the cell does not have any primary DL subcell in the L1 Pool. In such case, BBRM shall configure the first 'n' configured DL subcells irrespective of primary DL subcell

[End CB009890-C]

---

### 3.31.5.11 LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e

#### 3.31.5.11.0-1 LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e layerPRB pooling initialization for eCPRI 7-2e (ID: 11214028)

**3.31.5.11.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214032`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, **slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed for DL** [CB012605-D] and slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed for UL **[End CB012605-D](see 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_4283_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_RAN_OP_3723_replaced([11693470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D31Qwf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) are introduced to control layerPrb pooling algorithm**. They are retrieved from hidden NIDD flag (NRBTS.actBbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72e) by OAM/L3RT and provided to L2RT.***\****\*

At system startup, BBRM shall learn L1 Pool/subpool and its properties for eCPRI 7-2e.

The L1 Pool capacities for eCPRI 7-2e include:

* DL: max number of active subcells per pool

The L1 subpool capacities for eCPRI 7-2e include:

 DL: max number of layerPRBs per subpool

* **[CB012605-D] UL: max number of layerPRBs per subpool** [End CB012605-D]\*\*\*\*
* DL: max number of active subcells per subpool

The values of the configuration parameters are retrieved from the hidden NIDD (NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbCapacity) by L3RT and provided to L2RT. The initial value comes from NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbInitCapacity and cannot be modified. The total layerPRB capacity of L1 subpool is initiated with the initial value at system startup, and can be modified during run time.

Note: it is assumed that there is always enough pooled layerPRB processing capacity per L1 subpool if inter-L1 subpool layerPRB pooling (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26490\_replaced([11214449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is disabled. If it is enabled, per L1 pool at least BBRM supports the minimum layerPRB allocation configured by CPRT at cell setup (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**.**

**-When interL1 subpool layerPRB pooling functionality is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26490\_replaced([11214449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

* the initial total layerPRB capacity of the L1 subpool provided via the hidden NIDD NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbInitCapacity for TDD **DL** [CB012605-D]or UL respectively**[End CB012605-D], may change during run time due to the interL1subpool resource reallocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Thus, the updated value of the subpool capacity decided in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26501\_replaced([11214551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be applied. The initial value comes from NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbInitCapacity and cannot be modified. The total layerPRB capacity of L1 subpool is initiated with the initial value and can then be modified.**\*\*\*\*

**[CB012605-H]**

-When dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed **= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** and cellTechnology = TDD,\*\*\*\*

* max subcell capacity per L1 pool is provided via the hidden NIDD NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Pool for DL
* max subcell capacity per L1 subpool is provided via the hidden NIDD NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Sp for DL

**[End CB012605-H]**

Since eCPRI 7-2e layerPRB pooling use same parameter modeling/structure as legacy CPRI/eCPRI 7-2a, below parameters are not used for eCPRI 7-2e deployment.

NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Pool

NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Sp

NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbInitCapacity.maxNumStreamPrbL1Sp

NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbInitCapacity.maxNumWbStreamPrbL1Sp

---

#### 3.31.5.11.0-2 LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e Cell load measurement and layerPRB demand estimation (ID: 11214038)

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214046`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Spectral Efficiency per DL slot for Metric Based Algorithm

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214051`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Spectral Efficiency of one DL Scheduling slot (rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot) represents average number bits per resource element which has been used in the past for PDSCH transmission by 5G-L2-PS.

It is a cell specific variable and shall be calculated as an exponential filter in every DL slot where at least one UE specific PDSCH is scheduled.

PDSCH scheduled due to artificial load, RACH msg2, systemInformation and Paging shall be excluded from the Spectral Efficiency calculation.

Start value for rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot shall be 8. // 8 is rough average number based on rank2 and medium 64 QAM MCS.

rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot[n] = (1 - 1/rdAvgSpectralEffDlSlotFilterCoeff) \* rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot[n − 1] + 1/rdAvgSpectralEffDlSlotFilterCoeff \* rrmInstSpectralEffDlSlot

* rdAvgSpectralEffDlSlotFilterCoeff is R&D parameters defined in 5G\_L2\_1235\_replaced([11188082](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28Fi3_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmInstSpectralEffDlSlot shall be calculated as Sum(TBS) / SUM(REs), where
* Sum(TBS) is the sum of scheduled DL TBS (decided by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4624\_replaced([11192116](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvivWPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and provided as tbSize IE in LoCtrl\_PduMuxReq) of fresh transmissions for all scheduled DL UEs in this slot, and
* SUM(REs) is the sum of scheduled number of REs used for both fresh and retransmissions for all scheduled DL UEs in this slot, considering the number of layers used by UE

Scheduled number of REs is known by 5G-L2-PS since it is used to decide the TBS as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4635\_replaced([11192394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvkkgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as number (Nre \* Nrb \* Nu), where

* Nre is the number of data RE per RB, and
* Nrb is the number of allocated RB for the PDSCH
* Nu is the number of layers per UE

[CB012605-E]

* With MU-MIMO enabled,

If the scheduled UE is part of a virtual UE

Nu (number of layers per UE) shall consider the MU adapted rank (rankMuUe)(refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7563\_replaced([11142677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5ldPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for such a UE

End

[End CB012605-E]

Note: For eCPRI 7-2e, cell specific spectral efficiency shall be calculated per PRB per layer, then REs calculation shall be calculated with scheduled PRBs and layers.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214059`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Spectral Efficiency per UL slot for Metric Based Algorithm

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214071`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Spectral Efficiency of one UL Scheduling slot (rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot) represents average number of bytes per resource element which has been used in the past for PUSCH transmission by 5G-L2-PS.

It is a cell specific variable and shall be calculated as an exponential filter in every UL slot where at least one UE PUSCH is scheduled.

Start value for rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot shall be 8, same assumption used for DL in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5250\_replaced([11210238](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot [n] = (1 - 1/rdAvgSpectralEffUlSlotFilterCoeff) \* rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot [n − 1] + 1/rdAvgSpectralEffUlSlotFilterCoeff \* rrmInstSpectralEffUlSlot

* rdAvgSpectralEffUlSlotFilterCoeff is R&D parameters defined in 5G\_L2\_4661\_replaced([11188110](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ5PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmInstSpectralEffUlSlot shall be calculated as Sum(TBS) / SUM(REs), where
* Sum(TBS) is the sum of scheduled UL TBS of fresh transmissions (decided by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for all scheduled UL UEs in this slot, and
* SUM(REs) is the sum of scheduled number of REs used for both fresh and retransmissions for all scheduled UL UEs in this slot, considering the number of layers used by UE

Scheduled number of REs is known by 5G-L2-PS since it is used to decide the TBS as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5084\_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as number (Nre \* Nrb \* Nu), where

* Nre is the number of data RE per RB, and
* Nrb is the number of allocated RB for the PUSCH
* Nu is the number of layers per UE

[CB012605-I]

* With MU-MIMO enabled,

If the scheduled UE is a virtual UE

TBS and REs shall be individually determined for each UE in the virtual UE.

End

[End CB012605-I]

Note: For eCPRI 7-2e, cell specific spectral efficiency shall be calculated per PRB per layer, then REs calculation shall be calculated with scheduled PRBs and layers.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11214077`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
LayerPRB Demand Estimation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214084`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
GBR/nonGBR/CG Layer PRB Demand Estimation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11214096`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Every bbPoolingPeriod (NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) SFNs, the aggregate layerPRB demand per cell shall be calculated for DL/UL for GBR/nonGBR bearer separately as follows:

[CB010630-E] When NRBTS/NRCELL.actUlCgType2 is set to True (so for UL only), a number of layer PRBs for Configured Grant reservation 'layerPrbDemandCg' shall be requested from BBRM. This request shall have the highest priority.

* layerPrbDemandCg represent the maximum number of layer PRBs consumed by all the CG UEs in a firing state (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15099\_replaced([11172972](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuPu0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in a slot slot, computed as SUM(each CG UE k in the slot, numReqLayerPrb(k) ), over the maximum Configured Grant (CG) periodicity (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14663\_replaced([11172788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuOgsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) slots, considering CG UES at the end of the current pooling window.

See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for numReqLayerPrb calculation. [End CB010630-E]

for DL/UL:

* layerPrbDemandGbr(i)  = (gbrBufferLength(i,n) + rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor \* rrmAvgNewGbrDataArrivalEst ) / (cellSpectralEff(i)\*totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod),
* layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i)  = (nonGbrBufferLength(i,n) + rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor \* rrmAvgNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst ) / (cellSpectralEff(i)\*totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod),

where:

cellSpectralEff(i) = rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot \*"# PDSCH REs per PRB per layer"    // for DL

cellSpectralEff(i) = rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot \*"# PUSCH REs per PRB per layer"    // for UL

and

* layerPrbDemand(i): cell layerPRB demand of cell i
* # PDSCH REs per PRB per layer is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5248\_replaced([11210227](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw4MGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* # PUSCH REs per PRB per layer is taken as average (156 = 12 subcarriers x 13 PUSCH symbols)
* rrmAvgSpectralEffDlSlot: spectral efficiency of current DL slot defined as average number of bytes per resource element which has been used in the past for PDSCH transmission by 5G-L2-PS, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25727\_replaced([11214046](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* rrmAvgSpectralEffUlSlot: spectral efficiency of current UL slot defined as average number of bytes per resource element which has been used in the past for PUSCH transmission by 5G-L2-PS, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25729\_replaced([11214059](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* gbrBufferLength (i, n): the sum of all bufferedbytes of all GBR bearers from all UEs in the cell i at time n (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6784\_replaced([11212073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5yvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* nonGbrBufferLength: the sum of all bufferedbytes of all nonGBR bearers from all UEs in the cell i at time n(refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6784\_replaced([11212073](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5yvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* rrmAvgNewGbrDataArrivalEst / rrmAvgNewNonGbrDataArrivalEst as calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6785\_replaced([11212086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5zPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rdDataArrivalEstimatorFactor: R&D parameter to estimate traffic arrival, default value 1, defined in 5G\_L2\_4662\_replaced([11188098](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ4vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod: corresponds to the total number of DL/UL data slots within the bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod), respectively.
* For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed is TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), layerPRB demand is computed only for the DL
* For slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed is TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), layerPRB demand is computed only for the UL

[CB008600-F]

The resultant layer PRB demand of GBR, nonGBR, RIM, namely, layerPrbDemandGbr, layerPrbDemandNonGbr are reduced according to the value of the excess layer PRB demand requested for DC-GBR service in the cell as below:

If the excess layer PRB demand requested for the DC-GBR service in the cell in the corresponding DL/UL direction, namely layerPrbDemandDcGbrExcess (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32101\_replaced([11214109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 0,

layerPrbDemandGbr is reduced by the maxGbrloadReductionPossible which is given by min(layerPrbDemandDcGbrExcess , layerPrbDemandGbr )

layerPrbDemandDcGbrExcess is also reduced by the value of maxGbrloadReductionPossible and if still layerPrbDemandDcGbrExcess > 0

layerPrbDemandNonGbr is reduced by value of the maxNonGbrloadReductionPossible which is min(layerPrbDemandDcGbrExcess , layerPrbDemandNonGbr)

The resultant layer PRB demands shall be forwarded to the BBRM.

[End CB008600-F]

Note1: for simplification, cell spectral efficiency is used in DL/UL instead of the per-UE spectral efficiency for the layerPRB demand estimation.

Note2: # PUSCH REs is estimated considering not always 14 symbols is used for PUSCH, as one symbols could be scheduled for aSRS during the pooling window.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11214102`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
DC-GBR Layer PRB Demand Estimation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214109`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Layer PRB Demand Estimation for DC-GBR Service

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214116`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Every bbPoolEvalPeriod (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall calculate demand of the estimation of layer PRB demand in both DL/UL direction for the DC-GBR service in the cell, namely layerPrbDemandDcGbr, as below:

layerPrbDemandDcGbr = sum of first 'n' entries in the list of requiredNumLayerPrbsPerGrant (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32037\_replaced([11212205](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of all DC-GBR bearers in the cell, with the list being sorted in the descending order.

with

n = PxSCH demand of the DC-GBR service in the same DL/UL direction, namely dcGbrPxschDemandPerSlot (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31975\_replaced([11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), computed for the same pooling period.

Example: Given, DC GBR PDSCH Demand, namely dcGbrPdschDemandPerSlot, for pooling period k = 2 and there are 5 DC-GBR bearers in the cell with their requiredNumLayerPrbsPerGrant values in DL direction = {20, 10, 40, 25, 50}. In that case, the layerPrbDemandDcGbr for the DL direction for pooling period k = sum(50, 40) = 90.

In addition, gNB-DU shall also calculate excess DL/UL Layer PRB demand requested for DC-GBR service in the cell from BBRM, namely layerPrbDemandDcGbrExcess , as below

layerPrbDemandDcGbrExcess = layerPrbDemandDcGbr - (sum of (maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j)/avgUeSEPerLayerPrb (i)) over all DC-GBR bearers j of UEs i in the cell)/numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod

where

* maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j) is the maximum data volume that is expected from the DC-GBR bearer j per pooling period as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31898\_replaced([11211070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* avgUeSEPerLayerPrb shall be the average of the spectral efficiency of the UE with DC-GBR bearer  represented in bits/layerPrb in the corresponding DL/UL direction as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32103\_replaced([11214121](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuGfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numSchedSlotsPerPoolingPeriod is the number of scheduling slots (the slots with possible DL/UL grants) within the pooling period in the corresponding DL/UL direction. For details, pls refer to [11211040](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw6oXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
* Eventually, In the same pooling period, gNB-DU shall reduce layer PRB Demands of one or more of low prio services (GBR, nonGBR) in the corresponding direction (DL/UL) based on layerPrbDemandDcGbrExcess so that higher than needed layer DC-GBR PRB demand requested for the DC-GBR service, namely layerPrbDemandDcGbr can be re-used for the GBR and nonGBR services in the cell. Please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32098\_replaced([11214084](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) PRB demand reductions of low prio services (GBR, nonGBR) in DL and UL directions.
* Rationale: As the DC-GBR service is delay critical, higher than needed resources are requested for DC-GBR service from BBRM which would reduce the pooling efficiency. Hence, by reducing the resource demand of low priority services of the same cell which are not delay critical, the low priority services can utilise the excess allocated resources for DC-GBR services in the cell in the slots in which they are not used thereby freeing up resources for the other cells in the pool.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214121`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Layer PRB Demand Estimation for a DC-GBR bearer

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214128`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
gNB-DU shall compute the estimated number of DL/UL PRBs required per PxSCH allocation in a given slot for a given DC\_GBR bearer, namely requiredNumPrbsPerGrant, within any given pooling period as below

requiredNumLayerPrbsPerGrant(j) =  maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j)/(reqPxschPerPoolingPeriod(j) \* avgUeSEPerLayerPrb )

where:

* maxDataVolPerPoolingPeriod\_bits(j) is the maximum data volume estimated to be transmitted per DC-GBR bearer j within a pooling period, computed as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31898\_replaced([11211070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PYvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* reqPxschPerPoolingPeriod(j) is the required number of PxSCH allocations required for the DC-GBR bearer in the pooling period, computed as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31896\_replaced([11211056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw7PYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* avgUeSEPerLayerPrb shall be the average of the spectral efficiency of the UE with DC-GBR bearer in the corresponding DL/UL direction represented in bits/layerPrb. It shall be maintained via an exponential averaging filter and all the UE PxSCH grants (including the grants without any data for DC-GBR bearer) shall be considered for the filter. See [11214135: Max number of layers per cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for cellPrb to layerPrb conversion**.**

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11214135`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Max number of layers per cell

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11214149`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, the max number of layers that can be used per cell PRB is based on the type of subcell/s and the nrCellType configured for the cell.

Thus,

* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is :
* 2 : for a cell with C2 DL subcell **or C4'2 or C8'2 UL subcell**
* 4 : for a cell with C4 DL subcell **or C8'4 UL subcell**
* **[CB008235-A] 8 : for a cell with C8'8 UL subcell** [End CB008235-A]\*\*\*\*

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11214157`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Max layerPRB per cell calculation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `12709834`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, maximum cellPRBs in DL /UL for cell i should be calculated as below:

If the number of subcells for cell i is N (the number of subcells for the cell determined as in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27910\_replaced([11214237](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

For DL:

If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh=True, then

maxCellPrb(i) = N \* dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Else

maxCellPrb(i) = dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

End If

For UL:

If NRCELL.actDynUlResAlloc is false

maxCellPrb(i) = longPucchNumPuschPrb +  **[CB012299-A-UPD006] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]\*\*\*\*

Else

maxCellPrb(i) = longPucchNumDynPuschPrb + **[CB012299-A-UPD009] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD009]\*\*\*\*

End If

where

* longPucchNumPuschPrb and longPucchNumDynPuschPrb are received in cell setup message for the corresponding Bandwidth Part.

**[CB012299-A-UPD006]  
- longPucchNumPuschPrb2 is received in cell setup message for the corresponding Bandwidth Part if dedicated BWPs are non-aligned (CB012299) without PRB blanking and   
two contiguous PUSCH regions, separated by PUCCH  are defined in the large BWP,**

otherwise is set 0.

**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]**

**- In UL only 1 subcell per cell are supported for eCPRI 7-2e (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27910\_replaced([11214237](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

End If

Maximum layerPRBs in DL/UL **for cell i should be calculated as below:**

maxCellLayerPrb(i) = maxCellPrb(i) \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb(i)

where:

* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is **[CB012605-I]defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28507\_replaced([11214135](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**[End CB012605-I]\*\*\*\*

**[Before CB012605-I]**

* 2 : for a cell with C2 DL subcell **or C4'2 or C8'2 UL subcell**
* 4 : for a cell with C4 DL subcell **or C8'4 UL subcell**
* 1 : for a cell with C2 UL subcell

**[End CB012605-I]**

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11214176`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Max layerPRB for CG per cell calculation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `12709833`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, maximum cellPRBs for CG(applicable to UL only) for cell i should be calculated as below:

If NRCELL.actDynUlResAlloc is false

maxCellPrbForCg(i) = longPucchNumPuschPrb +  **[CB012299-A-UPD006] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]\*\*\*\*

Else

maxCellPrbForCg(i) = longPucchNumDynPuschPrb  **+ [CB012299-A-UPD009] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD009]\*\*\*\*

End If

maxCellPrbForCg(i) = MAX (maxCellPrbForCg(i), NIDD: NRBTS.NRCELL.ulConfiguredGrantType2.ulCgMaxNumPrbs for cell i)

where

* longPucchNumPuschPrb is received in cell setup message for the corresponding Bandwidth Part.

**[CB012299-A-UPD006]  
- longPucchNumPuschPrb2 is received in cell setup message for the corresponding Bandwidth Part if dedicated BWPs are non-aligned (CB012299) without PRB blanking and   
two contiguous PUSCH regions, separated by PUCCH  are defined in the large BWP,**

otherwise is set 0.

**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]**

**- longPucchNumDynPuschPrb refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**

Maximum layerPRBs for CG **for cell i should be calculated as below:**

maxCellLayerPrbForCg(i) = maxCellPrbForCg(i) \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb(i)

where:

* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb(i) is same as computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25734\_replaced([11214157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11214190`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Max layerPRB for GBR per cell calculation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `12709826`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, maximum cellPRBs for GBR in DL/UL for cell i should be calculated as below:

For DL: maxCellPrbForGbr(i) = dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

For UL:

If NRCELL.actDynUlResAlloc is false

maxCellPrbForGbr(i) = longPucchNumPuschPrb + **[CB012299-A-UPD006] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]\*\*\*\*

Else

maxCellPrbForGbr(i) = longPucchNumDynPuschPrb + **[CB012299-A-UPD009] longPucchNumPuschPrb2**[End CB012299-A-UPD009]\*\*\*\*

End If

where

* longPucchNumPuschPrb is received in cell setup message for the corresponding Bandwidth Part.

**[CB012299-A-UPD006]  
- longPucchNumPuschPrb2 is received in cell setup message for the corresponding Bandwidth Part if dedicated BWPs are non-aligned (CB012299) without PRB blanking and   
two contiguous PUSCH regions, separated by PUCCH  are defined in the large BWP,**

otherwise is set 0.

**[End CB012299-A-UPD006]**

**- longPucchNumDynPuschPrb refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**

Maximum layerPRBs for GBR in DL/UL **for cell i should be calculated as below:**

maxCellLayerPrbForGbr(i) = maxCellPrbForGbr(i) \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb(i)

where:

* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28507\_replaced([11214135](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-8**  (ID: `11214210`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Max layer PRB Limit for non-GBR allocation in a cell Based on MU-MIMO utilization

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11214217`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
This section defines the maximum layer PRB allocation limit for a cell that needs to be considered for non-GBR demand allocation considering the average rank (number of layers) used by a cell including MU-MIMO pairing reported by gnB as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28501\_replaced([11214251](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* maxMuMimoCellLayerPrbNonGbrLimit(i) = floor(min{ maxCellLayerPrb(i),  (rrmCellAvgMimoLayers(i, n) \* maxCellPrb(i)})
* Where:
* maxCellLayerPrb(i) is the maximum number of layer PRBs available for cell 'i' as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25734\_replaced([11214157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxCellPrb(i) is the maximum number of Physical PRBs available for cell 'i' as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25734\_replaced([11214157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmCellAvgMimoLayers(i, n) is the exponentially averaged average rank of cell 'i' for the current pooling period n described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28501\_replaced([11214251](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* This section is applicable for FR1-TDD UL only

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-9**  (ID: `12765207`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Max Layer PRB Limit for non-GBR allocation for historical usage

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `12765208`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
This section defines the maximum layer PRB allocation limit for a cell that needs to be considered for non-GBR historical usage allocation.

maxHistnonGBRCellLayerPrb(i) =  max {(rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsageTdd**)***maxPcellLayerPrb(i), (1+ rdPrbPooilngOverAllocFactor)*(AvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i) OR AvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i)}

where,

* rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsageTdd ([12879244](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Hv1F3LM8EfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), when If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1ULAllowed = True or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = True
* rdPrbPoolingOverAllocFactor ([12722864)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_OvVvKW3vEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* AvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR/ AvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR ([12721585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e1AtEG09EfCmnYHxzZN44w))
* maxPcellLayerPrb(i) ([12739529](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ew8VIHmcEfCiUemk-K-C4g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* i is the cell index

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-10**  (ID: `11214224`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Max layer PRB for EMF Load Generation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11214231`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
This section defines the maximum layer PRB for a cell that is configured with EMF Load genration with a given target load

* maxCellLayerPrbEmf(i) = min{ maxCellLayerPrb(i),  (maxCellPrb(i) \* maxLayersForEmfLoad(i))}
* Where:
* maxCellLayerPrb(i) is the maximum number of layer PRBs available for cell 'i' as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25734\_replaced([11214157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxCellPrb(i) is the maximum number of Physical PRBs available for cell 'i' as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25734\_replaced([11214157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxLayersForEmfLoad(i) is the maximum number of layers that can be used when generating an EMF load for cell 'i' = 2 (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17426\_replaced([11183931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-11**  (ID: `11214237`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Determination of Number of Subcells for a given Cell

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-11.0-1**  (ID: `11214244`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
The number of DL[CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D] subcells per cell (per L1 SP) for the calculation of max layer PRBs described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25734\_replaced([11214157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be calculated as below

DL:

* if nrCellType = 4DLxUL, number of subcells per cell = 1
* if nrCellType = 8DLxUL, number of subcells per cell = 2

[CB012605-H]

* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) :

number of subcells per cell = length(currentActiveDlSubcellList) for the cell for the current pooling period described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (the list is calculated in the previous pooling period).

proposedActiveDlSubcellList generated for the next pooling period (described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27687\_replaced([11214642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be used instead of currentActiveDlSubcellList if the "number of subcells per cell" is required while performing the Inter L1 subpool reconfiguration described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26490\_replaced([11214449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB012605-H]

[CB012605-D]

UL:  number of subcell per cell = 1

[End CB012605-D]

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-12**  (ID: `11214251`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
MU-MIMO average rank per cell

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-12.0-2**  (ID: `12744513`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
In FR1-TDD with UL MU-MIMO, the scheduler performs spatial domain multiplexing. Such a use of PRBs should be considered while allocating layer PRB resources for a cell since pairing multiple UEs on the same PRBs is not always possible and as such, in case pairing does not occur, the layer PRB resources could be wasted in a cell. Thus, this section estimates a rank based PRB utilization factor defined as the fraction of the average sum of ranks used by scheduler from the maximum number of layers available for a cell.

* mimoLayersPerCell = min{maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb, ((sum[all UL slots with PUSCH containing non-GBR data scheduled in previous pooling period]{averageMimoRankPerSlot} / (number of UL slots with PUSCH containing non-GBR data scheduled in previous pooling period)) \* rdMimoLayerOverEstimationFactor)}

where:

* averageMimoRankPerSlot = sum[all PUSCH allocations in a slot containing non-GBR data]{numLayerPrbPerAllocation} /  {total number of physical PRBs used for PUSCH allocations containing non-GBR data in the slot}
* "number of physical PRBs" shall consider a PRB only once in case it is used for MU-MIMO pairing.
* Note : numLayerPrbAllocation can be determined as numReqLayerPrb defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) which requires the number of PRBs and the rank used in the PUSCH allocation.
* rdMimoLayerOverEstimationFactor is an R&D param that shall be used to over estimate the average MIMO layers to allow for future increase in spectral efficiency gains for the current upcoming period. It is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28785\_replaced([11215333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is the maximum number of layers for a cell based on its subcell type described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28507\_replaced([11214135](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The mimoLayerPerCell for a pooling interval (n) shall be exponentially averaged to finally determine the average Mimo Layers Per cell

* rrmCellAvgMimoLayers(n) = (rdAvgExpMimoUtilizationFactor) \* mimoLayersPerCell(n - 1) + (1 - rdAvgExpMimoUtilizationFactor) \* rrmCellAvgMimoLayers(n - 1)

where:

* mimoLayersPerCell(n - 1) = mimoLayersPerCell calculated above at the end of the previous pooling period (n - 1) and used to calculate the average in the current pooling period (n)
* rrmCellAvgMimoLayers(n - 1) : Average MIMO Layer per cell calculated at the beginning of the previous pooling period.
* For the first pooling period (n = 0); rrmCellAvgMimoLayers(0) = **min{2, maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb in UL defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28507\_replaced([11214135](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))}**
* rdAvgExpMimoUtilizationFactor : R&D parameter to perform exponential averaging of the average MIMO Layer per cell defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28513\_replaced([11215320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmCellAvgMimoLayers shall be evaluated by the gnB for each cell and forwarded to BBRM together with the estimated layer PRB demand at the end of each pooling period.

[CB014094-C] Note: NRCELL.actUlMuMimo is online changed from false to true, gNB shall start filtering from the beginning. [End CB014094-C]

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-13**  (ID: `12721584`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Bookkeeping of the number of Layer PRBs used for non-GBR (DL/UL)

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-13.0-1**  (ID: `12731406`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
When slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE in DL or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed for UL, gNB-DU shall apply the following procedure during each pooling period:

For every slot, the L2PS computes the number of layer PRBs used separately for downlink (DL) and uplink (UL), considering non-GBR traffic, deprioritized GBR traffic, and nominal bit rate traffic. The following parameters are updated for each UE j in slot t:

* rrmUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, j, t): Number of Layer PRBs used for non-GBR traffic for UE j in slot t (DL)
* rrmUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, j, t): Number of Layer PRBs used for non-GBR traffic for UE j in slot t (UL)

L2PS then calculates a average of Layer PRBs used in each BB pooling period as follows:

* rrmAvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n) = Σ[j, t] (rrmUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, j, t)) / totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod,
* rrmAvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n) = Σ[j, t] (rrmUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, j, t)) / totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod.

Where,

* rrmAvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n): Average number of Layer PRBs used per slot in DL for non-GBR traffic during pooling period n,
* rrmAvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n): Average number of Layer PRBs used per slot in UL for non-GBR traffic during pooling period n,
* i: Cell index,
* j: UE index,
* t: Scheduling time,
* n:Pooling period index,
* totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod: Total number of slots in the pooling period.

Where totalSlotPerPoolingPeriod:

* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE in DL or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed for UL, the value corresponds to the total number of UL or DL (including special slot) data slots within the BB pooling period, respectively.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-14**  (ID: `12721585`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Historical Layer PRB usage of non-GBR traffic (DL/UL)

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `12731411`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
When slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE in DL or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed for UL, gNB-DU shall calculate the historical layer PRB usage during each pooling period and report this value to BBRM.

The historical average layer PRB usage for downlink and uplink non-GBR traffic is updated in each pooling period using an exponential moving average as follows:

* AvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n) = AvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n-1) \* (1 - 1/rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff) + rrmAvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n)\* (1/rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff),
* AvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n) = AvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n-1) \* (1 - 1/rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff) + rrmAvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n)\* (1/rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff),

Where:

* AvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n) and AvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n) represent the average number of layer PRBs used per cell for nonGBR traffic. And rdAvgUsedPRBSlotFilterCoeff is a value as specified in ([12723115)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7Ok1gG3_EfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
* AvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n) and AvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i, n), are reported to BBRM in every BBRM period interval.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-15**  (ID: `12739529`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Max LayerPRB of Primary SubCell Calculation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-2.0-15.0-1**  (ID: `12739530`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, maximum layer PRBs for the primary cell in DL /UL for cell i should be calculated as below:

For DL:

If NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh=True, then

maxPcellLayerPrb(i) = dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb

End If

For UL:

If NRCELL.actDynUlResAlloc is false

maxPcellLayerPrb(i) = longPucchNumPuschPrb \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb

Else

maxPcellLayerPrb(i) = longPucchNumDynPuschPrb \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb

End If

where:

* longPucchNumPuschPrb and longPucchNumDynPuschPrb are received in cell setup message for the corresponding Bandwidth Part.
* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28507\_replaced([11214135](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.31.5.11.0-3 LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e Intra-L1 subpool Load Metric Based LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm (ID: 11214266)

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214271`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Load Metric Based LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm Overview

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11214287`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, **when slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed** = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3723\_replaced([11693470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D31Qwf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg)))**, DL/UL resources are pooled separately and the BBRM determines the amount of DL/UL layerPRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool).**\*\*\*\*

When the NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolMode is set to ''1:load-metric', the amount of layerPRB available to be used by each cell in the same L1 subPool or in different L1 subpools **is determined by the BBRM depending on a load metric defined based on the Cell's traffic load (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  Assuming the end of the previous bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) is at SFN N,  the metric based algorithm determines a new allocation of layerPRB grant per cell (numAllocCellLayerPrb) for the next bbPoolingPeriod based on cell load metric measured in the previous pooling period until SFN N.**

When interL1 subpool layerPRB pooling functionality is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26490\_replaced([11214449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the time at which the intra-subpool algorithm decision takes place for each subpool shall be synchronized across all the subpools in the same pool **to ensure that any reconfiguration change at L1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is properly aligned time with the layerPRB capacity allocated to each cell.**

The load metric per cell is calculated in terms of Cell layerPRB demand ("Aggregate layerPRB demand" of a cell)  required for GBR and/or non-GBR traffic service and it is estimated separately for DL/UL as shown in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Metric-Based layerPRB allocation procedure is as follows:

* At each cell, each DL/UL 5G-L2-PS determines the load metric of aggregate layerPRB demand at the end of each bbPoolingPeriod (NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) SFN N per DL/UL respectively.
* In the first SFN of each bbPoolingPeriod (SFN N+1), BBRM receives load metric with the aggregate layerPRB demand from each Cell's DL/UL scheduler followed by a request for the amount of available layerPRBs that can be used by the cell starting from the next SFN.
* The BBRM determines the total amount of layerPRB granted to each cell of the same L1subPool based on the received load metric. This shall apply to all subpools of the L1 pool**.**
* The BBRM sends back the layerPRB grant, numAllocDlSubcells (numActiveDlSubcells), listOfDlSubcells (listOfActiveDlSubcells) to L2-PS of DL scheduler, and sends back the layerPRB grant, numAllocUlSubcells (numActiveUlSubcells), listOfUlSubcells (listOfActiveUlSubcells) to L2-PS of UL scheduler, and the new grant is to be used starting from SFN N+2.
* numActiveDlSubcells and listOfActiveDlSubcells for DL, numActiveUlSubcells and listOfActiveUlSubcells for UL should be initialized and activated during cell setup procedure if dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed **= FALSE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**
* numActiveDlSubcells, listOfActiveDlSubcells should be determined by subcell deactivation algorithm (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27687\_replaced([11214642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed **= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**
* The layerPRB grant corresponding to DL shall be sent for both DL and UL schedulers, since PDCCH limitation shall be known by both DL and UL scheduler.

Note: during SFN N+1 (beginning of the new bbPoolingPeriod), each cell is using the old allocation as a new allocation is yet to be determined.

* The following metric-based layerPRB pooling algorithm shall be used to distribute the L1 subPool layerPRB capacity to each cell mapped to the same L1subpool:

**- The algorithm is used to grant amount of usable layerPRB for DL and UL separately.**

**-Algorithm Input :**

* Algorithm Input parameters are described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**-Algorithm Output:**

-  numAllocSubcell(i) and subcell ID list for cell(i): total amount of usable subcells (numAllocSubcell(i)) and subcell ID list (subcellList)

-  numAllocCellLayerPrb(i): total usable cell layerPRB, granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell

[PR835287]

* intermediateAllocLayerPrb(i): total usable cell LayerPRB before the last step (step 4 in the following steps), granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell

[End PR835287]

**- Algorithm Steps:**

1) Each cell shall be allocated the minimum amount of layerPRB as per the configured min value (numMinLayerPRBAlloc ): refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25717\_replaced([11214316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

**[CB010630-E] 1') If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25717\_replaced([11214316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell based on Configured Grant demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_30494\_replaced([11214335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8NvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));** [End CB010630-E]\*\*\*\*

**[CB008600-F] 1'') If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_30494\_replaced([11214335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8NvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell based on DC-GBR demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32105\_replaced([11214349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));** [End CB008600-F]\*\*\*\*

2) If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 (**[Before CB010630-E] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25717\_replaced([11214316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** [CB010630-E] [Before CB008600-F]5G\_UP\_ALG\_30494\_replaced([11214335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8NvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) **[CB008600-F] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32105\_replaced([11214349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))** [End CB008600-F][End CB010630-E]), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell based on GBR demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25719\_replaced([11214364](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));***\****\*

3) If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25719\_replaced([11214364](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell based on Non GBR demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25721\_replaced([11214383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8P_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

4) If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25721\_replaced([11214383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8P_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell evenly, until remaining layerPRB are all allocated to the cells (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25723\_replaced([11214436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: DL and UL resources are separately pooled and the BBRM determines the amount of DL and UL layerPRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool).

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11214295`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Input Parameters for Load Metric Based LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12640626`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
nrPosCellType definition

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12640627`)

nrPosCellType definition for 0DL 4UL (Positioning Cell)

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-2.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12640625`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Subcells deployment for nrPosCellType 0DL4UL

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| 0 DL 4UL | NONE | 1 \* C4S | Scenario A for UL | GC4S | cellTechnology = TDD nrarfcn = FR1 Positioning cell on RU-SRS. | CB010680-C | L1 based HW: \* Loner: NO \* Loki: NO \* Thor: YES \* vDU:NO L2 based HW: \* Xeon: NO \* Snowfish: NO \* Marlin: YES \* vDU: NO | L1 based HW: \* Loner: NO \* Loki: NO \* Thor: NO \* vDU:NO L2 based HW: \* Xeon: NO \* Snowfish: NO \* Marlin: NO \* vDU: NO |

Algorithm to calculate subcells deployment:

* in all case, there is always 1 UL subcell per nrPosCell.
* Cell FAbioExt property is equal to FALSE.

Note (+): in case of a nrPosCell, nrCellGrp type corresponds to nrPosCell. Name nrCellGrp is kept even if there is no dedicated nrCellGroup object linked to a nrPosCell for CSM compability and simplicity purpose.

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11214316`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Allocation of the configured minimum resource per Cell

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11214330`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
- This section provides an allocation of the configured minimum resource per Cell.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Get the list of cells in the corresponding L1subpool with index i and give the initial minimum allocation per cell:

**[Before CB010630-D-UPD001]**

**[CB010630-D]**

Update the initial minimum allocation for cell 'i' based on artificial load in the current pooling period.

If artificial load for EMF is enabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17863\_replaced([11183915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_PvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for cell 'i'

* ConfiguredLoadInLayerPRBForEmf = Roundup ((NRCELL.emfTargetTotalLoad \* maxCellLayerPrbEmf (i)) / 100)
* numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i) = max (ConfiguredLoadInLayerPRBForEmf , numMinLayerPRBAlloc (i))

Note: There's no need to protect the initial assignment for the target EMF cell and other normal cells, since only one cell can be configured as EMF cell and min layer PRB can be always guaranteed with current TDD FR1 pooling configurations.

End If

where :

* maxCellLayerPrbEmf : Max Cell Layer PRBs required for artificial load generation (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29773\_replaced([11214224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

**[End CB010630-D]**

**[End CB010630-D-UPD001]**

numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i)

* With InterL1Sp layerPRB pooling enabled, the L1SP capacity may not be sufficient to support the minimum allocation for all cells of the SP, mainly when there is (are) newly added cell(s) to L1Sp with zero layerPRB BBRM grant in the past pooling period. In such case, BBRM shall deprioritize the min allocation to the newly added cells (if any) which has not yet received the first non-zero BBRM layerPRB grant as below;

If (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE)

If {maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp < sum [for all i] {numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i)}}; then

- Give the minimum allocation for the cells which had been receiving non-zero BBRM layerPRB grant in the previous pooling periods and set allocation to zero for the newly added cell :

**[CB010630-D-UPD001]**

-   If cell 'i' has a non-zero BBRM grant in the previous pooling period and there is a change in the artificial load for EMF for the cell (artificial load generation is enabled, or the NRCELL.emfTargetTotalLoad is increased) when compared to the  previous pooling period

o numAllocCellStreamPrb(i) = [Before PR833149-25R3] numMinStreamPrbAlloc(i) [PR833149-25R3]  numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i)  [End PR833149-25R3] granted to the cell 'i' in the previous pooling period

-   Else

**[End CB010630-D-UPD001]**

o numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i); for all cells i with non-zero layerPRB BBRM grant in the past pooling period

o numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = 0; for any newly added cells with cells i with zero layerPRB BBRM grant in the past pooling period.

- Cells with no minimum allocation in this step (i.e., numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = 0), shall be excluded from participating in the remaining intraSp resource allocation step.

**[CB010630-D-UPD001]**

-   End If

**[End CB010630-D-UPD001]**

Else

- numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i) // initial allocation is done here

End If

End If

* calculate the amount of the remaining capacity per the L1subpool to be shared:

L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare = maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp - sum[for all i]{numAllocCellLayerPrb(i)}

Note: due to the nature of the current intraSp resource allocation priority, the min allocation of the newly added cell can be satisfied as long as maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp >= sum [for all i] {numMinLayerPRBAlloc (i)}. With interL1Sp, however, if maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp was not increased after new cell addition, the remaining L1Sp capacity for the next step GBR demand based allocation would be reduced and any already admitted GBR traffic in the other cells may suffer from congestion.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11214335`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Allocation of additional layerPRB per cell based on Configured Grant (CG) demand

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11214342`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
- This section provides an allocation of additional layerPRB to a cell based on CG demand.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numAllocCellLayerPrb, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25717\_replaced([11214316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxCellLayerPrbForCg: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30496\_replaced([11214176](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i), layerPrbDemandCg(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different layerPrbDemandCg value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their layerPrbDemandCg value.
* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandCg(k)} =0; i.e. if CG layerPRB demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* AllocLayerPrbCg(i) = 0

Else

* AllocLayerPrbCg(i) = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare\*layerPrbDemandCg(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandCg(k)}
* AllocLayerPrbCg(i) = min{maxCellLayerPrbForCg(i) -  numAllocCellLayerPrb(i), layerPrbDemandCg(i), AllocLayerPrbCg(i)}

End If

* numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) + AllocLayerPrbCg(i)  // update allocation of cell i
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocLayerPrbGbr(i) // compute remaining capacity for the next cell

End For

End If

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no layerPRBs are left unused during the layerPRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured and then different maximum available layerPRB. Hence, some cells with lower BW (lower maxCellLayerPRB) and lower layerPRB demand are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11214349`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Allocation of additional layerPRB per cell based on DC-GBR demand

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11214356`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
- This section provides an allocation of additional layerPRB to a cell based on GBR demand.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numAllocCellLayerPrb, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30494\_replaced([11214335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8NvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i), layerPrbDemandDcGbr(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different layerPrbDemandDcGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their layerPrbDemandDcGbr value.
* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDLAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandDcGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if DC GBR layerPRB demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* AllocLayerPrbDcGbr(i) = 0

Else

* AllocLayerPrbDcGbr(i) = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare\*layerPrbDemandDcGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandDcGbr(k)}
* AllocLayerPrbDcGbr(i) = min{maxCellLayerPrbForGbr(i) -  numAllocCellLayerPrb(i), LayerPrbDemandDcGbr(i), AllocLayerPrbDcGbr(i)}

End If

* numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) + AllocLayerPrbDcGbr(i)  // update allocation of cell i
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocLayerPrbDcGbr(i) // compute remaining capacity for the next cell

End For

End If

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no layerPRBs are left unused during the layerPRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured and then different maximum available layerPRB. Hence, some cells with lower BW (lower maxCellLayerPRB) and lower layerPRB demand are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11214364`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Allocation of additional layerPRB per cell based on GBR demand

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11214376`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
- This section provides an allocation of additional layerPRB to a cell based on GBR demand.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numAllocCellLayerPrb, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: [Before CB010630-E] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25717\_replaced([11214316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB010630-E] [Before CB008600-F] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30494\_replaced([11214335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8NvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[CB008600-F] 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32105\_replaced([11214349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB008600-F] [End CB010630-E]
* sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i), layerPrbDemandGbr(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different layerPrbDemandGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their layerPrbDemandGbr value.
* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDLAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if GBR layerPRB demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* AllocLayerPrbGbr(i) = 0

Else

* AllocLayerPrbGbr(i) = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare\*layerPrbDemandGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandGbr(k)}
* AllocLayerPrbGbr(i) = min{maxCellLayerPrbForGbr(i) -  numAllocCellLayerPrb(i), LayerPrbDemandGbr(i), AllocLayerPrbGbr(i)}

End If

* numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) + AllocLayerPrbGbr(i)  // update allocation of cell i
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocLayerPrbGbr(i) // compute remaining capacity for the next cell

End For

End If

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no layerPRBs are left unused during the layerPRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured and then different maximum available layerPRB. Hence, some cells with lower BW (lower maxCellLayerPRB) and lower layerPRB demand are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.
