**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-7**  (ID: `11214383`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Allocation of additional layerPRB per cell based on non-GBR demand

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11214391`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Overview

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214396`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
When MU-MIMO is enabled in UL (NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo) for at least 1 cell in the L1 subpool, with spatial domain multiplexing, where gnB allocates multiple UEs on the same PRBs, BBRM shall perform a 2 step allocation approach as described below:

* Step 1: First provide additional layer-PRB allocation to each cell based on non GBR demand with a maximum value based on an estimate of the percentage of PRBs which have been allocated to multiple UEs. This is specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28495\_replaced([11214403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Step 2: If there is still remaining subpool capacity and there are cells which still have remaining non-GBR demand, they will be allocated as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28496\_replaced([11214416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

In all other cases, BBRM shall allocate resources based on non-GBR demand as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28496\_replaced([11214416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11214403`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Step 1: non-GBR demand based allocation restricted to MIMO usage

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214408`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
- This section provides an allocation of additional layerPRB per cell based on non GBR demand. The allocation is limited to the capacity of estimated PRBs used with MU-MIMO pairing during the previous pooling period as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26875\_replaced([11212968](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZWvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

This is to be performed only in UL and only in case UL MU-MIMO is enabled (NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo) in at least 1 cell in the subpool. In all other cases, only allocation as per step 2 (described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28496\_replaced([11214416](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be performed.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numAllocCellLayerPrb, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25719\_replaced([11214364](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxMuMimoCellLayerPrbNonGbrLimit(i) : 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28505\_replaced([11214210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxMuMimoCellLayerPrbNonGbrLimit(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) , layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i)}. In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different layerPrbDemandNonGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their layerPrbDemandNonGbr value.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE AND NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo = TRUE

For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if nonGBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* Break loop. Stop processing this step for further cells.

Else

* AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) =  min{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i), L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare\*layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}}
* AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) =  max{0, min{AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i), (maxMuMimoCellLayerPrbNonGbrLimit(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i))}}

End If

* numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) + AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i
* layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i) = max{0, (layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i) - AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i))} // update remaining non-GBR PRB demand for cell i
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) // compute remaining capacity for the next cell

End For

End If

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no layerPRBs are left unused during the layerPRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured and then different maximum available layerPRB. Hence, some cells with lower BW (lower maxCellLayerPRB) and lower layerPRB demand are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `11214416`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Step 2: non-GBR demand based allocation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-7.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11214429`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
\* - This section provides an allocation of additional layerPRB per cell based on non GBR demand.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB012605-I] If MU-MIMO is enabled in UL (NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo) in at least 1 cell in the subpool and only for UL, layerPrbDemandNonGbr shall be updated from 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28495\_replaced([11214403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CB012605-I]
* numAllocCellLayerPrb, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25719\_replaced([11214364](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB012605-I] If MU-MIMO is enabled in UL (NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo in at least 1 cell in the subpool and only for UL, use the values at the end of 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28495\_replaced([11214403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CB012605-I]

sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) , layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i)}. In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different layerPrbDemandNonGbr value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their layerPrbDemandNonGbr value.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDLAllowed = TRUE  or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE

For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if nonGBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* Break loop. Stop processing this step for further cells.

Else

* AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) =  min{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i), L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare\*layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(k)}}
* AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) =  max{0, min{AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i), (maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i))}}

End If

* numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) + AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) // compute remaining capacity for the next cell

End For

End If

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no layerPRBs are left unused during the layerPRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured and then different maximum available layerPRB. Hence, some cells with lower BW (lower maxCellLayerPRB) and lower layerPRB demand are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-8**  (ID: `11214436`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Allocation of remaining layerPRB per cell

---

**3.31.5.11.0-3.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11214441`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
- This section describes the distribution of any remaining layerPRBs after all other allocations per cell

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numAllocCellLayerPrb, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25721\_replaced([11214383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8P_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

After all demand based allocations, if there is still remaining resource, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare > 0, distribute the remaining resource to cells in the L1 subpool as below.

Sort all cells in the subpool with numAllocCellLayerPrb(i)>0 and { maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) >0 }, in the increasing order of {maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the increasing order sorting operation and take random order for the cells with same value.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDLAllowed = TRUE [CB012605-D] or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE [End CB012605-D]

For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

* Calculate the total already-allocated capacity for all the cells after the current cell in the sorted list
* allocatedLayerPrbSubsequentInclusive (i) = sum[k >= i] {numAllocCellLayerPrb(k)}
* Calculate the total maximum allocation potential remaining layerPrb (until the cell-level maximums are reached) for all the cells after the current cell in the sorted list
* potentialLayerPrbSubsequent(i) = sum[k > i] {(maxCellLayerPrb(k) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(k))}
* Calculate the additional capacity to be allocated for the current cell from the remaining capacity proportionally to the demand-based allocation and make sure that all layerPRB capacity will be allocated before running out of allocation potential in the subsequent cells
* AllocRemainingCellLayerPrb = max{floor{L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare \* numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) /(allocatedCellLayerPrbSubsequentInclusive (i)}, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - potentialLayerPrbSubsequent(i)}
* Do not exceed the maximum allocation of the cell and do not allocate negative capacity
* AllocRemainingCellLayerPrb = min{AllocRemainingCellLayerPrb, (maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i))}
* AllocRemainingCellLayerPrb = max{AllocRemainingCellLayerPrb , 0}
* update total allocated capacity of the cell
* numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) + AllocRemainingCellLayerPrb(i)
* compute remaining capacity for the next cell
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocRemainingCellLayerPrb(i)

End For

End If

---

#### 3.31.5.11.0-4 LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e Enhanced Intra-L1 subpool Load Metric Based LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm**** (ID: 12705617)

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `12711586`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Enhanced Load Metric Based LayerPRB Overview

---

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13428353`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, when slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3723\_replaced([11693470](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D31Qwf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))), and histUsageAllowed =TRUE, DL/UL resources are pooled separately. The BBRM determines the amount of DL/UL layerPRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool).

When histUsageAllowed =TRUE, the amount of layerPRB available to be used by each cell in the same L1 subPool or different L1 subpools is determined by the BBRM depending on an enhanced load metric defined based on the Cell's traffic load (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).  Assuming the end of the previous bbPoolingPeriod(NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) is at SFN N,  the metric-based algorithm determines a new allocation of layerPRB grant per cell (numAllocCellLayerPrb) for the next bbPoolingPeriod based on cell load metric measured in the previous pooling period until SFN N.

When interL1 subpool layerPRB pooling functionality is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26490\_replaced([11214449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the time at which the intra-subpool algorithm decision takes place for each subpool shall be synchronized across all the subpools in the same pool to ensure that any reconfiguration change at L1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is properly aligned time with the layerPRB capacity allocated to each cell.

The enhanced load metric per cell is calculated based on the Cell layerPRB demand ("Aggregate layerPRB demand" of a cell) required for GBR and/or demand of non-GBR traffic and historical usage of non-GBR traffic . The layerPRB load for GBR and non-GBR is estimated separately for DL/UL as shown in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced ([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), ([12711600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gKBk4Wa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) ), and ([12711601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq29gGa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

The enhanced Metric-Based layerPRB allocation procedure is as follows:

* At each cell, each DL/UL 5G-L2-PS determines the load metric of aggregate layerPRB demand and non-GBR demand and historical usage at the end of each bbPoolingPeriod (NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) SFN N per DL/UL respectively.
* In the first SFN of each bbPoolingPeriod (SFN N+1), BBRM receives load metric with the aggregate layerPRB demand and layerPRB for non-GBR demand and load from each Cell's DL/UL scheduler, followed by a request for available layerPRBs that can be used by the cell starting from the next SFN.
* The BBRM determines the total amount of layerPRB granted to each cell of the same L1subPool based on the received load metric. This shall apply to all subpools of the L1 pool.
* The BBRM sends back the layerPRB grant, numAllocDlSubcells (numActiveDlSubcells), listOfDlSubcells (listOfActiveDlSubcells) to L2-PS of DL scheduler, and sends back the layerPRB grant, numAllocUlSubcells (numActiveUlSubcells), listOfUlSubcells (listOfActiveUlSubcells) to L2-PS of UL scheduler. The new grant is to be used starting from SFN N+2.
* numActiveDlSubcells and listOfActiveDlSubcells for DL, numActiveUlSubcells and listOfActiveUlSubcells for UL should be initialized and activated during cell setup procedure if dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = FALSE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* numActiveDlSubcells, listOfActiveDlSubcells should be determined by subcell deactivation algorithm (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27687\_replaced([11214642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* The layerPRB grant corresponding to DL shall be sent for both DL and UL schedulers, since both DL and UL schedulers shall know PDCCH limitation.

Note: during SFN N+1 (beginning of the new bbPoolingPeriod), each cell is using the old allocation as a new allocation is yet to be determined.

* The following enhanced metric-based layerPRB pooling algorithm shall be used to distribute the L1 subPool layerPRB capacity to each cell mapped to the same L1subpool:
* The algorithm is used to grant an amount of usable layerPRB for DL and UL separately.

-Algorithm Input :

* Algorithm Input parameters are described in ([12711597](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PmZagWa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA)).

-Algorithm Output:

-  numAllocSubcell(i) and subcell ID list for cell(i): total amount of usable subcells (numAllocSubcell(i)) and subcell ID list (subcellList)

-  numAllocCellLayerPrb(i): total usable cell layerPRB, granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell

-   intermediateAllocLayerPrb(i): total usable cell LayerPRB before the last step (step 4 in the following steps), granted per cell according to total amount of usable subcells per cell

* Algorithm Steps:

1) Each cell shall be allocated the minimum amount of layerPRB as per the configured min value (numMinLayerPRBAlloc ): refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25717\_replaced([11214316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

1') If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25717\_replaced([11214316](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8M_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell based on Configured Grant demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_30494\_replaced([11214335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8NvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

1'') If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_30494\_replaced([11214335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8NvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell based on DC-GBR demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32105\_replaced([11214349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

2) If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0  5G\_UP\_ALG\_32105\_replaced([11214349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell based on GBR demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25719\_replaced([11214364](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

3) If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25719\_replaced([11214364](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell based on Non GBR demand and historical load as described in ([12711600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gKBk4Wa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) ), i.e, Round-1.

[CB014923-C] intra power pooling step) After Round-1 execution, if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed=true

BBRM shall suspend the execution of further PRB pooling steps for the current L1 Subpool. Then BBRM shall execute the first steps of all other L1 subpools till this point.

BBRM shall perform middle round of intra-power pooling (see [13237745: Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (middle round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_TmBNsr-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), and skip the cells with allocated power from further PRB pooling steps and update the L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare of its L1 subPool.  
then BBRM shall resume further PRB pooling steps for the all the L1 Subpools one by one. [End CB014923-C]

3\_1) If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 ([12711600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gKBk4Wa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) ), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell based on remaining Non GBR demand and graceful historical load as described in ([12711601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq29gGa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), i.e., Round-2.

4) If there is any remaining capacity of the subpool, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare >0 ([12711601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq29gGa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), allocate additional layerPRB to the cell evenly, until remaining layerPRB are all allocated to the cells (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25723\_replaced([11214436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB014923-C] intra power pooling step) then, if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed=true,   
BBRM shall perform post round of intra-power pooling for all the pwr pools if needed (see [13237746: Intra Power pooling procedure after the PRB pooling (post round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ZBCE4L-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), and update numAllocCellLayerPrb of the power pooling cell by excluding the excessive allocated PRBs according to minimum PSD principle.  [End CB014923-C]

Note: DL and UL resources are separately pooled and the BBRM determines the amount of DL and UL layerPRB resources for each cell within the same L1subpool (intra subpool).

---

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `12711597`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Input Parameters for Enhanced Load Metric Based LayerPRB Algorithm

---

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12729374`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
The input parameters for the enhanced load metric-based layer PRB pooling algorithm are described in the table below:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Input Parameter | Values |
| cell list per L1 subpool | 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp | If interL1 subpool layerPRB pooling functionality is enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26490\_replaced([11214449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) - DL/UL: currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26501\_replaced([11214551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) Else - DL/UL: NRBTS.bbL1SpPrbInitCapacity.maxNumLayerPrbL1Sp End |
| - layerPrbDemandCg - layerPrbDemandDcGbr - layerPrbDemandGbr - layerPrbDemandNonGbr | - layerPrbDemandCg - layerPrbDemandDcGbr - layerPrbDemandGbr - layerPrbDemandNonGbr (described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |
| numMinLayerPRBAlloc | If artificial load for EMF is enabled  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17863\_replaced([11183915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_PvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then     max (Roundup ( (NRCELL.emfTargetTotalLoad \* maxCellLayerPrbEmf) / 100) , numMinLayerPRBAlloc) where \* numMinlayerPRBAlloc defined in (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \* maxCellLayerPrbEmf : Max Cell Layer PRBs required for artificial load generation (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29773\_replaced([11214224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) else numMinlayerPRBAlloc (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) End |
| maxCellLayerPrb | maxCellLayerPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25734\_replaced([11214157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |
| maxCellLayerPrbForGbr | maxCellLayerPrbForGbr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25726\_replaced([11214190](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |
| AvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR | If histUsageAllowed = TRUE and If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDLAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE, historical usage of downlink Layer PRB for non-GBR for ([12721585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e1AtEG09EfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) |
| AvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR | If histUsageAllowed = TRUE and If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDLAllowed = TRUE or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE, historical usage of Uplink Layer PRB for non-GBR for ([12721585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e1AtEG09EfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) |
| maxPcellLayerPrb | maximum layer PRBs for the primary subcell in DL /UL for the cell in ([12739529](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ew8VIHmcEfCiUemk-K-C4g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) |

Note:

* The term layerPRB shall be counted as PRBs multiple layers as PRB in the frequency dimension and MIMO layer in the spatial dimension.
* maxCellLayerPrb shall refer to the maximum number of layerPRBs per L1 SP that can be allocated across all subcells available in the cell per L1 SP.
* maxCellLayerPrbForGbr shall refer to the maximum number of layerPRBs that can be allocated for GBR in a cell.

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12711600`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Allocation of additional LayerPRB per Cell based on non-GBR demand and Load (Round-1)

---

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `12729380`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
This section provides an allocation of additional layer PRB per cell based on non-GBR demand and historical load.

- Given:

* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([12711597](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PmZagWa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_UBmNVp5EEe2A-5U7tzedRA))
* numAllocCellLayerPrb, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25719\_replaced([11214364](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8OvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxHistnonGBRCellLayerPrb(i) ([12765207)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vM7wEoTeEfCOGMMH109ICw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

Sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i),  min{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i), maxHistnonGBRCellLayerPrb(i)}}. In case several cells have same value resulting from the outer min operation and if they have different values from the inner min operation, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of the result of the inner min operation.

If histUsageAllowed =TRUE ([12737865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1U3IUXhAEfCdZt6bzaG3fw "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_1u3iuxhaefcdzt6bzag3fw&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects%2f_pmhfqo3wee-rl47x_rccmw%2fcomponents%2f_fh7nqo3xee-rl47x_rccmw&oslc.configuration=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9"))

For i=0,1,2,3 ...N-1: where i is the index of sorted cell and N is the number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(k)} =0; i.e. if nonGBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* Break loop. Stop processing this step for further cells.

Else

* AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) = min (layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i), maxHistnonGBRCellLayerPrb(i), L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare\*layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i)/sum[N  >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(k)})
* AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) =  max{0, min{AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i), (maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i))}}

End If

* numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) + AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i
* Store cell i nonGBR allocation from round 1 to compute the updated “demand” for round 2:
* ​​​​​​​AllocLayerPrbNonGbrRound1(i) = AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i)
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) // compute remaining capacity for the next cell

End For

End If

Note: Sorting of the cells is done to ensure that no layerPRBs are left unused during the layerPRB allocation. Rationale: different cells in the same pool may have different BW configured and then different maximum available layerPRB. Hence, some cells with lower BW (lower maxCellLayerPRB) and lower layerPRB demand are allocated first as per the order in the sorted cell list.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `12711601`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Allocation of Remaining LayerPRB per Cell (Round-2)

---

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13244514`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
This section describes the distribution of layerPRBs [CB014923-C]after middle round of intra power pooling allocation if NRBTS/actPwrPoolingTDD = true, otherwise [End CB014923-C] after nonGBR based allocation Round-1 per cell.

* Given:
* Input parameters: ([12711597](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PmZagWa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* numAllocCellLayerPrb, L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare: (12711600) [CB014923-C] in case NRBTS/actPwrPoolingTDD = false, else if NRBTS/actPwrPoolingTDD =true, the updated L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare by middle round of intra power pooling allocation (see [13237745: Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (middle round) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TjMjML-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))  [End CB014923-C]
* layerPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i) ([12711601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq29gGa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq29gGa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9"))

After allocating demand-based and historical usage, if there is still a remaining resource (L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare > 0), distribute the remaining resource to cells in the L1 subpool as follows.

Sort the cells in the increasing order of min{maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i), layerPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i)}. In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different layerPrbDemandNonGbrRound2 value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their layerPrbDemandNonGbrRound2 value. [CB014923-C] If NRBTS/actPwrPoolingTDD = true, the cell with allocated power in the middle round of intra-power pooling shall be excluded from the sorted list [End CB014923-C]

If histUsageAllowed =TRUE ([12737865](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1U3IUXhAEfCdZt6bzaG3fw "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/web#action=com.ibm.rdm.web.pages.showartifactpage&artifacturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2fresources%2fbi_1u3iuxhaefcdzt6bzag3fw&componenturi=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2frm%2frm-projects%2f_pmhfqo3wee-rl47x_rccmw%2fcomponents%2f_fh7nqo3xee-rl47x_rccmw&oslc.configuration=https%3a%2f%2fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2fgc%2fconfiguration%2f9"))

For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list

If sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(k)} =0; i.e. if updated nonGBR demand = 0 for all cells k>=i,

* Break loop. Stop processing this step for further cells.

Else

* AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) =  min {layerPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i), L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare\*layerPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i)/sum[N >k>=i]{layerPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(k)}}
* AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) =  max{0, min{AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i), (maxCellLayerPrb(i) - numAllocCellLayerPrb(i))}}

End If

* numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) = numAllocCellLayerPrb(i) + AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i)   //update allocation for cell i
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare = L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare - AllocLayerPrbNonGbr(i) // compute remaining capacity for the next cell

End For

End If

---

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-5**  (ID: `12776032`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e

#### Layer PRB demand for nonGBR based allocation round 2

---

**3.31.5.11.0-4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `12776033`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
This section defines the updated nonGBR “demand” that will be used in allocation round 2. ([12711601](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq29gGa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g))

layerPrbDemandNonGbrRound2(i) = max{layerPrbDemandNonGbr (i)- AllocLayerPrbNonGbrRound1(i),  rdPrbPoolingGracefulAllocFactor \*[AvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR(i) OR AvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR(i)]- AllocLayerPrbNonGbrRound1(i)}

Where,

* layerPrbDemandNonGbr – (described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* AllocLayerPrbNonGbrRound1(i) – ([12711600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gKBk4Wa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))
* rdPrbPoolingGracefulAllocFactor - ([12722864)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_OvVvKW3vEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* AvgUsedDlLayerPRBnonGBR/AvgUsedUlLayerPRBnonGBR ([12721585](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e1AtEG09EfCmnYHxzZN44w))

#### 3.31.5.11.0-5 LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e Inter-L1 subpool Load Metric Based LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm (ID: 11214449)

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11214454`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Inter-L1 Subpool layerPRB pooling overview

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12574857`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
-With inter-L1 subpool layerPRB pooling, part or all of the layerPRB resources of subpool(s) can be shifted between the subpool(s) mapped to same L1pool (L1 instance) enabling a redistribution of capacities based on cell layerPrb demand report. Such re-allocation of resources between subpools is carried out by the BBRM in non-realtime or slow pooling fashion and targeting to address the imbalance of load and availability of unused resources within the subpools (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26501\_replaced([11214551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

-With inter-L1 subpool layerPRB pooling if dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed **= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and in case of TDD, BBRM shall also consider deactivating a certain number of subcells from any of the subpools of a L1 Pool based on required loads of the cells in the L1 pool as long as the maximum subcell capacities of the L1 Pool/subpool mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are exceeded. The list of activated subcells shall be used in the Inter L1 Subpool Pooling algorithm of the corresponding pooling period to define the max layerPRB capacities of each subpool.**

-The output of the L1 ARM capacity subcell deactivation procedure shall be used in the next pooling period while performing the layerPRB Pooling distribution with Intra-L1 SubPool Pooling for TDD.

* Once BBRM decides new resource(layerPRB) allocation per each subpool, the subpool capacity update is carried out via subpool resource reconfiguration and synchronization procedure as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* The inter-L1 subpool layerPRB pooling functionality is enabled/disabled [Before CNI-137616-B] via an R&D flag rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddDl (5G\_L2\_7674\_replaced([11188131](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ6PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for TDD in DL or rdSlowPrbPoolingRangeTddUl (5G\_L2\_6312\_replaced([11188119](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28GJ5vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for TDD in UL. In addition to R&D flags activation, to enable inter-L1 subpool layerPRB pooling functionality, there shall be more than one L1 subpool per L1 pool on all the L1 pools handled by a given L2-RT instance. [CNI-137616-B], see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10386\_replaced([11212985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxEZXfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)). [End CNI-137616-B]

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11214467`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Initialization of Inter-L1 Subpool layerPRB pooling and Parameter Definitions

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214474`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
-At system startup, BBRM shall learn the subpool list within the L1 pool and initializes the subpool capacity in DL[CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D] with a configured per subpool capacity value given by the NIDD described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25710\_replaced([11214028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHC_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). This NIDD given initial DL [CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D] subpool capacity is considered as default subpool capacity and corresponding layerPRB capacities are referred by defaultLayerPrbCapacityPerSp.

With inter-L1 subpool layerPRB pooling functionality enabled (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the subpool capacity may change from one pooling period to another due to the pooling decisions and re-allocation of resources between the subpools. Thus, the actual layerPRB capacities of a subpool at any given pooling period is given by currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp.

* At the BBRM startup (first pooling period), currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp = defaultLayerPrbCapacityPerSp.
* The maximum amount of layerPRBs available on the L1 Pool level is equal to the sum of the layerPRBs of all subpools within the L1 pool

poolMaxNumLayerPrb = sum[ all subpool per pool]{defaultLayerPrbCapacityPerSp}

* With inter-L1 subpool layerPRB pooling, the BBRM decides to reallocate resources between the different subpools in a pool at run time and sends reconfiguration request to L1 to apply the new subpool capacities (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The corresponding destination address of the L1 pool of the subpools for which the reconfiguration request it to be sent from BBRM shall be negotiated and provided by L1 during the pooling initialization phase. Thus, BBRM sends resource reconfiguration pool address request to L1 when the cell setup request is received for a cell mapped to one of the DL[CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D] subpool of the pool. In the response, L1 provides the destination pool address to be used later when subpools capacity reconfiguration is to be requested.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11214481`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Minimum Resource Reservation Per L1 Subpool

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214486`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
The minimum amount of layerPRBs that shall always be reserved in DL [CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D] per subpool is given by minLayerPrbCapacityPerSp and the value is equal to the total minimum layerPRBs (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of all cells within the subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

minLayerPrbCapacityPerSp = sum[for all cells i in the subpool]{minimum layerPRB for cell(i)}

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `11214492`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Maximum Potential Resource Per L1 Subpool

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11214499`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
- The maximum number of layerPRBs that can be used by each cell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25734\_replaced([11214157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) within the subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is restricted by the BWs and MU-MIMO enabled of each cell. Thus, the maximum amount of layerPRBs resource per subpool is the sum of the maximum layerPRBs of all cells within the subpool in DL [CB012605-D]/UL respectively.[End CB012605-D].

* Maximum layerPRBs per subpool (maxSpLayerPrb) is defined as the sum of the potential maximum number of layerPRBs (equivalent layerPRB of cell BW PRBs multiplied by the number of active subcells in case of MU-MIMO enabled) that can be used by each cells within the subpool in DL [CB012605-D]/UL respectively.[End CB012605-D]

maxSpLayerPrb = sum[for all cells i within subpool]{potential max number of layerPRBs (equivalent layerPRB of cell BW PRBs \* number of active subcells) that can be used by cell(i)}

[CB012605-H]

If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the calculation for the maximum number of layerPRBs for a cell shall consider only the list of active subcells proposed at the end of the L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure for the cell 'i' for the next pooling period. The procedure is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27692\_replaced([11214695](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxbfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The list of proposed active subcells for a cell is given by proposedActiveDlSubcellList(i) in DL described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27700\_replaced([11214753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxPYdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB012605-H]

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-5**  (ID: `11214505`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Total L1 Capacity Demand per SubPool

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11214526`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
At the beginning of every pooling period, the BBRM computes the total amount of layerPRB demands per subpool for all subpools mapped to the same L1 pool based on the load metrics received from the L2PS of each active cells within the subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in DL/UL respectively. The load metric from each cell received by the BBRM provides the amount of layerPRB demands for [CB010630-E] Configured Grant (CG), [End CB010630-E] [CB008600-F]DC-GBR, [End CB008600-F] GBR and nonGBR traffics of the cell.

Thus, BBRM maintains the total capacity demand for each subpool as total demand per subpool for [CB010630-E] Configured Grant (CG), [End CB010630-E] [CB008600-F]DC-GBR, [End CB008600-F] GBR and nonGBR services separately as:

* [CB010630-E] totalLayerPrbCgDemandPerSp(j) = sum[for all cells i within Sp j]{layerPrbDemandCg(i)} //UL only [End CB010630-E]
* [CB008600-F] totalLayerPrbDcGbrDemandPerSp(j) = sum[for all cells i within Sp j]{layerPrbDemandDcGbr(i)} [End CB008600-F]
* totalLayerPrbGbrDemandPerSp(j) = sum[for all cells i within Sp j]{layerPrbDemandGbr(i)}
* totalLayerPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(j) = sum[for all cells i within Sp j]{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i)}
* The sum of the layerPRB demands (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the minimum layerPRBs (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) indicated by each cell within a SP may exceed the maximum layerPRBs available per cell. Thus, the maximum layerPRB demand per SP that may receive an allocation from the BBRM, when possible, shall be limited taking this restriction into account and defined as below, in DL/UL respectively:
* [CB010630-E] maxLayerPrbCgAllocLimitSp(j) = sum[all cell i in Sp j] {min{layerPrbDemandCg(i), max{0, maxCellLayerPrbForCg(i) – numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i)}}}[End CB010630-E]
* [CB008600-F] maxLayerPrbDcGbrAllocLimitSp(j) = sum[all cell i in Sp j] {min{layerPrbDemandDcGbr(i), max{0, maxCellLayerPrbForGbr(i) – numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i) - layerPrbDemandCg(i)}}}[End CB008600-F]
* maxLayerPrbGbrAllocLimitSp(j) = sum[all cell i in Sp j] {min{layerPrbDemandGbr(i), max{0, maxCellLayerPrbForGbr(i) – numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i) [CB010630-E] – layerPrbDemandCg(i) [End CB010630-E] [CB008600-F] – layerPrbDemandDcGbr(i) [End CB008600-F]}}}
* maxLayerPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(j) = sum[all cell i in Sp j] {min{layerPrbDemandNonGbr(i), max{0,maxCellLayerPrb(i) – numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i) [CB010630-E] – layerPrbDemandCg(i) [End CB010630-E]  [CB008600-F] – layerPrbDemandDcGbr(i) [End CB008600-F] – layerPrbDemandGbr(i)}}}

If UL MIMO is enabled NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo in at least 1 cell in the L1 Pool and for FR1-TDD UL Only

* maxLayerPrbNonGbrMimoAllocLimitSp = sum[all cell i in Sp] {min{maxMuMimoCellLayerPrbNonGbrLimit(i), max{0,maxCellLayerPrb(i) – numMinLayerPRBAlloc(i) [CB010630-E] – layerPrbDemandCg(i) [End CB010630-E]  [CB008600-F] – layerPrbDemandDcGbr(i) [End CB008600-F] – layerPrbDemandGbr(i)}}
* where,
* maxMuMimoCellLayerPrbNonGbrLimit defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28505\_replaced([11214210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-For synchronized reconfiguration of resources across the subpools (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the time at which the cell load metric indication is received by the BBRM across all subpools (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in a pool shall aligned.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-6**  (ID: `11214533`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Synchronization Between L1 and L2 for Subpool Capacity Reconfiguration

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11214544`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
11214544:
LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
For TDD eCPRI 7-2e, the subpool capacity reconfiguration is to be done periodically and the BBRM triggers the reconfiguration procedure every pooling period.

BBRM sends out a reconfiguration request message, DlPool\_BbResourceReconfReq in DL [CB012605-D]or UlPool\_BbResourceReconfReq in UL[End CB012605-D], to L1 as depicted in Figure 1 below. The reconfiguration request is sent during the same SFN the new allocation proposal is computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26501\_replaced([11214551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (i.e. the second SFN of the pooling window) and this request message includes:

* the new reconfiguration capacity proposed for each subpool in the L1 pool: proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp(5G\_UP\_ALG\_26501\_replaced([11214551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* explicit indication of the time when the new subpool capacity shall be reconfigured and applied at L1, which is second SFN of the next pooling window.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a flowchart illustrating inter and intra L1 subpool PRB pooling and subpool capacity reconfiguration procedures, considering subcell deactivation. The flowchart is organized by SFN (System Frame Number) and pooling intervals.
The top row indicates SFN values from N to N+15. Below this, pooling intervals are shown, with `poolingInterval(n)` spanning from SFN N to N+5, `poolingInterval(n+1)` from SFN N+6 to N+11, and `poolingInterval(n+2)` from SFN N+12 onwards.
The main body of the flowchart details various procedures:
\* **L1 Level:**
\* At SFN N+6, a request `XXPool_BbResourceReconfReq` is initiated, specifying SP Capacity, proposed stream and layer PRB capacities, and an application time at SFN=N+6.
\* This request is followed by a response `XXPool_BbResourceReconfResp` which can be 'success' (0) or 'failure' (1).
\* An `update:SP capacity` action is indicated with a dashed yellow arrow.
\* `SubcellDeact(#1)` occurs at SFN N+6, followed by `Num Active Subcells` and `InterL1Sp (#1)`.
\* At SFN N+11, `newCap(#1)` is shown, with a dashed blue arrow indicating a response, and `SubcellDeact(#2)` occurs, followed by `Num Active Subcells` and `InterL1Sp(#2)`.
\* At SFN N+16 (implied by the continuation of `poolingInterval(n+2)`), `newCap(#2)` is shown, with a dashed blue arrow indicating a response, and `SubcellDeact(#3)` occurs, followed by `Num Active Subcells` and `InterL1Sp(#3)`.
\* **BBRM Level:**
\* `IntraL1Sp` is shown at SFN N.
\* `IntraL1Sp` is also shown at SFN N+5.
\* `IntraL1Sp` is shown at SFN N+10.
\* `IntraL1Sp` is shown at SFN N+15.
\* **Cell Level (L2PS):**
\* For `Cell#1(L2PS)`, `Cell#2(L2PS)`, and `Cell#3(L2PS)`, the action `apply newAlloc` is shown starting from SFN N+6 and continuing through SFN N+11 and SFN N+16.
Vertical dashed yellow lines mark the boundaries of the pooling intervals. Blue arrows generally represent requests or actions, while dashed blue arrows represent responses. Yellow arrows indicate updates or specific actions within a time frame.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_17244.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Note:

* For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, only layerPRB as new subpool capacity (proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp) is carried out via subpool resource reconfiguration and synchronization procedure as above, streamPRB (proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp) is not needed and then should be set to 0.
* XXPool\_BbResourceReconfReq/XXPool\_BbResourceReconfResp: represents DL/ULPool\_BbResourceReconfReq or DL/ULPool\_BbResourceReconfResp messages and shall refer to the corresponding resource reconfiguration request/response messages used for DL[CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D] PRB pooling, respectively.

[CB012605-H]

Note:

* SubcellDeact represents all the subcell deactivation procedures that are executed before the Inter-L1 Subpool Pooling Procedure for the next Pooling Interval (i.e. the second SFN of the pooling window as mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10390\_replaced([11213243](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxGOh_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* L1 ARM capacity based Subcell Deactivation Procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27687\_replaced([11214642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). It is applicable if dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in DL.

[End CB012605-H]

* The decision of reconfiguration by the BBRM and applying of the new subpool capacity by L1 is done in a separate pooling window due to the time needed by L1 to synchronize and reconfigure a new subpool capacity. Moreover, it is also required that the SFN at which L2PS of cells in a subpool starts to use the new PRB allocation received from the BBRM ( 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6959\_replaced([11213357](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxG1mfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the SFN at which new capacity reconfiguration is done by L1, shall be aligned.
* After DlPool\_BbResourceReconfReq [CB012605-D]/UlPool\_BbResourceReconfReq[End CB012605-D] is sent, BBRM expects to receive response (DlPool\_BbResourceReconfResp[CB012605-D]/UlPool\_BbResourceReconfResp[End CB012605-D]) from L1 before the end of the same pooling window, in which request was sent, about the status of the reconfiguration request, in DL[CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D]. Thus
* if received response status is 'success' (0):
* BBRM updates currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp with the proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp values(5G\_UP\_ALG\_26501\_replaced([11214551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) agreed with L1.

[CB012605-H]

* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DL, BBRM updates currentActiveDlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool with the proposedActiveDlSubcellList. [End CB012605-H]
* if received response status is 'failure' (1):
* BBRM keeps currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp unchanged.

[CB012605-H]

* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DL, BBRM keeps the currentActiveDlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool unchanged. [End CB012605-H]
* If DlPool\_BbResourceReconfResp for DL [CB012605-D]or UlPool\_BbResourceReconfResp for UL[End CB012605-D], is not received by the BBRM at all, it is uncertain about the reconfiguration attempt by L1, hence, BBRM shall take the minimum of subpool capacities between the new proposed allocation and the current allocation, i.e.
* currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp = min{currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp , proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp};

[CB012605-H]

* If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DL, currentActiveDlSubcellList = intersection{currentActiveDlSubcellList, proposedActiveDlSubcellList} for each of the cells in L1 pool. [End CB012605-H]
* Once reconfiguration is done, the new subpool capacity value (currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp) will be used by the intra-subpool PRB pooling algorithm computation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25712\_replaced([11214266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) carried out in the next pooling window.

[CB012605-H]

* Once reconfiguration is done, the new list of active subcells i.e. currentActiveDlSubcellList in DL will be used by the intra-subpool PRB pooling algorithm computation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25712\_replaced([11214266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) carried out in the next pooling window.
* The currentActiveDlSubcellList shall be forwarded to L2-PS as listOfActiveDlSubcells.

-If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = FALSE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), all the DL subcells for each cell in the L1 Pool shall always be considered to be active, currentActiveDlSubcellList = All DL subcells configured for the cell in the L1 Pool

[End CB012605-H]

If there is only one subpool in the L1 pool, the reconfiguration request message should not be sent to the L1, and

 BBRM keeps currentLayerPrbCapacityPerSp unchanged (which should be equal to defaultLayerPrbCapacityPerSp.)

[CB012605-H]

 If dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in DL, BBRM updates currentActiveDlSubcellList for each of the cells in L1 pool with the proposedActiveDlSubcellList.

[End CB012605-H]

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-7**  (ID: `11214551`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
New Subpool Capacity Computation for Inter-L1 Subpool Reconfiguration

---

**3.31.5.11.0-5.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `11214577`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
-At the second SFN of each pooling period, BBRM computes new layerPRB capacity allocation proposals for each subpool of the L1 pool and this computed allocation proposal values will be used when subpool capacity reconfiguration is triggered by the BBRM. The subpool capacity update is carried out via subpool resource reconfiguration and synchronization procedure as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

-The new allocation proposal per subpool (Sp) is computed from poolMaxNumLayerPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26493\_replaced([11214467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) based on the minimum subpool resource need to be reserved (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26495\_replaced([11214481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the total layerPRB demand determined per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and maxSpLayerPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26497\_replaced([11214492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The computation for each subpool is done in the following order:

(1) Firstly, new allocation proposal to support the minimum capacity needed per subpool is computed.

* newMinLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = newMinLayerPrbCapacityPerSp (as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26495\_replaced([11214481](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjTPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB010630-E]

(1') From the remaining pool layerPRBs after (1), if any, new allocation proposal is computed in proportion to the total Configured Grant (CG) layerPRB demand per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in UL only. At each subpool, the additional allocation in this step shall not exceed its CG layerPRB demand and maxLayerPrbCgAllocLimitSp(i) for SP i (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* Sort SPs in the pool in the increasing order of min{ totalLayerPrbCgDemandPerSp(i), maxLayerPrbCgAllocLimitSp(i) } and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list.
* newCgLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = floor{{remainingLayerPrbPerPool – sum[j=i]{totalLayerPrbCgDemandPerSp(k)}}; where i, j are index of SP with j<i
* newCgLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = min{maxLayerPrbCgAllocLimitSp(i), newCgLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) }

where: remainingLayerPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumLayerPrb - sum[all Sp k] {newMinLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k)}

[End CB010630-E]

[CB008600-F]

(1'') From the remaining pool layerPRBs after (1) and (1'), if any, new allocation proposal is computed in proportion to the total DC-GBR layerPRB demand per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). At each subpool, the additional allocation in this step shall not exceed its DC-GBR layerPRB demand and maxLayerPrbDcGbrAllocLimitSp(i) for SP i (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* Sort SPs in the pool in the increasing order of min{ totalLayerPrbDcGbrDemandPerSp(i), maxLayerPrbDcGbrAllocLimitSp(i) } and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list.
* newDcGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = floor{{remainingLayerPrbPerPool – sum[j=i]{totalLayerPrbDcGbrDemandPerSp(k)}}; where i, j are index of SP with j<i
* newDcGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = min{maxLayerPrbDcGbrAllocLimitSp(i), newDcGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) }

where: remainingLayerPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumLayerPrb - sum[all Sp k] {newMinLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) + newCgLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k)}

[End CB008600-F]

(2) From the remaining pool layerPRBs after (1) [CB010630-E] and (1') [End CB010630-E] [CB008600-F] and (1'')[End CB008600-F], if any, new allocation proposal is computed in proportion to the total GBR layerPRB demand per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). At each subpool, the additional allocation in this step shall not exceed its GBR layerPRB demand and maxLayerPrbGbrAllocLimitSp(i) for SP i (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

* Sort SPs in the pool in the increasing order of min{ totalLayerPrbGbrDemandPerSp(i), maxLayerPrbGbrAllocLimitSp(i) } and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list.
* newGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = floor{{remainingLayerPrbPerPool – sum[j=i]{totalLayerPrbGbrDemandPerSp(k)}}; where i, j are index of SP with j<i
* newGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = min{maxLayerPrbGbrAllocLimitSp(i), newGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) }
* where: remainingLayerPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumLayerPrb - sum[all Sp k] {newMinLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [CB010630-E] + newCgLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB010630-E] [CB008600-F] + newDcGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB008600-F] }

(3) From the remaining pool layerPRBs after (2), if any, new allocation proposal is computed in proportion to the total nonGBR layerPRB demand per subpool (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). At each subpool, the additional allocation in this step shall not exceed its nonGBR layerPRB demand and maxLayerPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(i) for SP i (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

In case UL MIMO is enabled NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo in at least 1 cell in the L1 Pool, with spatial domain multiplexing (i.e. gnB allocates multiple UEs on the same PRBs), BBRM shall perform a 2 step allocation only in UL, where, the allocation in step 1 is limited to the capacity of estimated PRBs used with MU-MIMO pairing during the previous pooling period. If there is still any remaining non-GBR demand, the allocation in step 2 shall then consider the remaining demand and L1 layer PRB pool resources after the allocations in step 1 as input.

For all other cases, only allocations as described in Step 2 shall be considered.

Step 1:

* Sort SPs in the pool in the increasing order of min{ totalLayerPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(i), maxLayerPrbNonGbrMimoAllocLimitSp(i)} and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list
* remainingLayerPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumLayerPrb - sum[all Sp k] {newMinLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [CB010630-E] + newCgLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB010630-E] [CB008600-F] + newDcGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB008600-F] + newGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k)}
* newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep1(i) = floor{{remainingLayerPrbPerPool – sum[j=i]{totalLayerPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(k)}}; where i, j are index of SP with j<i
* newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep1(i) = min{maxLayerPrbNonGbrMimoAllocLimitSp(i), newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep1(i) }

where :

maxLayerPrbNonGbrMimoAllocLimitSp(i) is the maximum layer PRB allocation (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26499\_replaced([11214505](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) evaluated based on maxMuMimoCellLayerPrbNonGbrLimit(5G\_UP\_ALG\_28505\_replaced([11214210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

//update remaining demands

* totalLayerPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(i) = max{0, (totalLayerPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(i) - newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep1(i))}
* maxLayerPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(i) = max{0, (maxLayerPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(i) - newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep1(i))}

Step 2:

* If step 1 was executed,
* Step 2 shall be executed only if there is any remaining non-GBR PRB demand for any subpool (sum[all Sp k](totalLayerPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(k)) > 0);
* totalLayerPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(i) determined for each subpool at the end of step 1 shall be used as input to step 2.
* maxLayerPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(i) determined for each subpool at the end of step 1 shall be used as input to step 2.
* remainingLayerPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumLayerPrb - sum[all Sp k] {newMinLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [CB010630-E] + newCgLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB010630-E] [CB008600-F] + newDcGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB008600-F] + newGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) + newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep1(k)}
* Else
* remainingLayerPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumLayerPrb - sum[all Sp k] {newMinLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [CB010630-E] + newCgLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB010630-E]  [CB008600-F] + newDcGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k) [End CB008600-F] + newGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(k)}
* [for all subpools i] newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep1(i) = 0
* End If
* Sort SPs in the pool in the increasing order of min{ totalLayerPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(i), maxLayerPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(i)} and allocate to each SP i starting from the first in the sorted list
* newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep2(i) = floor{{remainingLayerPrbPerPool – sum[j=i]{totalLayerPrbNonGbrDemandPerSp(k)}}; where i, j are index of SP with j<i

// update allocated layer PRBs for non-GBR to include also allocation from step 1

* newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep2(i) = min{maxLayerPrbNonGbrAllocLimitSp(i), newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep2(i)}
* newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) = newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep1(i) + newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSpStep2(i)

(4) Allocate remaining pool layerPRBs, if any, to each subpool up to maxSpLayerPrb of a subpool is reached. Each subpool is allocated the remaining layerPRBs in a proportional manner based on the total previously allocated layerPRBs to each subpool. Each subpool can only be allocated the layerPRBs only upto its maxSpLayerPrb capacity.

* To create the subpools list with increasing priority order, sort the subpools in the pool in increasing order of maxSpLayerPrb. In case of subpools in the list with same maxSpLayerPrb, prioritize them in increasing order of (maxSpLayerPrb – newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp). If this cannot break the tie, no sorting (keep random subpool order list).
* Given from step (1) to (3):
* newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp (i) = newMinLayerPrbAllocationPerSp (i) [CB010630-E] + newCgLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) [End CB010630-E]  [CB008600-F] + newDcGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp(i) [End CB008600-F] + newGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp (i) + newNonGbrLayerPrbAllocationPerSp (i)
* remainingLayerPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumLayerPrb - sum [all Sp k] {newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp (k)}
* For each subpool in the sorted order list with newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp (i) >= 0:

If newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp (i) = 0

* Do not allocate any resources to this subpool
* AllocLayerPrbSp(i) = 0

Else

* Calculate the total already-allocated capacity for all the subpools after the current subpool in the sorted list
* allocatedLayerPrbSubsequentInclusive(i) = sum[all Sp k>=i] { newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp(k) }
* Calculate the total maximum allocation potential remaining (until the subpool - level maximums are reached) for all the subpools after the current subpool in the sorted list
* potentialLayerPrbSubsequent(i) = sum[all Sp k>i] { maxSpLayerPrb(k) – newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp(k) }
* Calculate the additional capacity to be allocated for the current subpool from the remaining capacity proportionally to the demand-based allocation and make sure that all layerPRB capacity will be allocated before running out of allocation potential in the subsequent subpools
* AllocLayerPrbSp = max{floor(remainingLayerPrbPerPool \* newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp(i) / allocatedLayerPrbSubsequentInclusive(i)),remainingLayerPrbPerPool - potentialLayerPrbSubsequent(i)}
* Do not exceed the maximum allocation of the subpool and do not allocate negative capacity
* AllocLayerPrbSp = min {AllocLayerPrbSp , maxSpLayerPrb(i) - newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp(i)}
* AllocLayerPrbSp = max {AllocLayerPrbSp , 0}

-Add the capacity allocated at this iteration to the total cumulative allocation of the subpool

* newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp(i) = newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp(i) + AllocLayerPrbSp
* Deduct the capacity allocated at this iteration from the total remaining capacity:
* remainingLayerPrbPerPool = remainingLayerPrbPerPool - AllocLayerPrbSp

End If

End If

(5) Allocate the rest of remaining layerPRBs of the pool, if any, equally between the subpools

* This step ensures that no layerPRB capacity of the pool remain unallocated. Any possible additional layerPRB capacity allocated in this step, (5), may not be used by the subpool as allocation up to the maxSpLayerPrb may already be satisfied in (4).

For i=0,1... totalNumOfSubPoolsInPool – 1

* remainingLayerPrbPerPool = poolMaxNumLayerPrb - sum [all Sp k] {newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp (k)}
* newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp (i) = newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp(i) + floor {remainingLayerPrbPerPool/ (totalNumOfSubPoolsInPool - i)}

End

* The new layerPRB capacity reallocation proposal for each subpool becomes the sum of the new allocations computed in (1) to (5); i.e.

proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp(i) = newTotalAllocLayerPrbSp (i) ;

Note: For TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e, with inter-L1subpool PRB pooling, distribution of pool capacity between subpools is done on layerPRB basis, and new layerPRB capacity for each SP (proposedLayerPrbCapacityPerSp) is determined and carried out via subpool resource reconfiguration and synchronization procedure as above, streamPRB (proposedStreamPrbCapacityPerSp) is not needed and then should be set to 0.

---

#### 3.31.5.11.0-6 LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e eCPRI 7-2e Layer PRB Pooling Scheduler Constraints (ID: 11214584)

**3.31.5.11.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11214591`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
RRM Parameters

---

**3.31.5.11.0-6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214598`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE in DL [CB012605-D]or slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed for UL[End CB012605-D], gNB-DU shall determine and maintain in every slot a certain set of parameters which shall provide a constraint that needs to be checked while allocating FD resources to every UE to be scheduled in the slot [CB012605-D]in DL/UL respectively[End CB012605-D].

* Maximum number of available layer PRBs

rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot = numAllocCellLayerPrb (Layer PRBs allocated every pooling period as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25712\_replaced([11214266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB012605-D]in DL/UL separately[End CB012605-D]

This parameter is re-initialised at the beginning of every pooling period to the new value of numAllocCellLayerPrb determined every pooling period [CB012605-D]in DL/UL separately[End CB012605-D]

* Maximum number of usable PRBs

rrmMaxNumUsablePrb = min {dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB012605-D]in DL/ ulBandwidth in UL (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB012605-D], (numAllocCellLayerPrb / 1)}  (Layer PRBs allocated every pooling period as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25712\_replaced([11214266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB012605-D]in DL/UL separately[End CB012605-D]

This parameter is re-initialised at the beginning of every slot to min {dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB012605-D]in DL/ ulBandwidth in UL (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB012605-D], (numAllocCellLayerPrb / 1)}

Note : Division by 1 is only to provide a complete formula; 1 is the lowest possible rank for any transmission and provides the worst case scenario where all transmissions in a slot might be with rank 1.

[CB012605-E]

* Maximum number of usable MU-MIMO PRBs (In case of MU-MIMO, with spatial multiplexing, the same FD resource could be used by multiple UEs))

rrmMaxNumUsableMuMimoPrb = numAllocCellLayerPrb / 1  (Layer PRBs allocated every pooling period as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25712\_replaced([11214266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

This parameter is re-initialised at the beginning of every pooling period to the new value of (numAllocCellLayerPrb / 1) determined every pooling period

Note : Division by 1 is only to provide a complete formula; 1 is the lowest possible rank for any transmission and provides the worst case scenario where all transmissions in a slot might be with rank 1.

[End CB012605-E]

* Layer PRBs used for PDSCH every slot

rrmNumUsedPdschLayerPrbPerSlot = rrmNumUsedPdschLayerPrbPerSlot + rrmNumLayerPrbUsedPerAllocation (layer PRBs used by each UE (including SIB/Paging/OSI/MIB etc) during resource allocation)

This parameter is re-initialised at the beginning of every slot to 0

* Remaining layer PRBs for PDSCH every slot

rrmRemainingPdschLayerPrbPerSlot = rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot(DL) - rrmNumUsedPdschLayerPrbPerSlot

This parameter is re-initialised at the beginning of every slot to 0

[CB012605-D]

* Layer PRBs used for PUSCH every slot

rrmNumUsedPuschLayerPrbPerSlot = rrmNumUsedPuschLayerPrbPerSlot + rrmNumLayerPrbUsedPerAllocation (layer PRBs used by each UE during resource allocation)

This parameter is re-initialised at the beginning of every slot to 0

* Remaining layer PRBs for PUSCH every slot

rrmRemainingPuschLayerPrbPerSlot = rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot(UL) - rrmNumUsedPuschLayerPrbPerSlot

This parameter is re-initialised at the beginning of every slot to 0

[End CB012605-D]

* The number of layer PRBs consumed for each allocation is defined as:

rrmNumLayerPrbUsedPerAllocation = N­Prb \* Rank

Where,

N­Prb = Number of PRBs allocated to the UE for a DL[CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D] transmission in the current slot / Number of PRBs used for a PDCCH Candidate

Rank = Rank of the UE used for the current DL[CB012605-D]/UL[End CB012605-D] scheduling / In case of a PDCCH/SIB1/OSI/Paging/Msg2/Msg4[CB012605-D]/Msg5[End CB012605-D]/any DCI-1\_0 based[CB012605-D]/any DCI 0\_0 based[End CB012605-D] transmission, Rank is always 1

* The number of layer PRBs required for a given number of FD PRB resources (for various calculations in gNB-DU)

numReqLayerPrb = N­Prb \* Rank

Where,

N­Prb = Number of FD PRB resources (RBGs shall be converted to PRBs)

Rank = Rank of the transmission/ In case of a PDCCH transmission, Rank is always 1

* The available number of FD PRB resources for a given number of layer PRB resources (for various calculations in gNB-DU)

numReqFdPrb = N­LayerPrb / Rank

Where,

N­LayerPrb = Number of Layer PRB resources

Rank = Rank of the transmission/ In case of a PDCCH transmission, Rank is always 1

Note: The FD resources calculated here are in units of PRB. Conversion to RBGs is required if RAT0 allocation scheme is being used in DL.

---

**3.31.5.11.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11214606`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
PDSCH Layer PRB usage and constraint

---

**3.31.5.11.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214613`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
In every slot, gNB-DU shall make sure that rrmNumUsedPdschLayerPrbPerSlot <= rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot (in DL) (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**3.31.5.11.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `11214618`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
PUSCH Layer PRB usage and constraint

---

**3.31.5.11.0-6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214623`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
In every slot, gNB-DU shall make sure that rrmNumUsedPuschLayerPrbPerSlot <= rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot (in UL) (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**3.31.5.11.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `11214630`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
PDCCH Layer PRB usage and constraint

---

**3.31.5.11.0-6.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13244504`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, gNB-DU shall re-evaluate the number of available CCEs in a slot and provides N\_CCE(usable)

If rrmMaxNumUsablePrb(5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) < RB size (number of PRBs) of the largest splitted CORESET or the CORESET selected in the slot.

[CB014923-C] If NRBTS/actPwrPoolingTDD = true, N\_CCE(usable) = floor( min(rrmMaxNumUsablePrb, maxLayerPrbCapableTargetPsd ) \* coresetDuration / 6)

else [End CB014923-C] N\_CCE(usable) = floor(rrmMaxNumUsablePrb \* coresetDuration / 6)

Else

N\_CCE(usable) = floor(coresetSize \* coresetDuration / 6 )

End If

Where,

**coresetSize : CORESET size (RB) computed by gNB-DU from the coresetFreqDomain attribute (each bit represents 6 RBs) received in the PsCell\_CellSetupReq message and associated to the search space**

**coresetDuration : The coresetDuration IE received in the PsCell\_CellSteupReq message for the coreset associated to the search space**

[CB014923-C] maxLayerPrbCapableTargetPsd: the maximum DL layer PRB capable of target PSD, from [13244480: Calculation of Maximum DL layer PRB capable of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_bKUSQMLXEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

[End CB014923-C]

gNB-DU shall also ensure that **sum [all PDCCH candidates in a slot] {rrmNumLayerPrbUsedPerAllocation} <** rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot (in DL) (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))\*\*\*\*
