#### 3.31.5.11.0-7 LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e Subcell Deactivation Procedure for eCPRI 7-2e (ID: 11214642)

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11214648`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Overview

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214656`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
The CPU resources in the L1 ARM controller are finite and can support only a certain number of subcells per L1 Subpool as well as per L1 Pool. One mechanism to achieve this result is to deactivate certain subcells of some cells such that more cells can be accommodated within the available resources.

The procedure defined in this section describes a mechanism to deactivate some subcells of some cells in the L1 Pool. The cells selected for deactivation are decided based on their PRB demands.

The procedure is executed in DL per pooling period such that the result of the procedure is used in the Inter-L1 Subpool Pooling algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26490\_replaced([11214449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the corresponding BB pooling period, and then again in case of a successful sub pool reconfiguration procedure (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26623\_replaced([11214533](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), by the load metric based Intra-L1 Subpool Pooling algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25712\_replaced([11214266](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVLvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of the next BB pooling period.

* The capacity limits for the max number of subcells supported by the L1 per subpool and per pool are provided by hidden NIDD params NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1SP/NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Pool for DL (Note: NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Sp/NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Pool for UL is not needed and not applicable for eCPRI 7-2e)

In every BB pooling period, the subcell deactivation procedure shall ensure that if a cell has its primary DL subcell in the L1 pool, then at least 1 DL subcell shall remain active for such a cell.

DL subcell pooling for eCPRI 7-2e reuse same flag as legacy eCPRI 7-2, DL subcell pooling procedure is enabled/disabled based on same flag received from higher layers.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Deactivation Procedure | TDD |  |
| DL Feature Flag | UL Feature Flag |  |
| L1 Arm Capacity based Subcell Deactivation (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27687\_replaced([11214642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed | Not supported |

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11214662`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Input Parameters for L1 ARM capacity based Subcell Deactivation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214675`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
The input parameters for the L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation algorithm are described below:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Input Parameter | Value |
| List of cells in L1 Pool | 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| Configured DL subcell list for each cell in L1 Pool (primary subcell and secondary subcell of the cell should be in same L1 pool) | 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6849\_replaced([11212229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |
| [CB008600-F]-layerPrbDemandDcGbr [End CB008600-F] - layerPrbDemandGbr - layerPrbDemandNonGbr | [CB008600-F]-layerPrbDemandDcGbr [End CB008600-F] - layerPrbDemandGbr - layerPrbDemandNonGbr (described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25725\_replaced([11214038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |
| maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp | Maximum number of subcells supported per L1 subpool, provided by the hidden NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Sp for DL & (note: NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Sp for UL is not used for eCPRI 7-2e) |
| maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool | Maximum number of subcells supported per L1 pool, provided by the hidden NIDD parameter NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumDLSubcellL1Pool for DL (note: NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxNumULSubcellL1Pool for UL is not used for eCPRI 7-2e) |
| numActiveSubcells (i) | Number of active DL subcells per cell ‘i’ in the L1 pool |

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-3**  (ID: `11214682`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Input Parameter Initialization

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214688`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Initialization of the input parameters for the Subcell deactivation procedure defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27692\_replaced([11214695](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxbfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is described below.

For each cell 'i' in the L1 Pool

//Initialize the numActiveSubcells(i) in DL as below

If enhanced DL MU-MIMO is enabled (NRCELL.actDlMuMimoEnh = TRUE) for cell 'i' :

numActiveSubcells(i) = Total number of configured DL subcells for cell 'i' in the L1 Pool

Else

numActiveSubcells(i) = 1 // If MU-MIMO is disabled and the cell has multiple DL subcells, only 1 DL subcell is used, and it will always be the primary DL subcell.

End If

End For

The L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure shall be triggered if any of the following condition are satisfied :

* numActiveSubcellsPerPool > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool or
* for at least 1 L1 subpool in the L1 Pool : numActiveSubcellsPerSubpool > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp

Note: The condition shall be checked in DL, no need to check UL.

where:

- numActiveSubcellPerPool = sum [all cells 'i' in the L1 Pool] {numActiveSubcells(i)}

- maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- numActiveSubcellsPerSubpool = sum [each L1 Subpool k in L1 Pool] [all cells 'i' in L1 Subpool(k)]{numActiveSubcells(i)}

- maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-4**  (ID: `11214695`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Subcell Deactivation Procedure

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11214701`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
When dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure shall be executed in DL in every BB pooling period for eCPRI 7-2e. The procedure shall be executed before the Inter-L1 Subpool pooling algorithm for the next pooling period as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26490\_replaced([11214449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxNjR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

This algorithm shall be run in DL for each L1 Pool. The decision to execute the algorithm shall depend on the flag mentioned below that are received during pool configuration from higher layers:

* dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for DL

Algorithm Input:

* Algorithm Input parameters are described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Algorithm Output:

* The proposed list of active DL subcells (proposedActiveDlSubcellList(i)) for each of the cell 'i' in the L1 pool.

Algorithm Steps:

* Initialization of deactivation algorithm parameters as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27690\_replaced([11214682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxa_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* If any of the trigger conditions specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27696\_replaced([11214721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxPYcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are satisfied,
* compute numActiveSubcells(i) for each cell 'i' in the L1 pool using the subcell deactivation procedure described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27694\_replaced([11214707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxb_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Else
* all the subcells configured for a cell in the pool shall be considered as active
* End If

Derive the proposedActiveDlSubcellList for each of the cell in L1 pool for the next pooling period from the computed numActiveSubcells as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27700\_replaced([11214753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxPYdvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-5**  (ID: `11214707`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Subcell Deactivation Algorithm

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11214714`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Subcell deactivation algorithm shall be executed for each L1 pool in every pooling period if any of the trigger conditions mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27696\_replaced([11214721](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxPYcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are satisfied.

This algorithm shall be executed in DL per pooling period for each L1 pool

Given:

* Input parameters provided in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) & initialised as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27690\_replaced([11214682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxa_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Output:

numActiveSubcells(i) for each of the cells in the L1 pool.

Steps:

* For each cell 'i' in L1 pool, calculate absolutePrbDemand(i) as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27698\_replaced([11214733](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxPYc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Let numActiveSubcellsInPool = sum [all cells 'i' in L1 pool]{numActiveSubcells(i)}
* For each L1 Subpool in the L1 Pool
* Let numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp = sum [all cells 'i' in L1 Subpool]{numActiveSubcells(i)}
* While numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp :
* Sort all cells 'i' in the L1 Subpool in increasing order of their absolutePrbDemand(i)
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list
* Let minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell = (Total number of primary subcells of the cell(i) in the L1 Subpool) // it is always equal to 1 based on eCPRI 7-2e BB cell sets deployment
* If (numActiveSubcells (i) > minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell)
* numActiveSubcells (i) = numActiveSubcells (i) - 1
* numActiveSubcellsInPool = numActiveSubcellsInPool - 1
* numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp = numActiveSubcellsInL1Sp - 1
* Re-calculate absolutePrbDemand(i) for the updated cell as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27698\_replaced([11214733](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxPYc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Break For loop
* End If
* End For
* If (No cells were updated)
* Break While loop
* End If
* End While
* End For
* While numActiveSubcellsInPool > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool:
* Sort all cells 'i' in the L1 pool in increasing order of their absolutePrbDemand(i)
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list
* Let minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell = (Total number of primary subcells of the cell(i) in the L1 Pool) //it is always equal to 1 based on eCPRI 7-2e BB cell sets deployment
* If (numActiveSubcells (i) > minRequiredNumActiveSubcellsForCell )
* numActiveSubcells (i) = numActiveSubcells (i) - 1
* numActiveSubcellsInPool = numActiveSubcellsInPool - 1
* Re-calculate absolutePrbDemand(i) for the updated cell as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27698\_replaced([11214733](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxPYc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Break For loop
* End If
* End For
* If (No cells were updated)
* Break While loop
* End If
* End While

The information about the L1 Pool/subpool where the cell's primary subcell is configured is part of the set of input parameters described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-6**  (ID: `11214721`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Conditions to trigger Subcell Deactivation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11214729`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
The L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure shall be triggered if any of the following condition are satisfied :

* numActiveSubcellsPerPool > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool or
* for at least 1 L1 subpool in the L1 Pool : numActiveSubcellsPerSubpool > maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp

where:

- numActiveSubcellPerPool = sum [all cells 'i' in the L1 Pool] {numActiveSubcells(i)}

- maxNumSubcellsPerL1Pool described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

- numActiveSubcellsPerSubpool = sum [each L1 Subpool k in L1 Pool] [all cells 'i' in L1 Subpool(k)]{numActiveSubcells(i)}

* maxNumSubcellsPerL1Sp described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-7**  (ID: `11214733`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Absolute PRB Demand Calculation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11214746`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Absolute PRB demand for each cell shall be calculated as described below

totalLayerPrbDemand = [CB008600-F] layerPrbDemandDcGbr + [End CB008600-F] layerPrbDemandGbr + layerPrbDemandNonGbr

maxLayerPrbCell = maxCellPrb \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb

absolutePrbDemand = totalLayerPrbDemand / maxLayerPrbCell

where :

-  numActiveSubcells is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

-  [CB008600-F] layerPrbDemandDcGbr, [End CB008600-F] layerPrbDemandGbr and layerPrbDemandNonGbr are described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

-  maxCellPrb is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where, instead of using the number of subcells calculated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), numActiveSubcells shall be used.

-  maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25734\_replaced([11214157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuHvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-8**  (ID: `11214753`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
Proposed Active Subcell List Creation

---

**3.31.5.11.0-7.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11214758`)

LayerPRB Pooling Algorithm for eCPRI 7-2e
The proposed DL active subcell list for each cell in L1 pool for the next BB pooling period is created as described below.

For each cell 'i' in L1 pool:

proposedActiveDlSubcellList (i) = First 'n' configured DL subcells for the cell 'i', starting with the primary subcell (the subcell in index=0 of the cell(i) configured DL subcell list)

where,

n= numActiveSubcells(i) for the cell 'i' in DL, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27688\_replaced([11214662](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxaPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

## 3.31.6 Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling

### 3.31.6.0-1 Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling Overview (ID: 11214770)

**3.31.6.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11214782`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
With increased PRB processing capacity at L1, each cell can be allocated much more PRBs with PRB pooling enabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5265\_replaced([11211936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-Ss_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This however does not translate into an increased throughput available at L1 in the same proportion to the increase in PRB processing. Hence, in order to maintain the expected peak throughput capacities of the L1 hardware, BBRM performs an additional pooling based on the available throughput capacities of each L1 Pool. The throughput capacity can also be limited due to constraint in the L2 Pool. This throughput pooling shall be dynamic in nature and shall provide an instantaneous throughput capacity (throughput per slot in a cell; i.e. sum of TBS of all PDSCH (for DL)/PUSCH(for UL) in a slot) for each cell in the L1 Pool based on the allocated [Before CB013527-A]PRBs[CB013527-A]cell PRBs/layer PRBs[End CB013527-A] provided to each cell at the end of the slow PRB pooling mechanism (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5265\_replaced([11211936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-Ss_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB013527-A]With eCPRI 7-2e based configurations, the slow PRB pooling mechanism mentioned above shall be considered as the Layer PRB pooling mechanism mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25709\_replaced([11214021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CB013527-A]

* The schedulers of each cell shall then ensure that the throughput capacities provided to them are not exceeded neither in DL nor UL.
* The BBRM shall re-evaluate the throughput allocations for cells within the L1 pool once within a predefined period, called the bbPoolEvalPeriod which is provided by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod for TDD.
* Instantaneous throughput pooling shall be performed only for TDD in DL/UL
* The throughput pooling allocation provided to each cell shall be applicable only to the TBS in PDSCH transmission in DL and PUSCH reception in UL

This functionality shall be controlled via the parameter tddInstTputPoolingAllowed received in AddressDistributionReq\_t message (refer 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3986\_replaced([11693605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D33F-P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))).

---

### 3.31.6.0-2 Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling Throughput Pooling Algorithm (ID: 11214789)

**3.31.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214796`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Throughput Pooling Initialization

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11214808`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
At system startup, BBRM shall learn L1 Pool/subpool and its properties.

The L1 Pool capacities for

* DL: Max number of supported active subcells per pool
* UL: Max number of supported active subcells per pool
* DL: Max throughput per L1 Pool
* UL: Max throughput per L1 Pool
* DL: Max throughput per L2 Pool
* UL: Max throughput per L2 Pool

shall be initialized at system startup.

The values of the configuration parameters will be retrieved from the hidden NIDD (NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity) (5G\_RAN\_OP\_3986\_replaced([11693605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D33F-P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) by CP-RT and provided to L2-RT.

Note: it is assumed that there is always enough pooled throughput processing capacity per L1 Pool to support at least the minimum [Before CB013527-A]PRB[CB013527-A]cell PRB/layer PRB[End CB013527-A] allocation configured by CPRT at cell setup (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214814`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Throughput Pooling Cell Measurements

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214820`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Nominal Cell Spectral Efficiency

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214827`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Overview

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214832`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
The nominal spectral efficiency is calculated differently for stream PRB pooling based allocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and layer PRB pooling based allocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25709\_replaced([11214021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This is because the layer PRB pooling machanism allocates layer PRBs to each cell which have considered the maximum number of layers that a cell can support, thus the spectral efficiency does not need to consider the number of layers.

Nominal spectral efficiency with Stream PRB pooling is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31080\_replaced([11214838](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxP_hPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Nominal spectral efficiency with Layer PRB pooling is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31081\_replaced([11214851](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxP_hvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11214838`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Nominal spectral efficiency with Stream PRB pooling

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214846`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
For each cell 'i', the nominal cell spectral efficiency (in units of bits per layer per prb) for DL/UL is defined as :

nominalCellSpecEff(i) = minActiveSubcellsPerCell \* minLayerPerCell \* rdSpectralEffForMinAlloc \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* numSymbolsPerSlot

where :

* minActiveSubcellsPerCell is the minimum number of active subcells for any cell in DL/UL.
* minActiveSubcellsPerCell = 1 (Each cells requires at least 1 subcell i.e. the primary subcell to be active for the cell to be on air)
* minLayerPerCell is the minimum number of layers used for any DL/UL transmission in any cell.
* minLayerPerCell = 1
* rdSpectralEffForMinAlloc is an R&D parameter that shall determine the number of bits per resource element for each layer. It shall depend on the modulation scheme proposed to be used for the nominal spectral efficiency estimation. It is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28825\_replaced([11215346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxTC0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numSubCarrierPerPrb is the number of sub carriers per PRB = 12
* numSymbolsPerSlot is the number of symbols used for a PDSCH/PUSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 13

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11214851`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Nominal spectral efficiency with Layer PRB pooling

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214858`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
For each cell 'i', the nominal cell spectral efficiency (in units of bits per prb) for DL/UL is defined as :

nominalCellSpecEff(i) = minActiveSubcellsPerCell \* rdSpectralEffForMinAlloc \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* numSymbolsPerSlot

where :

* minActiveSubcellsPerCell is the minimum number of active subcells for any cell in DL/UL.
* minActiveSubcellsPerCell = 1 (Each cells requires at least 1 subcell i.e. the primary subcell to be active for the cell to be on air)
* rdSpectralEffForMinAlloc is an R&D parameter that shall determine the number of bits per resource element for each layer. It shall depend on the modulation scheme proposed to be used for the nominal spectral efficiency estimation. It is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28825\_replaced([11215346](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxTC0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numSubCarrierPerPrb is the number of sub carriers per PRB = 12
* numSymbolsPerSlot is the number of symbols used for a PDSCH/PUSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 13

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214864`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Maximum Cell Spectral Efficiency

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11214870`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Overview

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11214876`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
The maximum spectral efficiency is calculated differently for stream PRB pooling based allocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and layer PRB pooling based allocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25709\_replaced([11214021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This is because the layer PRB pooling mechanism allocates layer PRBs to each cell which have considered the maximum number of layers that a cell can support, thus the spectral efficiency does not need to consider the number of layers.

Maximum spectral efficiency with Stream PRB pooling is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31084\_replaced([11214883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxP_i_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Maximum spectral efficiency with Layer PRB pooling is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31085\_replaced([11214896](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxP_jfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214883`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Maximum spectral efficiency with Stream PRB pooling

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12741165`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
For each cell 'i', the maximum cell spectral efficiency (in units of bits per layer per prb) is defined as :

For DL

* **maxCellSpecEff(i) = numLayersPerSubcell(i) \* maxBitsPerRe \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* numSymbolsPerSlot**
* **typicalmaxCellSpecEff(i) = numLayersPerSubcell(i) \* maxBitsPerRe \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* typicalnumSymbolsPerSlot**

where :

* numLayersPerSubcell(i) is the maximum number of layers supported by each subcell for cell 'i' in DL defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxBitsPerRe shall depend on the highest modulation scheme possible in the cell.

[CB008949-C]

if 1024 QAM is enabled in the cell (NIDD:NRCELL.actDl1024Qam is equal to value other than 'disabled')

maxBitsPerRe = 10

else [End CB008949-C]  if 256 QAM is enabled in the cell (NIDD:NRCELL.actDl256Qam)

maxBitsPerRe = 8

else

maxBitsPerRe = 6

end if

* numSubCarrierPerPrb is the number of sub carriers per PRB = 12
* numSymbolsPerSlot is the maximum number of symbols used for a PDSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 13.

- typicalnumSymbolsPerSlot is the number of symbols used for a PDSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 12 (assuming 2 symbols in a DL slot will be used for PDCCH)

For UL

* **maxCellSpecEff(i) = numLayersPerSubcell(i) \* maxBitsPerRe \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* numSymbolsPerSlot**
* **typicalmaxCellSpecEff(i) = numLayersPerSubcell(i) \* maxBitsPerRe \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* typicalnumSymbolsPerSlot**

where :

* numLayersPerSubcell(i) is the maximum number of layers supported by each subcell for cell 'i' in UL defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxBitsPerRe shall depend on the highest modulation scheme possible in the celll.

if 256 QAM is enabled in the cell (NIDD:NRCELL.actUl256Qam)

maxBitsPerRe = 8

else

maxBitsPerRe = 6

end if

* numSubCarrierPerPrb is the number of sub carriers per PRB = 12
* numSymbolsPerSlot is the maximum number of symbols used for a PUSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 13.
* typicalnumSymbolsPerSlot is the number of symbols used for a PUSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 13

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11214896`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Maximum spectral efficiency with Layer PRB pooling

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12741167`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
For each cell 'i', the maximum cell spectral efficiency (in units of bits per prb) is defined as :

For DL

* **maxCellSpecEff(i) = maxBitsPerRe \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* numSymbolsPerSlot**
* **typicalmaxCellSpecEff(i) = maxBitsPerRe \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* typicalnumSymbolsPerSlot**

where :

* maxBitsPerRe shall depend on the highest modulation scheme possible in the cell.

[CB008949-C]

if 1024 QAM is enabled in the cell (NIDD:NRCELL.actDl1024Qam is equal to value other than 'disabled')

maxBitsPerRe = 10

else [End CB008949-C] if 256 QAM is enabled in the cell (NIDD:NRCELL.actDl256Qam)

maxBitsPerRe = 8

else

maxBitsPerRe = 6

end if

* numSubCarrierPerPrb is the number of sub carriers per PRB = 12
* numSymbolsPerSlot is the maximum number of symbols used for a PDSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 13.

- typicalnumSymbolsPerSlot is the number of symbols used for a PDSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 12 (assuming 2 symbols in a DL slot will be used for PDCCH)

For UL

* **maxCellSpecEff(i) = maxBitsPerRe \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* numSymbolsPerSlot**
* **typicalmaxCellSpecEff(i) = maxBitsPerRe \* numSubCarrierPerPrb \* typicalnumSymbolsPerSlot**

where :

* maxBitsPerRe shall depend on the highest modulation scheme possible in the celll.

if 256 QAM is enabled in the cell (NIDD:NRCELL.actUl256Qam)

maxBitsPerRe = 8

else

maxBitsPerRe = 6

end if

* numSubCarrierPerPrb is the number of sub carriers per PRB = 12
* numSymbolsPerSlot is the maximum number of symbols used for a PUSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 13.
* typicalnumSymbolsPerSlot is the number of symbols used for a PUSCH transmission in a slot. It's value is set to 13.

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11214909`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Cell Throughput Demands/Capacities Determination

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12803250`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
For each cell 'i', the minimum throughput allocation in DL/UL is defined as :

* **minDataPerSlotAlloc(i) = numMinPrbPoolingAlloc(i) \* nominalCellSpecEff(i)**

where,

* numMinPrbPoolingAlloc(i) is the minimum allocation for cell 'i' based on the PRB pooling algorithm as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* nominalCellSpecEff(i) is the nominal spectral efficiency used to calculate a minimum throughput allocation for cell 'i' as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28819\_replaced([11214820](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxP_gfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For each cell 'i', the maximum possible throughput capacity in DL/UL is defined as :

* **maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) = numPrbPoolingAlloc(i) \* maxCellSpecEff(i)**

where,

* numPrbPoolingAlloc(i) is the allocated number of PRBs for cell 'i' based on the PRB pooling algorithm as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* maxCellSpecEff(i) is the maximum cell spectral efficiency for cell 'i' as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28821\_replaced([11214864](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxP_iPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**[PR849371-26R1**]\*\*\*\*

For each cell 'i', the maximum possible throughput capacity in DL/UL is defined as :

* **typicalmaxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) = numPrbPoolingAlloc(i) \* typicalmaxCellSpecEff(i)**

where,

* numPrbPoolingAlloc(i) is the allocated number of PRBs for cell 'i' based on the PRB pooling algorithm as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* typicalmaxCellSpecEff(i) is the typical maximum cell spectral efficiency for cell 'i' as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28821\_replaced([11214864](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxP_iPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End PR849371-26R1]

For each cell 'i', the estimated throughput demand in DL/UL is defined as :

* **dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc(i) = numPrbPoolingAlloc(i) \* cellSpecEff(i) \* 8(=>Bytes to Bits)**

where,

* numPrbPoolingAlloc(i) is the allocated number of PRBs for cell 'i' based on the PRB pooling algorithm as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* cellSpecEff(i) is the estimated cell spectral efficiency for cell 'i' as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For each cell 'i', the intermediate estimated throughput demand in DL/UL is defined as :

* dataPerSlotForPrbDemand(i) = intermediateAllocatedBbrmPrb(i) \* cellSpecEff(i) \* 8(=>Bytes to Bits)

where,

* intermediateAllocatedBbrmPrb(i) is the allocated number of PRBs for cell 'i' based on the PRB pooling algorithm as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* cellSpecEff(i) is the estimated cell spectral efficiency for cell 'i' as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

NOTE:

If stream PRB pooling is used (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

All spectral efficiencies are calculated in bits per layer per prb

else

All spectral efficiencies are calculated in bits per prb

End If

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11214933`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Cell PRB Demand Estimate

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11214936`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Overview

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11214951`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
For each cell 'i', the overall cell PRB demand estimate (input parameter cellPrbDemand; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is required during the throughput demand based allocation procedure.

The demand estimate is calculated differently for stream PRB pooling based allocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and layer PRB pooling based allocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25709\_replaced([11214021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Cell PRB demand estimate (cellPrbDemand; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with Stream PRB pooling is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32719\_replaced([11214958](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQml_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB013527-A-UPD002]

Cell PRB demand estimate (cellPrbDemand; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with Layer PRB pooling is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32720\_replaced([11214978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmmvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB013527-A-UPD002]

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11214958`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Cell PRB Demand Estimate with Stream PRB Pooling

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11214970`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
The input parameter cellPrbDemand with Stream PRB pooling is defined as below

* PRB Demand Estimate for DL :
* cellPrbDemand = streamPrbDemandGbr + [CB008600-F]streamPrbDemandDcGbr +[End CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandNonGbr
* PRB Demand Estimate for UL :
* cellPrbDemand = streamPrbDemandGbr + [CB008600-F]streamPrbDemandDcGbr +[End CB008600-F] streamPrbDemandNonGbr + streamPrbDemandCg

Where,

* streamPrbDemandGbr, streamPrbDemandNonGbr, streamPrbDemandCg [CB008600-F],streamPrbDemandDcGbr[End CB008600-F]  : PRB demand estimates with stream PRB pooling described as input parameters to the stream PRB pooling mechanism in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13412\_replaced([11212449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11214978`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Cell PRB Demand Estimate with Layer PRB Pooling

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-2.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214983`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
The input parameter cellPrbDemand with Layer PRB pooling is defined as below

* PRB Demand Estimate for DL :
* cellPrbDemand = layerPrbDemandGbr + layerPrbDemandDcGbr + layerPrbDemandNonGbr
* PRB Demand Estimate for UL :
* cellPrbDemand = layerPrbDemandGbr + layerPrbDemandDcGbr + layerPrbDemandCg + layerPrbDemandNonGbr

Where,

* layerPrbDemandGbr , layerPrbDemandNonGbr, layerPrbDemandCg, layerPrbDemandDcGbr : PRB demand estimates with layer PRB pooling described as input parameters to the layer PRB pooling mechanism in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25715\_replaced([11214295](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxM8MPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11214990`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Load Metric Based Throughput Pooling Algorithm

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11214997`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Overview

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12705831`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Throughput pooling is performed based on the number of PRBs/Layer PRBs (in case of eCPRI 7-2a stream PRB based pooling, refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); in case of eCPRI 7-2e layer PRB based pooling, refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25709\_replaced([11214021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) allocated to each cell at the end of the slow PRB Pooling procedure. The allocation is calculated separately for UL/DL.

The procedure overview is as follows :

* At each cell, each DL/UL 5G-L2-RT (scheduler) determines the spectral efficiency at the end of each bbPoolEvalPeriod (which is provided **by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod for TDD) SFN N per DL/UL, respectively.**
* In the first SFN of each bbPoolEvalPeriod (SFN N+1), BBRM receives the spectral efficiency measurement from each Cell's UL and DL scheduler along with a request for the amount of available PRBs that can be used by the cell starting from the next SFN.
* The BBRM determines the total throughput to allocate to each cell of the L1 Pool based on the throughput demand calculated for each cell using the allocated number of PRBs/layer PRBs at the end of the slow PRB pooling algorithm (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5265\_replaced([11211936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-Ss_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the received cell spectral efficiencies.
* The BBRM sends back the throughput capacity allocated to the cell scheduler (DL/UL) of each cell.
* The new grant is to be used starting from SFN N+2.

Note: during SFN N+1 (beginning of the new bbPoolEvalPeriod ), each cell is using the old allocation as a new allocation is yet to be determined.

**-Algorithm Input :**

* Algorithm Input parameters are described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

**-Algorithm Output :**

* allocDataPerSlot : total usable throughput per slot (in bytes/slot), granted per cell including the configured minimum allocation per cell.

**- Algorithm Steps :**

Note1: allocation of PRB grant per cell is started in algorithm step2 with the configured min PRB value and updated in consecutive algorithm steps

* Each cell shall be allocated the minimum amount of throughput as per the configured min value (numMinAlloc) and nominal spectral efficiency : 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28795\_replaced([11215033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* Then, if there is any remaining throughput capacity of the pool, poolDataPerSlotToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28795\_replaced([11215033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional throughput to the cell based on allocated PRBs/layer PRBs to the cell and its estimated cell spectral efficiency upto the cell's estimated throughput demand (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28796\_replaced([11215046](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
* Then, if there is any remaining throughput capacity of the pool, poolDataPerSlotToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28796\_replaced([11215046](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate additional throughput to the cell based on allocated PRBs/layer PRBs to the cell and its estimated cell spectral efficiency upto the cell's maximum possible throughput capacity(5G\_UP\_ALG\_28797\_replaced([11215059](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
* Then, if there is any remaining throughput capacity of the pool, poolDataPerSlotToShare >0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28797\_replaced([11215059](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), allocate the remaining throughput capacity to each cell in proportion to the combined throughput allocated in the previous steps for each cell (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28798\_replaced([11215075](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
* [CB015330-A] If rdTddInstTputPoolingUlEnhEnable = True, the uplink cell throughput reduction factor (i.e., ulCellTpRedFactorInSch) is computed as in ([12688989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_eCvq4FZNEfC45IKMrv0u7Q)) [End CB015330-A]
* Convert the allocated throughput into the appropriate unit (from bits/slot to bytes/slot) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28836\_replaced([11215089](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNqvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

- DL and UL resources are pooled separately and the BBRM determines the amount of DL and UL throughput resources for each cell within the same L1 pool

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11215011`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Input Parameters for Load Metric Based Throughput Pooling Algorithm

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13370295`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
A lot of inputs to the throughput pooling algorithm require the outputs and other parameters from slow PRB pooling. BBRM supports two independent and mutually exclusive mechanisms to perform PRB pooling: Stream PRB based PRB pooling (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and layer PRB based PRB pooling (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25709\_replaced([11214021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Each mechanism can be enabled separately in DL/UL. However, for a given L1 Pool, it is not possible to have a mix of layer and stream PRB pooling.

Stream PRB Pooling is activated by :

* slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed in DL for TDD
* slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed in UL for TDD

Layer PRB Pooling is activated by :

* slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed in DL for TDD
* slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed in UL for TDD

-The input parameters for the load metric based throughput pooling algorithm for the different PRB pooling mechanisms are described in the table below:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Input Parameters** | **Value** |  |
|  | **Stream PRB Pooling** | **Layer PRB Pooling** |
| Cell List | Cell list per L1 Pool with numAllocCellPrb > 0 (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | Cell list per L1 Pool with numAllocCellLayerPrb > 0 (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25713\_replaced([11214271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |
| maxL1PoolThroughput | Maximum throughput supported per L1 Pool. The value is provided via hidden NIDD parameters in NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity (5G\_RAN\_OP\_3986\_replaced([11693605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D33F-P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) DL: maxPdschTpSlotL1Pool UL: maxPuschTpSlotL1Pool | Maximum throughput supported per L1 Pool. The value is provided via hidden NIDD parameters in NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity (5G\_RAN\_OP\_3986\_replaced([11693605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D33F-P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) DL: maxPdschTpSlotL1Pool UL: maxPuschTpSlotL1Pool |
| maxL2PoolThroughput | Maximum throughput supported per L2 Pool. The value is provided via hidden NIDD parameters in NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity (5G\_RAN\_OP\_3986\_replaced([11693605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D33F-P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) DL: maxPdschTpSlotL2Pool UL: maxPuschTpSlotL2Pool | Maximum throughput supported per L2 Pool. The value is provided via hidden NIDD parameters in NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity (5G\_RAN\_OP\_3986\_replaced([11693605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D33F-P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) DL: maxPdschTpSlotL2Pool UL: maxPuschTpSlotL2Pool |
| numMinPrbPoolingAlloc | [PR869830] If artificial load for EMF is enabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17863\_replaced([11183915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_PvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))     max (Roundup (NRCELL.targetTotalLoadForEmf \* maxCellPrb# (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7012\_replaced([11212774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDLPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) / 100), numMinPRBAlloc# (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) else [End PR869830]     numMinPRBAlloc# (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [PR869830] End [End PR869830] | [PR869830] If artificial load for EMF is enabled  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17863\_replaced([11183915](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvN_PvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then     max (Roundup ( (NRCELL.emfTargetTotalLoad \* maxCellLayerPrbEmf) / 100) , numMinLayerPRBAlloc) where \* numMinlayerPRBAlloc defined in (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \* maxCellLayerPrbEmf : Max Cell Layer PRBs required for artificial load generation (Refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29773\_replaced([11214224](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVKPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) else [End PR869830] numMinlayerPRBAlloc (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4304\_replaced([11277361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpMt7PvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [PR869830] End [End PR869830] |
| numPrbPoolingAlloc | numAllocCellPrb (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (Separate value for DL/UL) | numAllocCellLayerPrb (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25713\_replaced([11214271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (Separate value for DL/UL) |
| intermediateAllocatedBbrmPrb | intermediateAllocCellPrb (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (Separate value for DL/UL) | intermediateAllocLayerPrb (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25713\_replaced([11214271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (Separate value for DL/UL) |
| numActiveSubcells | DL : numAllocDlSubcell (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) UL : numAllocUlSubcell (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13527\_replaced([11212361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAu-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) | DL : numAllocDlSubcell (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25713\_replaced([11214271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) UL : numAllocUlSubcell (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25713\_replaced([11214271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) |

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11215033`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Allocation of the configured minimum resource per Cell

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11215040`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
- This section provides an allocation of the configured minimum resource per Cell.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* poolDataPerSlotToShare = ((min {maxL1PoolThroughput, maxL2PoolThroughput}) \* 1000)
* Multiplication by 1000 since the unit of maxL1PoolThroughput is kbits/slot

For each cell 'i' in the cell list mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), provide the initial minimum allocation per cell:

* allocDataPerSlot(i) = minDataPerSlotAlloc(i)
* poolDataPerSlotToShare = poolDataPerSlotToShare - allocDataPerSlot(i)

End For

If poolDataPerSlotToShare <= 0,

* Stop further allocation steps and end throughput pooling.

End If

where :

* minDataPerSlotAlloc(i) : minimum throughput allocation for cell 'i' defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28823\_replaced([11214909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note : Cells which are not allocated any PRB resources during slow PRB Pooling are not allocated any throughput capacity.

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11215046`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Allocation of additional throughput per cell based on estimated spectral efficiency with allocated PRB resources upto the cell's estimated throughput demand

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12803275`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
- This section provides an allocation of additional throughput capacity to a cell based on the allocated PRB resources from slow PRB pooling and the cell's estimated spectral efficiency (refer cellSpecEff: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), upto its estimated throughput demand.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* poolDataPerSlotToShare :  5G\_UP\_ALG\_28795\_replaced([11215033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* allocDataPerSlot(i) : 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28795\_replaced([11215033](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Only consider cells from the cell list that have traffic (cellPrbDemand(i) >0)
* Sort all the remaining cells from the cell list **in the increasing order of** min{([Before PR849371-26R1] maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) [PR849371-26R1] typicalmaxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) [End PR849371-26R1] - allocDataPerSlot(i)), dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc(i)**}.** In case several cells have same value resulting from the **min operation and if they have different dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc value.*****\****\*
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..*N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and* N is number of cells in the sorted list\*\*
* allocData(i) = min{dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc(i), poolDataPerSlotToShare \* dataPerSlotForPrbDemand(i) / sum[*N >k>=i]{dataPerSlotForPrbDemand(k)}}*
* allocData(i) = min{allocData(i), ([Before PR849371-26R1] maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) [PR849371-26R1] typicalmaxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) [End PR849371-26R1] - allocDataPerSlot(i))}
* poolDataPerSlotToShare = poolDataPerSlotToShare - allocData(i) //Update available capacity for remaining cells
* allocDataPerSlot(i) = allocDataPerSlot(i) + allocData(i) // update allocation of cell 'i'

End For

If poolDataPerSlotToShare <= 0,

* Stop further allocation steps and end throughput pooling.

End If

where :

[Before PR849371-26R1]

* maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) : maximum throughput demand for cell 'i' defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28823\_replaced([11214909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[PR849371-26R1]

* typicalmaxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) : typical maximum throughput demand for cell 'i' defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28823\_replaced([11214909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with typicalMaxCellSpecEff

[End PR849371-26R1]

* dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc(i) : estimated throughput demand for cell 'i' defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28823\_replaced([11214909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* dataPerSlotForPrbDemand(i): the intermediate estimated throughput demand for cell 'i' defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28823\_replaced([11214909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* cellPrbDemand(i) : Estimated PRB demand for cell 'i' mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11215059`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Allocation of additional throughput per cell based on estimated spectral efficiency with allocated PRB resources upto the cell's maximum possible throughput capacity

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11215068`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
- This section provides an allocation of additional throughput capacity to a cell based on the allocated PRB resources from slow PRB pooling and the cell's estimated spectral efficiency (refer cellSpecEff: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), upto its maximum possible throughput capacity

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* poolDataPerSlotToShare :  5G\_UP\_ALG\_28796\_replaced([11215046](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* allocDataPerSlot(i) : 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28796\_replaced([11215046](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNpPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[PR808068]

* Only consider cells from the cell list that have traffic (cellPrbDemand(i) >0)

[End PR808068]

* Sort all [PR808068]the remaining[End PR808068] cells from the cell list in the increasing order of min{(maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) - allocDataPerSlot(i)), dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc(i)}.  In case several cells have same value resulting from the min operation and if they have different dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc value, then these cells are sorted in increasing order of their dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc value.
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list
* If sum[N >k>=i]{dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc(k)} =0; i.e. throughput demand = 0 for all cells k >= i,
* Break loop. Stop processing this step for the remaining cells.
* Else
* allocData(i) = poolDataPerSlotToShare \* dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc(i) / sum[N >k>=i]{dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc(k)}
* allocData(i) = min{allocData(i), (maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) - allocDataPerSlot(i))}
* poolDataPerSlotToShare = poolDataPerSlotToShare - allocData(i) //Update available capacity for remaining cells
* allocDataPerSlot(i) = allocDataPerSlot(i) + allocData(i) .// update allocation of cell 'i'
* End If

End For

If poolDataPerSlotToShare <= 0,

* Stop further allocation steps and end throughput pooling.

End If

where :

* maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) : maximum throughput demand for cell 'i' defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28823\_replaced([11214909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* dataPerSlotForPrbAlloc(i) : estimated throughput demand for cell 'i' defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28823\_replaced([11214909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[PR808068]

* cellPrbDemand(i) : Estimated PRB demand for cell 'i' mentioned in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End PR808068]

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-6**  (ID: `11215075`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Allocation of any remaining throughput capacity

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11215084`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
- This section provides an allocation of any remaining throughput capacity to a cell based on its current throughput allocation.

* Given:
* input parameters: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28793\_replaced([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* poolDataPerSlotToShare :  5G\_UP\_ALG\_28797\_replaced([11215059](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* allocDataPerSlot(i) : 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28797\_replaced([11215059](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNpvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* Only consider cells from the cell list that have not achieved their maximum throughput capacity i.e. (maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) - allocDataPerSlot(i)) > 0
* Sort the cells from above in the increasing order of (maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) - allocDataPerSlot(i)).  In case several cells have same value, sort those cells in any order.
* For i=0,1,2,3 ..N-1:  where i= index of sorted cell and N is number of cells in the sorted list
* Calculate already allocated capacity for all the remaining cells in the sorted list including the current cell
* allocDataPerSlotSubsequentInclusive(i) = sum[N >k>=i]{allocDataPerSlot(k)}
* Calculate the total potential allocation for the remaining cells upto their maximum allocation capacity
* potentialDataPerSlotSubsequent(i) = sum[N >k>i]{(maxDataPerSlotAlloc(k) - allocDataPerSlot(k)}
* Proportionally allocate the remaining capacity to the current cell based on its current allocation and the potential demand from the remaining cells
* allocRemainingDataPerSlot(i) = max{(poolDataPerSlotToShare \* allocDataPerSlot(i) / allocDataPerSlotSubsequentInclusive(i)), (poolDataPerSlotToShare - potentialDataPerSlotSubsequent(i))}
* Check max/min constraints
* allocRemainingDataPerSlot(i) = min{allocRemainingDataPerSlot(i),  (maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) - allocDataPerSlot(i))}
* allocRemainingDataPerSlot(i) = max{0, allocRemainingDataPerSlot (i)}
* allocDataPerSlot(i) = allocDataPerSlot(i) + allocRemainingDataPerSlot(i) // update allocation of cell 'i'
* poolDataPerSlotToShare = poolDataPerSlotToShare - allocRemainingDataPerSlot(i) //Update available capacity for remaining cells

End For

* maxDataPerSlotAlloc(i) : maximum throughput demand for cell 'i' defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28823\_replaced([11214909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmkPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-7**  (ID: `12688989`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Uplink Throughput Scaling in Enhanced TDD Scheduling

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `12688994`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
If rdTddInstTputPoolingUlEnhEnable = True, the uplink cell throughput reduction factor (i.e., ulCellTpRedFactorInSch) is determined as follows:

• If ulCellTpRedFactor < 1 and the sum of allocDataPerSlot(i, t) across all cells p in L1 pool l exceeds MaxUplinkThroughputLimit:

○ Set ulCellTpRedFactorInSch = ulCellTpRedFactor for all cells.

• Else:

○ Set ulCellTpRedFactorInSch = 1 for all cells.

Else

ulCellTpRedFactorInSch = ulCellTpRedFactor.

Where:

MaxUplinkThroughputLimit is the maximum uplink throughput limit and is defined as:

MaxUplinkThroughputLimit = NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxUlPoolTpLimit \* min(NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxPuschTpSlotL1Pool, NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxPuschTpSlotL2Pool).

Where:

* NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxUlPoolTpLimit is a Ul cell throughput reduction factor and defined as per ([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
* NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxPuschTpSlotL1Pool is defined as per ([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))
* NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.maxPuschTpSlotL2Pool is defined as per ([11215011](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxQmn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))

ulCellTpRedFactorInSch shall be reported in every BBRM interval to L2PS and will be used by L2PS ([11215139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-8**  (ID: `11215089`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Convert allocated throughput into required unit

---

**3.31.6.0-2.0-3.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11215095`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
- This section converts the allocated throughput into the units expected by the DL/UL scheduler (bytes/slot)

* Given:
* allocDataPerSlot(i) : 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28798\_replaced([11215075](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The throughput allocated by BBRM is in bits/slot, it shall be converted to the units expected by the DL/UL scheduler (bytes/slot)

For each cell 'i' in the L1 Pool

* allocDataPerSlot(i) = floor(allocDataPerSlot(i) / 8)

End For

Rounding off errors can be handled in entity level specification

---

### 3.31.6.0-3 Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling RRM Parameters (ID: 11215102)

**3.31.6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11215111`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
If tddInstTputPoolingAllowed = TRUE (refer 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3986\_replaced([11693605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D33F-P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))), gNB-DU shall determine and maintain in every slot the following parameters which shall provide a constraint that needs to be checked while allocating DL/UL throughput (TBS) to every UE to be scheduled in the slot in DL/UL respectively.

* Throughput used per slot

rrmUsedCellThroughputPerSlot(DL/UL) = rrmUsedCellThroughputPerSlot(DL/UL) + TBS calculated for the current UE being scheduled in DL/UL respectively

This parameter is re-initialised at the beginning of every slot to 0

---

### 3.31.6.0-4 Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling Throughput pooling constraints and scheduler actions (ID: 11215118)

**3.31.6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11215125`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Overview

---

**3.31.6.0-4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13314395`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
If tddInstTputPoolingAllowed = TRUE (refer 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3986\_replaced([11693605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D33F-P9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))), the scheduler of each cell shall keep track of the used throughput capacity per slot independently in DL/UL (rrmUsedCellThroughputPerSlot; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29086\_replaced([11215102](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For each UE to be scheduled (PDSCH/PUSCH messages to be sent towards L1/L2LO) in a slot in DL/UL, the scheduler shall check and ensure that the following condition is satisfied :

* rrmUsedCellThroughputPerSlot <= allowedDataPerSlot

where,

* rrmUsedCellThroughputPerSlot : The total throughput (sum of TBS) used in the cell in a slot in DL/UL (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29086\_replaced([11215102](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxRNrPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This includes the TBS of all previously scheduled UEs in the slot and the TBS of the current UE being scheduled in DL/UL.
* allowedDataPerSlot : The allowed throughput to be considered by the scheduler of each cell in DL/UL described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_30277\_replaced([11215139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0svvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

This check shall be performed by the scheduler of each cell in DL/UL respectively before scheduling each UE (i.e. sending PDSCH/PUSCH messages to L1/L2LO) in DL/UL for the current slot.

In case the constraint mentioned above is violated for a cell i.e. rrmUsedCellThroughputPerSlot > allowedDataPerSlot**either in DL or in UL, the respective DL/UL scheduler of the cell shall do the following:**

* Reduce the PRB allocation for the current UE as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29119\_replaced([11215165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0tvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the UE except for any Random Access UE (Msg2/Msg3/Msg4/Msg5) or a HARQ reTx UE, or a fake UE for artificial load generation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_17426\_replaced([11183931](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvOmQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or a Configured Grant UE.
* If reducing the number of PRBs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29119\_replaced([11215165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0tvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) does not reduce the throughput to be within the constraint mentioned earlier, or, it is one of the exceptional UEs mentioned ealier, then the current UE shall be stopped from being scheduled i.e.
* Remove/discard any PDCCH and PUCCH resources allocated to the current UE 'i' for this Tx/Rx
* Discard any updates done to any scheduling parameters that would be sent to the UE 'i' for this Tx/Rx (via PDCCH, such as NDI, rvIndex etc.)
* In UL, if the current UE had UCI on PUSCH, allocate and schedule the PUCCH resource that has been reserved for UCI reception for this UE
* Regarding the HARQ handling,
* the HARQ Process shall be released, if a new transmission is dropped
* if ReTx HARQ process is dropped due to the TP limit is exceeded, it shall be put for ReTx Scheduling so that the scheduler can pick it for retransmission in subsequent slots.In addition, the HARQ Tx counter shall be incremented even after dropping the reTx.
* All remaining UEs in DL/UL shall be stopped from being scheduled i.e.
* Remove/discard any PDCCH and PUCCH resources allocated to the remaining UEs for Tx/Rx in the current slot.
* Discard any updates done to any scheduling parameters that would be sent to the UE 'i' for this Tx/Rx (via PDCCH, such as NDI, rvIndex etc.)
* In UL, if any of the stopped UEs had UCI on PUSCH, allocate and schedule the PUCCH resource that has been reserved for UCI reception for that UE

Note: The UEs that are stopped from being scheduled can belong to any priority class i.e. there will be no sorting of the UEs based on traffic priority. For the purposes of the throughput pooling feature, based on simulation, the throughput constraint will be rarely exceeded hence, for the sake of simplicity, all UEs are considered to have equal priorities in case some UEs are to be dropped.

Note: If the PRB allocation for the current UE is reduced (also reduction due to rate matching (e.g. 5GC002538/CB008026, CB012269) , it shall be considered in the calculation of numRateMatchingResIE in all DlData\_PdschSendReqmessages.

[PR853223]Note: If the UEs being stopped from scheduling are UL MU MIMO UEs, the scheduling information of their paired UL MU MIMO UEs must also be updated.[End PR853223]

---

**3.31.6.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11215139`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Throughput Allowed Per Cell

---

**3.31.6.0-4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `12687482`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
If tddInstTputPoolingAllowed = TRUE (refer 5G\_RAN\_OP\_3986\_replaced(11693605)), the DL/UL scheduler of each cell receives the throughput capacity allocated by BBRM as allocDataPerSlot (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28790\_replaced(11214990)) in DL/UL respectively.

However, due to certain additional constraints at L1 with eCPRI 7-2a based configurations, the allocated throughput from BBRM shall be further reduced in UL by the scheduler of each cell in proportion to the number of PRBs used for PUCCH.

Thus, the throughput to be considered by the scheduler of each cell in DL/UL at each slot (allowedDataPerSlot) shall be calculated independently as below :

For UL:

If  slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE

allowedDataPerSlot(i, t) = allocDataPerSlot(i)

else

allowedDataPerSlot(i, t) = allocDataPerSlot(i) \* max(0, (1 - (numPrbToBeUsedForPucch(i, t) / (numAllocCellPrbUl(i) \* [Before CB015330-A]ulCellTpRedFactor [CB015330-A]ulCellTpRedFactorInSch[End CB015330-A]))))

end If

For DL:

allowedDataPerSlot(i, t) = allocDataPerSlot(i)

where :

* allowedDataPerSlot(i,t) is the throughput to be considered by the scheduler of cell 'i' in DL/UL in slot 't'
* allocDataPerSlot(i) is the throughput allocated by BBRM to the cell 'i' in DL/UL for the current pooling period (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28790\_replaced(11214990))
* numPrbToBeUsedForPucch(i, t) is the number of PRBs used for PUCCH in cell 'i' at slot 't' (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced(11196884), 5G\_L2\_11505\_replaced(11151739))
* numAllocCellPrbUl(i) is the number of PRBs allocated by BBRM  in UL to cell 'i' with the PRB pooling procedure in the current pooling period (refer numAllocCellPrb in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13411\_replaced(11212398))
* ulCellTpRedFactor is the throughput reduction factor for UL provided in NIDD bbPoolCapacity structure as NRBTS.bbPoolCapacity.ulCellTpRedFactor

[CB015330-A]

**- ulCellTpRedFactorInSch is the throughput reduction factor for UL, which is computed in (**[12688989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_eCvq4FZNEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

[End CB015330-A]

---

**3.31.6.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11215160`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Throughput Reduction for a Cell (DL/UL)

---

**3.31.6.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11215165`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
Reduce PRBs from UEs

---

**3.31.6.0-4.0-3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13453560`)

Slow Instantaneous Throughput Pooling
In order to reduce the used throughput in DL/UL for a cell, the DL/UL scheduler of the respective cell shall start reducing the number of allocated FD resources (i.e. PRB\_GRANULARITY in case of DL with RAT1 or PRBs in case of UL, RBGs otherwise) of the UE being scheduled currently until the throughput constraint (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29094\_replaced([11215125](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is satisfied. It should be noted that the number of resources that are reduced shall not be less than the minimum number of  resources that are required for DL/UL transmission (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21155\_replaced([11179648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku52LfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL; 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11483\_replaced([11196751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwE63PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11447\_replaced([11196591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwDsuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL).

where:

* PRB\_GRANULARITY is defined in 5G\_UP\_11022\_replaced([11350898](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubpjFvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and can vary depending on the type of slot and the type of beam forming used for the cell.

[PR836408]  
When transform precoding (TP) is enabled via MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/actUlDftSOfdm:

* The number of remaining PRBs for UL shall still fulfill the requirements as in [11101605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_0gbEmfvGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
* If the number remaining PRBs do not support anymore the requirements as in [11101605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_0gbEmfvGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), the UE shall be stopped from being scheduled, by considering the same actions as for the case that a reduction does not reduce the throughput to be within the throughput limit ([11215125](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0sPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

[End PR836408]

For UEs that are allocated partial RBGs, if reducing the number of PRBs in the partial RBG is enough to reduce the used throughput within the limit, these partial RBGs shall be prioritized for removal.

Note: partial RBGs will not be prioritized for removal if rrmUeAllowedPrb is less than 1 full RBG.

The minimum required PRBs for a UE is described below:

* minRequiredPrb = max{1, Minimum number of PRBs required for a PxSCH for the current UE considering all use cases such as MAC CEs, UCI (on PUSCH) etc.}

If the UE is allocated FD resources in RBGs

* minRequiredPrb = max {minRequiredPrb, min{(Number of PRBs in the partial first/last RBG, if it is  allocated to the UE), (Number of PRBs in 1 full RBG for the cell)}}

End if

---

## 3.31.7 L1 RIM RS detection capacity Pooling

### 3.31.7.1 L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling framework

#### 3.31.7.1.0-1 L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling framework L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling overview (ID: 11215191)

**3.31.7.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11215196`)

L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling framework
If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = true, L1 RS detection resource pooling is enabled for L1 RIM-RS detection capabilities.

To support dynamic L1 RIM-RS detection capacity pooling among cells of a L1 subpool, gNB-DU shall allocate the amount of usable L1 RIM-RS detection capacity available to the cell schedulers. At the same time, such central L1 RS detection capacity allocation avoids L1 overload.

The available pooled L1 RS detection capacity shall be shared between those cells with active requesting RIM RS detection resource (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24197\_replaced([11215205](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and mapped to the same L1 subpool.

gNB-DU shall re-evaluate the L1 RS detection capacity allocations for active RS detection cells within the L1 subpool once within a predefined  slow pooling window (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

L1 RS detection capacity allocated to cell schedulers shall only be valid for the entire duration of the next slow pooling window.

---

#### 3.31.7.1.0-2 L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling framework L1 RIM RS detection capacity resource (ID: 11215205)

**3.31.7.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11215212`)

L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling framework
~~If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = true~~~~,~~ gNB-DU shall maintain L1 RIM RS detection capacity resource which defined as below:

- If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = true, gNB-DU shall fetch proper Maximum RIM-RS detection resource units per L1 pool (L1RsPoolCap) corresponding to following configurations.

• if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/*numRbForRs = 48, L1RsPoolCap = NRBTS.*bbRimRsL1Capacity.maxResourcesPerL1PoolForFc48Prbs\*\*

• if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/*numRbForRs = 96,* L1RsPoolCap = NRBTS.**bbRimRsL1Capacity.maxResourcesPerL1PoolForFc96Prbs**

- gNB-DU shall fetch proper Maximum RIM-RS detection resource units per subcell (L1RsSubcellCap) corresponding to following configurations.

• if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/*numRbForRs = 48, L1RsSubcellCap = NRBTS.*bbRimRsL1Capacity.maxResourcesPerSubcellForFc48Prbs\*\*

• if NRBTS/NRCELL/NRRIM\_PROFILE/*numRbForRs = 96,* L1RsSubcellCap = NRBTS.**bbRimRsL1Capacity.maxResourcesPerSubcellForFc96Prbs**

---

#### 3.31.7.1.0-3 L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling framework RIM RS detection status of the cell (ID: 11215219)

**3.31.7.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11215225`)

L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling framework
If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = true**, and during a slow pooling window (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , gNB-DU shall request L1 RS detection capacity of each cell with following contents,**

~~- The RS detection Command, which shall be defined as RIM-RS detection status of the cell~~

~~o 0.. de-active RIM-RS detection~~

~~o 1..  active RIM-RS detection~~

~~o if no RS detection command in any slow pooling window, it shall be viewed as “0” case~~

**[Before CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- RS detection request weight, which shall be defined based on RIM-RS detection processing status of the cell

o 2..  the request for "ongoing" new RS detection during one RS period

o 1..  the request for "first" new RS detection during one RS period

o 0… no capacity request for new RS detection

**[CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- “new RS period” tag, defining RIM-RS detection processing status of the cell

o 1-true, the request for "first" new RS detection during one RS period

o 0-false, the request for "ongoing" new RS detection during one RS period

**[End CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- Minimum RS detection capacity request (minRsRequest, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24215\_replaced([11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

o the value of requested RS detection capacity that shall be guaranteed for RS detection in the cell

- maximum RS detection capacity request (maxRsRequest, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24217\_replaced([11161819](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

o the value of total requested RS detection capacity that shall be satisfied as much as possible for RS detection in the cell

gNB-DU shall maintain following RS detection status of one cell

* If the cell has the request with RS detection command  >=1, the cell shall be viewed as active cell from this slow pooling window onward
* If RS detection command =0, or no RS detection request, the cell shall be viewed as de-active RS detection Cell immediately.

**[Before CB011127-A-UPD001]- If NRBTS.actNrRimRsResourcePooling becomes "false"**,  all cells shall be viewed as de-active RS detection Cell immediately.**[End CB011127-A-UPD001]**\*\*\*\*
