#### 3.31.7.1.0-4 L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling framework history RIM RS detection allocation of the cell (not valid) (ID: 11215234)

**3.31.7.1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11215241`)

L1 RIM RS detection capacity pooling framework
[Before PR831007] If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = true**, upon the active RS detection request status from one cell (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), before allocating L1 RIM RS detection capacity to the cell schedulers, gNB-DU shall create or update history allocation record for that cell.**

- When the cell becomes active RS detection cell (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), its corresponding history allocation record shall be created and set as 0

- When gNB-DU allocated L1 RS detection capacity to the cell, the corresponding history allocation record shall be increment with the allocation result (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24202\_replaced([11215255](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- When one cell becomes de-active RS detection status (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , its corresponding history allocation record shall be set as 0.

[PR831007] note: this requirement is not valid any more [End PR831007]

---

### 3.31.7.2 allocation of L1 RIM RS detection capacity

#### 3.31.7.2.0-1 allocation of L1 RIM RS detection capacity allocation processing of L1 RS detection capacity (ID: 11215255)

**3.31.7.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11215264`)

allocation of L1 RIM RS detection capacity
**[Before CB011127-A-UPD001]If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = false**, gNB-DU shall use allocate L1 RS detection capacity (allocL1RsCap) with *L1RsSubcellCap (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24197\_replaced([11215205](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for each cell.**[End CB011127-A-UPD001]***\***\*

If NRBTS/actNrRimRsResourcePooling = true**, [Before CB011127-A-UPD001] during a slow pooling window (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), assuming each RS detection cells has single weight level of RS detection capacity request,**[CB011127-A-UPD001] for a target slow pooling window  (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6781\_replaced([11211947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-StfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), **[End** CB011127-A-UPD001] upon active RS detection capacity request from those RS detection cells (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , and depending on *L1RsPoolCap (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24197\_replaced([11215205](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall use following steps to allocate L1 RS detection capacity:****\****\*

1） gNB-DU shall set remaining L1 RS capacity (remainL1RsCap)as total L1 RS detection capacity, i.e. remainL1RsCap = L1RsPoolCap

2） gNB-DU shall set current RS detection capacity allocation of each cell (cell\_i) with 0, i.e. currentRsCap(cell\_i)=0.

**[Before CB011127-A-UPD001]**

3） gNB-DUshall first try to satisfy the minimum RS detection capacity requests for cells one by one.

gNB-DU shall loop those cells (cell\_i) with active RS detection request along the ascending order of their history allocation records (historyAllocRsCap(cell\_i), see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24201\_replaced([11215249](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 If there is valid minimum RS detection request (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall allocates cell\_i with   
allocResult(cell\_i, w) = min (remainL1RsCap , min.request (Cell\_i))

 update the history record of cell\_i, historyAllocRsCap(cell\_i) += allocResult(cell\_i, w)

 update remainL1RsCap -=allocResult(cell\_i, w) ;

 update the currentRsCap(cell\_i) += allocResult(cell\_i, w)

4） then, gNB-DU shall try to satisfy the maximum RS detection capacity requests for cells one by one.

gNB-DU shall loop those requests along the descending order of their requesting weights,

- In each weight, gNB-DU shall loop those cells with active RS detection request along the ascending order of their history allocation records (historyAllocRsCap(cell\_i)).

 If there is valid maximum RS detection request (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), gNB-DU shall allocates cell\_i with   
allocResult(cell\_i, w) = min (remainL1RsCap , RSGranularity\* (w==1), remainRequestRsCap(cell\_i))   
where

> RSGranularity shall be the measurement cost of one RS element in UL slot (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , which shall be considered only when weight =1 (corresponding to first RS detection request)
>
> remainRequestRsCap indicates the remaining RS detection request of the cell\_i need to be satisfied, and is calculated as

remainRequestRsCap(cell\_i) = min (maxRsCapRequest (cell\_i) , L1RsSubcellCap) - currentRsCap(cell\_i)

> L1RsSubcellCap can be given as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24197\_replaced([11215205](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
>
> maxRsRequest (cell\_i) can be seen in G\_UP\_ALG\_24206

 update the history record of cell\_i, historyAllocRsCap(cell\_i) += allocResult(cell\_i, w)

 update remainL1RsCap -=allocResult(cell\_i, w) ;

 update the currentRsCap(cell\_i) += allocResult(cell\_i, w)

- if (remainL1RsCap >0) OR remainRequestRsCap(cell\_i) >0 , gNB-DU shall continue looping cell regarding updated history allocation record and perform the same actions in step 4).

- final value of currentRsCap(cell\_i) shall be the final allocation result of RS detection capacity allocL1RsCap) for cell\_i.

5)

**[CB011127-A-UPD001]**

- gNB-DU shall firstly try to perform **Stable allocation for those cells with active RS detection request along the ascending of detection-waiting normal RS elements  (see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_24213\_replaced([11161791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

o if not a request for new RS period, gNB-DU shall allocates cell\_i with allocResult(cell\_i) = stableRsCap(cell\_i)

where, stableRsCap(cell\_i) is determined during maximum capacity allocation for the preceding new period

o update remainL1RsCap -=allocResult(cell\_i) ;

o update the currentRsCap(cell\_i) += allocResult(cell\_i)

- gNB-DU shall secondly try to perform **maximum capacity allocation for those cells with active RS detection request for new RS period, the allocation shall be performed by looping those cells as below:**

o active RS detection cells shall be sorted along the ascending order of detection-complete RS elements (see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_24213\_replaced([11161791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) firstly

o then active RS detection cells shall be sorted along the descending order of detection-waiting normal RS elements  (see  5G\_UP\_ALG\_24213\_replaced([11161791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) secondly

o In each time of allocation for each looped cell\_i ,  if the request is for new RS period (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , gNB-DU shall allocate cell\_i with allocResult(cell\_i) = min (remainL1RsCap , RSGranularity, remainRequestRsCap(cell\_i))

where

> RSGranularity shall be the measurement cost of one RS element in UL slot (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13194\_replaced([11162620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
>
> remainRequestRsCap indicates the remaining RS detection request of the cell\_i need to be satisfied, and is calculated as

remainRequestRsCap(cell\_i) = min (maxRsCapRequest (cell\_i) , L1RsSubcellCap) - currentRsCap(cell\_i)

> L1RsSubcellCap can be given as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24197\_replaced([11215205](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
>
> maxRsRequest (cell\_i) can be seen in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

 update remainL1RsCap -=allocResult(cell\_i) ;

 update the currentRsCap(cell\_i) += allocResult(cell\_i)

o if (remainL1RsCap >0) AND remainRequestRsCap(cell\_i) >0 , gNB-DU shall continue looping cells and perform above allocation. gNB-DU shall start from beginning after looping the last cell.

o The final value of currentRsCap(cell\_i) shall be the final allocation result of RS detection capacity allocL1RsCap) for cell\_i.

o The final currentRsCap(cell\_i) during **maximum capacity allocation shall be the  “stable allocation” for cell\_i during following ongoing RS detection resource allocation, as  stableRsCap(cell\_i) = currentRsCap(cell\_i) .**

- as the third allocation, gNB-DU shall try to satisfy the **minimum RS detection capacity requests for cells one by one. Purpose of this algorithm is to satisfy minimum requested allocation for as many cells as possible,  prioritizing cells by ascending order of detection-complete RS elements (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24201\_replaced([11215249](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

o gNB-DU shall loop those active RS detection cells (cell\_i) along the ascending order of detection-complete RS elements (further used as detectionOrder) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24201\_replaced([11215249](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxSbwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

o If the valid minimum RS detection request (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is higher than L1SubcellCap, i.e. min.request (cell\_i) > L1SubcellCap, for that cell\_i:

 min.request (cell\_i) = L1SubcellCap

o If the valid minimum RS detection request (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24206\_replaced([11215219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) that was not satisfied , i.e. min.request (Cell\_i)> currentRsCap(cell\_i), gNB-DU shall calculate for cell\_i:

 needed\_allocation (cell\_i) =min.request (Cell\_i)-currentRsCap(cell\_i)

[PR831007]

o firstly,to satisfy minimum RS detection request, gNB-DU shall  try to use remaining resources, if there are any:

 unusedResourcesToAlloc = min(needed\_allocation(cell\_i), reaminL1RsCap)

 currentRsCap(cell\_i) += unusedResourcesToAlloc

 remainL1RsCap -= unusedResourcesToAlloc

 needed\_allocation(cell\_i) -= unusedResourcesToAlloc

o secondly [End PR831007]  gNB-DU shall loop those cells (cell\_j, j ≠ i) with active RS detection request along the descending order of their detection-complete RS elements (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_24213\_replaced([11161791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv6_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

 If the needed\_allocation(cell\_i) > 0:

> If detectionOrder(cell\_i) < detectionOrder(cell\_j):
>
> > possible\_allocation(cell\_j) = min(needed\_allocation(cell\_i), currentRsCap(cell\_j))
>
> else (do not take resources from higher priority cell below needed\_allocation(cell\_j)):
>
> > possible\_allocation(cell\_j) = min(needed\_allocation(cell\_i), currentRsCap(cell\_j)-min.request (cell\_j))
>
> gNB-DU shall reduce RS capacity resource from cell\_j with: currentRsCap(cell\_j) -= possible\_allocation(cell\_j).
>
> gNB-DU shall assign RS capacity resource to cell\_i from cell\_j with currentRsCap(cell\_i) += possible\_allocation(cell\_j).
>
> gNB-DU shall update remaining needed allocation: needed\_allocation(cell\_i) -= possible\_allocation(cell\_j).

 After all cells (cell\_j) are relocated, if currentRsCap(cell\_i) < min.request (cell\_i), means there are no more resources to be relocated, algorithm should stop there.

[PR831007]

- as the fourth allocation, gNB-DU shall distribute the remaining L1 RS resources if there are any and if they are needed.

If remainL1RsCap > 0:

* + gNB-DU shall loop active RS detection cells (cell\_i) along the ascending order of detection-complete RS elements
* for cell\_i:
  + gNB-DU shall calculate the additional\_allocation(cell\_i) as
  + additional\_allocation(cell\_i) = min[maxRsRequest(cell\_i) + L1CapForExtraRevalid(cell\_i), L1RsSubcellCap] - currentRsCap(cell\_j)]  
    where
    - L1CapForExtraRevalid(cell\_i) is defined in [11161808](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVv7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)
    - L1RsSubcellCap can be given as [11215205](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0vPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)
  + additional\_allocation(cell\_i) = min[additional\_allocation(cell\_i), remainL1RsCap]
  + if additional\_allocation(cell\_i) > 0:
  + currentRsCap(cell\_j) += additional\_allocation(cell\_i)
  + remainL1RsCap -= additional\_allocation(cell\_i)
  + next, gNB-DU shall update stableRsCap(cell\_i):
    - stableRsCap(cell\_i) = min(maxRsRequest(cell\_i), currentRsCap(cell\_j))
  + if remainL1RsCap == 0, gNB-DU shall finish looping cells in this allocation step. [End PR831007]

**[End CB011127-A-UPD001]**

gNB-DU shall response the allocation result of RS detection capacity allocL1RsCap (= currentRsCap(cell\_i) ) to the cell\_i.

---

## 3.31.8 Power pooling

### 3.31.8.0-1 Power pooling Overview of Intra Power pooling procedure (ID: 13237755)

**3.31.8.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13242831`)

Power pooling
13242831:
Power pooling
To support dynamic power pooling among cells configured within a power pool (pwrPool) ,the BBRM (BaseBand Resource Manager) as part of L2RT shall allocate the pooled power resource to those [Before CB015284-C] TDD [End CB015284-C] cells sharing same Power Amplifiers (PAs)’ capabilities within a pwrPool, assuming the pwrPool was created with a unique power pool ID based on a power pooling cell set which was set to the same BB pool.

The power pooling algorithm doesn't cover those power pool cell sets which cannot be created as a power pool, or those individual cells not in any power pool cell sets.

The intra-power pooling aims to

* Most completely allocate sharable max pooling power resource among all power pool cells within a valid pwrPool.
* The power allocation results of intra-power pooling targets to ensure allocated power can satisfy PDSCH transmission on the allocated DL (layer) PRBs of the power pool cell with an available power spectral density ( PSD ) which is not lower than the minimum PSD configured by operator, and not higher than the target PSD determinate by RA capability configuration.
* Coordinate the PRB pooling and power pooling to avoid wasting allocated power resource due to less DL (layer) PRBs or wasting usable PRB due to lack of available power.
* allocate pooling power for PDSCH demand only, but depend on cell scheduler to determine further limitation for PDCCH .

NRBTS/actPwrPoolingTDD was introduced to control activation of the power pooling, and PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed is an internal activation flag sent from BOAM and used for TDD FR1 DL power pooling with eCPRI 7-2e. [CB015284-C] NRBTS/actPwrPoolingFDD was introduced and PwrPoolingFddAllowed is an internal activation flag sent from BOAM and used for FDD. [End CB015284-C]

If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], for each independent pwrPool created in the same BB pool , BBRM shall re-evaluate the pooled power allocations for cells inside the pwrPool (intra-power pooling) once within a predefined period, called the slow pooling window or bbPoolEvalPeriod given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod.

BBRM shall use the predefined timing to schedule the intra power pooling procedure aligning to the timing of PRB pooling ( see [13248843: Timing of intra power pooling procedure (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aJpBkcUKEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) )

Intra-power pooling algorithm shall initialize the properties of the pwrPool based on the newest applied configurations. (see [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))

BBRM shall firstly perform static round of allocation for the pwrPool if its own maximum pooled power can satisfy the maximum output power configuration of all its power pool cells (see [13244874: Intra Power pooling procedure with static allocation (static round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_gLRlFMNjEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) and skip the pwrPool from further intra-power pooling steps.

For remaining pwrPools, BBRM shall estimate power demand for each power pool cell (pwrPoolCell) in the pwrPool based on allocated PRB by PRB pooling allocation with minimum PSD principle, including

* before middle round and post round step start, BBRM shall estimate the minimum power demand based on the allocated PRB part for minimum PRB demand, see [13237734: Calculation of minimum power demand for the power pool cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0xiCQL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).

BBRM shall perform pooled power allocation interleaving to PRB pooling steps in either of below rounds :

* middle round: in the middle step of PRB pooling,
* after the non-GBR round-1 execution of PRB pooling for all L1 subpools, BBRM shall suspend the remaining execution of PRB pooling, BBRM shall perform the middle round of power pooling for those pwrPools in the BB pool,  as [13237745: Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (middle round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_TmBNsr-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).
* Independently for each pwrPool, BBRM shall estimate its additional power demand based on the remaining allocated PRB part excluding minimum PRB allocation, see [13237735: Calculation of additional power demand estimation for the power pool cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6D8XEL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).
* If its own maximum pooled power is not higher than total power demand,
  + BBRM shall execute power allocation for the pwrPool:
  + BBRM shall estimate and free excessive allocated PRB from the pwrPoolCell based on minimum PSD ([13237754: excess DL layer PRB amount of the power pool cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_HR_a0b-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)).
  + then BBRM shall return these excessive PRBs from the pwrPoolCell to its corresponding L1 subpool and skip all pwrPoolCells from further PRB pooling allocation.
  + BBRM shall skip the pwrPool from further intra-power pooling steps
* else, BBRM shall allow the pwrPool entering further intra-power pooling steps.
* post round :  if there are remaining pwrPools without middle round allocation after all the PRB pooling finished for all L1 subpools
* independently for each pwrPool, BBRM shall estimate its additional power demand based on the remaining allocated PRB part excluding minimum PRB allocation, see [13237735: Calculation of additional power demand estimation for the power pool cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6D8XEL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).
* BBRM shall perform the post round of power pooling ([13237746: Intra Power pooling procedure after the PRB pooling (post round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ZBCE4L-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) .
* BBRM shall estimate and free excessive allocated PRB from the pwrPoolCell based on minimum PSD ([13237754: excess DL layer PRB amount of the power pool cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_HR_a0b-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)).

After BBRM finished the post round of power pooling, all pwrPools finished power pooling allocation result of each pwrPoolCell, including:

* allocCellPwr
* updated numAllocCellLayerPrb [CB015284-C] in case of PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true or numAllocCellStreamPrb In case of PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C].

The flow of intra power pooling could be viewed as :  
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a power pooling process. The flowchart begins with a blue rectangle labeled "A valid power pool," followed by a yellow rectangle labeled "Initialization of properties."
A diamond shape, "MaxPoolPwr enough for total pMax ?", presents a decision point.
If the answer is "No," a red arrow leads to a yellow rectangle "Calculate Minimum power demand." From there, a dashed blue box encloses two yellow rectangles: "1) allocated the minimum amount of PRB;" and "PRB pooling nonGBR round 1, i.e, Round-1." A red arrow connects these two boxes and then leads to a larger dashed blue box.
If the answer to "MaxPoolPwr enough for total pMax ?" is "Yes," a red arrow leads to a yellow rectangle "Allocate pMax for pwrPoolCell," followed by a yellow rectangle "End power pooling."
The flowchart then branches into a section that appears to be a loop or a subsequent stage. A dashed blue box encloses a yellow rectangle "Calculate additional power demand." This is followed by another diamond shape, "MaxPoolPwr higher than total demand ?".
If the answer to "MaxPoolPwr higher than total demand ?" is "No," a blue arrow leads to a yellow rectangle "Allocate pooling power," then to "Estimate excessive PRB of pwrPoolCell," and finally to "End power pooling."
If the answer to "MaxPoolPwr higher than total demand ?" is "Yes," a red arrow leads to a larger dashed blue box. This box contains a yellow rectangle "For all L1 subpools of the L1 pool, i.e., Round-2." and another yellow rectangle "(last step) remaining PRB evenly allocated to the cells." A red arrow connects these two boxes and then leads to the same larger dashed blue box as the "No" branch from the previous decision point.
The flowchart also shows a connection from the "Calculate Minimum power demand" step to the "Calculate additional power demand" step.
The overall structure suggests a process of allocating power, potentially in rounds, with checks for sufficient power and subsequent adjustments based on demand.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/flow of intra power pooling.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

The intra power pooling allocation result will lead to constraints in pwrPoolCell scheduler (see [13237725: Constraints from intra Power Pooling (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FFE0I7-PEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))

In the same SFN of each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) during which BBRM sent the allocated DL layerPRB grant to the DL schedulers of the pwrPoolCell, BBRM shall send the allocated DL power results for the DL schedulers of the pwrPoolCell as well.

The allocation results sent to the cell schedulers shall be valid for usage only in the same valid duration as the valid allocated DL layerPRB grant result (see [13248843: Timing of intra power pooling procedure (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aJpBkcUKEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) .

---

### 3.31.8.0-2 Power pooling Timing of intra power pooling procedure (ID: 13248843)

**3.31.8.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13248844`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true for TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], BBRM shall use the following timing for the intra power pooling procedure reference to the timing of PRB pooling ([12711586: Enhanced Load Metric Based LayerPRB Overview (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XkY2tGa8EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g)) .

1) during the SFNs within a bbPoolingPeriod when BBRM determines the total amount of layerPRB granted[CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true, or the total amount of (sub)cellPRB granted if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], BBRM shall perform intra power pooling procedure (see [13237755: Overview of Intra Power pooling procedure (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_POZQsL-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))

2) At the SFN of a bbPoolingPeriod when BBRM sends back the allocation result to cell scheduler, BBRM shall also send back the power allocation results of the cell .

3) During the SFNs after receiving allocation results in current period and the SFNs of next period before next allocation received, as the duration of the current PRB allocation result is available as the usable resource limit, the cell scheduler shall consider the current power allocation results be available as the usable power resource limit.

---

### 3.31.8.0-3 Power pooling Initialization of intra power pooling (ID: 13237732)

**3.31.8.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13242812`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true for TDD FR1 eCPRI 7-2e [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true[End CB015284-C], during the startup time, BBRM shall learn the power pool (pwrPool) and its properties.

For each pwrPool which was created from a power pool cell sets within the BB pool:

* pwrPoolId, the ID of the power pool, given by NRBTS/NRPWRPOOL/pwrPoolId.
* maxPoolPwr [dBm], Maximum power per TRX which can be used by the power pool and allocated to the cells within the power pooling, given by NRBTS/NRPWRPOOL/maxPoolPwr.
* pwrPoolCellList, the cells which are members of this power pool (pwrPoolCell), given by the current configuration of NRBTS/NRPWRPOOL/pwrPoolCellList.
* NumOfTrx, the number of TRXs for the cell, which is calculated as ：
* If NRCELL.actBeamforming = true,  NumOfTrx = ruNumOfTrxInRow \* ruNumOfTrxInColumn,
  + where  ruNumOfTrxInRow, ruNumOfTrxInColumn can be fetched from bfsetup structure in [11053298: bfSetup structure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BB1LCf_KEe-D3seUwaI0tg?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_NS8shu3xEe-rL47x_rCCmw)  [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true,  else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true, then in  [12560468: bfSetupFdd structure content [ 12679724]](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_yGVbMio-EfCNjfqfyUlvmw?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_NS8shu3xEe-rL47x_rCCmw) [End CB015284-C].
* else  NRCELL.actBeamforming =false,  NumOfTrx is given by the value of DL of NRCELL.nrCellType, e.g.  NumOfTrx =4 if NRCELL.nrCellType=4DL2UL .
* For each power pool cell (pwrPoolCell) in the pwrPoolCellList of the pwrPool:
* NrCelIId, the Cell ID of the cell member within the power pool, given by NRBTS/NRPWRPOOL/pwrPoolCellList.NrCelIId.
* minPSD[W/MHz], the minimum PSD combined with all TRX of the cell required by the customer, given by NRBTS/NRPWRPOOL/pwrPoolCellList.minPSD.
  + note: assumption has been ensured at NIDD configuration, that minPSD shall not exceed the level of maximum output power over the system bandwidth[mHz].
* pMax[dBm], the maximum output power per TRX configured for the pwrPoolCell in the power pool, given by NRBTS/NRCEL/pMax of the cell.
* BBRM shall calculate PSD configuration for used in power pooling algorithm
  + minPsdOfCellPrb, indicates the minimum power [mw] per TRX which can be used on the cell DL PRB, see [13237741: Calculation of Minimum PSD for cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DQeioL-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
  + minPsdOfLayerPrb, the minimum power [mw] per TRX which can be used on the cell DL layer PRB , calculated as[13237742: Conversion between Minimum PSD for layer PRB (minPSDOfLayerPrb) and cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_IvDEJb-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) [CB015284-C] If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true.
  + else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true, minPsdOfStreamPrb, the minimum power [mw] per TRX which can be used on the cell DL stream PRB, calculated as  [13387710: Conversion between Minimum PSD for stream PRB (minPSDOfSteamPrb) and cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_EqG6QgKJEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew) [End CB015284-C].

---

### 3.31.8.0-4 Power pooling Calculation of power spectral density (PSD) for the power pool cell (ID: 13242866)

**3.31.8.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13237741`)

Power pooling
Calculation of Minimum PSD for cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb)

---

**3.31.8.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13237865`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], during initialization phase for the power pool (pwrPool) in [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jCM5wb-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) , BBRM shall calculate the minimum PSD for the cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) that indicates the minimum power level (in unit of [mw]) per TRX used on a cell DL PRB for the power pool cell (pwrPoolCell). The calculation is as below:

minPSDOfCellPrb[mw/cellPrb] = min( targetPsdOfCellPrb, minPSD*1000* chBw[MHz]/(NumOfTrx \*NDLPRB) )

Where，

* minPSD [W/MHz] from [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* chBW[MHz] is the system bandwidth of the pwrPoolCell, given by NRCELL/chBw.
* NDLPRBis the number of cell DL PRB corresponding to the system bandwidth, seen in [11094258: Bandwidth Configuration (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmaoiPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)
* NumOfTrx is the number of TRXs for the cell, seen in [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* targetPsdOfCellPrb is the target power level (in unit of [mw]) on a cell DL PRB from [13244478: calculation of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_t3FsscLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

---

**3.31.8.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13237742`)

Power pooling
Conversion between Minimum PSD for layer PRB (minPSDOfLayerPrb) and cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb)

---

**3.31.8.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13237872`)

Power pooling
If NPwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true, during initialization of intra power pooling procedure in each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod), for each power pool cell in the pwrPool, BBRM shall use below algorithm to convert between the minimum PSD for the layer PRB (minPSDOfLayerPrb) and the minimum PSD for the Cell DL PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) :

* minPSDOfLayerPrb= min ( targetPsdOfLayerPrb, minPSDOfCellPrb/maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb )
* minPSDOfCellPrb= min ( targetPsdOfCellPrb,  minPSDOfLayerPrb \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb )
* Where,
* minPSDOfCellPrb is the minimum power level [mw] per TRX of a cell DL PRB from [13237741: Calculation of Minimum PSD for cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DQeioL-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).
* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is the max number of layers per cell PRB from [11214135: Max number of layers per cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* targetPsdOfLayerPrb is the target power level [mw] on a cell layer PRB from [13244478: calculation of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_t3FsscLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* targetPsdOfCellPrb is the target power level [mw] on a cell PRB from [13244478: calculation of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_t3FsscLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

**3.31.8.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `13387710`)

Power pooling
Conversion between Minimum PSD for stream PRB (minPSDOfSteamPrb) and cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb)

---

**3.31.8.0-4.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13387711`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingFddAllowed = true, during initialization of intra power pooling procedure in each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod), for each power pool cell in the pwrPool, BBRM shall use below algorithm to convert between the minimum PSD for the stream PRB and the minimum PSD for the Cell DL PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) :

* minPSDOfstreamPrb=min(targetPsdOfCellPrb,minPSDOfCellPrb )/ maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb
* minPSDOfCellPrb= min( targetPsdOfCellPrb, minPSDOfStreamPrb \* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb )
* Where,
* minPSDOfCellPrb is the minimum power level [mw] per TRX of a cell DL PRB from [13237741: Calculation of Minimum PSD for cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DQeioL-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).
* maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb is from  [11211964: Conversion Between Cell-PRB and Stream PRB](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ON0rUPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)
* targetPsdOfCellPrb is the target power level [mw] on a cell PRB from [13244478: calculation of target PSD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_t3FsscLSEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

### 3.31.8.0-5 Power pooling Calculation of power demand for intra-power pooling (ID: 13242867)

**3.31.8.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13237734`)

Power pooling
Calculation of minimum power demand for the power pool cell

---

**3.31.8.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13237878`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], during intra power pooling procedure in each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod), before middle round and post round of power pooling allocation, for the power pool cell (pwrPoolCell) with a unique NrCelIId in the pwrPool, BBRM shall calculate its minimum power demand (MinPwrDmd) based on its allocated PRB result in the step of minimum PRB resource allocation , as below:

* As preconditions:
* BBRM shall initialize the MinPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell) as 0.
* BBRM shall finish the minimum PRB resource allocation for all L1 SubPool (see [11214316: Allocation of the configured minimum resource per Cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_aGdtQfvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with result of numAllocCellLayerPrb for each pwrPoolCell [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed=true .
* else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true, BBRM shall finish the minimum PRB resource allocation for all L1 SubPool (see [11212500: Allocation of the configured minimum resource per Cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_Q9yRgPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), with result of numAllocCellStreamPrb for each pwrPoolCell [End CB015284-C].
* before middle round and post round of power pooling allocation starts ([13237755: Overview of Intra Power pooling procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_R33NUL-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))
* [CB015284-C] If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true ,  [End CB015284-C] BBRM shall calculate MinPwrDmd of the pwrPoolCell based on its numAllocCellLayerPrb from the minimum PRB resource allocation:

minPwrDmd( pwrPoolCell ) = numAllocCellLayerPrb( pwrPoolCell ) \* minPSDOfLayerPrb( pwrPoolCell )

* where
* minPSDOfLayerPrb, the minimum PSD which can be used on a cell layer DL PRB from [13237742: Conversion between Minimum PSD for layer PRB (minPSDOfLayerPrb) and cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_IxhJVL-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* [CB015284-C] else If PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true, BBRM shall calculate MinPwrDmd of the pwrPoolCell based on its numAllocCellStreamPrb from the minimum PRB resource allocation:   
   minPwrDmd( pwrPoolCell ) = numAllocCellStreamPrb( pwrPoolCell ) \* minPSDOfStreamPrb( pwrPoolCell )  
  •   where
* minPSDOfStreamPrb, the minimum PSD which can be used on a cell stream DL PRB from  [13387710: Conversion between Minimum PSD for stream PRB (minPSDOfSteamPrb) and cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CawGxwKJEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew)  [End CB015284-C]

---

**3.31.8.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13237735`)

Power pooling
Calculation of additional power demand for the power pool cell

---

**3.31.8.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13237902`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], during the middle round or the post round of intra power pooling in each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod), for the power pool cell (pwrPoolCell) within the pwrPool, BBRM shall calculate its additional power demand (AddPwrDmd).

* In the middle round ([13237745: Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (middle round) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TjMjML-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) , BBRM shall calculate AddPwrDmd based on the allocation result (numAllocCellLayerPrb) from additional PRB resource allocation from [12711600: Allocation of additional LayerPRB per Cell based on non-GBR demand and Load (Round-1)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gKBk4Wa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [CB015284-C] in case of PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true, else based on the allocation result (numAllocCellStreamPrb) from additional PRB resource allocation from ([11212737: Allocation of additional stream-PRB per cell based on RIM PRB demand](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_SM2FoPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C],
* In the post round ([13237746: Intra Power pooling procedure after the PRB pooling (post round) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YtwjmL-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) : BBRM shall calculate AddPwrDmd based on the final PRB allocation result (numAllocCellLayerPrb)  of PRB pooling [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true, else based on the final allocation result (numAllocCellStreamPrb) if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C].

In either above case,

[CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true, [End CB015284-C]

* BBRM shall set AddPwrDmd (NrCelIId ) as 0 before the calculation.
* then BBRM shall calculate its value based on the corresponding PRB allocation result numAllocCellLayerPrb of the power pool cell :

AddPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell)=numAllocCellLayerPrb(pwrPoolCell)\* minPSDOfLayerPrb(pwrPoolCell)-minPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell)

where

* minPSDOfLayerPrb is the minimum power which can be used on a cell layer DL PRB for the power pool cell, from [13237741: Calculation of Minimum PSD for cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DQeioL-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).
* minPwrDmd is the minimum power demand of the power pool cell, calculated in [13237734: Calculation of minimum power demand for the power pool cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0xiCQL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

[CB015284-C]  else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed = true,

* BBRM shall set AddPwrDmd (NrCelIId ) as 0 before the calculation.
* then BBRM shall calculate its value based on the corresponding PRB allocation result numAllocCellStreamPrb of the power pool cell :

AddPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell)=numAllocCellStreamPrb(pwrPoolCell)\* minPSDOfStreamPrb(pwrPoolCell)-minPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell)

where

* minPSDOfStreamPrb is the minimum power which can be used on a cell stream DL PRB for the power pool cell, from  [13387710: Conversion between Minimum PSD for stream PRB (minPSDOfSteamPrb) and cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CawGxwKJEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew).
* minPwrDmd is the minimum power demand of the power pool cell, calculated in  [13237734: Calculation of minimum power demand for the power pool cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0xiCQL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) [End CB015284-C]

---

**3.31.8.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13237737`)

Power pooling
Calculation of total power demand for the Power Pool Cell

---

**3.31.8.0-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13237942`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], during intra power pooling procedure in each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod), for the pwrPoolCell in the pwrPool, BBRM shall calculate its total power demand (TotalCellPwrDmd) as below,

TotalCellPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell )=MinPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell )+AddPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell )

where

MinPwrDmd is the minimum power demand of the pwrPoolCell , from [13237734: Calculation of minimum power demand for the power pool cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0xiCQL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

AddPwrDmd is additional power demand of the pwrPoolCell , from [13237735: Calculation of additional power demand estimation for the power pool cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6D8XEL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

**3.31.8.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `13237739`)

Power pooling
Calculation of total power demand for the Power Pool

---

**3.31.8.0-5.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13237948`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], during intra power pooling procedure in each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod) , for the pwrPool created with a unique pwrPoolId, BBRM shall calculate the total power demand (TotalPoolPwrDmd) by summing up all the power demand of its belonging power pool cell (pwrPoolCell), as below:

TotalPoolPwrDmd(pwrPool)=Sum(TotalCellPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell))

where,

TotalCellPwrDmd indicates the total power demand of the pwrPoolCell, calculated in [13237737: Calculation of total power demand for the Power Pool Cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tv8bML-REfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

### 3.31.8.0-6 Power pooling Intra Power pooling procedure (ID: 13242868)

**3.31.8.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `13244874`)

Power pooling
Intra Power pooling procedure with static allocation (static round)

---

**3.31.8.0-6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13244875`)

Power pooling
If NPwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], during initialization phase for the power pool (pwrPool)  in each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod), BBRM shall perform static allocation for the pwrPool whose maxPwrPool can satisfy the maximum output power configuration of all belonging power pool cells (pwrPoolCell).

As the preconditions, BBRM shall perform initialization for the pwrPool (see [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), and provides the configuration of pMax of each pwrPoolCell and maximum pooled power configuration (maxPwrPool) for the pwrPool.

* Step1: BBRM shall calculate total maximum output power configuration of the pwrPool (TotalPMaxOfPwrPool), as
* TotalPMaxOfPwrPool [mw] = sum ( 10^(0.1\*pMax(pwrPoolCell) ))
* Step2: BBRM shall compare TotalPMaxOfPwrPool to maxPwrPool for the pwrPool and determine whether to allocate pooled power to satisfy the pMax of each pwrPoolCell.
* calculate remaining Pool Power : remainPoolPwr[mw] = 10^(0.1\*maxPwrPool);
* if TotalPMaxOfPwrPool < = remainPoolPwr , then for each pwrPoolCell, BBRM shall set allocCellPwr (pwrPoolCell) = 10^(0.1\*pMax(pwrPoolCell) )

If the pwrPool was performed by successful static round of allocation, BBRM shall skip it from the following rounds of intra-power pooling procedures ( seen in [13237755: Overview of Intra Power pooling procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_R33NUL-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)).

---

**3.31.8.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13237745`)

Power pooling
Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (middle round)

---

**3.31.8.0-6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13387824`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true[End CB015284-C], during each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod), BBRM shall use following procedures for the power pool (pwrPool) in the middle step of PRB pooling procedure (middle round) :

As the preconditions,

* BBRM shall determine minimum power demand for each pwrPoolCell (see [13237734: Calculation of minimum power demand for the power pool cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0xiCQL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)).
* BBRM shall ensure PRB pooling finished allocation for all L1 subpools in the step of[12711600: Allocation of additional LayerPRB per Cell based on non-GBR demand and Load (Round-1)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_gKBk4Wa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true , else in the step of [12710038: Enhanced non-GBR demand- and load-based allocation (Round-1)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_HIjHsWX-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g) if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C],
* and BBRM shall suspend the PRB pooling incoming allocation step in[12711601: Allocation of Remaining LayerPRB per Cell (Round-2)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq29gGa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true , else suspend the PRB pooling in the step of ([12707889: Allocation of any remaining stream-PRB per cell based on non-GBR Load (Round-2)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ryyIIGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA)) if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true  [End CB015284-C] before BBRM starts the middle round of intra power pooling procedure:

The middle round of intra power pooling procedure:

Step1: BBRM shall determine additional power demand for each pwrPoolCell (see [13237735: Calculation of additional power demand for the power pool cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6D8XEL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)).

if the TotalPoolPwrDmd of the pwrPool (from [13237739: Calculation of total power demand for the Power Pool (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_hrgXIL-REfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) is equal to or higher than the maximum pooling power (need to convert unit to [mw]) (see in [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) , BBRM shall execute power pooling allocation for the pwrPool as below:

* Step2: BBRM shall allocate remaining pooled power for each pwrPoolCell (see [13237751: Power pooling allocation for the power pool (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_7wiJ0L-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))
* Step3: BBRM shall estimate and free the excessive layer PRBs and update the numAllocCellLayerPrb of each pwrPoolCell [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true , else BBRM shall estimate and free the excessive stream PRBs and update the numAllocCellStreamPrb of each pwrPoolCell (from [12707005: Enhanced Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm Overview](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_yUqFsGJSEfC3KtQ77je1xA)) if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true, as [End CB015284-C] [13237754: excess DL PRB amount of the power pool cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_HR_a0b-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* Step4:BBRM shall update the L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare for the pwrPoolCell's corresponding L1 SubPool with the freed excessive layer PRBs ([12711586: Enhanced Load Metric Based LayerPRB Overview](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_XoJVUWa8EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g)) [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true , else BBRM shall update the L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare of each pwrPoolCell if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true. [End CB015284-C].
* Step5:BBRM shall resume the PRB pooling allocation step in[12711601: Allocation of Remaining LayerPRB per Cell (Round-2)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq29gGa-EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed =true , else in ([12707889: Allocation of any remaining stream-PRB per cell based on non-GBR Load (Round-2)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ryyIIGLWEfC3KtQ77je1xA)) if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true. [End CB015284-C]
* finally :
* BBRM shall exclude all pwrPoolCells from remaining PRB allocation procedure for their corresponding L1 subPools.finally,
* BBRM shall skip the pwrPool with execution of power allocation from further power pooling steps (in [13237755: Overview of Intra Power pooling procedure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_R33NUL-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))

---

**3.31.8.0-6.0-3**  (ID: `13237746`)

Power pooling
Intra Power pooling procedure after the PRB pooling (post round)

---

**3.31.8.0-6.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13388145`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], during each bbPoolingPeriod (given by NRBTS.bbPoolEvalPeriod), for the pwrPool without execution of middle round of power allocation ([13237745: Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (middle round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_TmBNsr-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) ,  BBRM shall apply post round of intra power pooling procedures for the power pool (pwrPool)

As the preconditions:

* BBRM shall determine minimum power demand for each pwrPoolCell in the pwrPool(see [13237734: Calculation of minimum power demand for the power pool cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_06-5ML-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))
* BBRM shall finish final step of PRB pooling allocation for all L1SubPools [11214436: Allocation of remaining layerPRB per cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_apPDIPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ) [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed=true, else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true as ([11212760: Enhanced allocation of any remaining stream-PRB per cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_SVKUIPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  [End CB015284-C].

BBRM shall perform the post round of intra-Power pooling:

Step1: BBRM shall determine additional power demand for each pwrPoolCell in the pwrPool (see [13237735: Calculation of additional power demand for the power pool cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_85eZwL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))

Step2: BBRM shall perform power pooling allocation for the pwrPool (see [13237751: Power pooling allocation for the power pool](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_717nML-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))

step3: BBRM shall estimate and free the excessive layer PRBs and update the numAllocCellLayerPrb of each pwrPoolCell [CB015284-C] if PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed=true, else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true BBRM shall estimate and free the excessive stream PRBs and update the numAllocCellStreamPrb of each pwrPoolCell [End CB015284-C] in [13237754: excess DL PRB amount of the power pool cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_HR_a0b-TEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).

---

**3.31.8.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `13237751`)

Power pooling
Power pooling allocation for the power pool

---

**3.31.8.0-6.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13388172`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], during the determination of power pooling period  (see [13248843: Timing of intra power pooling procedure (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_aJpBkcUKEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)), in the step of [13237745: Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TjMjML-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) or in the step of [13237746: Intra Power pooling procedure after the PRB pooling (post round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ZBCE4L-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ), BBRM shall allocate pooled power for every pwrPoolCell belonging to the power pool (pwrPool) step by step based on the minimum power demand and additional power demand of the pwrPoolCell, as below:

* BBRM shall reset the intermediate variables for the pwrPool at the beginning of allocation, including:
* The remaining pooled power for the pwrPool   
  remainPoolPwr [mw] = 10^ (0.1 \* maxPoolPwr[dBm])
* The maximum power capability for every pwrPoolCell in the pwrPool  
  [Before CB014923-C-UPD003] maxPwr(pwrPoolCell) [CB014923-C-UPD003] maxPwrCap(pwrPoolCell) [End CB014923-C-UPD003][mw] = 10^(0.1\* pMax(pwrPoolCell))
* [CB014923-C-UPD003] The maximum usable power for every pwrPoolCell in the pwrPool to ensure target PSD used for allocated DL PRB :   
  If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true  
   maxUsablePwr(pwrPoolCell) [mw] = maxPwrCap(pwrPoolCell) \* numAllocCellLayerPrb ( pwrPoolCell) / （ NDLPRB \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb） [End CB014923-C-UPD003]   
  [CB015284-C-UPD001] Else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true  
  maxUsablePwr(pwrPoolCell) [mw] = maxPwrCap(pwrPoolCell) \* numAllocCellStreamPrb ( pwrPoolCell) / （ NDLPRB \* maxNumberOfStreamCellPrb） [End CB015284-C-UPD001]
* where,  
  pMax(pwrPoolCell) is from [13237732: Initialization of intra power pooling](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_jESkcL-QEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ).  
  [CB014923-C-UPD003] maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is the max number of layers per cell PRB from [11214135: Max number of layers per cell](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ZTKBAPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ)  
  [CB015284-C-UPD001] maxNumberOfStreamPerCellPrb is from [11211964: Conversion Between Cell-PRB and Stream PRB](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ON0rUPvREe-AqvopbP1qhQ) [End CB015284-C-UPD001],  
  NDLPRB  is the number of cell DL PRB corresponding to the system bandwidth, seen in [11094258: Bandwidth Configuration](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_yYrKYPvFEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) [End CB014923-C-UPD003]
* total additional power demand for the pwrPool, AddPoolPwrDmd = 0;
* For every pwrPoolCell, BBRM resets 0 for below variables:
* Total allocated power for the cell, allocCellPwr(pwrPoolCell) =0;
* Allocated power for minimum power demand of the pwrPoolCell, allocMinPwr =0;
* Allocated power for additional power demand of the pwrPoolCell, allocAddPwr =0;
* [CB014923-C-UPD003] If remaining pooled power resources are more or equal to total maximum usable power of all pwrPoolCells, i.e. all remainPoolPwr [mw] >= sum(maxUsablePwr(N>k>=0)), then BBRM shall allocate pooled power equal to maximum usable power for each cell.
* Else, [End CB014923-C-UPD003]
* BBRM shall sort the pwrPoolCelllist in descending order of the total power demand of each pwrPoolcell (see [13237737: Calculation of total power demand estimation for the Power Pool Cell (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tv8bML-REfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))
* BBRM shall stop below allocation steps when remainPoolPwr becomes 0.
* step 1: BBRM shall allocate remaining pooled DL power resource (remainPoolPwr) to satisfy the minimum power demand of the pwrPoolCell one by one.
  + For each pwrPoolCell, if remainPoolPwr>0,
  + BBRM shall calculate the actual minimum power allocation for the minPwrDmd with considering the remaining pooled power resource
    - allocMinPwr(pwrPoolCell)=min(minPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell), remainPoolPwr)
  + BBRM shall update the Total allocated power for the pwrPoolCell,
    - allocCellPwr(pwrPoolCell) += allocMinPwr(pwrPoolCell)
  + BBRM shall update the remaining Pooled power
    - remainPoolPwr -= allocMinPwr(pwrPoolCell)
* step2: BBRM shall allocate remaining pooled DL power (remainPoolPwr) in proportion to the additional power demand of the pwrPoolCells.  
  If remainPoolPwr>0,
  + BBRM shall sort the pwrPoolCells [CB014923-C-UPD003]with addPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell)>0[End CB014923-C-UPD003] in ascending order of the pwrPoolCell's metric equal to min ( ([Before CB014923-C-UPD003] maxPwr(pwrPoolCell)[CB014923-C-UPD003] maxUsablePwr(pwrPoolCell) [End CB014923-C-UPD003] - allocCellPwr(pwrPoolCell) ), addPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell) )
  + for each pwrPoolCell(i) along the sorting list[N], where N is the total number of the cell members in the pwrPool.
  + BBRM shall calculate the proportion for each pwrPoolCell=i among all un-allocated pwrPoolCells (index is from i to N):
    - PropOfAddPwr(pwrPoolCell) = addPwrDmd(pwrPoolCell) / sum[N>k>=i](addPwrDmd(k))
  + BBRM shall calculate the actual power allocation based on the proportion and considering the [Before CB014923-C-UPD003] maxPwr[CB014923-C-UPD003] maxUsablePwr [End CB014923-C-UPD003] limitation
    - allocAddPwr (pwrPoolCell) = min( ([Before CB014923-C-UPD003] maxPwr(pwrPoolCell)[CB014923-C-UPD003] maxUsablePwr (pwrPoolCell)[End CB014923-C-UPD003] - allocCellPwr (pwrPoolCell) ) ,  remainPoolPwr \* PropOfAddPwr(pwrPoolCell)   )
  + BBRM shall update the total allocated power for the pwrPoolCell,
    - allocCellPwr (pwrPoolCell) += allocAddPwr (pwrPoolCell)
  + BBRM shall update the remaining pooled power
    - remainPoolPwr -= allocAddPwr (pwrPoolCell)
* [CB014923-C-UPD003] Then, if remainPoolPwr>0, BBRM shall allocate remaining pooled DL power (remainPoolPwr) in proportion to the remaining power capability of the pwrPoolCells.
* BBRM shall sort the pwrPoolCells in ascending order of the pwrPoolCell's remaining power capability (remainCellPwrCap) excluding those pwrPoolCells remainCellPwrCap<=0
  + remainCellPwrCap = maxPwrCap (pwrPoolCell) - allocCellPwr(pwrPoolCell) ))
* for each pwrPoolCell along the sorting list,
  + if remainCellPwrCap(pwrPoolCell)>0, BBRM shall calculate the proportion for each pwrPoolCell:   
    PropOfRemainPwr(pwrPoolCell) = remainCellPwrCap (pwrPoolCell) / sum[N>k>=i](remainCellPwrCap (k))
  + BBRM shall calculate the actual power allocation based on the proportion and considering the maxPwrCap limitation:  
    allocRemainPwr (pwrPoolCell) = min( (maxPwrCap (pwrPoolCell) - allocCellPwr (pwrPoolCell) ) ,  remainPoolPwr \* PropOfRemainPwr (pwrPoolCell) )
  + BBRM shall update the total allocated power for the pwrPoolCell,   
    allocCellPwr (pwrPoolCell) += allocRemainPwr (pwrPoolCell)
  + BBRM shall update the remaining pooled power   
    remainPoolPwr -= allocRemainPwr (pwrPoolCell) .[End CB014923-C-UPD003]

Note: finally it's possible that the pooling power wasting exists.

---

**3.31.8.0-6.0-5**  (ID: `13237754`)

Power pooling
excess DL PRB amount of the power pool cell

---

**3.31.8.0-6.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13388173`)

Power pooling
If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [CB015284-C] or PwrPoolingFddAllowed =true [End CB015284-C], during intra power pooling determination procedure and in the middle round  ([13237745: Intra Power pooling procedure in the middle step of PRB pooling (middle round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_TmBNsr-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)) or post round ([13237746: Intra Power pooling procedure after the PRB pooling (post round)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_ZBCE4L-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ))for a power pool (pwrPool), BBRM shall estimate and free the excessive PRBs from each pwrPoolCell:

For each cell in the pwrPool,

[CB015284-C] If PwrPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eAllowed = true [End CB015284-C]

* BBRM shall calculate its excess DL cell layer PRB amount:
* ExcessAllocLayerPrb (pwrPoolCell)=max⁡(0, numAllocCellLayerPrb(pwrPoolCell)- rounddown( AllocCellPwr (pwrPoolCell) / minPsdOfLayerPrb(pwrPoolCell) )
* Where,
  + AllocCellPwr is the allocated power for the pwrPoolCell in [13237751: Power pooling allocation for the power pool](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_717nML-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
  + numAllocCellLayerPrb of the pwrPoolCell is from[12711586: Enhanced Load Metric Based LayerPRB Overview](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_XoJVUWa8EfCwWbD4x7Iu-g)
  + minPsdOfLayerPrb is from [13237741: Calculation of Minimum PSD for cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_DQeioL-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
* then, BBRM shall free the excessive DL layer PRB from the pwrPoolCell
* numAllocCellLayerPrb (pwrPoolCell) -= ExcessAllocLayerPrb (pwrPoolCell)
* BBRM shall return the freed layer PRBs to the pwrPoolCell's corresponding L1 subpool:
* L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare + = ExcessAllocLayerPrb (pwrPoolCell)

Note: finally it's possible that the pooling PRB wasting (L1SpPoolLayerPrbToShare > 0) exists.

[CB015284-C] else if PwrPoolingFddAllowed = true

* BBRM shall calculate its excess DL cell stream PRB amount:
* ExcessAllocStreamPrb (pwrPoolCell)=max⁡(0, numAllocCellStreamPrb(pwrPoolCell)- rounddown( AllocCellPwr (pwrPoolCell) / minPsdOfStreamPrb(pwrPoolCell) )
* Where,
  + AllocCellPwr is the allocated power for the pwrPoolCell in [13237751: Power pooling allocation for the power pool](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_717nML-SEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)
  + numAllocCellStreamPrb of the pwrPoolCell is from [12707005: Enhanced Load Metric Based PRB Pooling Algorithm Overview](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_yUqFsGJSEfC3KtQ77je1xA)
  + minPsdOfStreamPrb is from [13387710: Conversion between Minimum PSD for stream PRB (minPSDOfSteamPrb) and cell PRB (minPSDOfCellPrb) (In Module: 5G UP Algorithms)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CawGxwKJEfGhFrIQm2O4Ew)
* then, BBRM shall free the excessive DL Stream PRB from the pwrPoolCell
* numAllocCellStreamPrb (pwrPoolCell) -= ExcessAllocStreamPrb (pwrPoolCell)
* BBRM shall return the freed layer PRBs to the pwrPoolCell's corresponding L1 subpool:
* L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare + = ExcessAllocStreamPrb (pwrPoolCell)

Note: finally Pooled PRB waste may exist (L1SpPoolStreamPrbToShare > 0).  [End CB015284-C]

---

### 3.31.9.0-19 R&amp;D Parameters rdPrbPoolingTypicalUsage T dd **** (ID: 12879244)

**3.31.9.0-19.0-2**  (ID: `13491726`)

R&D Parameters
rdZabOptimization

---

**3.31.9.0-19.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13491727`)

R&D Parameters
This parameter, rdZabOptimization, enables/disables the ZAB optimization solution.

default: 3     Online modificable. Step Size: 1[0..3], Online Modifiable: Yes"

0 - disabled,

1 - enable single csiRsPoolingGroup active solution,

2 - enable two csiRsPoolingGroups active solution,

3 - enable Both, one or two csiRsPoolingGroups active solution.

---
